FILE: SemanticMetadataNormalizer.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog.semantics;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.common.Semantic;

import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class SemanticMetadataNormalizer {
  private SemanticMetadataNormalizer() {}

  public static Semantic normalize(
      Semantic semantic,
      Semantic.Type inferredType,
      String assetGroup,
      String assetName) {
    Semantic.Type semanticType = inferredType == null ? Semantic.Type.DOCUMENT : inferredType;
    String normalizedGroup = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(assetGroup), "platform");
    String normalizedName = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(assetName), "unknown");
    String assetId = normalizedGroup + "/" + normalizedName;

    Semantic base = semantic;

    String title = SemanticValues.text(base == null ? null : base.title(), normalizedName);
    String description =
        SemanticValues.text(base == null ? null : base.description(), "TODO: describe " + assetId);
    String businessMeaning =
        SemanticValues.text(
            base == null ? null : base.businessMeaning(),
            "TODO: define business meaning for " + assetId);
    String domain = SemanticValues.text(base == null ? null : base.domain(), "default");
    String subdomain = SemanticValues.text(base == null ? null : base.subdomain(), "default");
    List<String> tags = SemanticValues.textList(base == null ? null : base.tags(), List.of("todo"));
    List<String> aliases = SemanticValues.textList(base == null ? null : base.aliases());
    List<String> keywords =
        SemanticValues.textList(base == null ? null : base.keywords(), List.of(normalizedName));

    Semantic.Ownership ownership = normalizeOwnership(base == null ? null : base.ownership());
    Semantic.DataShape dataShape =
        normalizeDataShape(base == null ? null : base.dataShape(), semanticType, assetId);
    Semantic.Freshness freshness = normalizeFreshness(base == null ? null : base.freshness(), assetId);
    Semantic.Trust trust = normalizeTrust(base == null ? null : base.trust(), assetId);
    Semantic.Usage usage = normalizeUsage(base == null ? null : base.usage(), assetId);
    Semantic.ToolHints toolHints = normalizeToolHints(base == null ? null : base.toolHints(), semanticType);
    List<Semantic.RelationshipHint> relationshipHints =
        SemanticValues.objectList(base == null ? null : base.relationshipHints());

    return new Semantic(
        title,
        description,
        businessMeaning,
        domain,
        subdomain,
        tags,
        aliases,
        keywords,
        ownership,
        dataShape,
        freshness,
        trust,
        usage,
        toolHints,
        relationshipHints);
  }

  private static Semantic.Ownership normalizeOwnership(Semantic.Ownership ownership) {
    if (ownership == null) {
      return new Semantic.Ownership("group:platform", "group:platform", "group:platform", List.of("group:platform"));
    }
    String ownerId = SemanticValues.text(ownership.ownerId(), "group:platform");
    String stewardId = SemanticValues.text(ownership.stewardId(), ownerId);
    String teamId = SemanticValues.text(ownership.teamId(), "group:platform");
    List<String> contactIds = SemanticValues.textList(ownership.contactIds(), List.of(ownerId));
    return new Semantic.Ownership(ownerId, stewardId, teamId, contactIds);
  }

  private static Semantic.DataShape normalizeDataShape(
      Semantic.DataShape shape, Semantic.Type semanticType, String assetId) {
    if (shape == null) {
      return new Semantic.DataShape(
          semanticType,
          "TODO: define grain for " + assetId,
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of());
    }
    return new Semantic.DataShape(
        semanticType,
        SemanticValues.text(shape.grain(), "TODO: define grain for " + assetId),
        SemanticValues.textList(shape.keyFields()),
        SemanticValues.textList(shape.timeFields()),
        SemanticValues.textList(shape.measureFields()),
        SemanticValues.textList(shape.dimensionFields()),
        SemanticValues.objectList(shape.fieldRoles()));
  }

  private static Semantic.Freshness normalizeFreshness(Semantic.Freshness freshness, String assetId) {
    if (freshness == null) {
      return new Semantic.Freshness(
          "TODO: define update cadence for " + assetId,
          "TODO: define freshness SLA for " + assetId,
          "unknown");
    }
    return new Semantic.Freshness(
        SemanticValues.text(freshness.updateCadence(), "TODO: define update cadence for " + assetId),
        SemanticValues.text(freshness.freshnessSla(), "TODO: define freshness SLA for " + assetId),
        SemanticValues.text(freshness.latencyClass(), "unknown"));
  }

  private static Semantic.Trust normalizeTrust(Semantic.Trust trust, String assetId) {
    if (trust == null) {
      return new Semantic.Trust(
          Semantic.Certification.NONE,
          Semantic.QualityStatus.UNKNOWN,
          "TODO: define source of truth for " + assetId,
          "TODO: define usage restrictions for " + assetId);
    }
    return new Semantic.Trust(
        trust.certification() == null ? Semantic.Certification.NONE : trust.certification(),
        trust.qualityStatus() == null ? Semantic.QualityStatus.UNKNOWN : trust.qualityStatus(),
        SemanticValues.text(trust.sourceOfTruth(), "TODO: define source of truth for " + assetId),
        SemanticValues.text(trust.usageRestrictions(), "TODO: define usage restrictions for " + assetId));
  }

  private static Semantic.Usage normalizeUsage(Semantic.Usage usage, String assetId) {
    if (usage == null) {
      return new Semantic.Usage(
          List.of("TODO: add an example question for " + assetId),
          List.of("TODO: add an example query for " + assetId),
          List.of("TODO: add usage hint for " + assetId),
          List.of("TODO: add known pitfall for " + assetId));
    }
    return new Semantic.Usage(
        SemanticValues.textList(usage.exampleQuestions(), List.of("TODO: add an example question for " + assetId)),
        SemanticValues.textList(usage.exampleQueries(), List.of("TODO: add an example query for " + assetId)),
        SemanticValues.textList(usage.usageHints(), List.of("TODO: add usage hint for " + assetId)),
        SemanticValues.textList(usage.knownPitfalls(), List.of("TODO: add known pitfall for " + assetId)));
  }

  private static Semantic.ToolHints normalizeToolHints(Semantic.ToolHints hints, Semantic.Type semanticType) {
    Semantic.ActionClass actionClass = hints == null || hints.actionClass() == null
        ? inferActionClass(semanticType)
        : hints.actionClass();
    Boolean readOnly = hints == null ? null : hints.readOnly();
    if (readOnly == null) {
      readOnly = actionClass == Semantic.ActionClass.READ || actionClass == Semantic.ActionClass.ANALYZE;
    }
    Boolean idempotent = hints == null ? null : hints.idempotent();
    if (idempotent == null) {
      idempotent = actionClass == Semantic.ActionClass.READ || actionClass == Semantic.ActionClass.ANALYZE;
    }
    Integer safeLimit = hints == null ? null : hints.safeDefaultLimit();
    if (safeLimit == null || safeLimit <= 0) {
      safeLimit = 1000;
    }
    String timeout = hints == null ? null : hints.safeDefaultTimeout();
    timeout = SemanticValues.text(timeout, "PT30S");
    String riskClass = hints == null ? null : hints.riskClass();
    if (Strings.trimToNull(riskClass) == null) {
      riskClass = readOnly ? "LOW" : "HIGH";
    }
    return new Semantic.ToolHints(actionClass, readOnly, idempotent, safeLimit, timeout, riskClass);
  }

  private static Semantic.ActionClass inferActionClass(Semantic.Type type) {
    if (type == null) {
      return Semantic.ActionClass.READ;
    }
    return switch (type) {
      case DATASET, SCHEMA, CONFIG, DOCUMENT -> Semantic.ActionClass.READ;
      case SERVICE, STREAM, TOOL -> Semantic.ActionClass.ANALYZE;
      case INGEST, INGEST_SOURCE -> Semantic.ActionClass.WRITE;
    };
  }
}



FILE: SemanticMetadataValidator.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog.semantics;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.common.Semantic;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class SemanticMetadataValidator {
  private static final String TODO_PREFIX = "TODO:";
  private static final String DEFAULT_DOMAIN = "default";
  private static final String DEFAULT_OWNER_ID = "group:platform";
  private static final String DEFAULT_TAG = "todo";
  private static final String DEFAULT_LATENCY_CLASS = "unknown";

  private SemanticMetadataValidator() {}

  public static boolean hasPlaceholders(Semantic metadata) {
    return !placeholderIssues(metadata).isEmpty();
  }

  public static List<String> placeholderIssues(Semantic metadata) {
    List<String> issues = new ArrayList<>();
    if (metadata == null) {
      issues.add("semantic metadata is missing");
      return List.copyOf(issues);
    }
    checkTodo(issues, "title", metadata.title());
    checkTodo(issues, "description", metadata.description());
    checkTodo(issues, "businessMeaning", metadata.businessMeaning());
    if (isDefaultDomain(metadata.domain())) {
      issues.add("domain uses default placeholder");
    }
    if (containsDefaultTag(metadata.tags())) {
      issues.add("tags include todo placeholder");
    }
    if (metadata.ownership() != null && isDefaultOwnerId(metadata.ownership().ownerId())) {
      issues.add("ownership.ownerId uses default placeholder");
    }
    if (metadata.trust() != null && metadata.trust().certification() == Semantic.Certification.NONE) {
      issues.add("trust.certification is NONE");
    }
    if (metadata.trust() != null && metadata.trust().qualityStatus() == Semantic.QualityStatus.UNKNOWN) {
      issues.add("trust.qualityStatus is UNKNOWN");
    }
    if (metadata.dataShape() != null) {
      checkTodo(issues, "dataShape.grain", metadata.dataShape().grain());
    }
    if (metadata.freshness() != null) {
      checkTodo(issues, "freshness.updateCadence", metadata.freshness().updateCadence());
      checkTodo(issues, "freshness.freshnessSla", metadata.freshness().freshnessSla());
      if (DEFAULT_LATENCY_CLASS.equalsIgnoreCase(Strings.trimToNull(metadata.freshness().latencyClass()))) {
        issues.add("freshness.latencyClass uses default placeholder");
      }
    }
    if (metadata.trust() != null) {
      checkTodo(issues, "trust.sourceOfTruth", metadata.trust().sourceOfTruth());
      checkTodo(issues, "trust.usageRestrictions", metadata.trust().usageRestrictions());
    }
    if (metadata.usage() != null) {
      checkTodoList(issues, "usage.exampleQuestions", metadata.usage().exampleQuestions());
      checkTodoList(issues, "usage.exampleQueries", metadata.usage().exampleQueries());
      checkTodoList(issues, "usage.usageHints", metadata.usage().usageHints());
      checkTodoList(issues, "usage.knownPitfalls", metadata.usage().knownPitfalls());
    }
    return List.copyOf(issues);
  }

  public static boolean isPlaceholderText(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized != null && normalized.toUpperCase().startsWith(TODO_PREFIX);
  }

  public static boolean isDefaultDomain(String value) {
    return DEFAULT_DOMAIN.equalsIgnoreCase(Strings.trimToNull(value));
  }

  public static boolean containsDefaultTag(List<String> tags) {
    if (tags == null || tags.isEmpty()) {
      return false;
    }
    for (String tag : tags) {
      if (DEFAULT_TAG.equalsIgnoreCase(Strings.trimToNull(tag))) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  public static boolean isDefaultOwnerId(String ownerId) {
    return DEFAULT_OWNER_ID.equalsIgnoreCase(Strings.trimToNull(ownerId));
  }

  private static void checkTodo(List<String> issues, String field, String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      issues.add(field + " is missing");
      return;
    }
    if (isPlaceholderText(normalized)) {
      issues.add(field + " uses TODO placeholder");
    }
  }

  private static void checkTodoList(List<String> issues, String field, List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    for (String value : values) {
      if (isPlaceholderText(value)) {
        issues.add(field + " includes TODO placeholder");
        return;
      }
    }
  }
}



FILE: SemanticValidationPolicy.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog.semantics;

import java.util.Locale;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public record SemanticValidationPolicy(
    String lane,
    boolean allowPlaceholderDefaults,
    boolean enforcePlaceholderRejection) {

  public static SemanticValidationPolicy fromTier(String tier) {
    String normalized = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(tier), "dev").toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if ("dev".equals(normalized)) {
      return new SemanticValidationPolicy(normalized, true, false);
    }
    return new SemanticValidationPolicy(normalized, false, true);
  }

  public SemanticFindingSeverity placeholderSeverity() {
    return allowPlaceholderDefaults ? SemanticFindingSeverity.WARN : SemanticFindingSeverity.ERROR;
  }
}



FILE: SemanticValues.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog.semantics;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class SemanticValues {
  private SemanticValues() {}

  static String text(String value, String fallback) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? fallback : normalized;
  }

  static List<String> textList(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      String item = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      if (item != null) {
        normalized.add(item);
      }
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  static List<String> textList(List<String> values, List<String> fallbackWhenEmpty) {
    List<String> normalized = textList(values);
    if (!normalized.isEmpty()) {
      return normalized;
    }
    return fallbackWhenEmpty == null || fallbackWhenEmpty.isEmpty()
        ? List.of()
        : List.copyOf(fallbackWhenEmpty);
  }

  static <T> List<T> objectList(List<T> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<T> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    for (T value : values) {
      if (value != null) {
        normalized.add(value);
      }
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(normalized);
  }
}

FILE: ConfigDecoder.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.core.type.TypeReference;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.util.Iterator;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.BiFunction;
import java.util.regex.Matcher;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;

@FunctionalInterface
public interface ConfigDecoder<T> {
  Pattern TEMPLATE_TOKEN_PATTERN = Pattern.compile("\\{\\{\\s*([^{}]+?)\\s*\\}\\}");
  Pattern TEMPLATE_DEFAULT_PATTERN =
      Pattern.compile("^(.*?)\\|\\s*default\\((['\"])(.*?)\\2\\)\\s*$");

  @FunctionalInterface
  interface Transformer<T> {
    T transform(JsonNode groupedPayload) throws Exception;
  }

  T decode(ObjectMapper mapper, JsonNode payload) throws Exception;

  static <T> ConfigDecoder<T> asPojo(Class<T> type) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(type, "type");
    return (mapper, payload) -> mapper.convertValue(payload, type);
  }

  static <T> ConfigDecoder<T> asTransformed(
      Class<T> targetType, Transformer<? extends T> transformer) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(targetType, "targetType");
    Objects.requireNonNull(transformer, "transformer");
    return (mapper, payload) -> targetType.cast(transformer.transform(payload));
  }

  static <T> ConfigDecoder<T> asTransformed(Transformer<T> transformer) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(transformer, "transformer");
    return (mapper, payload) -> transformer.transform(payload);
  }

  static ConfigDecoder<JsonNode> asJsonNode() {
    return (mapper, payload) -> payload;
  }

  static ConfigDecoder<Map<String, Object>> asMap() {
    return (mapper, payload) ->
        mapper.convertValue(payload, new TypeReference<Map<String, Object>>() {});
  }

  static ConfigDecoder<String> asJsonString() {
    return (mapper, payload) -> mapper.writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(payload);
  }

  static ConfigDecoder<String> asTemplate(String template) {
    String requiredTemplate = Objects.requireNonNull(template, "template");
    return (mapper, payload) -> renderTemplate(requiredTemplate, mapper, payload);
  }

  static <T> ConfigDecoder<T> asCustom(BiFunction<ObjectMapper, JsonNode, T> fn) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(fn, "fn");
    return (mapper, payload) -> {
      try {
        return fn.apply(mapper, payload);
      } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
        Throwable cause = ex.getCause();
        if (cause instanceof Exception checked) {
          throw checked;
        }
        throw ex;
      }
    };
  }

  private static String renderTemplate(String template, ObjectMapper mapper, JsonNode payload)
      throws Exception {
    Matcher matcher = TEMPLATE_TOKEN_PATTERN.matcher(template);
    StringBuffer rendered = new StringBuffer(template.length() + 64);
    while (matcher.find()) {
      String expression = matcher.group(1) == null ? "" : matcher.group(1).trim();
      String replacement = resolveExpression(expression, mapper, payload);
      matcher.appendReplacement(rendered, Matcher.quoteReplacement(replacement));
    }
    matcher.appendTail(rendered);
    return rendered.toString();
  }

  private static String resolveExpression(String expression, ObjectMapper mapper, JsonNode payload)
      throws Exception {
    String[] parsed = parseExpression(expression);
    String path = parsed[0];
    String defaultValue = parsed[1];
    if (path.isEmpty()) {
      return defaultValue == null ? "" : defaultValue;
    }

    JsonNode value = readPath(payload, path);
    if (value == null && path.indexOf('.') < 0) {
      value = findByKey(payload, path);
    }

    boolean missing = value == null || value.isNull() || value.isMissingNode();
    if (missing && defaultValue != null) {
      return defaultValue;
    }
    return toTemplateValue(value, mapper);
  }

  private static String[] parseExpression(String expression) {
    String normalized = expression == null ? "" : expression.trim();
    if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
      return new String[] {"", null};
    }
    Matcher matcher = TEMPLATE_DEFAULT_PATTERN.matcher(normalized);
    if (!matcher.matches()) {
      return new String[] {normalized, null};
    }
    String path = matcher.group(1) == null ? "" : matcher.group(1).trim();
    String defaultValue = matcher.group(3);
    return new String[] {path, defaultValue};
  }

  private static JsonNode readPath(JsonNode node, String path) {
    if (node == null) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode current = node;
    String[] parts = path.split("\\.");
    for (String part : parts) {
      String key = part == null ? null : part.trim();
      if (key == null || key.isEmpty()) {
        return null;
      }
      if (current == null || current.isNull() || current.isMissingNode()) {
        return null;
      }
      if (current.isArray() && isInteger(key)) {
        int index = Integer.parseInt(key);
        if (index < 0 || index >= current.size()) {
          return null;
        }
        current = current.get(index);
      } else {
        current = current.get(key);
      }
    }
    return current;
  }

  private static JsonNode findByKey(JsonNode node, String key) {
    if (node == null || key == null || key.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    if (node.isObject()) {
      JsonNode direct = node.get(key);
      if (direct != null) {
        return direct;
      }
      Iterator<Map.Entry<String, JsonNode>> fields = node.fields();
      while (fields.hasNext()) {
        JsonNode found = findByKey(fields.next().getValue(), key);
        if (found != null) {
          return found;
        }
      }
      return null;
    }
    if (node.isArray()) {
      for (JsonNode child : node) {
        JsonNode found = findByKey(child, key);
        if (found != null) {
          return found;
        }
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String toTemplateValue(JsonNode node, ObjectMapper mapper) throws Exception {
    if (node == null || node.isNull() || node.isMissingNode()) {
      return "";
    }
    if (node.isValueNode()) {
      return node.asText();
    }
    return mapper.writeValueAsString(node);
  }

  private static boolean isInteger(String value) {
    try {
      Integer.parseInt(value);
      return true;
    } catch (NumberFormatException ignore) {
      return false;
    }
  }

}



FILE: ConfigManager.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import java.io.ByteArrayInputStream;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Arrays;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.util.zip.ZipEntry;
import java.util.zip.ZipInputStream;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigLayer;

public interface ConfigManager {

  enum Language {
    JAVA,
    PYTHON
  }

  ConfigAdmin admin();

  List<ConfigInfo> listConfigs();

  List<String> listLayers(String configId);

  <T> T resolve(String configId, String layerId, ConfigDecoder<T> decoder);

  <T> T resolveAt(String configId, String layerId, Instant at, ConfigDecoder<T> decoder);

  ConfigLineage lineage(String configId, String layerId);

  ConfigLineage lineageAt(String configId, String layerId, Instant at);

  ConfigCodegen generate(String configId, Language language, String basePackageOrModule);

  ConfigCodegen generate(String configId, String layerId, Language language, String basePackageOrModule);

  ConfigSubscription subscribe(String configId, String layerId, ConfigUpdateListener listener);

  interface ConfigAdmin {

    List<WorkflowStatus> list();

    List<WorkflowStatus> list(int auditLimit);

    UpdateResult update(UpdateRequest request);

    WorkflowStatus approveAndPublish(String configId, String layerId, String comment, String subject);

    WorkflowStatus reject(String configId, String layerId, String comment, String subject);

    WorkflowStatus cancel(String configId, String layerId, String comment, String subject);

    enum ChangeState {
      NONE,
      DRAFT,
      PROPOSED,
      APPROVED,
      REJECTED
    }

    enum ChangeMode {
      IMMEDIATE,
      SCHEDULED
    }

    enum DecisionAction {
      PROPOSE,
      APPROVE,
      REJECT,
      CANCEL,
      PUBLISH
    }

    record UpdateRequest(
        String configId,
        String layerId,
        JsonNode declaredPayload,
        boolean approvalRequired,
        ChangeMode mode,
        Instant effectiveTimeUtc,
        Instant expiresAtUtc,
        String comment,
        String subject) {}

    record UpdateResult(
        String configId,
        String layerId,
        boolean approvalRequired,
        String status,
        WorkflowStatus workflow,
        PublishedConfig published) {}

    record WorkflowStatus(
        String group,
        String configId,
        String layerId,
        String schemaKey,
        ChangeState state,
        ChangeMode mode,
        String effectiveAtUtc,
        String expiresAtUtc,
        String baseConfigId,
        String baseEffectiveConfigId,
        String lastPublishedConfigId,
        String createdTimeUtc,
        String createdBySubject,
        String updatedTimeUtc,
        String updatedBySubject,
        String rationale,
        String decisionMessage,
        List<AuditEvent> audit) {}

    record AuditEvent(
        String timeUtc,
        String subject,
        DecisionAction action,
        String message,
        String fromState,
        String toState,
        String targetConfigId) {}

    record PublishedConfig(
        String group,
        String configId,
        String layerId,
        String schemaKey,
        String publishedConfigId,
        String effectiveConfigId,
        String updatedTimeUtc,
        String updatedBySubject,
        JsonNode declared,
        List<EffectiveEntry> effective) {}

    record EffectiveEntry(String effectiveTimeUtc, String expiresAtUtc, JsonNode declared) {}
  }

  record ConfigCodegen(byte[] zipBytes, String filename, Map<String, String> stats) {

    public ConfigCodegen {
      zipBytes = zipBytes == null ? new byte[0] : Arrays.copyOf(zipBytes, zipBytes.length);
      filename = filename == null ? "config-codegen.zip" : filename;
      stats = stats == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(stats);
    }

    @Override
    public byte[] zipBytes() {
      return Arrays.copyOf(zipBytes, zipBytes.length);
    }

    public List<String> autogenCode() {
      if (zipBytes.length == 0) {
        return List.of();
      }
      List<String> generated = new ArrayList<>();
      try (ZipInputStream zip =
          new ZipInputStream(new ByteArrayInputStream(zipBytes), StandardCharsets.UTF_8)) {
        ZipEntry entry;
        while ((entry = zip.getNextEntry()) != null) {
          if (entry.isDirectory()) {
            continue;
          }
          String text = new String(zip.readAllBytes(), StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
          generated.add(entry.getName() + "\n" + text);
        }
        return List.copyOf(generated);
      } catch (Exception ex) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to decode generated code zip", ex);
      }
    }
  }

  record ConfigInfo(String configId, String displayName, String schemaKey) {}

  interface ConfigSubscription extends AutoCloseable {
    @Override
    void close();
  }

  record ConfigUpdate(
      String group,
      String configName,
      String layerId,
      String schemaKey,
      String configId,
      String effectiveConfigId,
      String configUuid,
      String updatedTimeUtc,
      JsonNode declared,
      List<DefinitionConfigLayer.Effective> effective) {}

  @FunctionalInterface
  interface ConfigUpdateListener {
    void onUpdate(ConfigUpdate update);
  }

  record ConfigLineage(
      String baseConfigId,
      int chainDepth,
      boolean chainValid,
      List<String> resolvedNodeIds,
      List<String> resolvedLayers,
      String payloadHash,
      String effectiveTreeHash,
      String effectiveTreeHashVersion) {}

}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.connections;

FILE: ConnectionOptions.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.connections;

import java.time.Duration;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class ConnectionOptions {
  private static final ConnectionOptions DEFAULTS = new Builder().build();

  private final String clientName;
  private final Duration timeout;
  private final int maxInflight;
  private final String pinnedInstance;

  private ConnectionOptions(Builder builder) {
    this.clientName = Strings.trimToNull(builder.clientName);
    this.timeout = validateTimeout(builder.timeout);
    this.maxInflight = validateMaxInflight(builder.maxInflight);
    this.pinnedInstance = Strings.trimToNull(builder.pinnedInstance);
  }

  public static ConnectionOptions defaults() {
    return DEFAULTS;
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public String clientName() {
    return clientName;
  }

  public Duration timeout() {
    return timeout;
  }

  public int maxInflight() {
    return maxInflight;
  }

  public String pinnedInstance() {
    return pinnedInstance;
  }

  @Override
  public boolean equals(Object other) {
    if (this == other) {
      return true;
    }
    if (!(other instanceof ConnectionOptions that)) {
      return false;
    }
    return maxInflight == that.maxInflight
        && Objects.equals(clientName, that.clientName)
        && Objects.equals(timeout, that.timeout)
        && Objects.equals(pinnedInstance, that.pinnedInstance);
  }

  @Override
  public int hashCode() {
    return Objects.hash(clientName, timeout, maxInflight, pinnedInstance);
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String clientName;
    private Duration timeout;
    private int maxInflight;
    private String pinnedInstance;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withClientName(String value) {
      this.clientName = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTimeout(Duration value) {
      this.timeout = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMaxInflight(int value) {
      this.maxInflight = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPinnedInstance(String value) {
      this.pinnedInstance = value;
      return this;
    }

    public ConnectionOptions build() {
      return new ConnectionOptions(this);
    }
  }

  private static Duration validateTimeout(Duration value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (value.isNegative() || value.isZero()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("timeout must be > 0 when provided");
    }
    return value;
  }

  private static int validateMaxInflight(int value) {
    if (value < 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("maxInflight must be >= 0");
    }
    return value;
  }
}

PACKAGE: org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.amps

FILE: AmpsConfig.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.amps;

import java.net.URI;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.security.MessageDigest;
import java.security.NoSuchAlgorithmException;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class AmpsConfig {
  
  private static final int MAX_LENGTH = 128;
  private static final int HASH_BYTES = 4;
  private static final String PREFIX = "fabric";
  private static final String UNKNOWN = "UNKNOWN";
  private static final Pattern HOST_PORT = Pattern.compile("^[A-Za-z0-9.\\-]+:\\d{1,5}$");

  private AmpsConfig() {}

  public static String buildCpClientId(String group, String name, String instanceName) {
    return buildClientId(group, name, instanceName, "cp", null);
  }

  public static List<String> parseDiscoveryUrls(Collection<String> values) {
    if (values == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String entry : values) {
      if (entry == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String trimmed = entry.trim();
      if (trimmed.isEmpty()) {
        continue;
      }
      String[] parts = trimmed.split(",");
      for (String part : parts) {
        String candidate = part.trim();
        if (candidate.isEmpty()) {
          continue;
        }
        normalized.add(normalizeDiscoveryUrl(candidate));
      }
    }
    if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> deduped = new LinkedHashSet<>(normalized);
    return List.copyOf(deduped);
  }

  public static String normalizeDiscoveryUrl(String candidate) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(candidate, "candidate");
    return requireHostPort(candidate.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT), "discoveryUrl");
  }

  public static String requireHostPort(String raw, String contextLabel) {
    String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(raw);
    String context = Strings.trimToNull(contextLabel);
    if (trimmed == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(describeContext(context) + " is required and must be host:port");
    }
    String candidate = trimmed;
    if (trimmed.regionMatches(true, 0, "tcp://", 0, 6)) {
      try {
        URI uri = URI.create(trimmed);
        String host = Strings.trimToNull(uri.getHost());
        int port = uri.getPort();
        if (host == null || port <= 0) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(describeContext(context) + " must be host:port (got '" + raw + "')");
        }
        candidate = host + ":" + port;
      } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException(describeContext(context) + " must be host:port (got '" + raw + "')");
      }
    }
    if (!HOST_PORT.matcher(candidate).matches()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(describeContext(context) + " must be host:port (got '" + raw + "')");
    }
    int colonIdx = candidate.lastIndexOf(':');
    String host = candidate.substring(0, colonIdx).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    String port = candidate.substring(colonIdx + 1);
    int portNum = Integer.parseInt(port);
    if (portNum < 1 || portNum > 65535) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(describeContext(context) + " must include a valid port (got '" + raw + "')");
    }
    return host + ":" + port;
  }

  private static String buildClientId(
      String group, String name, String instanceName, String plane, String shortUuid) {
    List<String> prefixParts = new ArrayList<>();
    appendRequiredPart(prefixParts, PREFIX, PREFIX);
    appendRequiredPart(prefixParts, group, UNKNOWN);
    appendRequiredPart(prefixParts, name, UNKNOWN);
    appendRequiredPart(prefixParts, instanceName, UNKNOWN);
    String prefix = String.join("-", prefixParts);

    List<String> suffixParts = new ArrayList<>();
    appendRequiredPart(suffixParts, plane, UNKNOWN);
    if (shortUuid != null) {
      appendRequiredPart(suffixParts, shortUuid, UNKNOWN);
    }
    String suffix = String.join("-", suffixParts);
    return enforceMaxLength(prefix, suffix);
  }

  private static void appendRequiredPart(List<String> parts, String value, String fallback) {
    String normalized = normalizeClientNamePart(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      normalized = normalizeClientNamePart(fallback);
    }
    if (normalized != null) {
      parts.add(normalized);
    }
  }

  private static String normalizeClientNamePart(String value) {
    String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (trimmed == null) {
      return null;
    }
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder(trimmed.length());
    boolean lastDash = false;
    for (int i = 0; i < trimmed.length(); i++) {
      char ch = trimmed.charAt(i);
      boolean allowed =
          (ch >= 'a' && ch <= 'z')
              || (ch >= 'A' && ch <= 'Z')
              || (ch >= '0' && ch <= '9')
              || ch == '-'
              || ch == '_'
              || ch == '.';
      if (allowed) {
        builder.append(ch);
        lastDash = false;
      } else if (!lastDash) {
        builder.append('-');
        lastDash = true;
      }
    }
    if (builder.length() == 0) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = builder.toString();
    while (normalized.endsWith("-")) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(0, normalized.length() - 1);
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? null : normalized;
  }

  private static String enforceMaxLength(String prefix, String suffix) {
    String safePrefix = Strings.trimToNull(prefix);
    if (safePrefix == null) {
      safePrefix = PREFIX;
    }
    String safeSuffix = Strings.trimToNull(suffix);
    if (safeSuffix == null) {
      return enforceMaxLength(safePrefix);
    }
    String joined = safePrefix + "-" + safeSuffix;
    if (joined.length() <= MAX_LENGTH) {
      return joined;
    }
    String hash = shortHash(joined);
    int maxPrefix = MAX_LENGTH - safeSuffix.length() - 1;
    if (maxPrefix <= 0) {
      return safeSuffix.length() <= MAX_LENGTH ? safeSuffix : safeSuffix.substring(0, MAX_LENGTH);
    }
    if (safePrefix.length() > maxPrefix) {
      int hashSpace = hash.length() + 1;
      int prefixSpace = maxPrefix - hashSpace;
      if (prefixSpace <= 0) {
        safePrefix = hash.substring(0, Math.min(hash.length(), maxPrefix));
      } else {
        String base = safePrefix.substring(0, Math.min(safePrefix.length(), prefixSpace));
        base = trimTrailingDash(base);
        if (base.isEmpty()) {
          safePrefix = hash.substring(0, Math.min(hash.length(), maxPrefix));
        } else {
          safePrefix = base + "-" + hash;
        }
      }
    }
    return safePrefix + "-" + safeSuffix;
  }

  private static String enforceMaxLength(String name) {
    if (name.length() <= MAX_LENGTH) {
      return name;
    }
    String hash = shortHash(name);
    int maxPrefix = MAX_LENGTH - hash.length() - 1;
    if (maxPrefix <= 0) {
      return hash.substring(0, Math.min(hash.length(), MAX_LENGTH));
    }
    String prefix = name.substring(0, maxPrefix);
    prefix = trimTrailingDash(prefix);
    if (prefix.isEmpty()) {
      return hash.substring(0, Math.min(hash.length(), MAX_LENGTH));
    }
    return prefix + "-" + hash;
  }

  private static String trimTrailingDash(String value) {
    if (Strings.isEmpty(value)) {
      return value;
    }
    String trimmed = value;
    while (trimmed.endsWith("-")) {
      trimmed = trimmed.substring(0, trimmed.length() - 1);
      if (trimmed.isEmpty()) {
        break;
      }
    }
    return trimmed;
  }

  private static String shortHash(String value) {
    try {
      MessageDigest digest = MessageDigest.getInstance("SHA-256");
      byte[] bytes = digest.digest(value.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
      StringBuilder hex = new StringBuilder(HASH_BYTES * 2);
      for (int i = 0; i < HASH_BYTES && i < bytes.length; i++) {
        int b = bytes[i] & 0xff;
        if (b < 16) {
          hex.append('0');
        }
        hex.append(Integer.toHexString(b));
      }
      return hex.toString();
    } catch (NoSuchAlgorithmException ex) {
      return Integer.toHexString(value.hashCode());
    }
  }

  private static String describeContext(String context) {
    return context == null ? "endpoint" : context;
  }
  
}

FILE: HttpConnection.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.http;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.net.URI;
import java.net.http.HttpClient;
import java.net.http.HttpRequest;
import java.net.http.HttpResponse;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class HttpConnection implements AutoCloseable {
  private final URI baseUri;
  private final HttpClient client;
  private final Duration timeout;

  public HttpConnection(URI baseUri, HttpClient client, Duration timeout) {
    this.baseUri = Objects.requireNonNull(baseUri, "baseUri");
    this.client = Objects.requireNonNull(client, "client");
    this.timeout = timeout;
  }

  public URI baseUri() {
    return baseUri;
  }

  public HttpResponse<String> get(String path) {
    HttpRequest.Builder request = HttpRequest.newBuilder(resolve(path)).GET();
    applyTimeout(request);
    return send(request.build());
  }

  public HttpResponse<String> post(String path, String body) {
    HttpRequest.Builder request =
        HttpRequest.newBuilder(resolve(path))
            .header("Content-Type", "text/plain; charset=utf-8")
            .POST(
                HttpRequest.BodyPublishers.ofString(
                    body == null ? "" : body, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
    applyTimeout(request);
    return send(request.build());
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    // java.net.http.HttpClient does not require explicit close.
  }

  private URI resolve(String path) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(path);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return baseUri;
    }
    if (normalized.startsWith("//")) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("path must not contain authority override");
    }
    URI relative = URI.create(normalized);
    if (relative.isAbsolute() || relative.getAuthority() != null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("path must be relative");
    }
    return baseUri.resolve(relative);
  }

  private HttpResponse<String> send(HttpRequest request) {
    try {
      return client.send(request, HttpResponse.BodyHandlers.ofString(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
    } catch (IOException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("HTTP request failed: " + request.uri(), ex);
    } catch (InterruptedException ex) {
      Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
      throw new IllegalStateException("HTTP request interrupted: " + request.uri(), ex);
    }
  }

  private void applyTimeout(HttpRequest.Builder request) {
    if (timeout != null) {
      request.timeout(timeout);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control;

import com.crankuptheamps.client.HAClient;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.amps.AmpsConnection;

public final class ControlConnection {
  private final AmpsConnection amps;
  private final String name;

  private ControlConnection(AmpsConnection amps, String name) {
    this.amps = Objects.requireNonNull(amps, "amps");
    this.name = name;
  }

  public static ControlConnection of(HAClient client, String name) {
    return new ControlConnection(AmpsConnection.shared(client), name);
  }

  public static ControlConnection of(AmpsConnection amps, String name) {
    return new ControlConnection(amps, name);
  }

  public AmpsConnection amps() {
    return amps;
  }

  public Subscription sowAndSubscribe(
      String topic, String options, String filter, SubscriptionListener listener) throws Exception {
    Objects.requireNonNull(listener, "listener");
    AmpsConnection.Subscription delegate =
        amps.sowAndSubscribe(topic, options, filter, message -> listener.onMessage(new Message(message)));
    return new Subscription(delegate);
  }

  public Subscription subscribe(
      String topic, String options, String filter, SubscriptionListener listener) throws Exception {
    Objects.requireNonNull(listener, "listener");
    AmpsConnection.Subscription delegate =
        amps.subscribe(topic, options, filter, message -> listener.onMessage(new Message(message)));
    return new Subscription(delegate);
  }

  public String name() {
    return name;
  }

  public static final class Subscription implements AutoCloseable {
    private final AmpsConnection.Subscription delegate;

    private Subscription(AmpsConnection.Subscription delegate) {
      this.delegate = Objects.requireNonNull(delegate, "delegate");
    }

    @Override
    public void close() {
      delegate.close();
    }

    public void replaceFilter(String filter) throws Exception {
      delegate.replaceFilter(filter);
    }
  }

  @FunctionalInterface
  public interface SubscriptionListener {
    void onMessage(Message message);
  }

  public static final class Message {
    private final AmpsConnection.AmpsMessage delegate;

    private Message(AmpsConnection.AmpsMessage delegate) {
      this.delegate = Objects.requireNonNull(delegate, "delegate");
    }

    public String topic() {
      return delegate.topic();
    }

    public String data() {
      return delegate.data();
    }

    public String bookmark() {
      return delegate.bookmark();
    }

    public com.crankuptheamps.client.Message raw() {
      return delegate.raw();
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache;

import java.util.EnumMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfig;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigLayer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConfigChange;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEntitlement;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvironment;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngest;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngestSource;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionPlatform;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionSchema;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStream;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;

final class DiscoveryCacheType {

  private DiscoveryCacheType() {}

  static DefinitionType toType(
      Class<?> clazz,
      Map<Class<? extends Definition>, DefinitionType> classToType,
      Set<String> unmappedDefinitionClasses,
      Logger logger) {
    if (clazz == null || !Definition.class.isAssignableFrom(clazz)) {
      return DefinitionType.UNKNOWN;
    }
    @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    Class<? extends Definition> definitionClass = (Class<? extends Definition>) clazz;
    DefinitionType type = classToType.get(definitionClass);
    if (type != null) {
      return type;
    }
    String className = definitionClass.getName();
    if (unmappedDefinitionClasses.add(className)) {
      logger.warn(
          "[DiscoveryCache][Compatibility] unmapped definition class {}; treating as UNKNOWN",
          className);
    }
    return DefinitionType.UNKNOWN;
  }

  static boolean isCacheableType(
      DefinitionType type, Map<DefinitionType, Class<? extends Definition>> cacheableDefinitions) {
    return type != null && type != DefinitionType.UNKNOWN && cacheableDefinitions.containsKey(type);
  }

  static DefinitionType definitionType(Definition definition) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = definitionEnvelope(definition);
    return envelope == null ? null : envelope.type();
  }

  static String definitionGroup(Definition definition) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = definitionEnvelope(definition);
    return envelope == null ? null : envelope.group();
  }

  static String definitionName(Definition definition) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = definitionEnvelope(definition);
    return envelope == null ? null : envelope.name();
  }

  static DefinitionEnvelope definitionEnvelope(Definition definition) {
    return definition == null ? null : definition.envelope();
  }

  static String normalize(String value) {
    return Strings.trimToNull(value);
  }

  static String safe(Object value) {
    return value == null ? "" : String.valueOf(value);
  }

  static String schemaName(DefinitionSchema schema) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = schema == null ? null : schema.envelope();
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(envelope == null ? null : envelope.name(), "");
  }

  static String schemaTypeName(DefinitionSchema schema) {
    return schema == null || schema.schemaType() == null ? "" : schema.schemaType().name();
  }

  static Map<DefinitionType, Class<? extends Definition>> cacheableDefinitions() {
    EnumMap<DefinitionType, Class<? extends Definition>> map = new EnumMap<>(DefinitionType.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.APP, DefinitionApp.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.CONNECTION, DefinitionConnection.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.DATASET, DefinitionDataset.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.STREAM, DefinitionStream.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.INGEST, DefinitionIngest.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.INGEST_SOURCE, DefinitionIngestSource.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.ENVIRONMENT, DefinitionEnvironment.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.PLATFORM, DefinitionPlatform.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.SCHEMA, DefinitionSchema.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.SERVICE, DefinitionService.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.ENTITLEMENT, DefinitionEntitlement.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.CONFIG_LAYER, DefinitionConfigLayer.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.CONFIG, DefinitionConfig.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.CONFIG_CHANGE, DefinitionConfigChange.class);
    map.put(DefinitionType.STATUS_APP, DefinitionStatusApp.class);
    // No concrete class is modeled yet, but the bootstrap record is still cacheable.
    map.put(DefinitionType.SECRETS_KDF, Definition.class);
    return Map.copyOf(map);
  }

  static Map<Class<? extends Definition>, DefinitionType> classToType(
      Map<DefinitionType, Class<? extends Definition>> cacheableDefinitions) {
    ConcurrentHashMap<Class<? extends Definition>, DefinitionType> reverse = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<DefinitionType, Class<? extends Definition>> entry : cacheableDefinitions.entrySet()) {
      Class<? extends Definition> definitionClass = entry.getValue();
      if (definitionClass == Definition.class) {
        continue;
      }
      reverse.putIfAbsent(definitionClass, entry.getKey());
    }
    return Map.copyOf(reverse);
  }
}

FILE: DefinitionConfigChange.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonEnumDefaultValue;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonInclude;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;

@JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
public record DefinitionConfigChange(
    @JsonProperty("envelope") DefinitionEnvelope envelope,
    String group,
    String configId,
    String layerId,
    String schemaKey,
    ChangeState state,
    ChangeMode mode,
    String effectiveAtUtc,
    String expiresAtUtc,
    JsonNode draftDeclared,
    String baseConfigId,
    String baseEffectiveConfigId,
    String lastPublishedConfigId,
    String createdTimeUtc,
    String createdBySubject,
    String updatedTimeUtc,
    String updatedBySubject,
    String rationale,
    String decisionMessage,
    List<AuditEntry> audit,
    List<ChangeEntry> changes)
    implements Definition {

  public DefinitionConfigChange {
    audit = immutableCopy(audit);
    changes = immutableCopy(changes);
  }

  public DefinitionConfigChange(
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope,
      String group,
      String configId,
      String layerId,
      String schemaKey,
      ChangeState state,
      ChangeMode mode,
      String effectiveAtUtc,
      String expiresAtUtc,
      JsonNode draftDeclared,
      String baseConfigId,
      String baseEffectiveConfigId,
      String lastPublishedConfigId,
      String createdTimeUtc,
      String createdBySubject,
      String updatedTimeUtc,
      String updatedBySubject,
      String rationale,
      String decisionMessage,
      List<AuditEntry> audit) {
    this(
        envelope,
        group,
        configId,
        layerId,
        schemaKey,
        state,
        mode,
        effectiveAtUtc,
        expiresAtUtc,
        draftDeclared,
        baseConfigId,
        baseEffectiveConfigId,
        lastPublishedConfigId,
        createdTimeUtc,
        createdBySubject,
        updatedTimeUtc,
        updatedBySubject,
        rationale,
        decisionMessage,
        audit,
        List.of());
  }

  public ChangeEntry latestChange() {
    if (changes == null || changes.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    for (ChangeEntry change : changes) {
      if (change != null) {
        return change;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  public enum ChangeState {
    NONE,
    DRAFT,
    PROPOSED,
    APPROVED,
    REJECTED,
    @JsonEnumDefaultValue
    UNKNOWN
  }

  public enum ChangeMode {
    IMMEDIATE,
    SCHEDULED,
    @JsonEnumDefaultValue
    UNKNOWN
  }

  public enum DecisionAction {
    PROPOSE,
    APPROVE,
    REJECT,
    CANCEL,
    PUBLISH,
    @JsonEnumDefaultValue
    UNKNOWN
  }

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record AuditEntry(
      String timeUtc,
      String subject,
      DecisionAction action,
      String message,
      String fromState,
      String toState,
      String targetConfigId) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record ChangeEntry(
      String changeId,
      ChangeState state,
      ChangeMode mode,
      String effectiveAtUtc,
      String expiresAtUtc,
      JsonNode draftDeclared,
      String baseConfigId,
      String baseEffectiveConfigId,
      String lastPublishedConfigId,
      String createdTimeUtc,
      String createdBySubject,
      String updatedTimeUtc,
      String updatedBySubject,
      String rationale,
      String decisionMessage,
      List<AuditEntry> audit) {

    public ChangeEntry {
      audit = immutableCopy(audit);
    }
  }

  private static <T> List<T> immutableCopy(List<T> source) {
    if (source == null || source.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<T> copy = new ArrayList<>();
    for (T value : source) {
      if (value != null) {
        copy.add(value);
      }
    }
    return copy.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(copy);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonInclude;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.common.EntitlementsProvider;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.common.Semantic;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

@JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
public record DefinitionDataset(
    @JsonProperty("envelope") DefinitionEnvelope envelope,
    DatasetType type,
    String namespace,
    Binding binding,
    View view,
    String accessMode,
    Semantic semantic,
    EntitlementsProvider entitlements
) implements Definition {

  public DefinitionDataset(
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope, DatasetType type, String namespace, Binding binding) {
    this(envelope, type, namespace, binding, null, null, null, null);
  }

  public DefinitionDataset(
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope, DatasetType type, String namespace, Binding binding, View view) {
    this(envelope, type, namespace, binding, view, null, null, null);
  }

  public DefinitionDataset(
      DefinitionEnvelope envelope,
      DatasetType type,
      String namespace,
      Binding binding,
      View view,
      String accessMode,
      Semantic semantic) {
    this(envelope, type, namespace, binding, view, accessMode, semantic, null);
  }

  public static final String ACCESS_MODE_PRIVATE = "PRIVATE";
  public static final String ACCESS_MODE_PUBLIC = "PUBLIC";

  public String effectiveAccessMode() {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(accessMode);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return ACCESS_MODE_PRIVATE;
    }
    if (ACCESS_MODE_PUBLIC.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
      return ACCESS_MODE_PUBLIC;
    }
    return ACCESS_MODE_PRIVATE;
  }

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record Binding(
      DuckdbBinding duckdb,
      ParquetBinding parquet,
      ExternalBinding external,
      OdbcBinding odbc
  ) {
    public Binding(DuckdbBinding duckdb, ParquetBinding parquet, ExternalBinding external) {
      this(duckdb, parquet, external, null);
    }
  }

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record View(
      String querySql,
      List<String> dependencies,
      Refresh refresh,
      Target target,
      String schemaName,
      String schemaCompatibility,
      LastRefresh lastRefresh
  ) {
    public View {
      dependencies = normalizeDependencies(dependencies);
    }
  }

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record Refresh(
      String type,
      Long intervalMillis,
      Boolean runOnStart
  ) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record Target(
      String duckdbTableName,
      String parquetPath,
      String targetType
  ) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record LastRefresh(
      String lastRefreshStartUtc,
      String lastRefreshEndUtc,
      Long lastDurationMs,
      String lastStatus,
      String lastError,
      Long lastRowCount,
      Map<String, String> lastInputFingerprints,
      String lastOutputSnapshot
  ) {
    public LastRefresh {
      if (lastInputFingerprints == null || lastInputFingerprints.isEmpty()) {
        lastInputFingerprints = Map.of();
      } else {
        lastInputFingerprints = Map.copyOf(lastInputFingerprints);
      }
    }
  }

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record DuckdbBinding(
      String relationName,
      String targetType,
      List<String> primaryKey,
      Boolean memory,
      String databasePath,
      String parquetHistoryPath,
      Boolean persistOnStop,
      Boolean createIfMissing
  ) {
    public DuckdbBinding {
      primaryKey = primaryKey == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(new ArrayList<>(primaryKey));
    }

    public DuckdbBinding(String relationName) {
      this(relationName, null, List.of(), null, null, null, null, null);
    }
  }

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record ParquetBinding(
      String uri,
      String glob,
      Boolean hivePartitioning,
      List<String> partitionColumns,
      String partitionKey,
      String partitionValueField,
      String connectionName
  ) {
    public ParquetBinding(
        String uri,
        String glob,
        Boolean hivePartitioning,
        List<String> partitionColumns,
        String partitionKey,
        String partitionValueField) {
      this(
          uri,
          glob,
          hivePartitioning,
          partitionColumns,
          partitionKey,
          partitionValueField,
          null);
    }

  }

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record ExternalBinding(
      String externalType,
      String reference,
      Map<String, String> options
  ) {
    public ExternalBinding(String externalType, String reference) {
      this(externalType, reference, null);
    }
  }

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record OdbcBinding(
      String connectionName,
      DefinitionConnection.Odbc.DatabaseType databaseType,
      String catalogName,
      String schemaName,
      String tableName,
      String querySql,
      String primaryKey,
      Map<String, String> options
  ) {}

  private static List<String> normalizeDependencies(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    LinkedHashSet<String> deduped = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      if (normalized != null) {
        deduped.add(normalized);
      }
    }
    if (deduped.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(deduped);
    sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER.thenComparing(Comparator.naturalOrder()));
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }
}



FILE: DefinitionEntitlement.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonIgnoreProperties;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonInclude;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

@JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
public record DefinitionEntitlement(
    @JsonProperty("envelope") DefinitionEnvelope envelope,
    String scopeType,
    String scopeId,
    List<PolicyDocument> policies,
    List<RelationshipTuple> relationships,
    Map<String, String> labels,
    List<String> notes
) implements Definition {

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record PolicyDocument(
      String schemaVersion,
      String policyId,
      String group,
      String name,
      String type,
      String scopeType,
      String resourceId,
      String policyUsage,
      String usageGroup,
      String description,
      String version,
      Boolean enabled,
      String lifecycleStatus,
      Map<String, String> metadata,
      List<PolicyBinding> bindings) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record PolicyBinding(
      String bindingId,
      String subject,
      String action,
      String effect,
      Boolean enabled,
      ObligationSet obligations,
      Map<String, String> attributes,
      Map<String, Object> context) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record ObligationSet(
      List<RowFilter> rowFilters,
      List<String> columnsAllow,
      List<ColumnMask> columnsMask,
      List<String> datasetScope,
      List<String> methodsAllow,
      Map<String, Object> parameters) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record RowFilter(String expression, Boolean replace, Map<String, Object> parameters) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record ColumnMask(String column, String strategy, Integer scale, String replacement) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record RelationshipTuple(
      String resourceType,
      String resourceId,
      String relation,
      String subject,
      String resourceSubject) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonInclude;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;
import java.util.List;

@JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
public record DefinitionEnvironment(
    @JsonProperty("envelope") DefinitionEnvelope envelope,
    Integer version,
    List<Environment> environments,
    Entitlements entitlements,
    Configs configs,
    Otel otel,
    Cadence cadence,
    String configId,
    String effectiveConfigId
) implements Definition {

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record Entitlements(
      String implementation,
      Events events,
      String defaultProviderId,
      List<ProviderRegistration> providers
  ) {
    public Entitlements(String implementation, Events events) {
      this(implementation, events, null, List.of());
    }

    public Entitlements {
      providers = providers == null || providers.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(providers);
    }

    @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
    public record ProviderRegistration(
        String id,
        String type,
        Boolean enabled,
        java.util.Map<String, Object> config) {

      public ProviderRegistration {
        config = config == null || config.isEmpty() ? java.util.Map.of() : java.util.Map.copyOf(config);
      }
    }
  }

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record Configs(
      String implementation,
      Events events
  ) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record Events(
      Boolean enabled,
      String transport,
      EventsAmps amps
  ) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record EventsAmps(
      String connection,
      String topic,
      Integer maxRetries,
      Long initialBackoffMillis,
      Long maxBackoffMillis,
      Double backoffMultiplier
  ) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record Otel(
      Boolean enabled,
      String serviceNamespace,
      String deploymentEnvironment,
      String otlpEndpoint,
      Boolean tracesEnabled,
      Boolean metricsEnabled
  ) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record Cadence(
      Integer serviceHeartbeatSeconds,
      Integer serviceStatusSeconds,
      Integer dataStatusSeconds
  ) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record Environment(
      String environment,
      List<EnvironmentRegion> regions
  ) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record EnvironmentRegion(
      String region,
      List<EnvironmentSite> sites
  ) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record EnvironmentSite(
      String site,
      List<EnvironmentAmps> amps
  ) {}

  @JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
  public record EnvironmentAmps(
      String name,
      List<String> endpoints
  ) {}

}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions;

public record DefinitionService(
    @JsonProperty("envelope") DefinitionEnvelope envelope,

        grpc,
        arrow,

        semantic,
        null);

  ) {}

FILE: SchemaReference.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.common;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonIgnore;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonInclude;

@JsonInclude(JsonInclude.Include.NON_NULL)
public record SchemaReference(
    String schemaId,
    String group,
    String type,
    String name,
    Integer version,
    String messageTypeName
) {

  public String getSchemaId() {
    return schemaId;
  }

  public String getGroup() {
    return group;
  }

  public String getType() {
    return type;
  }

  public String getName() {
    return name;
  }

  public Integer getVersion() {
    return version;
  }

  public String getMessageTypeName() {
    return messageTypeName;
  }

  @JsonIgnore
  public boolean isResolvedById() {
    return schemaId != null;
  }

  @JsonIgnore
  public boolean isResolvableByName() {
    return group != null && name != null;
  }
}

    INTERNAL,
    CONFIDENTIAL,
    RESTRICTED

  private static String text(String value, String fallback) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return normalized == null ? fallback : normalized;
  }

  private static List<String> textList(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      String item = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      if (item != null) {
        normalized.add(item);
      }
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static List<String> textList(List<String> values, List<String> fallbackWhenEmpty) {
    List<String> normalized = textList(values);
    if (!normalized.isEmpty()) {
      return normalized;
    }
    return fallbackWhenEmpty == null || fallbackWhenEmpty.isEmpty()
        ? List.of()
        : List.copyOf(fallbackWhenEmpty);
  }

  private static <T> List<T> objectList(List<T> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<T> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
    for (T value : values) {
      if (value != null) {
        normalized.add(value);
      }
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(normalized);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle;

public record AssetLifecycleEdge(
    String fromAssetId,
    String toAssetId,
    RelationshipType relationshipType,
    OwnershipType ownershipType,
    PromotionBehavior promotionBehavior,
    DeleteBehavior deleteBehavior,
    RetentionBehavior retentionBehavior,
    boolean required,
    boolean shared,
    String source,
    String notes,
    String targetLocator) {

  public AssetLifecycleEdge {
    fromAssetId = normalize(fromAssetId, "<unknown-from>");
    toAssetId = normalize(toAssetId, "<unknown-to>");
    relationshipType = relationshipType == null ? RelationshipType.REFERENCES : relationshipType;
    ownershipType = ownershipType == null ? OwnershipType.SHARED : ownershipType;
    promotionBehavior =
        promotionBehavior == null ? PromotionBehavior.OPTIONAL_WITH_PARENT : promotionBehavior;
    deleteBehavior = deleteBehavior == null ? DeleteBehavior.MANUAL : deleteBehavior;
    retentionBehavior =
        retentionBehavior == null ? RetentionBehavior.KEEP_HISTORY : retentionBehavior;
    source = normalize(source, "inferred");
    notes = normalize(notes, "");
    targetLocator = normalize(targetLocator, "");
  }

  private static String normalize(String value, String fallback) {
    if (value == null) {
      return fallback;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? fallback : trimmed;
  }
}


FILE: AssetLifecycleGraph.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;

public record AssetLifecycleGraph(
    Map<String, AssetLifecycleNode> nodes,
    List<AssetLifecycleEdge> edges,
    Map<String, List<AssetLifecycleEdge>> outgoingEdges,
    Map<String, List<AssetLifecycleEdge>> incomingEdges) {

  public AssetLifecycleGraph {
    nodes = nodes == null ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(nodes);
    edges = edges == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(edges);
    outgoingEdges = outgoingEdges == null ? Map.of() : copyEdgeMap(outgoingEdges);
    incomingEdges = incomingEdges == null ? Map.of() : copyEdgeMap(incomingEdges);
  }

  public Optional<AssetLifecycleNode> node(String assetId) {
    if (assetId == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    return Optional.ofNullable(nodes.get(assetId.trim()));
  }

  public boolean hasAsset(String assetId) {
    return node(assetId).isPresent();
  }

  public List<AssetLifecycleEdge> outgoing(String assetId) {
    if (assetId == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return outgoingEdges.getOrDefault(assetId.trim(), List.of());
  }

  public List<AssetLifecycleEdge> incoming(String assetId) {
    if (assetId == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return incomingEdges.getOrDefault(assetId.trim(), List.of());
  }

  public String resolveAssetId(String token) {
    if (token == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = token.trim();
    if (normalized.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    if (nodes.containsKey(normalized)) {
      return normalized;
    }
    String lower = normalized.toLowerCase();
    List<String> matches = new ArrayList<>();
    for (AssetLifecycleNode node : nodes.values()) {
      if (node == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (node.name().equalsIgnoreCase(lower)
          || (node.group() + "/" + node.name()).equalsIgnoreCase(lower)
          || node.assetId().equalsIgnoreCase(lower)) {
        matches.add(node.assetId());
      }
    }
    if (matches.size() == 1) {
      return matches.getFirst();
    }
    return null;
  }

  public Map<DefinitionType, Integer> countsByDefinitionType() {
    Map<DefinitionType, Integer> counts = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (AssetLifecycleNode node : nodes.values()) {
      if (node == null) {
        continue;
      }
      counts.put(node.type(), counts.getOrDefault(node.type(), 0) + 1);
    }
    return Map.copyOf(counts);
  }

  private static Map<String, List<AssetLifecycleEdge>> copyEdgeMap(
      Map<String, List<AssetLifecycleEdge>> input) {
    Map<String, List<AssetLifecycleEdge>> copied = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, List<AssetLifecycleEdge>> entry : input.entrySet()) {
      List<AssetLifecycleEdge> values = entry.getValue() == null ? List.of() : entry.getValue();
      List<AssetLifecycleEdge> sorted = new ArrayList<>(values);
      sorted.sort(
          Comparator.comparing(AssetLifecycleEdge::toAssetId)
              .thenComparing(AssetLifecycleEdge::relationshipType));
      copied.put(entry.getKey(), List.copyOf(sorted));
    }
    return Map.copyOf(copied);
  }
}


FILE: AssetLifecycleGraphSummary.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle;

import java.util.EnumMap;
import java.util.Map;

public record AssetLifecycleGraphSummary(
    int nodeCount,
    int edgeCount,
    Map<RelationshipType, Integer> relationshipTypeCounts,
    Map<OwnershipType, Integer> ownershipTypeCounts,
    Map<PromotionBehavior, Integer> promotionBehaviorCounts,
    Map<DeleteBehavior, Integer> deleteBehaviorCounts,
    int referencesEdgeCount) {

  public static AssetLifecycleGraphSummary from(AssetLifecycleGraph graph) {
    if (graph == null) {
      return new AssetLifecycleGraphSummary(
          0, 0, Map.of(), Map.of(), Map.of(), Map.of(), 0);
    }
    EnumMap<RelationshipType, Integer> relationshipCounts =
        new EnumMap<>(RelationshipType.class);
    EnumMap<OwnershipType, Integer> ownershipCounts =
        new EnumMap<>(OwnershipType.class);
    EnumMap<PromotionBehavior, Integer> promotionCounts =
        new EnumMap<>(PromotionBehavior.class);
    EnumMap<DeleteBehavior, Integer> deleteCounts =
        new EnumMap<>(DeleteBehavior.class);

    int references = 0;
    for (AssetLifecycleEdge edge : graph.edges()) {
      if (edge == null) {
        continue;
      }
      RelationshipType relationshipType = edge.relationshipType();
      if (relationshipType != null) {
        relationshipCounts.merge(relationshipType, 1, Integer::sum);
        if (relationshipType == RelationshipType.REFERENCES) {
          references++;
        }
      }
      OwnershipType ownershipType = edge.ownershipType();
      if (ownershipType != null) {
        ownershipCounts.merge(ownershipType, 1, Integer::sum);
      }
      PromotionBehavior promotionBehavior = edge.promotionBehavior();
      if (promotionBehavior != null) {
        promotionCounts.merge(promotionBehavior, 1, Integer::sum);
      }
      DeleteBehavior deleteBehavior = edge.deleteBehavior();
      if (deleteBehavior != null) {
        deleteCounts.merge(deleteBehavior, 1, Integer::sum);
      }
    }

    return new AssetLifecycleGraphSummary(
        graph.nodes().size(),
        graph.edges().size(),
        Map.copyOf(relationshipCounts),
        Map.copyOf(ownershipCounts),
        Map.copyOf(promotionCounts),
        Map.copyOf(deleteCounts),
        references);
  }
}

FILE: DeleteOptions.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;

public record DeleteOptions(
    boolean deleteOwnedDependencies,
    boolean deleteOrphanedSchemas,
    boolean deleteOrphanedEntitlements,
    boolean deleteHistory,
    boolean deleteData,
    boolean hardDeleteData,
    boolean force,
    boolean dryRun,
    List<DefinitionType> cascadeAssetTypes) {

  public DeleteOptions {
    cascadeAssetTypes = cascadeAssetTypes == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(cascadeAssetTypes);
  }

  public static DeleteOptions defaults() {
    return new DeleteOptions(true, true, true, false, false, false, false, true, List.of());
  }

  public DeleteOptions forExecution() {
    if (!dryRun) {
      return this;
    }
    return new DeleteOptions(
        deleteOwnedDependencies,
        deleteOrphanedSchemas,
        deleteOrphanedEntitlements,
        deleteHistory,
        deleteData,
        hardDeleteData,
        force,
        false,
        cascadeAssetTypes);
  }

  public boolean allowsCascadeType(DefinitionType definitionType) {
    if (cascadeAssetTypes.isEmpty()) {
      return true;
    }
    DefinitionType resolved = definitionType == null ? DefinitionType.UNKNOWN : definitionType;
    for (DefinitionType allowed : cascadeAssetTypes) {
      if (allowed == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (allowed == resolved) {
        return true;
      }
      if (allowed.name().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).equals(resolved.name().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT))) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.lifecycle;

import java.util.ArrayDeque;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Set;
