public final class PromotionPlanner {
  private PromotionPlanner() {}

  public static PromotionPlan plan(AssetLifecycleGraph graph, String rootAssetIdOrToken, String targetLane) {
    return plan(graph, rootAssetIdOrToken, targetLane, null, PromotionOptions.defaults());
  }

  public static PromotionPlan plan(
      AssetLifecycleGraph graph,
      String rootAssetIdOrToken,
      String targetLane,
      AssetLifecycleGraph targetGraph,
      PromotionOptions options) {
    PromotionOptions resolvedOptions = options == null ? PromotionOptions.defaults() : options;
    String normalizedRootToken = trim(rootAssetIdOrToken);
    String resolvedRoot = resolveRootAssetId(graph, normalizedRootToken);

    List<PromotionBlocker> blockers = new ArrayList<>();
    LinkedHashSet<String> assetsToPromote = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    LinkedHashSet<String> assetsToRebind = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    LinkedHashSet<String> assetsSkipped = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    LinkedHashSet<String> missingTargetAssets = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    LinkedHashSet<String> sharedAssets = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    LinkedHashSet<String> manualActions = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    LinkedHashSet<String> warnings = new LinkedHashSet<>();

    if (graph == null) {
      blockers.add(
          new PromotionBlocker(
              normalizedRootToken,
              "<graph>",
              "GRAPH_UNAVAILABLE",
              "Lifecycle graph is required for promotion planning."));
      return new PromotionPlan(
          normalizedRootToken,
          trim(targetLane),
          resolvedOptions,
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          blockers,
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of());
    }
    if (resolvedRoot == null || !graph.hasAsset(resolvedRoot)) {
      blockers.add(
          new PromotionBlocker(
              normalizedRootToken,
              "<graph>",
              "ROOT_NOT_FOUND",
              "Root asset was not found in lifecycle graph."));
      return new PromotionPlan(
          normalizedRootToken,
          trim(targetLane),
          resolvedOptions,
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          blockers,
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of(),
          List.of());
    }

    if (targetGraph == null && resolvedOptions.failIfMissingRequiredTargetDependency()) {
      warnings.add(
          "Target lane graph not provided; missing required rebind dependencies cannot be fully verified.");
    }

    ArrayDeque<String> queue = new ArrayDeque<>();
    queue.add(resolvedRoot);
    while (!queue.isEmpty()) {
      String current = queue.removeFirst();
      if (!assetsToPromote.add(current)) {
        continue;
      }
      for (AssetLifecycleEdge edge : graph.outgoing(current)) {
        String dependency = edge.toAssetId();
        if (dependency == null || dependency.equals(current)) {
          continue;
        }

        boolean required = edge.required() || edge.promotionBehavior() == PromotionBehavior.REQUIRED_WITH_PARENT;
        DefinitionType dependencyType =
            graph.node(dependency).map(AssetLifecycleNode::type).orElse(DefinitionType.UNKNOWN);
        if (dependencyType == DefinitionType.UNKNOWN && isInternalAssetId(dependency)) {
          warnings.add(
              "Compatibility: unresolved dependency type for internal asset "
                  + dependency
                  + "; dependency skipped");
          assetsSkipped.add(dependency);
          if (required) {
            blockers.add(
                new PromotionBlocker(
                    current,
                    dependency,
                    "UNKNOWN_DEPENDENCY_TYPE",
                    "Dependency type is UNKNOWN for internal asset; cannot safely plan promotion."));
          }
          continue;
        }
        if (!isEdgeAllowedByOptions(graph, dependency, edge, resolvedOptions)) {
          assetsSkipped.add(dependency);
          if (required) {
            blockers.add(
                new PromotionBlocker(
                    current,
                    dependency,
                    "REQUIRED_CATEGORY_EXCLUDED",
                    "Required dependency excluded by promotion options."));
          }
          continue;
        }

        if (edge.promotionBehavior() == PromotionBehavior.MANUAL) {
          manualActions.add(current + " -> " + dependency + " (" + edge.relationshipType() + ")");
          assetsSkipped.add(dependency);
          if (required) {
            blockers.add(
                new PromotionBlocker(
                    current,
                    dependency,
                    "MANUAL_REQUIRED",
                    "Required dependency needs manual promotion action."));
          }
          continue;
        }
        if (edge.promotionBehavior() == PromotionBehavior.NEVER_PROMOTE) {
          assetsSkipped.add(dependency);
          if (required && isInternalAssetId(dependency)) {
            blockers.add(
                new PromotionBlocker(
                    current,
                    dependency,
                    "REQUIRED_NEVER_PROMOTE",
                    "Required dependency is marked NEVER_PROMOTE."));
          }
          continue;
        }

        boolean rebindCandidate =
            edge.promotionBehavior() == PromotionBehavior.REBIND_IN_TARGET
                || edge.ownershipType() == OwnershipType.SHARED
                || edge.ownershipType() == OwnershipType.EXTERNAL;
        if (rebindCandidate) {
          sharedAssets.add(dependency);
          if (resolvedOptions.rebindSharedAssetsInTarget()) {
            assetsToRebind.add(dependency);
          } else {
            assetsSkipped.add(dependency);
          }
          if (required
              && resolvedOptions.failIfMissingRequiredTargetDependency()
              && isInternalAssetId(dependency)
              && targetGraph != null
              && !targetGraph.hasAsset(dependency)) {
            missingTargetAssets.add(dependency);
            blockers.add(
                new PromotionBlocker(
                    current,
                    dependency,
                    "MISSING_TARGET_DEPENDENCY",
                    "Required dependency must be rebound in target lane but is missing."));
          }
          continue;
        }

        if (required && !resolvedOptions.includeRequiredDependencies()) {
          assetsSkipped.add(dependency);
          blockers.add(
              new PromotionBlocker(
                  current,
                  dependency,
                  "REQUIRED_DEPENDENCY_DISABLED",
                  "Required dependencies are disabled in promotion options."));
          continue;
        }
        if (!required && !resolvedOptions.includeOptionalDependencies()) {
          assetsSkipped.add(dependency);
          continue;
        }

        if (graph.hasAsset(dependency)) {
          queue.addLast(dependency);
        } else {
          assetsSkipped.add(dependency);
          if (required && isInternalAssetId(dependency)) {
            blockers.add(
                new PromotionBlocker(
                    current,
                    dependency,
                    "UNRESOLVED_REQUIRED_DEPENDENCY",
                    "Required dependency is not present in source lifecycle graph."));
          }
        }
      }
    }

    List<String> promote = sortStrings(assetsToPromote);
    List<String> rebind = sortStrings(assetsToRebind);
    List<String> skipped = sortStrings(assetsSkipped);
    List<String> shared = sortStrings(sharedAssets);
    List<String> missing = sortStrings(missingTargetAssets);
    List<String> manual = sortStrings(manualActions);
    List<String> warningList = sortStrings(warnings);
    List<String> order = buildPromotionExecutionOrder(graph, assetsToPromote);

    blockers.sort(
        Comparator.comparing(PromotionBlocker::assetId)
            .thenComparing(PromotionBlocker::blockedByAssetId)
            .thenComparing(PromotionBlocker::code));

    return new PromotionPlan(
        resolvedRoot,
        trim(targetLane),
        resolvedOptions,
        promote,
        rebind,
        skipped,
        blockers,
        warningList,
        order,
        missing,
        shared,
        manual);
  }

  private static boolean isEdgeAllowedByOptions(
      AssetLifecycleGraph graph, String dependency, AssetLifecycleEdge edge, PromotionOptions options) {
    if (edge.relationshipType() == RelationshipType.DOCUMENTED_BY && !options.includeDocs()) {
      return false;
    }
    DefinitionType type = graph.node(dependency).map(AssetLifecycleNode::type).orElse(DefinitionType.UNKNOWN);
    if (type == DefinitionType.SCHEMA && !options.includeSchemas()) {
      return false;
    }
    if (type == DefinitionType.ENTITLEMENT && !options.includeEntitlements()) {
      return false;
    }
    if (type == DefinitionType.CONFIG_LAYER && !options.includeConfigs()) {
      return false;
    }
    return true;
  }

  private static List<String> buildPromotionExecutionOrder(
      AssetLifecycleGraph graph, Set<String> selectedAssets) {
    Map<String, Integer> indegree = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    Map<String, LinkedHashSet<String>> edges = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String asset : selectedAssets) {
      indegree.put(asset, 0);
      edges.put(asset, new LinkedHashSet<>());
    }
    for (String dependent : selectedAssets) {
      for (AssetLifecycleEdge edge : graph.outgoing(dependent)) {
        String dependency = edge.toAssetId();
        if (!selectedAssets.contains(dependency) || dependent.equals(dependency)) {
          continue;
        }
        if (edge.promotionBehavior() == PromotionBehavior.REBIND_IN_TARGET
            || edge.promotionBehavior() == PromotionBehavior.NEVER_PROMOTE) {
          continue;
        }
        if (edges.get(dependency).add(dependent)) {
          indegree.put(dependent, indegree.get(dependent) + 1);
        }
      }
    }

    ArrayDeque<String> queue = new ArrayDeque<>();
    List<String> sortedRoots = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, Integer> entry : indegree.entrySet()) {
      if (entry.getValue() == 0) {
        sortedRoots.add(entry.getKey());
      }
    }
    sortedRoots.sort(String::compareToIgnoreCase);
    for (String root : sortedRoots) {
      queue.add(root);
    }

    List<String> order = new ArrayList<>(selectedAssets.size());
    while (!queue.isEmpty()) {
      String next = queue.removeFirst();
      order.add(next);
      List<String> dependents = new ArrayList<>(edges.getOrDefault(next, new LinkedHashSet<>()));
      dependents.sort(String::compareToIgnoreCase);
      for (String dependent : dependents) {
        int remaining = indegree.get(dependent) - 1;
        indegree.put(dependent, remaining);
        if (remaining == 0) {
          queue.addLast(dependent);
        }
      }
    }

    if (order.size() < selectedAssets.size()) {
      List<String> cyclic = new ArrayList<>();
      for (String asset : selectedAssets) {
        if (!order.contains(asset)) {
          cyclic.add(asset);
        }
      }
      cyclic.sort(String::compareToIgnoreCase);
      order.addAll(cyclic);
    }
    return List.copyOf(order);
  }

  private static boolean isInternalAssetId(String assetId) {
    String value = trim(assetId);
    if (value == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return value.startsWith("dataset:")
        || value.startsWith("service:")
        || value.startsWith("stream:")
        || value.startsWith("schema:")
        || value.startsWith("config:")
        || value.startsWith("connection:")
        || value.startsWith("ingest:")
        || value.startsWith("ingest-source:")
        || value.startsWith("entitlement:");
  }

  private static String resolveRootAssetId(AssetLifecycleGraph graph, String rootAssetIdOrToken) {
    if (graph == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (rootAssetIdOrToken == null || rootAssetIdOrToken.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    if (graph.hasAsset(rootAssetIdOrToken)) {
      return rootAssetIdOrToken;
    }
    return graph.resolveAssetId(rootAssetIdOrToken);
  }

  private static List<String> sortStrings(Set<String> values) {
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(values);
    sorted.sort(String::compareToIgnoreCase);
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }

  private static String trim(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;

public record EntitlementObligations(
    List<String> rowFilters, List<String> columnsAllow, Map<String, String> columnsMask) {
  private static final EntitlementObligations EMPTY =
      new EntitlementObligations(List.of(), List.of(), Map.of());

  public EntitlementObligations {
    rowFilters = immutableList(rowFilters);
    columnsAllow = immutableList(columnsAllow);
    columnsMask = immutableMap(columnsMask);
  }

  public static EntitlementObligations empty() {
    return EMPTY;
  }

  public boolean isEmpty() {
    return rowFilters.isEmpty() && columnsAllow.isEmpty() && columnsMask.isEmpty();
  }

  private static List<String> immutableList(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return Collections.unmodifiableList(new ArrayList<>(values));
  }

  private static Map<String, String> immutableMap(Map<String, String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    return Collections.unmodifiableMap(new LinkedHashMap<>(values));
  }
}


FILE: EntitlementsAction.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonCreator;
import java.util.Locale;

public enum EntitlementsAction {
  START,
  INVOKE,
  READ,
  WRITE;

  @JsonCreator
  public static EntitlementsAction fromWire(String raw) {
    if (raw == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("action is required");
    }
    String trimmed = raw.trim();
    if (trimmed.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("action is required");
    }

    String lower = trimmed.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return switch (lower) {
      case "start", "service.start" -> START;
      case "invoke", "service.invoke" -> INVOKE;
      case "read", "data.read" -> READ;
      case "write", "data.write" -> WRITE;
      default -> {
        String normalized = trimmed.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT).replace('-', '_').replace(' ', '_');
        yield switch (normalized) {
          case "START", "SERVICE_START" -> START;
          case "INVOKE", "SERVICE_INVOKE" -> INVOKE;
          case "READ", "DATA_READ" -> READ;
          case "WRITE", "DATA_WRITE" -> WRITE;
          default -> throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported action: " + raw);
        };
      }
    };
  }

  public String toWire() {
    return name();
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonCreator;
import java.util.Locale;

public enum EntitlementsScopeType {
  SERVICE,
  DATASET,
  NAMESPACE,
  APP,
  GROUP,
  FEED,
  STREAM,
  MATERIALIZED,
  ENDPOINT,
  ROLE,
  TOPIC;

  @JsonCreator
  public static EntitlementsScopeType fromWire(String raw) {
    if (raw == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("scopeType is required");
    }
    String trimmed = raw.trim();
    if (trimmed.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("scopeType is required");
    }
    String normalized = trimmed.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT).replace('-', '_').replace(' ', '_');
    return switch (normalized) {
      case "SERVICE" -> SERVICE;
      case "DATASET", "SCHEMA", "TABLE" -> DATASET;
      case "NAMESPACE" -> NAMESPACE;
      case "APP", "APPLICATION" -> APP;
      case "GROUP" -> GROUP;
      case "FEED" -> FEED;
      case "STREAM" -> STREAM;
      case "MATERIALIZED" -> MATERIALIZED;
      case "ENDPOINT" -> ENDPOINT;
      case "ROLE" -> ROLE;
      case "TOPIC" -> TOPIC;
      default -> throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported scopeType: " + raw);
    };
  }

  public String toWire() {
    return name();
  }
}

FILE: AmpsEntitlementEventPublisher.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.events;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.ControlConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryTopics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class AmpsEntitlementEventPublisher implements EntitlementEventPublisher {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AmpsEntitlementEventPublisher.class);
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = DiscoveryCodec.mapper();

  private final ControlConnection controlConnection;
  private final Settings settings;

  public AmpsEntitlementEventPublisher(ControlConnection controlConnection, Settings settings) {
    this.controlConnection = java.util.Objects.requireNonNull(controlConnection, "controlConnection");
    this.settings = settings == null ? Settings.defaults() : settings.normalized();
  }

  @Override
  public void publish(EntitlementEvent event) {
    if (event == null) {
      return;
    }
    String payload;
    try {
      payload = MAPPER.writeValueAsString(event);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      LOGGER.error("[Entitlements][Events][AMPS] encode failed message={}", ex.toString(), ex);
      return;
    }

    long backoff = settings.initialBackoffMillis();
    for (int attempt = 0; ; attempt++) {
      try {
        controlConnection.amps().publish(settings.topic(), payload);
        return;
      } catch (Exception ex) {
        if (attempt >= settings.maxRetries()) {
          LOGGER.error("[Entitlements][Events][AMPS] publish failed topic={} retries={} message={}", settings.topic(), settings.maxRetries(), ex.toString(), ex);
          return;
        }
        LOGGER.warn("[Entitlements][Events][AMPS] publish retry topic={} attempt={} backoffMs={} message={}", settings.topic(), attempt + 1, backoff, ex.toString());
        sleep(backoff);
        backoff = nextBackoff(backoff, settings.maxBackoffMillis(), settings.backoffMultiplier());
      }
    }
  }

  private static long nextBackoff(long current, long maxBackoffMillis, double multiplier) {
    long scaled = Math.max(1L, (long) Math.ceil(current * multiplier));
    return Math.min(maxBackoffMillis, scaled);
  }

  private static void sleep(long millis) {
    try {
      Thread.sleep(Math.max(0L, millis));
    } catch (InterruptedException ex) {
      Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
    }
  }

  public record Settings(
      String connection,
      String topic,
      int maxRetries,
      long initialBackoffMillis,
      long maxBackoffMillis,
      double backoffMultiplier) {

    public Settings normalized() {
      String normalizedConnection = Strings.firstNonBlank(connection, "amps-fabric-discovery");
      String normalizedTopic = Strings.firstNonBlank(topic, DiscoveryTopics.EVENTS_ENTITLEMENTS);
      int normalizedRetries = Math.max(0, maxRetries);
      long normalizedInitial = Math.max(1L, initialBackoffMillis);
      long normalizedMax = Math.max(normalizedInitial, maxBackoffMillis);
      double normalizedMultiplier = backoffMultiplier <= 1.0d ? 2.0d : backoffMultiplier;
      return new Settings(
          normalizedConnection,
          normalizedTopic,
          normalizedRetries,
          normalizedInitial,
          normalizedMax,
          normalizedMultiplier);
    }

    public static Settings defaults() {
      return new Settings("amps-fabric-discovery", DiscoveryTopics.EVENTS_ENTITLEMENTS, 3, 100L, 2_000L, 2.0d);
    }
  }
}

FILE: PublishingDataEntitlements.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.events;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.UUID;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.data.DataEntitlements;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class PublishingDataEntitlements implements DataEntitlements {
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = DiscoveryCodec.mapper();

  private final DataEntitlements delegate;
  private final EntitlementEventPublisher publisher;
  private final Supplier<EntitlementEventContext> contextSupplier;
  private final String implementation;

  public PublishingDataEntitlements(
      DataEntitlements delegate,
      EntitlementEventPublisher publisher,
      Supplier<EntitlementEventContext> contextSupplier,
      String implementation) {
    this.delegate = Objects.requireNonNull(delegate, "delegate");
    this.publisher =
        publisher == null ? NoopEntitlementEventPublisher.INSTANCE : publisher;
    this.contextSupplier = Objects.requireNonNull(contextSupplier, "contextSupplier");
    this.implementation = Strings.firstNonBlank(implementation, "UNKNOWN");
  }

  @Override
  public Decision authorizeRead(Identity identity, String datasetCanonicalId) {
    Decision decision = delegate.authorizeRead(identity, datasetCanonicalId);
    publish(identity, datasetCanonicalId, "READ", decision);
    return decision;
  }

  @Override
  public Decision authorizeWrite(Identity identity, String datasetCanonicalId) {
    Decision decision = delegate.authorizeWrite(identity, datasetCanonicalId);
    publish(identity, datasetCanonicalId, "WRITE", decision);
    return decision;
  }

  private void publish(
      Identity identity, String datasetCanonicalId, String action, Decision decision) {
    EntitlementEventContext context = contextSupplier.get();
    publisher.publish(
        new EntitlementEvent(
            EntitlementEvent.SCHEMA_VERSION,
            UUID.randomUUID().toString(),
            Instant.now().toString(),
            implementation,
            "DATASET",
            action,
            "DIRECT",
            datasetCanonicalId,
            "data." + Strings.firstNonBlank(action, "read").toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT),
            identity == null ? null : identity.subject(),
            identity == null ? null : identity.delegatedSubject(),
            decision != null && decision.allowed(),
            decisionReason(decision),
            context == null ? null : context.sessionId(),
            context == null ? null : context.sessionGroup(),
            context == null ? null : context.sessionApp(),
            context == null ? null : context.sessionInstance(),
            context == null ? null : context.environment(),
            context == null ? null : context.region(),
            context == null ? null : context.site(),
            null,
            null,
            toJson(decision == null ? null : decision.obligations())));
  }

  private static String toJson(Object value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return MAPPER.writeValueAsString(value);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      return "{\"error\":\"serialization\"}";
    }
  }

  private static String decisionReason(Decision decision) {
    if (decision == null) {
      return "DENIED";
    }
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(decision.reason()), "DENIED");
  }
}


FILE: PublishingServiceEntitlements.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.events;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.UUID;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.services.ServiceEntitlements;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class PublishingServiceEntitlements implements ServiceEntitlements {
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = DiscoveryCodec.mapper();

  private final ServiceEntitlements delegate;
  private final EntitlementEventPublisher publisher;
  private final Supplier<EntitlementEventContext> contextSupplier;
  private final String implementation;

  public PublishingServiceEntitlements(
      ServiceEntitlements delegate,
      EntitlementEventPublisher publisher,
      Supplier<EntitlementEventContext> contextSupplier,
      String implementation) {
    this.delegate = Objects.requireNonNull(delegate, "delegate");
    this.publisher =
        publisher == null ? NoopEntitlementEventPublisher.INSTANCE : publisher;
    this.contextSupplier = Objects.requireNonNull(contextSupplier, "contextSupplier");
    this.implementation = Strings.firstNonBlank(implementation, "UNKNOWN");
  }

  @Override
  public Decision authorize(Identity identity, Request request) {
    Decision decision = delegate.authorize(identity, request);
    publish(identity, request, decision);
    return decision;
  }

  public ServiceEntitlements delegate() {
    return delegate;
  }

  private void publish(Identity identity, Request request, Decision decision) {
    EntitlementEventContext context = contextSupplier.get();
    String action = request == null || request.action() == null ? null : request.action().name();
    String transport =
        request == null || request.transport() == null ? null : request.transport().name();
    String reason = Strings.firstNonBlank(decisionReason(decision), "DENIED");
    publisher.publish(
        new EntitlementEvent(
            EntitlementEvent.SCHEMA_VERSION,
            UUID.randomUUID().toString(),
            Instant.now().toString(),
            implementation,
            "SERVICE",
            action,
            transport,
            request == null ? null : request.serviceResourceId(),
            request == null ? null : request.operationName(),
            identity == null ? null : identity.subject(),
            identity == null ? null : identity.delegatedSubject(),
            decision != null && decision.allowed(),
            reason,
            context == null ? null : context.sessionId(),
            context == null ? null : context.sessionGroup(),
            context == null ? null : context.sessionApp(),
            context == null ? null : context.sessionInstance(),
            context == null ? null : context.environment(),
            context == null ? null : context.region(),
            context == null ? null : context.site(),
            toJson(request == null ? null : request.bindings()),
            toJson(request == null ? null : request.metadata()),
            null));
  }

  private static String toJson(Map<String, String> map) {
    if (map == null || map.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return MAPPER.writeValueAsString(map);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      return "{\"error\":\"serialization\"}";
    }
  }

  private static String decisionReason(Decision decision) {
    if (decision == null) {
      return "DENIED";
    }
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(decision.reason()), "DENIED");
  }
}

================================================================================
PACKAGE: org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.manager

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.manager;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.CloseSupport;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.UUID;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.ControlConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryTopics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvironment;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.data.DataEntitlements;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.services.ServiceEntitlements;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.events.AmpsEntitlementEventPublisher;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.events.EntitlementEventContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.events.EntitlementEventPublisher;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.events.NoopEntitlementEventPublisher;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.events.PublishingDataEntitlements;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.events.PublishingServiceEntitlements;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.noop.data.DataEntitlementsNoop;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.noop.services.ServiceEntitlementsNoop;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.provider.DefaultEntitlementProviderRegistry;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.provider.EntitlementProviderRegistry;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.provider.EntitlementProviderSelector;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.simple.data.DataEntitlementsSimple;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.simple.services.ServiceEntitlementsSimpleManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class EntitlementsManagerImpl implements AutoCloseable {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(EntitlementsManagerImpl.class);
  private static final String PLATFORM_GROUP = "platform";
  private static final String ENVIRONMENT_NAME = "environment";
  private static final String DISCOVERY_CONNECTION_NAME = "amps-fabric-discovery";

  public record RuntimeInfo(
      String implementation,
      boolean eventsEnabled,
      String eventsTransport,
      String eventsConnection,
      String eventsTopic) {}

  private final ServiceEntitlements serviceEntitlements;
  private final DataEntitlements dataEntitlements;
  private final String implementation;
  private final EntitlementEventsSettings eventsSettings;
  private final EntitlementEventPublisher publisher;
  private final AutoCloseable implementationRuntime;

  public EntitlementsManagerImpl(
      DiscoveryCache cache,
      ControlConnection controlConnection,
      String sessionId,
      String group,
      String appName,
      String instance,
      String environment,
      String region,
      String site,
      boolean serviceEntitlementsLogDecisions) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(cache, "cache");
    String resolvedGroup = Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "group");
    ResolvedEntitlements resolved = resolveEntitlementsRuntime(cache);
    this.implementation = resolved.mode().name();
    this.eventsSettings = resolved.events();
    this.publisher = createEntitlementEventPublisher(resolved.events(), controlConnection);
    String resolvedSessionId = resolveAuditSessionId(sessionId, appName, instance);
    if (Strings.trimToNull(sessionId) == null) {
      LOGGER.warn("[Entitlements][Events] missing sessionId; generated fallback sessionId={} app={} instance={}", resolvedSessionId, Strings.trimToNull(appName), Strings.trimToNull(instance));
    }

    Supplier<EntitlementEventContext> contextSupplier =
        () ->
            new EntitlementEventContext(
                resolvedSessionId, resolvedGroup, appName, instance, environment, region, site);

    AutoCloseable createdImplementationRuntime = null;
    ServiceEntitlements baseService;
    DataEntitlements baseData;
    if (resolved.mode() == EntitlementsImplementation.SIMPLE) {
      EntitlementProviderRegistry providerRegistry =
          new DefaultEntitlementProviderRegistry(cache);
      EntitlementProviderSelector providerSelector =
          new EntitlementProviderSelector(cache, providerRegistry);
      ServiceEntitlementsSimpleManager simpleManager =
          new ServiceEntitlementsSimpleManager(
              cache, resolvedGroup, serviceEntitlementsLogDecisions, providerRegistry, providerSelector);
      createdImplementationRuntime = simpleManager;
      baseService = simpleManager.serviceEntitlements();
      baseData = new DataEntitlementsSimple(cache, resolvedGroup, providerRegistry, providerSelector);
    } else if (resolved.mode() == EntitlementsImplementation.NONE) {
      baseService = new ServiceEntitlementsNoop(serviceEntitlementsLogDecisions);
      baseData = DataEntitlementsNoop.INSTANCE;
    } else {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Unsupported entitlements implementation in fabric-lite session: " + resolved.mode());
    }
    this.implementationRuntime = createdImplementationRuntime;
    this.serviceEntitlements =
        new PublishingServiceEntitlements(
            baseService, publisher, contextSupplier, resolved.mode().name());
    this.dataEntitlements =
        new PublishingDataEntitlements(baseData, publisher, contextSupplier, resolved.mode().name());
  }

  public ServiceEntitlements serviceEntitlements() {
    return serviceEntitlements;
  }

  public DataEntitlements dataEntitlements() {
    return dataEntitlements;
  }

  public String implementation() {
    return implementation;
  }

  public RuntimeInfo runtimeInfo() {
    return new RuntimeInfo(
        implementation,
        eventsSettings.enabled(),
        eventsSettings.transport().name(),
        eventsSettings.connection(),
        eventsSettings.topic());
  }

  public void close() {
    CloseSupport.closeQuietly(implementationRuntime);
    CloseSupport.closeQuietly(publisher);
  }


  private static String resolveAuditSessionId(String sessionId, String appName, String instance) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(sessionId);
    if (normalized != null) {
      return normalized;
    }
    String app = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(appName), "unknown-app");
    String node = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(instance), "default");
    return "app:" + app + "|" + node + "|" + UUID.randomUUID();
  }

  private static ResolvedEntitlements resolveEntitlementsRuntime(DiscoveryCache cache) {
    DefinitionEnvironment.Entitlements entitlements =
        cache
            .get(DefinitionEnvironment.class, PLATFORM_GROUP, ENVIRONMENT_NAME)
            .map(DefinitionEnvironment::entitlements)
            .orElse(null);
    EntitlementsImplementation implementation =
        EntitlementsImplementation.fromWire(entitlements == null ? null : entitlements.implementation());
    EntitlementEventsSettings events =
        EntitlementEventsSettings.fromModel(entitlements == null ? null : entitlements.events());
    LOGGER.info("[Entitlements] implementation={} eventsEnabled={} eventsTransport={} eventsTopic={} eventsConnection={}", implementation, events.enabled(), events.transport(), events.topic(), events.connection());
    return new ResolvedEntitlements(implementation, events);
  }

  private static EntitlementEventPublisher createEntitlementEventPublisher(
      EntitlementEventsSettings settings, ControlConnection controlConnection) {
    EntitlementEventsSettings resolved =
        settings == null ? EntitlementEventsSettings.disabled() : settings;
    if (!resolved.enabled() || resolved.transport() == EntitlementEventsTransport.NOOP) {
      return NoopEntitlementEventPublisher.INSTANCE;
    }
    if (resolved.transport() == EntitlementEventsTransport.S3) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Entitlements event transport S3 is not implemented yet");
    }
    if (resolved.transport() != EntitlementEventsTransport.AMPS) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Unsupported entitlements event transport: " + resolved.transport());
    }
    String connection = Strings.firstNonBlank(resolved.connection(), DISCOVERY_CONNECTION_NAME);
    if (!DISCOVERY_CONNECTION_NAME.equalsIgnoreCase(connection)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Unsupported entitlements AMPS connection '"
              + connection
              + "' (expected "
              + DISCOVERY_CONNECTION_NAME
              + ")");
    }
    if (controlConnection == null) {
      LOGGER.warn(
          "[Entitlements][Events] AMPS transport requested but ControlConnection is unavailable; using NOOP publisher");
      return NoopEntitlementEventPublisher.INSTANCE;
    }
    return new AmpsEntitlementEventPublisher(
        controlConnection,
        new AmpsEntitlementEventPublisher.Settings(
            connection,
            resolved.topic(),
            resolved.maxRetries(),
            resolved.initialBackoffMillis(),
            resolved.maxBackoffMillis(),
            resolved.backoffMultiplier()));
  }

  private enum EntitlementsImplementation {
    NONE,
    SIMPLE,
    ZANZIBAR;

    static EntitlementsImplementation fromWire(String raw) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(raw);
      if (normalized == null) {
        return SIMPLE;
      }
      return switch (normalized.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT)) {
        case "NONE" -> NONE;
        case "SIMPLE" -> SIMPLE;
        case "ZANZIBAR" -> ZANZIBAR;
        default ->
            throw new IllegalStateException(
                "Unsupported entitlements implementation '"
                    + raw
                    + "' (expected NONE, SIMPLE, or ZANZIBAR)");
      };
    }
  }

  private enum EntitlementEventsTransport {
    NOOP,
    AMPS,
    S3;

    static EntitlementEventsTransport fromWire(String raw) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(raw);
      if (normalized == null) {
        return NOOP;
      }
      return switch (normalized.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT)) {
        case "NOOP", "NONE" -> NOOP;
        case "AMPS" -> AMPS;
        case "S3" -> S3;
        default ->
            throw new IllegalStateException(
                "Unsupported entitlements events transport '"
                    + raw
                    + "' (expected NOOP, AMPS, or S3)");
      };
    }
  }

  private record EntitlementEventsSettings(
      boolean enabled,
      EntitlementEventsTransport transport,
      String connection,
      String topic,
      int maxRetries,
      long initialBackoffMillis,
      long maxBackoffMillis,
      double backoffMultiplier) {

    static EntitlementEventsSettings disabled() {
      return new EntitlementEventsSettings(
          false,
          EntitlementEventsTransport.NOOP,
          DISCOVERY_CONNECTION_NAME,
          DiscoveryTopics.EVENTS_ENTITLEMENTS,
          0,
          100L,
          2_000L,
          2.0d);
    }

    static EntitlementEventsSettings fromModel(DefinitionEnvironment.Events model) {
      if (model == null || !Boolean.TRUE.equals(model.enabled())) {
        return disabled();
      }
      EntitlementEventsTransport transport = EntitlementEventsTransport.fromWire(model.transport());
      DefinitionEnvironment.EventsAmps amps = model.amps();
      String connection =
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              amps == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(amps.connection()),
              DISCOVERY_CONNECTION_NAME);
      String topic =
          Strings.firstNonBlank(
              amps == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(amps.topic()),
              DiscoveryTopics.EVENTS_ENTITLEMENTS);
      int maxRetries = amps == null || amps.maxRetries() == null ? 3 : Math.max(0, amps.maxRetries());
      long initialBackoffMillis =
          amps == null || amps.initialBackoffMillis() == null
              ? 100L
              : Math.max(1L, amps.initialBackoffMillis());
      long maxBackoffMillis =
          amps == null || amps.maxBackoffMillis() == null
              ? 2_000L
              : Math.max(initialBackoffMillis, amps.maxBackoffMillis());
      double backoffMultiplier =
          amps == null || amps.backoffMultiplier() == null
              ? 2.0d
              : amps.backoffMultiplier() <= 1.0d ? 2.0d : amps.backoffMultiplier();
      return new EntitlementEventsSettings(
          true,
          transport,
          connection,
          topic,
          maxRetries,
          initialBackoffMillis,
          maxBackoffMillis,
          backoffMultiplier);
    }
  }

  private record ResolvedEntitlements(
      EntitlementsImplementation mode, EntitlementEventsSettings events) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.noop.services;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.services.ServiceEntitlements;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class ServiceEntitlementsNoop implements ServiceEntitlements {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ServiceEntitlementsNoop.class);

  private final boolean logDecisions;

  public ServiceEntitlementsNoop() {
    this(false);
  }

  public ServiceEntitlementsNoop(boolean logDecisions) {
    this.logDecisions = logDecisions;
  }

  @Override
  public Decision authorize(Identity identity, Request request) {
    if (logDecisions) {
      String action = request == null || request.action() == null ? "<unknown>" : request.action().name();
      String serviceId = request == null ? null : request.serviceResourceId();
      String operation = request == null ? null : request.operationName();
      LOGGER.info("[Entitlements][NOOP] action={} serviceId={} operation={} allowed=true", action, serviceId, operation);
    }
    return new Decision(true, "NOOP", null);
  }
}

PACKAGE: org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.simple

FILE: PlatformModelMembership.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.simple;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionPlatform;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.provider.EntitlementSubjectCandidates;

public final class PlatformModelMembership {
  private PlatformModelMembership() {}

  public static Set<String> membershipSubjectCandidates(String subject) {
    return EntitlementSubjectCandidates.membershipSubjectCandidates(subject);
  }

  public static Map<String, Set<String>> buildMembershipIndex(DefinitionPlatform model) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(model, "platform model is required");
    DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode root = model.root();
    if (root == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("platform model root is required");
    }

    Map<String, Set<String>> membership = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    walk(root, Set.of(), membership);

    Map<String, Set<String>> immutable = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, Set<String>> entry : membership.entrySet()) {
      immutable.put(entry.getKey(), Set.copyOf(entry.getValue()));
    }
    return Map.copyOf(immutable);
  }

  private static void walk(
      DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node,
      Set<String> inheritedContainerGroups,
      Map<String, Set<String>> membership) {
    if (node == null) {
      return;
    }

    Set<String> containerAtNode = new LinkedHashSet<>(inheritedContainerGroups);
    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup> groups = node.groups();
    if (groups != null) {
      for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup group : groups) {
        if (group == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String id = groupId(group);
        if (id == null) {
          continue;
        }

        Set<String> perGroup = new LinkedHashSet<>(inheritedContainerGroups);
        perGroup.add(id);
        addMembership(membership, group.userIds(), perGroup);
        addMembership(membership, group.serviceIds(), perGroup);

        if (isContainerGroup(node, id)) {
          containerAtNode.add(id);
        }
      }
    }

    List<DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode> children = node.ous();
    if (children == null) {
      return;
    }
    for (DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode child : children) {
      walk(child, containerAtNode, membership);
    }
  }

  private static void addMembership(
      Map<String, Set<String>> membership,
      List<String> principals,
      Set<String> groups) {
    if (principals == null || principals.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    for (String principal : principals) {
      if (principal == null) {
        continue;
      }
      membership.computeIfAbsent(principal, ignored -> new LinkedHashSet<>()).addAll(groups);
    }
  }

  private static String groupId(DefinitionPlatform.OrgGroup group) {
    if (group.name() != null) {
      return group.name();
    }
    if (group.nodeName() != null) {
      return group.nodeName();
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static boolean isContainerGroup(DefinitionPlatform.OrgNode node, String groupId) {
    if (node == null || groupId == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return groupId.equals(node.name()) || groupId.equals(node.nodeName());
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = value.trim();
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? null : normalized;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.view;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Set;

public record DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView(List<String> apps, List<String> groups, List<String> users) {

  public DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView {
    apps = normalize(apps);
    groups = normalize(groups);
    users = normalize(users);
  }

  public static DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView empty() {
    return new DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView(List.of(), List.of(), List.of());
  }

  private static List<String> normalize(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Set<String> dedup = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      if (value == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String trimmed = value.trim();
      if (!trimmed.isEmpty()) {
        dedup.add(trimmed);
      }
    }
    if (dedup.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(dedup);
    sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }
}


FILE: DatasetEntitlementsView.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.view;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Set;

public record DatasetEntitlementsView(
    String datasetId,
    int direct,
    int effective,
    DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView read,
    DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView write,
    Map<String, ColumnEntitlement> columnRules,
    Map<String, RowEntitlement> rowRules) {

  public DatasetEntitlementsView {
    read = read == null ? DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView.empty() : read;
    write = write == null ? DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView.empty() : write;
    columnRules = normalizeColumnRules(columnRules);
    rowRules = normalizeRowRules(rowRules);
  }

  public static DatasetEntitlementsView empty(String datasetId) {
    return new DatasetEntitlementsView(
        datasetId,
        0,
        0,
        DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView.empty(),
        DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView.empty(),
        Map.of(),
        Map.of());
  }

  public DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView subjectsForAction(String action) {
    if (action == null || action.isBlank()) {
      return DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView.empty();
    }
    String normalized = action.trim().toUpperCase(java.util.Locale.ROOT);
    return switch (normalized) {
      case "READ", "DATA.READ" -> read;
      case "WRITE", "DATA.WRITE" -> write;
      default -> DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView.empty();
    };
  }

  public DatasetEntitlementsView withActionSubjects(
      String action, DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView subjects) {
    if (action == null || action.isBlank()) {
      return this;
    }
    DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView nextSubjects =
        subjects == null ? DatasetEntitlementSubjectsView.empty() : subjects;
    String normalized = action.trim().toUpperCase(java.util.Locale.ROOT);
    if ("READ".equals(normalized) || "DATA.READ".equals(normalized)) {
      return new DatasetEntitlementsView(
          datasetId, direct, effective, nextSubjects, write, columnRules, rowRules);
    }
    if ("WRITE".equals(normalized) || "DATA.WRITE".equals(normalized)) {
      return new DatasetEntitlementsView(
          datasetId, direct, effective, read, nextSubjects, columnRules, rowRules);
    }
    return this;
  }

  private static Map<String, ColumnEntitlement> normalizeColumnRules(
      Map<String, ColumnEntitlement> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    Map<String, ColumnEntitlement> normalized = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, ColumnEntitlement> entry : values.entrySet()) {
      String key = normalizeKey(entry.getKey());
      if (key == null) {
        continue;
      }
      ColumnEntitlement value = entry.getValue();
      normalized.put(
          key,
          value == null
              ? new ColumnEntitlement(List.of(), Map.of())
              : new ColumnEntitlement(value.allowedColumns(), value.maskedColumns()));
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static Map<String, RowEntitlement> normalizeRowRules(Map<String, RowEntitlement> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    Map<String, RowEntitlement> normalized = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, RowEntitlement> entry : values.entrySet()) {
      String key = normalizeKey(entry.getKey());
      if (key == null) {
        continue;
      }
      RowEntitlement value = entry.getValue();
      if (value == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String filterExpression = value.filterExpression() == null ? "" : value.filterExpression().trim();
      if (filterExpression.isEmpty()) {
        continue;
      }
      normalized.put(key, new RowEntitlement(filterExpression, Math.max(0, value.ruleCount())));
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static String normalizeKey(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }

  public record ColumnEntitlement(List<String> allowedColumns, Map<String, String> maskedColumns) {
    public ColumnEntitlement {
      allowedColumns = normalizeColumns(allowedColumns);
      maskedColumns = normalizeMasks(maskedColumns);
    }

    private static List<String> normalizeColumns(List<String> values) {
      if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      Set<String> dedup = new LinkedHashSet<>();
      for (String value : values) {
        if (value == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String trimmed = value.trim();
        if (!trimmed.isEmpty()) {
          dedup.add(trimmed);
        }
      }
      if (dedup.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(dedup);
      sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
      return List.copyOf(sorted);
    }

    private static Map<String, String> normalizeMasks(Map<String, String> values) {
      if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
        return Map.of();
      }
      Map<String, String> normalized = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : values.entrySet()) {
        String column = entry.getKey() == null ? null : entry.getKey().trim();
        String maskType = entry.getValue() == null ? null : entry.getValue().trim();
        if (column == null || column.isEmpty() || maskType == null || maskType.isEmpty()) {
          continue;
        }
        normalized.put(column, maskType);
      }
      return normalized.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(normalized);
    }
  }

  public record RowEntitlement(String filterExpression, int ruleCount) {}
}


FILE: EntitlementSubjectsView.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.view;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Set;

public record EntitlementSubjectsView(List<String> apps, List<String> groups, List<String> users) {

  public EntitlementSubjectsView {
    apps = normalize(apps);
    groups = normalize(groups);
    users = normalize(users);
  }

  public static EntitlementSubjectsView empty() {
    return new EntitlementSubjectsView(List.of(), List.of(), List.of());
  }

  public List<String> forType(EntitlementSubjectType subjectType) {
    if (subjectType == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return switch (subjectType) {
      case APP -> apps;
      case GROUP -> groups;
      case USER -> users;
    };
  }

  public EntitlementSubjectsView withType(EntitlementSubjectType subjectType, List<String> values) {
    List<String> normalized = normalize(values);
    if (subjectType == null) {
      return this;
    }
    return switch (subjectType) {
      case APP -> new EntitlementSubjectsView(normalized, groups, users);
      case GROUP -> new EntitlementSubjectsView(apps, normalized, users);
      case USER -> new EntitlementSubjectsView(apps, groups, normalized);
    };
  }

  private static List<String> normalize(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Set<String> dedup = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      if (value == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String trimmed = value.trim();
      if (!trimmed.isEmpty()) {
        dedup.add(trimmed);
      }
    }
    if (dedup.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(dedup);
    sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    return List.copyOf(sorted);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.view;

import java.util.Locale;

public enum EntitlementSubjectType {
  APP,
  GROUP,
  USER;

  public static EntitlementSubjectType fromWire(String value) {
    if (value == null || value.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("subjectType is required");
    }
    String normalized = value.trim().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return switch (normalized) {
      case "APP", "APPS" -> APP;
      case "GROUP", "GROUPS" -> GROUP;
      case "USER", "USERS" -> USER;
      default -> throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported subjectType: " + value);
    };
  }
}


FILE: ServiceEntitlementsView.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.view;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Set;

public record ServiceEntitlementsView(
    String serviceId,
    String group,
    String serviceName,
    String serviceType,
    List<String> actions,
    Map<String, EntitlementSubjectsView> actionSubjects,
    Map<String, EntitlementSubjectsView> effectiveActionSubjects,
    EntitlementSubjectsView start,
    EntitlementSubjectsView invoke,
    TechnicalDetails technical) {

  public static final List<String> DEFAULT_SERVICE_ACTIONS = List.of("START", "INVOKE");

  public ServiceEntitlementsView {
    actions = normalizeActions(actions);
    actionSubjects = normalizeActionSubjects(actionSubjects);
    effectiveActionSubjects = normalizeActionSubjects(effectiveActionSubjects);
    start = start == null ? EntitlementSubjectsView.empty() : start;
    invoke = invoke == null ? EntitlementSubjectsView.empty() : invoke;
    technical = technical == null ? TechnicalDetails.empty() : technical;

    Map<String, EntitlementSubjectsView> merged = new LinkedHashMap<>(actionSubjects);
    merged.putIfAbsent("START", start);
    merged.putIfAbsent("INVOKE", invoke);
    actionSubjects = Map.copyOf(merged);
  }

  public static ServiceEntitlementsView empty(String group, String serviceName, String serviceId, String serviceType) {
    return new ServiceEntitlementsView(
        serviceId,
        group,
        serviceName,
        serviceType,
        DEFAULT_SERVICE_ACTIONS,
        Map.of(
            "START", EntitlementSubjectsView.empty(),
            "INVOKE", EntitlementSubjectsView.empty()),
        Map.of(
            "START", EntitlementSubjectsView.empty(),
            "INVOKE", EntitlementSubjectsView.empty()),
        EntitlementSubjectsView.empty(),
        EntitlementSubjectsView.empty(),
        TechnicalDetails.empty());
  }

  public List<String> actionsOrDefault(List<String> fallback) {
    if (actions != null && !actions.isEmpty()) {
      return actions;
    }
    return normalizeActions(fallback);
  }

  public EntitlementSubjectsView subjectsForAction(String action) {
    String normalized = normalizeAction(action);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return EntitlementSubjectsView.empty();
    }
    EntitlementSubjectsView direct = actionSubjects.get(normalized);
    if (direct != null) {
      return direct;
    }
    return switch (normalized) {
      case "START" -> start;
      case "INVOKE" -> invoke;
      default -> EntitlementSubjectsView.empty();
    };
  }

  public EntitlementSubjectsView effectiveSubjectsForAction(String action) {
    String normalized = normalizeAction(action);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return EntitlementSubjectsView.empty();
    }
    EntitlementSubjectsView effective = effectiveActionSubjects.get(normalized);
    return effective == null ? EntitlementSubjectsView.empty() : effective;
  }

  public ServiceEntitlementsView withActionSubjects(String action, EntitlementSubjectsView subjects) {
    String normalized = normalizeAction(action);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return this;
    }
    EntitlementSubjectsView normalizedSubjects = subjects == null ? EntitlementSubjectsView.empty() : subjects;
    Map<String, EntitlementSubjectsView> merged = new LinkedHashMap<>(actionSubjects);
    merged.put(normalized, normalizedSubjects);
    EntitlementSubjectsView nextStart = "START".equals(normalized) ? normalizedSubjects : start;
    EntitlementSubjectsView nextInvoke = "INVOKE".equals(normalized) ? normalizedSubjects : invoke;
    return new ServiceEntitlementsView(
        serviceId,
        group,
        serviceName,
        serviceType,
        actions,
        merged,
        effectiveActionSubjects,
        nextStart,
        nextInvoke,
        technical);
  }

  private static List<String> normalizeActions(List<String> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    Set<String> dedup = new LinkedHashSet<>();
    for (String value : values) {
      String normalized = normalizeAction(value);
      if (normalized != null) {
        dedup.add(normalized);
      }
    }
    if (dedup.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return List.copyOf(dedup);
  }

  private static Map<String, EntitlementSubjectsView> normalizeActionSubjects(
      Map<String, EntitlementSubjectsView> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    Map<String, EntitlementSubjectsView> normalized = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, EntitlementSubjectsView> entry : values.entrySet()) {
      String key = normalizeAction(entry.getKey());
      if (key == null) {
        continue;
      }
      normalized.put(key, entry.getValue() == null ? EntitlementSubjectsView.empty() : entry.getValue());
    }
    return normalized.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(normalized);
  }

  private static String normalizeAction(String action) {
    if (action == null || action.isBlank()) {
      return null;
    }
    return action.trim().toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  public record TechnicalDetails(
      String rawResourceId,
      List<String> resolvedPolicies,
      List<String> overrides,
      List<String> inheritance,
      int directPolicyCount,
      int effectivePolicyCount) {

    public TechnicalDetails {
      resolvedPolicies = normalize(resolvedPolicies);
      overrides = normalize(overrides);
      inheritance = normalize(inheritance);
    }

    public static TechnicalDetails empty() {
      return new TechnicalDetails(null, List.of(), List.of(), List.of(), 0, 0);
    }

    private static List<String> normalize(List<String> values) {
      if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      Set<String> dedup = new LinkedHashSet<>();
      for (String value : values) {
        if (value == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String trimmed = value.trim();
        if (!trimmed.isEmpty()) {
          dedup.add(trimmed);
        }
      }
      if (dedup.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      List<String> copy = new ArrayList<>(dedup);
      return List.copyOf(copy);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.plugins;

import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.List;

/** Service Provider Interface (SPI) for optional connection implementations. */
public interface ConnectionProvider {

  /** Canonical provider identifier (for example: {@code mongodb}). */
  String providerId();

  /** Optional aliases that also resolve to this provider. */
  default Collection<String> aliases() {
    return List.of();
  }

  /** Concrete handle type returned by this provider. */
  Class<?> handleType();

  /**
   * Builder type accepted by this provider.
   *
   * <p>Return {@link Object} when no builder is required.
   */
  default Class<?> builderType() {
    return Object.class;
  }

  /** Opens a connection using the supplied context. */
  Object open(ConnectionProviderContext context) throws Exception;
}

      return null;

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.plugins;

import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connections.ConnectionOptions;

/** Generic connection lookup request resolved by {@code ConnectionManager}. */
public final class ConnectionRequest<H> {
  private final Class<H> handleType;
  private final Object builder;
  private final String providerId;
  private final String connectionName;
  private final ConnectionOptions options;

  private ConnectionRequest(Builder<H> builder) {
    this.handleType = builder.handleType;
    this.builder = builder.builder;
    this.providerId = builder.providerId;
    this.connectionName = builder.connectionName;
    this.options = builder.options;
  }

  public static <H> Builder<H> builder(Class<H> handleType) {
    return new Builder<>(handleType);
  }

  public Class<H> handleType() {
    return handleType;
  }

  public Object builder() {
    return builder;
  }

  public String providerId() {
    return providerId;
  }

  public String connectionName() {
    return connectionName;
  }

  public ConnectionOptions options() {
    return options;
  }

  public static final class Builder<H> {
    private final Class<H> handleType;
    private Object builder;
    private String providerId;
    private String connectionName;
    private ConnectionOptions options;

    private Builder(Class<H> handleType) {
      this.handleType = Objects.requireNonNull(handleType, "handleType");
    }

    public Builder<H> withBuilder(Object value) {
      this.builder = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder<H> withProviderId(String value) {
      this.providerId = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder<H> withConnectionName(String value) {
      this.connectionName = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder<H> withOptions(ConnectionOptions value) {
      this.options = value;
      return this;
    }

    public ConnectionRequest<H> build() {
      return new ConnectionRequest<>(this);
    }
  }
}


FILE: FabricPlugins.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.plugins;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.ServiceLoader;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestSourceModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestTargetModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

/** ServiceLoader-backed registry for optional Fabric Lite providers. */
public final class FabricPlugins {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FabricPlugins.class);
  private static final Object SYSTEM_LOCK = new Object();
  private static volatile FabricPlugins system;

  private final Map<String, ConnectionProvider> connectionProviders;
  private final Map<String, IngestSourceProvider> ingestSourceProviders;
  private final Map<String, IngestTargetProvider> ingestTargetProviders;
  private final List<IngestSourceProvider> ingestSourceProvidersOrdered;
  private final List<IngestTargetProvider> ingestTargetProvidersOrdered;

  private FabricPlugins(
      Map<String, ConnectionProvider> connectionProviders,
      Map<String, IngestSourceProvider> ingestSourceProviders,
      Map<String, IngestTargetProvider> ingestTargetProviders,
      List<IngestSourceProvider> ingestSourceProvidersOrdered,
      List<IngestTargetProvider> ingestTargetProvidersOrdered) {
    this.connectionProviders = Map.copyOf(connectionProviders);
    this.ingestSourceProviders = Map.copyOf(ingestSourceProviders);
    this.ingestTargetProviders = Map.copyOf(ingestTargetProviders);
    this.ingestSourceProvidersOrdered = List.copyOf(ingestSourceProvidersOrdered);
    this.ingestTargetProvidersOrdered = List.copyOf(ingestTargetProvidersOrdered);
  }

  /** Loads the process-level plugin registry from the thread context classloader. */
  public static FabricPlugins system() {
    FabricPlugins current = system;
    if (current != null) {
      return current;
    }
    synchronized (SYSTEM_LOCK) {
      current = system;
      if (current == null) {
        ClassLoader loader = Thread.currentThread().getContextClassLoader();
        if (loader == null) {
          loader = FabricPlugins.class.getClassLoader();
        }
        current = load(loader);
        system = current;
      }
    }
    return current;
  }

  /** Loads plugins from the supplied classloader. */
  public static FabricPlugins load(ClassLoader loader) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(loader, "loader");

    List<ConnectionProvider> loadedConnectionProviders = new ArrayList<>();
    ServiceLoader.load(ConnectionProvider.class, loader)
        .forEach(
            provider -> {
              if (provider != null) {
                loadedConnectionProviders.add(provider);
              }
            });

    List<IngestSourceProvider> loadedIngestSourceProviders = new ArrayList<>();
    ServiceLoader.load(IngestSourceProvider.class, loader)
        .forEach(
            provider -> {
              if (provider != null) {
                loadedIngestSourceProviders.add(provider);
              }
            });

    List<IngestTargetProvider> loadedIngestTargetProviders = new ArrayList<>();
    ServiceLoader.load(IngestTargetProvider.class, loader)
        .forEach(
            provider -> {
              if (provider != null) {
                loadedIngestTargetProviders.add(provider);
              }
            });

    Map<String, ConnectionProvider> connectionById = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (ConnectionProvider provider : loadedConnectionProviders) {
      registerById(connectionById, provider.providerId(), provider.aliases(), provider);
    }

    Map<String, IngestSourceProvider> ingestSourceById = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (IngestSourceProvider provider : loadedIngestSourceProviders) {
      registerById(ingestSourceById, provider.providerId(), provider.aliases(), provider);
    }

    Map<String, IngestTargetProvider> ingestTargetById = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (IngestTargetProvider provider : loadedIngestTargetProviders) {
      registerById(ingestTargetById, provider.providerId(), provider.aliases(), provider);
    }

    return new FabricPlugins(
        connectionById,
        ingestSourceById,
        ingestTargetById,
        loadedIngestSourceProviders,
        loadedIngestTargetProviders);
  }

  public ConnectionProvider findConnectionProvider(String providerId) {
    String normalized = normalizeId(providerId);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return connectionProviders.get(normalized);
  }

  public IngestSourceProvider findIngestSourceProvider(String providerId) {
    String normalized = normalizeId(providerId);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return ingestSourceProviders.get(normalized);
  }

  public IngestTargetProvider findIngestTargetProvider(String providerId) {
    String normalized = normalizeId(providerId);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return ingestTargetProviders.get(normalized);
  }

  public IngestSourceProvider findIngestSourceProviderForModel(
      Class<? extends IngestSourceModel> modelType) {
    if (modelType == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (IngestSourceProvider provider : ingestSourceProvidersOrdered) {
      Class<? extends IngestSourceModel> providerType = provider.modelType();
      if (providerType != null && providerType.isAssignableFrom(modelType)) {
        return provider;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  public IngestTargetProvider findIngestTargetProviderForModel(
      Class<? extends IngestTargetModel> modelType) {
    if (modelType == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (IngestTargetProvider provider : ingestTargetProvidersOrdered) {
      Class<? extends IngestTargetModel> providerType = provider.modelType();
      if (providerType != null && providerType.isAssignableFrom(modelType)) {
        return provider;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static <T> void registerById(
      Map<String, T> byId, String providerId, Collection<String> aliases, T provider) {
    if (provider == null) {
      return;
    }
    String canonical = normalizeId(providerId);
    if (canonical == null) {
      LOGGER.warn("Ignoring provider {} because providerId is blank", provider.getClass().getName());
      return;
    }
    registerNormalizedId(byId, canonical, provider);
    if (aliases == null || aliases.isEmpty()) {
      return;
    }
    for (String alias : aliases) {
      String normalizedAlias = normalizeId(alias);
      if (normalizedAlias != null) {
        registerNormalizedId(byId, normalizedAlias, provider);
      }
    }
  }

  private static <T> void registerNormalizedId(Map<String, T> byId, String id, T provider) {
    T existing = byId.get(id);
    if (existing != null && existing != provider) {
      LOGGER.warn("Provider {} ignored for id '{}' (already handled by {})", provider.getClass().getName(), id, existing.getClass().getName());
      return;
    }
    byId.put(id, provider);
  }

  private static String normalizeId(String value) {
    String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    return trimmed == null ? null : trimmed.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.plugins;

import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngestSource;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestSourceModel;

/** SPI for optional ingest source model mappings. */
public interface IngestSourceProvider {
  /** Canonical provider identifier (for example: {@code kafka}). */
  String providerId();

  /** Optional aliases that also resolve to this provider. */
  default Collection<String> aliases() {
    return List.of();
  }

  /** External source model type handled by this provider. */
  Class<? extends IngestSourceModel> modelType();

  /** Maps a model to discovery definition payload. */
  DefinitionIngestSource.ExternalSource toExternalSource(IngestSourceModel model) throws Exception;

  /** Rebuilds an ingest source model from discovery definition payload. */
  IngestSourceModel fromExternalSource(IngestSourceProviderContext context) throws Exception;

  /** Whether this provider supports runtime source execution. */
  default boolean supportsRuntime() {
    return false;
  }

  /** Starts runtime source execution. Return a handle that stops the source when closed. */
  default AutoCloseable startRuntime(IngestSourceRuntimeContext context) throws Exception {
    throw new UnsupportedOperationException(
        "Ingest source provider '" + providerId() + "' does not implement runtime execution");
  }
}

import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.Fabric;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngestSource;

/** Runtime context for plugin-backed ingest source execution. */
public final class IngestSourceRuntimeContext {
  private final Fabric.Session session;
  private final String ingestName;
  private final DefinitionIngestSource sourceDefinition;
  private final DefinitionIngestSource.ExternalSource external;
  private final Sink sink;

  public IngestSourceRuntimeContext(
      Fabric.Session session,
      String ingestName,
      DefinitionIngestSource sourceDefinition,
      DefinitionIngestSource.ExternalSource external,
      Sink sink) {
    this.session = Objects.requireNonNull(session, "session");
    this.ingestName = Objects.requireNonNull(ingestName, "ingestName");
    this.sourceDefinition = Objects.requireNonNull(sourceDefinition, "sourceDefinition");
    this.external = Objects.requireNonNull(external, "external");
    this.sink = Objects.requireNonNull(sink, "sink");
  }

  public Fabric.Session session() {
    return session;
  }

  public String ingestName() {
    return ingestName;
  }

  public DefinitionIngestSource sourceDefinition() {
    return sourceDefinition;
  }

  public DefinitionIngestSource.ExternalSource external() {
    return external;
  }

  public Sink sink() {
    return sink;
  }

  public interface Sink {
    void appendJson(String payload) throws Exception;

    void appendNvfix(String payload) throws Exception;

    void appendIpc(byte[] arrowIpcStreamBytes) throws Exception;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.plugins;

import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestTargetModel;

/** SPI for optional ingest target model mappings and runtime append handlers. */
public interface IngestTargetProvider {
  /** Canonical provider identifier (for example: {@code mongodb}). */
  String providerId();

  /** Optional aliases that also resolve to this provider. */
  default Collection<String> aliases() {
    return List.of();
  }

  /** External target model type handled by this provider. */
  Class<? extends IngestTargetModel> modelType();

  /** Maps a model to discovery dataset external binding payload. */
  DefinitionDataset.ExternalBinding toExternalBinding(IngestTargetModel model) throws Exception;

  /** Rebuilds an ingest target model from discovery dataset external binding payload. */
  IngestTargetModel fromExternalBinding(IngestTargetProviderContext context) throws Exception;

  /**
   * Handles append delivery for external targets.
   *
   * <p>Default behavior signals that runtime append is not implemented.
   */
  default void append(IngestTargetAppendContext context) throws Exception {
    throw new UnsupportedOperationException(
        "Ingest target provider '" + providerId() + "' does not implement append");
  }
}
