package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.headers;

import io.grpc.Metadata;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.UUID;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.CallHeaders;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.identity.CallerAppIdentity;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class FabricRequestHeaders {
  public static final String HEADER_OBO_USER = "x-fabric-obo-user";
  public static final String HEADER_CALLER_APP_GROUP = "x-fabric-caller-app-group";
  public static final String HEADER_CALLER_APP_NAME = "x-fabric-caller-app-name";
  public static final String HEADER_CALLER_APP_INSTANCE = "x-fabric-caller-app-instance";
  public static final String HEADER_REQUEST_ID = "x-fabric-request-id";
  public static final String HEADER_TRACE_ID = "x-fabric-trace-id";
  public static final String HEADER_ENV = "x-fabric-env";
  public static final String HEADER_REGION = "x-fabric-region";
  public static final String HEADER_SITE = "x-fabric-site";

  public static final Metadata.Key<String> KEY_OBO_USER =
      Metadata.Key.of(HEADER_OBO_USER, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);
  public static final Metadata.Key<String> KEY_CALLER_APP_GROUP =
      Metadata.Key.of(HEADER_CALLER_APP_GROUP, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);
  public static final Metadata.Key<String> KEY_CALLER_APP_NAME =
      Metadata.Key.of(HEADER_CALLER_APP_NAME, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);
  public static final Metadata.Key<String> KEY_CALLER_APP_INSTANCE =
      Metadata.Key.of(HEADER_CALLER_APP_INSTANCE, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);
  public static final Metadata.Key<String> KEY_REQUEST_ID =
      Metadata.Key.of(HEADER_REQUEST_ID, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);
  public static final Metadata.Key<String> KEY_TRACE_ID =
      Metadata.Key.of(HEADER_TRACE_ID, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);
  public static final Metadata.Key<String> KEY_ENV =
      Metadata.Key.of(HEADER_ENV, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);
  public static final Metadata.Key<String> KEY_REGION =
      Metadata.Key.of(HEADER_REGION, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);
  public static final Metadata.Key<String> KEY_SITE =
      Metadata.Key.of(HEADER_SITE, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);

  private static final Pattern APP_TOKEN = Pattern.compile("^[A-Za-z0-9._-]+$");
  private static final String REQUEST_ID_PREFIX = "fabric-req-";

  private final String authenticatedPrincipal;
  private final CallerAppIdentity callerApp;
  private final String oboUser;
  private final RequestMetadata requestMetadata;

  private FabricRequestHeaders(
      String authenticatedPrincipal,
      CallerAppIdentity callerApp,
      String oboUser,
      RequestMetadata requestMetadata) {
    this.authenticatedPrincipal = sanitizeValue(authenticatedPrincipal, "authenticatedPrincipal");
    this.callerApp = callerApp == null ? new CallerAppIdentity(null, null, null) : callerApp;
    this.oboUser = sanitizeValue(oboUser, HEADER_OBO_USER);
    this.requestMetadata =
        requestMetadata == null ? new RequestMetadata(null, null, null, null, null) : requestMetadata;
  }

  public static FabricRequestHeaders empty(String authenticatedPrincipal) {
    return new FabricRequestHeaders(
        authenticatedPrincipal,
        new CallerAppIdentity(null, null, null),
        null,
        new RequestMetadata(null, null, null, null, null));
  }

  public static FabricRequestHeaders outbound(
      CallerAppIdentity callerApp, String oboUser, RequestMetadata requestMetadata) {
    return new FabricRequestHeaders(null, callerApp, oboUser, requestMetadata);
  }

  public static String generateRequestId() {
    return REQUEST_ID_PREFIX + UUID.randomUUID();
  }

  public static FabricRequestHeaders fromGrpc(Metadata metadata, String authenticatedPrincipal) {
    String callerGroup = sanitizeValue(read(metadata, KEY_CALLER_APP_GROUP), HEADER_CALLER_APP_GROUP);
    String callerName = sanitizeValue(read(metadata, KEY_CALLER_APP_NAME), HEADER_CALLER_APP_NAME);
    String callerInstance = sanitizeValue(read(metadata, KEY_CALLER_APP_INSTANCE), HEADER_CALLER_APP_INSTANCE);
    validateCallerApp(callerGroup, callerName, callerInstance);
    return new FabricRequestHeaders(
        authenticatedPrincipal,
        new CallerAppIdentity(callerGroup, callerName, callerInstance),
        sanitizeValue(read(metadata, KEY_OBO_USER), HEADER_OBO_USER),
        new RequestMetadata(
            sanitizeValue(read(metadata, KEY_REQUEST_ID), HEADER_REQUEST_ID),
            sanitizeValue(read(metadata, KEY_TRACE_ID), HEADER_TRACE_ID),
            sanitizeValue(read(metadata, KEY_ENV), HEADER_ENV),
            sanitizeValue(read(metadata, KEY_REGION), HEADER_REGION),
            sanitizeValue(read(metadata, KEY_SITE), HEADER_SITE)));
  }

  public static FabricRequestHeaders fromFlight(CallHeaders headers, String authenticatedPrincipal) {
    String callerGroup = sanitizeValue(read(headers, HEADER_CALLER_APP_GROUP), HEADER_CALLER_APP_GROUP);
    String callerName = sanitizeValue(read(headers, HEADER_CALLER_APP_NAME), HEADER_CALLER_APP_NAME);
    String callerInstance =
        sanitizeValue(read(headers, HEADER_CALLER_APP_INSTANCE), HEADER_CALLER_APP_INSTANCE);
    validateCallerApp(callerGroup, callerName, callerInstance);
    return new FabricRequestHeaders(
        authenticatedPrincipal,
        new CallerAppIdentity(callerGroup, callerName, callerInstance),
        sanitizeValue(read(headers, HEADER_OBO_USER), HEADER_OBO_USER),
        new RequestMetadata(
            sanitizeValue(read(headers, HEADER_REQUEST_ID), HEADER_REQUEST_ID),
            sanitizeValue(read(headers, HEADER_TRACE_ID), HEADER_TRACE_ID),
            sanitizeValue(read(headers, HEADER_ENV), HEADER_ENV),
            sanitizeValue(read(headers, HEADER_REGION), HEADER_REGION),
            sanitizeValue(read(headers, HEADER_SITE), HEADER_SITE)));
  }

  public FabricRequestHeaders withAuthenticatedPrincipal(String principal) {
    return new FabricRequestHeaders(principal, callerApp, oboUser, requestMetadata);
  }

  public String authenticatedPrincipal() {
    return authenticatedPrincipal;
  }

  public CallerAppIdentity callerApp() {
    return callerApp;
  }

  public String oboUser() {
    return oboUser;
  }

  public RequestMetadata requestMetadata() {
    return requestMetadata;
  }

  public Metadata toGrpcMetadata() {
    Metadata metadata = new Metadata();
    applyToGrpcMetadata(metadata);
    return metadata;
  }

  public void applyToGrpcMetadata(Metadata metadata) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(metadata, "metadata");
    put(metadata, KEY_CALLER_APP_GROUP, callerApp.group());
    put(metadata, KEY_CALLER_APP_NAME, callerApp.name());
    put(metadata, KEY_CALLER_APP_INSTANCE, callerApp.instance());
    put(metadata, KEY_OBO_USER, oboUser);
    put(metadata, KEY_REQUEST_ID, requestMetadata.requestId());
    put(metadata, KEY_TRACE_ID, requestMetadata.traceId());
    put(metadata, KEY_ENV, requestMetadata.env());
    put(metadata, KEY_REGION, requestMetadata.region());
    put(metadata, KEY_SITE, requestMetadata.site());
  }

  public void applyToFlightHeaders(CallHeaders headers) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(headers, "headers");
    put(headers, HEADER_CALLER_APP_GROUP, callerApp.group());
    put(headers, HEADER_CALLER_APP_NAME, callerApp.name());
    put(headers, HEADER_CALLER_APP_INSTANCE, callerApp.instance());
    put(headers, HEADER_OBO_USER, oboUser);
    put(headers, HEADER_REQUEST_ID, requestMetadata.requestId());
    put(headers, HEADER_TRACE_ID, requestMetadata.traceId());
    put(headers, HEADER_ENV, requestMetadata.env());
    put(headers, HEADER_REGION, requestMetadata.region());
    put(headers, HEADER_SITE, requestMetadata.site());
  }

  private static void validateCallerApp(String group, String name, String instance) {
    boolean hasGroup = group != null;
    boolean hasName = name != null;
    if (hasGroup != hasName) {
      throw new ParseException(
          "Invalid caller app headers: both "
              + HEADER_CALLER_APP_GROUP
              + " and "
              + HEADER_CALLER_APP_NAME
              + " are required together");
    }
    if (group != null && !APP_TOKEN.matcher(group).matches()) {
      throw new ParseException("Invalid caller app group header: " + HEADER_CALLER_APP_GROUP);
    }
    if (name != null && !APP_TOKEN.matcher(name).matches()) {
      throw new ParseException("Invalid caller app name header: " + HEADER_CALLER_APP_NAME);
    }
    if (instance != null && !APP_TOKEN.matcher(instance).matches()) {
      throw new ParseException("Invalid caller app instance header: " + HEADER_CALLER_APP_INSTANCE);
    }
  }

  private static String sanitizeValue(String value, String label) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return null;
    }
    for (int i = 0; i < normalized.length(); i++) {
      char ch = normalized.charAt(i);
      if (ch < 0x20 || ch == 0x7f) {
        throw new ParseException("Invalid header value for " + label);
      }
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String read(Metadata metadata, Metadata.Key<String> key) {
    if (metadata == null || key == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return metadata.get(key);
  }

  private static String read(CallHeaders headers, String key) {
    if (headers == null || key == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String direct = Strings.trimToNull(headers.get(key));
    if (direct != null) {
      return direct;
    }
    String normalized = key.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    for (String candidate : headerKeys(headers)) {
      if (candidate != null && candidate.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).equals(normalized)) {
        String value = Strings.trimToNull(headers.get(candidate));
        if (value != null) {
          return value;
        }
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static List<String> headerKeys(CallHeaders headers) {
    if (headers == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> keys = new ArrayList<>();
    headers.keys().forEach(keys::add);
    return keys;
  }

  private static void put(Metadata metadata, Metadata.Key<String> key, String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return;
    }
    metadata.put(key, normalized);
  }

  private static void put(CallHeaders headers, String key, String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return;
    }
    headers.insert(key, normalized);
  }

  public record RequestMetadata(
      String requestId, String traceId, String env, String region, String site) {
    public RequestMetadata {
      requestId = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(requestId), generateRequestId());
      traceId = Strings.trimToNull(traceId);
      env = Strings.trimToNull(env);
      region = Strings.trimToNull(region);
      site = Strings.trimToNull(site);
    }
  }

  public static final class ParseException extends IllegalArgumentException {
    public ParseException(String message) {
      super(message);
    }
  }
}

PACKAGE: org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.manager

FILE: SecurityManagerImpl.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.manager;

import java.security.SecureRandom;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.ZoneOffset;
import java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Set;
import java.util.Base64;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.SecurityManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.secrets.SecretCrypto;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.IdentityParsingSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class SecurityManagerImpl implements SecurityManager {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(SecurityManagerImpl.class);
  private static final int DEFAULT_KEK_BYTES = 32;
  private static final String PLATFORM_GROUP = "platform";
  private static final String KEK_BACKUP_SUFFIX = "-kek-backup-";
  private static final DateTimeFormatter KEK_BACKUP_TIMESTAMP_FORMAT =
      DateTimeFormatter.ofPattern("yyyyMMdd_HHmmss_SSS", Locale.ROOT).withZone(ZoneOffset.UTC);
  private static final Set<String> PLAINTEXT_CREDENTIAL_KEYS =
      Set.of(
          "accesskeyid",
          "secretaccesskey",
          "sessiontoken",
          "aws_access_key_id",
          "aws_secret_access_key",
          "aws_session_token",
          "s3_access_key_id",
          "s3_secret_access_key",
          "s3_session_token");

  private final Supplier<DiscoveryCache> configCacheSupplier;
  private final Supplier<String> groupSupplier;
  private final Consumer<String> onS3ConnectionReencoded;
  private final Supplier<Instant> nowSupplier;
  private final SecureRandom random = new SecureRandom();

  public SecurityManagerImpl(Supplier<DiscoveryCache> configCacheSupplier, Supplier<String> groupSupplier) {
    this(configCacheSupplier, groupSupplier, ignored -> {}, Instant::now);
  }

  public SecurityManagerImpl(
      Supplier<DiscoveryCache> configCacheSupplier,
      Supplier<String> groupSupplier,
      Consumer<String> onS3ConnectionReencoded) {
    this(configCacheSupplier, groupSupplier, onS3ConnectionReencoded, Instant::now);
  }

  SecurityManagerImpl(
      Supplier<DiscoveryCache> configCacheSupplier,
      Supplier<String> groupSupplier,
      Consumer<String> onS3ConnectionReencoded,
      Supplier<Instant> nowSupplier) {
    this.configCacheSupplier = Objects.requireNonNull(configCacheSupplier, "configCacheSupplier");
    this.groupSupplier = Objects.requireNonNull(groupSupplier, "groupSupplier");
    this.onS3ConnectionReencoded =
        Objects.requireNonNull(onS3ConnectionReencoded, "onS3ConnectionReencoded");
    this.nowSupplier = Objects.requireNonNull(nowSupplier, "nowSupplier");
  }

  @Override
  public String generateKekText() {
    return generateKekText(DEFAULT_KEK_BYTES);
  }

  @Override
  public String generateKekText(int keyBytes) {
    if (keyBytes <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("keyBytes must be > 0");
    }
    byte[] raw = new byte[keyBytes];
    random.nextBytes(raw);
    return Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(raw);
  }

  @Override
  public boolean reencodeS3Connection(
      String connectionName, S3Credentials credentials, String kekAlias, String kekText) {
    String normalizedName = Strings.requireNonBlank(connectionName, "connectionName");
    DiscoveryCache cache = requireConfigCache();
    Optional<DefinitionConnection> resolved = resolveS3Connection(cache, normalizedName);
    if (resolved.isEmpty()) {
      return false;
    }
    DefinitionConnection connection = resolved.get();
    S3Credentials normalizedCreds = requireCredentials(credentials);

    String alias = Strings.requireNonBlank(kekAlias, "kekAlias");
    String normalizedKek = Strings.requireNonBlank(kekText, "kek text");
    String accessKeyIdEnc = SecretCrypto.encrypt(normalizedKek, normalizedCreds.accessKeyId());
    String secretAccessKeyEnc = SecretCrypto.encrypt(normalizedKek, normalizedCreds.secretAccessKey());
    String sessionTokenEnc =
        Strings.trimToNull(normalizedCreds.sessionToken()) == null
            ? null
            : SecretCrypto.encrypt(normalizedKek, normalizedCreds.sessionToken());

    DefinitionConnection backupConnection = buildBackupConnection(cache, connection);
    String backupName = backupConnection.envelope() == null ? "unknown" : backupConnection.envelope().name();
    try {
      cache.upsert(backupConnection);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to create KEK backup for S3 connection '"
              + normalizedName
              + "' (backup='"
              + backupName
              + "')",
          ex);
    }

    DefinitionConnection.S3 s3 = Objects.requireNonNull(connection.s3(), "connection.s3");
    DefinitionConnection.S3 updatedS3 =
        new DefinitionConnection.S3(
            s3.region(),
            s3.bucket(),
            s3.endpoint(),
            s3.pathStyleAccess(),
            s3.basePrefix(),
            sanitizeCredentialMap(s3.attributes()),
            accessKeyIdEnc,
            secretAccessKeyEnc,
            sessionTokenEnc,
            alias,
            SecretCrypto.ENCRYPTION_FORMAT);

    DefinitionConnection updatedConnection =
        new DefinitionConnection(
        connection.envelope(),
        connection.connectionType(),
        connection.providerId(),
        sanitizeCredentialMap(connection.properties()),
        connection.amps(),
        connection.http(),
        updatedS3,
        connection.odbc(),
        connection.mongoDb(),
        connection.autosys(),
        connection.bitbucketRepo(),
        connection.physicalSites(),
        connection.physical(),
        connection.client(),
        connection.mode());

    try {
      cache.upsert(updatedConnection);
      onS3ConnectionReencoded.accept(normalizedName);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      rollbackConnection(cache, connection, normalizedName, backupName, ex);
    }
    LOGGER.warn("S3 connection credentials rotated for '{}' (backup='{}'); reacquire connection handle or restart session to ensure active clients use new credentials", normalizedName, backupName);
    return true;
  }

  private DiscoveryCache requireConfigCache() {
    return IdentityParsingSupport.requireNonNullRuntime(
        configCacheSupplier.get(), "Session DiscoveryCache is not available");
  }

  private Optional<DefinitionConnection> resolveS3Connection(DiscoveryCache cache, String connectionName) {
    String group = Strings.trimToNull(groupSupplier.get());
    if (group == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session group is not resolved");
    }

    Optional<DefinitionConnection> optional = cache.get(DefinitionConnection.class, group, connectionName);
    if (optional.isEmpty()) {
      optional = cache.get(DefinitionConnection.class, PLATFORM_GROUP, connectionName);
    }
    if (optional.isEmpty()) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    DefinitionConnection connection = optional.get();
    validateS3Connection(connection);
    return Optional.of(connection);
  }

  private DefinitionConnection buildBackupConnection(DiscoveryCache cache, DefinitionConnection connection) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = Objects.requireNonNull(connection.envelope(), "connection.envelope");
    String backupName = nextBackupName(cache, envelope.group(), envelope.name());
    Instant now = nowInstant();
    String nowText = now.toString();
    String actor = Strings.firstNonBlank(envelope.updatedBy(), envelope.createdBy(), "security-manager");
    DefinitionEnvelope backupEnvelope =
        new DefinitionEnvelope(
            envelope.group(),
            envelope.type(),
            backupName,
            null,
            envelope.enabled(),
            envelope.lifecycleStatus(),
            Strings.firstNonBlank(envelope.createdTimeUtc(), nowText),
            Strings.firstNonBlank(envelope.createdBy(), actor),
            nowText,
            actor);
    return new DefinitionConnection(
        backupEnvelope,
        connection.connectionType(),
        connection.providerId(),
        connection.properties(),
        connection.amps(),
        connection.http(),
        connection.s3(),
        connection.odbc(),
        connection.mongoDb(),
        connection.autosys(),
        connection.bitbucketRepo(),
        connection.physicalSites(),
        connection.physical(),
        connection.client(),
        connection.mode());
  }

  private String nextBackupName(DiscoveryCache cache, String group, String name) {
    String normalizedGroup = Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "connection group");
    String normalizedName = Strings.requireNonBlank(name, "connection name");
    String baseName =
        normalizedName + KEK_BACKUP_SUFFIX + KEK_BACKUP_TIMESTAMP_FORMAT.format(nowInstant());
    String candidate = baseName;
    int suffix = 1;
    while (cache.get(DefinitionConnection.class, normalizedGroup, candidate).isPresent()) {
      candidate = baseName + "-" + suffix;
      suffix++;
    }
    return candidate;
  }

  private Instant nowInstant() {
    Instant now = nowSupplier.get();
    return now == null ? Instant.now() : now;
  }

  private void rollbackConnection(
      DiscoveryCache cache,
      DefinitionConnection previousConnection,
      String connectionName,
      String backupName,
      RuntimeException originalFailure) {
    RuntimeException rollbackFailure = null;
    try {
      cache.upsert(previousConnection);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      rollbackFailure = ex;
    }
    if (rollbackFailure == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to rotate S3 connection '"
              + connectionName
              + "'; previous configuration restored (backup='"
              + backupName
              + "')",
          originalFailure);
    }
    IllegalStateException combined =
        new IllegalStateException(
            "Failed to rotate S3 connection '"
                + connectionName
                + "' and rollback failed (backup='"
                + backupName
                + "')",
            originalFailure);
    combined.addSuppressed(rollbackFailure);
    throw combined;
  }

  private static void validateS3Connection(DefinitionConnection connection) {
    if (connection.connectionType() != DefinitionConnection.ConnectionType.S3) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Connection '" + connectionName(connection) + "' is not S3 (type=" + connection.connectionType() + ")");
    }
    if (connection.s3() == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Connection '" + connectionName(connection) + "' is missing s3 configuration");
    }
  }

  private static S3Credentials requireCredentials(S3Credentials credentials) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(credentials, "credentials");
    return new S3Credentials(
        Strings.requireNonBlank(credentials.accessKeyId(), "s3.accessKeyId"),
        Strings.requireNonBlank(credentials.secretAccessKey(), "s3.secretAccessKey"),
        Strings.trimToNull(credentials.sessionToken()));
  }

  private static Map<String, String> sanitizeCredentialMap(Map<String, String> source) {
    if (source == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (source.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    Map<String, String> cleaned = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : source.entrySet()) {
      String key = entry.getKey();
      if (isPlaintextCredentialKey(key)) {
        continue;
      }
      cleaned.put(key, entry.getValue());
    }
    return cleaned.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(cleaned);
  }

  private static boolean isPlaintextCredentialKey(String key) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(key);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return PLAINTEXT_CREDENTIAL_KEYS.contains(normalized.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
  }

  private static String connectionName(DefinitionConnection connection) {
    return connection == null || connection.envelope() == null ? "unknown" : Strings.firstNonBlank(connection.envelope().name(), "unknown");
  }
}

FILE: SecretCrypto.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.secrets;

import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.security.GeneralSecurityException;
import java.security.MessageDigest;
import java.security.SecureRandom;
import java.util.Base64;
import java.util.Objects;
import javax.crypto.Cipher;
import javax.crypto.spec.GCMParameterSpec;
import javax.crypto.spec.SecretKeySpec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class SecretCrypto {
  private static final String CIPHER_TRANSFORM = "AES/GCM/NoPadding";
  private static final int GCM_TAG_BITS = 128;
  private static final int IV_BYTES = 12;
  private static final String WIRE_PREFIX = "v1";
  public static final String ENCRYPTION_FORMAT = "FABRIC_AES_GCM_V1";
  private static final SecureRandom SECURE_RANDOM = new SecureRandom();

  private SecretCrypto() {}

  public static String encrypt(String kekText, String plaintext) {
    String normalizedKek = Strings.requireNonBlank(kekText, "kek text");
    Objects.requireNonNull(plaintext, "plaintext");
    byte[] keyBytes = hashSha256(normalizedKek.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
    byte[] iv = new byte[IV_BYTES];
    SECURE_RANDOM.nextBytes(iv);
    byte[] ciphertext = encryptAesGcm(keyBytes, iv, plaintext.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
    return WIRE_PREFIX
        + ":"
        + Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(iv)
        + ":"
        + Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(ciphertext);
  }

  public static String decrypt(byte[] kekBytes, String encrypted) {
    byte[] normalizedKekBytes = Objects.requireNonNull(kekBytes, "kekBytes");
    String normalizedEncrypted = Strings.requireNonBlank(encrypted, "encrypted");
    String[] segments = normalizedEncrypted.split(":", -1);
    if (segments.length != 3 || !WIRE_PREFIX.equals(segments[0])) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid encrypted secret format; expected v1:<iv>:<ciphertext>");
    }
    byte[] iv;
    byte[] ciphertext;
    try {
      iv = Base64.getDecoder().decode(segments[1]);
      ciphertext = Base64.getDecoder().decode(segments[2]);
    } catch (IllegalArgumentException ex) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid encrypted secret format; expected v1:<iv>:<ciphertext>");
    }
    if (iv.length != IV_BYTES || ciphertext.length == 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid encrypted secret format; expected v1:<iv>:<ciphertext>");
    }
    byte[] keyBytes = hashSha256(normalizedKekBytes);
    byte[] plaintextBytes = decryptAesGcm(keyBytes, iv, ciphertext);
    return new String(plaintextBytes, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
  }

  private static byte[] encryptAesGcm(byte[] keyBytes, byte[] iv, byte[] plaintextBytes) {
    try {
      Cipher cipher = Cipher.getInstance(CIPHER_TRANSFORM);
      cipher.init(Cipher.ENCRYPT_MODE, new SecretKeySpec(keyBytes, "AES"), new GCMParameterSpec(GCM_TAG_BITS, iv));
      return cipher.doFinal(plaintextBytes);
    } catch (GeneralSecurityException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Secret encryption failed");
    }
  }

  private static byte[] decryptAesGcm(byte[] keyBytes, byte[] iv, byte[] ciphertext) {
    try {
      Cipher cipher = Cipher.getInstance(CIPHER_TRANSFORM);
      cipher.init(Cipher.DECRYPT_MODE, new SecretKeySpec(keyBytes, "AES"), new GCMParameterSpec(GCM_TAG_BITS, iv));
      return cipher.doFinal(ciphertext);
    } catch (GeneralSecurityException ex) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unable to decrypt secret with provided KEK");
    }
  }

  private static byte[] hashSha256(byte[] value) {
    try {
      MessageDigest digest = MessageDigest.getInstance("SHA-256");
      return digest.digest(value);
    } catch (GeneralSecurityException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("SHA-256 digest is unavailable");
    }
  }
}


FILE: SessionSecrets.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.secrets;

import java.io.IOException;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class SessionSecrets {
  public static final String DEFAULT_KEK_ALIAS = "default";
  private final Map<String, byte[]> clientKeks;

  private SessionSecrets(Map<String, byte[]> clientKeks) {
    this.clientKeks = clientKeks;
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public static SessionSecrets empty() {
    return new SessionSecrets(Map.of());
  }

  public boolean hasClientKek(String alias) {
    String normalizedAlias = normalizeAlias(alias);
    return clientKeks.containsKey(normalizedAlias);
  }

  public String decrypt(String alias, String encryptedValue) {
    String normalizedAlias = normalizeAlias(alias);
    byte[] kekBytes = clientKeks.get(normalizedAlias);
    if (kekBytes == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "S3 credentials are encrypted but no KEK was provided (alias=" + normalizedAlias + ")");
    }
    try {
      return SecretCrypto.decrypt(kekBytes, encryptedValue);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Unable to decrypt S3 credential with provided KEK (alias=" + normalizedAlias + ")");
    }
  }

  private static String normalizeAlias(String alias) {
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(alias, DEFAULT_KEK_ALIAS);
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final Map<String, byte[]> clientKeks = new LinkedHashMap<>();

    public Builder withClientKekBytes(String alias, byte[] kekBytes) {
      String normalizedAlias = Strings.requireNonBlank(alias, "kek alias");
      Objects.requireNonNull(kekBytes, "kekBytes");
      if (kekBytes.length == 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("kek bytes are required");
      }
      clientKeks.put(normalizedAlias, copyBytes(kekBytes));
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withClientKekBytes(byte[] kekBytes) {
      return withClientKekBytes(DEFAULT_KEK_ALIAS, kekBytes);
    }

    public Builder withClientKekFile(String alias, Path kekFile) {
      String normalizedAlias = Strings.requireNonBlank(alias, "kek alias");
      Path normalizedPath = Objects.requireNonNull(kekFile, "kekFile");
      String kekText = readKekText(normalizedPath);
      return withClientKekBytes(normalizedAlias, kekText.getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
    }

    public Builder withClientKekFile(Path kekFile) {
      return withClientKekFile(DEFAULT_KEK_ALIAS, kekFile);
    }

    public SessionSecrets build() {
      if (clientKeks.isEmpty()) {
        return SessionSecrets.empty();
      }
      Map<String, byte[]> copy = new LinkedHashMap<>(clientKeks.size());
      for (Map.Entry<String, byte[]> entry : clientKeks.entrySet()) {
        copy.put(entry.getKey(), copyBytes(entry.getValue()));
      }
      return new SessionSecrets(Map.copyOf(copy));
    }

    private static byte[] copyBytes(byte[] value) {
      Objects.requireNonNull(value, "value");
      byte[] copy = new byte[value.length];
      System.arraycopy(value, 0, copy, 0, value.length);
      return copy;
    }

    private static String readKekText(Path kekFile) {
      try {
        String raw = Files.readString(kekFile, StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
        if (raw.startsWith("\uFEFF")) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException(
              "kek file contains UTF-8 BOM; save without BOM: " + kekFile.toAbsolutePath());
        }
        String value = Strings.trimToNull(raw);
        if (value == null) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("kek file is empty: " + kekFile.toAbsolutePath());
        }
        return value;
      } catch (IOException ex) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to read KEK file: " + kekFile.toAbsolutePath(), ex);
      }
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session;

import com.crankuptheamps.client.Command;
import com.crankuptheamps.client.Message;
import com.crankuptheamps.client.MessageStream;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.ControlConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryTopics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class SessionDuplication {
  private static final Duration DEFAULT_DUPLICATE_HEARTBEAT_GRACE = Duration.ofSeconds(12);
  public static final String STATUS_FILTER_PATHS = "/group,/type,/name,/instance";

  private final ControlConnection control;

  public SessionDuplication(ControlConnection control) {
    this.control = Objects.requireNonNull(control, "control");
  }

  public Decision detect(
      String group, String appName, String instance, long nowEpochMs, Duration staleHeartbeatGrace)
      throws Exception {
    String normalizedGroup = requireField(group, "group");
    String normalizedName = requireField(appName, "name");
    String normalizedInstance = requireField(instance, "instance");
    String filter = buildStatusFilter(normalizedGroup, normalizedName, normalizedInstance);

    Command command = new Command(Message.Command.SOW);
    command.setTopic(DiscoveryTopics.STATUS);
    command.setFilter(filter);

    try (MessageStream stream = control.amps().client().execute(command)) {
      for (Message message : stream) {
        if (message == null) {
          continue;
        }
        int commandType = message.getCommand();
        if (commandType != Message.Command.SOW && commandType != Message.Command.Publish) {
          continue;
        }
        String payload = message.getData();
        if (Strings.isBlank(payload)) {
          continue;
        }
        DefinitionStatusApp status = decodeStatus(payload);
        if (status == null) {
          continue;
        }
        DuplicateInstanceInfo conflict = DuplicateInstanceInfo.from(status);
        DuplicateInstanceEvaluation evaluation =
            evaluateDuplicateInstance(
                conflict, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS.toNanos(Math.max(0L, nowEpochMs)), staleHeartbeatGrace);
        if (!evaluation.isActiveState()) {
          return Decision.ok(filter);
        }
        if (evaluation.isStale()) {
          return Decision.ok(filter);
        }
        return Decision.duplicate(
            status,
            filter,
            conflict.lastSeenField(),
            conflict.lastSeenEpochMs(),
            evaluation.ageMillis(),
            TimeUnit.SECONDS.toMillis(evaluation.timeoutSeconds()));
      }
    }
    return Decision.ok(filter);
  }

  public static boolean duplicateDetectionEnabled(DefinitionApp appDefinition) {
    if (appDefinition == null
        || appDefinition.runtimeControls() == null
        || appDefinition.runtimeControls().duplicateDetection() == null) {
      return true;
    }
    Boolean enabled = appDefinition.runtimeControls().duplicateDetection().enabled();
    return enabled == null || enabled;
  }

  private static DuplicateInstanceEvaluation evaluateDuplicateInstance(
      DuplicateInstanceInfo conflict, long nowEpochNanos, Duration fallbackGrace) {
    long lastSeenEpochNanos = conflict == null ? 0L : conflict.lastSeenEpochNanos();
    long timeoutSeconds = resolveHeartbeatTimeoutSeconds(conflict, fallbackGrace);
    long timeoutNanos = TimeUnit.SECONDS.toNanos(timeoutSeconds);
    long ageMillis = -1L;
    boolean stale = true;
    if (lastSeenEpochNanos > 0L) {
      long ageNanos = nowEpochNanos - lastSeenEpochNanos;
      if (ageNanos >= 0L) {
        ageMillis = TimeUnit.NANOSECONDS.toMillis(ageNanos);
        stale = ageNanos > timeoutNanos;
      }
    }
    return new DuplicateInstanceEvaluation(
        timeoutSeconds,
        ageMillis,
        stale,
        isDuplicateCandidateState(conflict == null ? null : conflict.state()));
  }

  private static boolean isDuplicateCandidateState(DefinitionStatusApp.State state) {
    if (state == null) {
      return true;
    }
    return switch (state) {
      case RUNNING, STARTED, UNKNOWN, ERROR -> true;
      case STOPPED -> false;
    };
  }

  private static long resolveHeartbeatTimeoutSeconds(
      DuplicateInstanceInfo conflict, Duration fallbackGrace) {
    Duration fallback =
        fallbackGrace == null ? DEFAULT_DUPLICATE_HEARTBEAT_GRACE : fallbackGrace;
    long fallbackSeconds =
        fallback.isNegative()
            ? DEFAULT_DUPLICATE_HEARTBEAT_GRACE.getSeconds()
            : fallback.getSeconds();
    if (fallbackSeconds <= 0L) {
      fallbackSeconds = DEFAULT_DUPLICATE_HEARTBEAT_GRACE.getSeconds();
    }
    if (conflict != null
        && conflict.heartbeatTimeoutSeconds() != null
        && conflict.heartbeatTimeoutSeconds() > 0L) {
      return Math.min(conflict.heartbeatTimeoutSeconds(), fallbackSeconds);
    }
    return fallbackSeconds;
  }

  private static DefinitionStatusApp decodeStatus(String payload) {
    try {
      Definition definition = DiscoveryCodec.decode(payload);
      if (definition instanceof DefinitionStatusApp status) {
        return status;
      }
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
      return null;
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String buildStatusFilter(String group, String appName, String instance) {
    return "/group='"
        + escapeFilterValue(group)
        + "' and /type='"
        + DefinitionType.STATUS_APP.name()
        + "' and /name='"
        + escapeFilterValue(appName)
        + "' and /instance='"
        + escapeFilterValue(instance)
        + "'";
  }

  private static String requireField(String value, String field) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(field + " is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String escapeFilterValue(String value) {
    return value == null ? "" : value.replace("'", "''");
  }

  private record DuplicateInstanceInfo(
      long lastSeenEpochNanos,
      long lastSeenEpochMs,
      String lastSeenField,
      Long heartbeatTimeoutSeconds,
      DefinitionStatusApp.State state) {
    static DuplicateInstanceInfo from(DefinitionStatusApp status) {
      if (status == null) {
        return new DuplicateInstanceInfo(0L, 0L, "none", null, null);
      }
      Long lastHeartbeatEpochMs = status.lastHeartbeatEpochMs();
      Long lastStateChangeEpochMs = status.lastStateChangeEpochMs();
      Long startedAtEpochMs = status.startedAtEpochMs();
      long lastSeenEpochMs = 0L;
      String lastSeenField = "none";
      if (lastHeartbeatEpochMs != null && lastHeartbeatEpochMs > 0L) {
        lastSeenEpochMs = lastHeartbeatEpochMs;
        lastSeenField = "lastHeartbeatEpochMs";
      } else if (lastStateChangeEpochMs != null && lastStateChangeEpochMs > 0L) {
        lastSeenEpochMs = lastStateChangeEpochMs;
        lastSeenField = "lastStateChangeEpochMs";
      } else if (startedAtEpochMs != null && startedAtEpochMs > 0L) {
        lastSeenEpochMs = startedAtEpochMs;
        lastSeenField = "startedAtEpochMs";
      }
      return new DuplicateInstanceInfo(
          lastSeenEpochMs <= 0L ? 0L : lastSeenEpochMs * 1_000_000L,
          Math.max(0L, lastSeenEpochMs),
          lastSeenField,
          status.heartbeatTimeoutSeconds() == null
              ? null
              : Long.valueOf(status.heartbeatTimeoutSeconds()),
          status.state());
    }
  }

  private record DuplicateInstanceEvaluation(
      long timeoutSeconds, long ageMillis, boolean stale, boolean activeState) {
    boolean isStale() {
      return stale;
    }

    boolean isActiveState() {
      return activeState;
    }
  }

  public record Decision(
      boolean duplicateActive,
      DefinitionStatusApp existingStatus,
      String statusFilter,
      String timestampField,
      long lastSeenEpochMs,
      long ageMillis,
      long timeoutMillis) {
    static Decision ok(String filter) {
      return new Decision(false, null, filter, "none", 0L, -1L, 0L);
    }

    static Decision duplicate(
        DefinitionStatusApp existingStatus,
        String filter,
        String timestampField,
        long lastSeenEpochMs,
        long ageMillis,
        long timeoutMillis) {
      return new Decision(
          true,
          existingStatus,
          filter,
          timestampField == null ? "none" : timestampField,
          Math.max(0L, lastSeenEpochMs),
          ageMillis,
          Math.max(0L, timeoutMillis));
    }
  }
}








FILE: SessionImplLifecycle.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session;

import java.time.Duration;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.ControlConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.app.AppMetrics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;

final class SessionImplLifecycle {
  private SessionImplLifecycle() {}

  static void runDuplicateInstanceCheck(
      Logger logger,
      ControlConnection controlPlaneConnection,
      DefinitionApp appDefinition,
      SessionImpl.SessionConfig cfg,
      String group,
      String appName,
      String instance,
      Duration defaultDuplicateHeartbeatGrace,
      int defaultDuplicateInstanceCheckAttempts,
      long defaultDuplicateInstanceCheckDelayMillis)
      throws Exception {
    if (controlPlaneConnection == null) {
      return;
    }
    if (!SessionDuplication.duplicateDetectionEnabled(appDefinition)) {
      logger.debug(
          "Duplicate instance detection skipped (runtimeControls.duplicateDetection.enabled=false) app={}/{} instance={}",
          group,
          appName,
          instance);
      return;
    }
    SessionDuplication detector = new SessionDuplication(controlPlaneConnection);
    Duration staleHeartbeatGrace = resolveDuplicateHeartbeatGrace(appDefinition, defaultDuplicateHeartbeatGrace);
    int attempts = resolveDuplicateInstanceCheckAttempts(cfg, defaultDuplicateInstanceCheckAttempts);
    long delayMillis =
        resolveDuplicateInstanceCheckDelayMillis(cfg, defaultDuplicateInstanceCheckDelayMillis);
    long duplicateCheckStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
    logger.info(
        "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=duplicate-check.start app={}/{} instance={} attempts={} delayMs={} graceSeconds={}",
        group,
        appName,
        instance,
        attempts,
        delayMillis,
        staleHeartbeatGrace == null ? null : staleHeartbeatGrace.toSeconds());
    for (int attempt = 1; attempt <= attempts; attempt++) {
      long attemptStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
      SessionDuplication.Decision decision =
          detector.detect(group, appName, instance, System.currentTimeMillis(), staleHeartbeatGrace);
      long detectElapsedMs = elapsedMillis(attemptStartNanos);
      logger.info(
          "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=duplicate-check.detect attempt={}/{} elapsedMs={} duplicateActive={} filter={}",
          attempt,
          attempts,
          detectElapsedMs,
          decision.duplicateActive(),
          decision.statusFilter());
      if (!decision.duplicateActive()) {
        if (attempt > 1) {
          logger.debug(
              "Duplicate instance detection cleared on attempt {}/{} app={}/{} instance={} filter={}",
              attempt,
              attempts,
              group,
              appName,
              instance,
              decision.statusFilter());
        }
        logger.info(
            "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=duplicate-check.complete elapsedMs={} attemptsUsed={}",
            elapsedMillis(duplicateCheckStartNanos),
            attempt);
        return;
      }

      String existingSessionId =
          decision.existingStatus() == null ? null : decision.existingStatus().sessionId();
      String existingHost = duplicateStatusHost(decision.existingStatus());
      String existingPid = duplicateStatusPid(decision.existingStatus());
      logger.warn(
          "Duplicate instance detection attempt {}/{} active app={}/{} instance={} ageMs={} timeoutSeconds={} existingSessionId={} existingHost={} existingPid={} filter={}",
          attempt,
          attempts,
          group,
          appName,
          instance,
          decision.ageMillis(),
          decision.timeoutMillis() / 1000L,
          Strings.trimToNull(existingSessionId),
          existingHost,
          existingPid,
          decision.statusFilter());
      logger.warn(
          "Duplicate instance diagnostics timeoutSeconds={} ageMs={} timestampField={} app={}/{} instance={} existingHost={} existingPid={}",
          decision.timeoutMillis() / 1000L,
          decision.ageMillis(),
          decision.timestampField(),
          group,
          appName,
          instance,
          existingHost,
          existingPid);

      if (attempt == attempts) {
        throw duplicateInstanceActive(decision, attempt, attempts, group, appName, instance);
      }

      try {
        Thread.sleep(delayMillis);
      } catch (InterruptedException ex) {
        Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
        throw new IllegalStateException("Duplicate instance detection interrupted", ex);
      }
    }
  }

  private static Duration resolveDuplicateHeartbeatGrace(
      DefinitionApp appDefinition, Duration defaultDuplicateHeartbeatGrace) {
    long heartbeatSeconds = 0L;
    if (appDefinition != null
        && appDefinition.runtimeControls() != null
        && appDefinition.runtimeControls().status() != null) {
      Integer configured = appDefinition.runtimeControls().status().publishIntervalSeconds();
      if (configured != null && configured > 0) {
        heartbeatSeconds = configured.longValue();
      }
    }
    if (heartbeatSeconds > 0L) {
      return Duration.ofSeconds(
          Math.max(defaultDuplicateHeartbeatGrace.getSeconds(), heartbeatSeconds * 2L));
    }
    return defaultDuplicateHeartbeatGrace;
  }

  private static int resolveDuplicateInstanceCheckAttempts(
      SessionImpl.SessionConfig cfg, int defaultDuplicateInstanceCheckAttempts) {
    Integer configured = cfg.duplicateInstanceCheckAttempts();
    if (configured != null && configured > 0) {
      return configured;
    }
    return defaultDuplicateInstanceCheckAttempts;
  }

  private static long resolveDuplicateInstanceCheckDelayMillis(
      SessionImpl.SessionConfig cfg, long defaultDuplicateInstanceCheckDelayMillis) {
    Duration configured = cfg.duplicateInstanceCheckDelay();
    if (configured == null || configured.isNegative() || configured.isZero()) {
      return defaultDuplicateInstanceCheckDelayMillis;
    }
    return Math.max(1L, configured.toMillis());
  }

  private static IllegalStateException duplicateInstanceActive(
      SessionDuplication.Decision decision,
      int attempt,
      int attempts,
      String group,
      String appName,
      String instance) {
    DefinitionStatusApp existingStatus = decision.existingStatus();
    String existingSessionId = existingStatus == null ? null : existingStatus.sessionId();
    String existingHost = duplicateStatusHost(existingStatus);
    String existingPid = duplicateStatusPid(existingStatus);
    return new IllegalStateException(
        "DUPLICATE_INSTANCE_ACTIVE: duplicate session is alive for "
            + group
            + "/"
            + appName
            + "/"
            + instance
            + " existingSessionId="
            + Strings.trimToNull(existingSessionId)
            + " existingHost="
            + existingHost
            + " existingPid="
            + existingPid
            + " lastSeenEpochMs="
            + decision.lastSeenEpochMs()
            + " ageMs="
            + decision.ageMillis()
            + " timeoutSeconds="
            + (decision.timeoutMillis() / 1000L)
            + " timestampField="
            + decision.timestampField()
            + " filterPaths="
            + SessionDuplication.STATUS_FILTER_PATHS
            + " filter="
            + decision.statusFilter()
            + " attempt="
            + attempt
            + "/"
            + attempts);
  }

  private static String duplicateStatusHost(DefinitionStatusApp status) {
    if (status == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(status.host());
  }

  private static String duplicateStatusPid(DefinitionStatusApp status) {
    if (status == null) {
      return null;
    }
    Map<String, String> tags = status.tags();
    String pid =
        tags == null
            ? null
            : Strings.firstNonBlank(tags.get("pid"), tags.get("processId"), tags.get("process.id"));
    if (pid != null) {
      return pid;
    }
    AppMetrics metrics = status.metrics();
    if (metrics != null && metrics.process() != null && metrics.process().pid() != null) {
      return Long.toString(metrics.process().pid());
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static long elapsedMillis(long startNanos) {
    return Math.max(0L, (System.nanoTime() - startNanos) / 1_000_000L);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session;

import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog.CatalogManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.catalog.manager.CatalogServiceImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connections.manager.ConnectionManagerImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.DeleteManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.DiscoveryManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.DataManagers;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.DataOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.checkpoints.CheckpointStore;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.manager.DataPlanesImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.data.DataEntitlements;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.services.ServiceEntitlements;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.manager.EntitlementsManagerImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.manager.SchemaManagerImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.configs.manager.ConfigManagerImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.manager.ServiceManagerImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.streams.manager.StreamManagerImpl;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;

final class SessionImplManagers {
  private SessionImplManagers() {}

  static StartedManagers initialize(
      SessionImpl session,
      SessionImpl.SessionConfig cfg,
      SessionBootstrap.BootstrapResult result,
      String sessionId,
      CheckpointStore checkpointStore,
      ConnectionManagerImpl connectionManager,
      boolean serviceEntitlementsLogDecisions,
      Logger logger) {
    long initializeStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
    long phaseStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
    DiscoveryManager resolvedDiscoveryManager = session.publishedDiscoveryManager();
    if (resolvedDiscoveryManager == null) {
      resolvedDiscoveryManager =
          new DiscoveryManager(
              result.controlPlaneConnection(),
              result.group(),
              result.configCacheAdmin(),
              cfg.verbose(),
              session::defaultCatalogSubject,
              () -> null);
      resolvedDiscoveryManager.start();
    }
    DiscoveryManager discoveryManager = resolvedDiscoveryManager;
    DiscoveryCache cache = discoveryManager.discoveryCache();
    if (cache == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("DiscoveryCache is not initialized");
    }
    logger.info(
        "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=managers.discovery elapsedMs={} recovered={} offline={}",
        elapsedMillis(phaseStartNanos),
        cache.recovered(),
        cache.offlineMode());
    // Preserve pre-extraction startup ordering: publish discovery manager before data plane init.
    session.publishDiscoveryManager(discoveryManager);

    phaseStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
    DeleteManager deleteManager =
        new DeleteManager(
            () -> {
              DiscoveryCache active = discoveryManager.discoveryCache();
              return active == null ? List.of() : active.allDefinitions();
            },
            session::deleteDefinition);
    session.publishDeleteManager(deleteManager);
    logger.info(
        "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=managers.delete-manager elapsedMs={}",
        elapsedMillis(phaseStartNanos));

    phaseStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
    EntitlementsManagerImpl entitlementsManager =
        new EntitlementsManagerImpl(
            cache,
            result.controlPlaneConnection(),
            sessionId,
            result.group(),
            result.appName(),
            result.instance(),
            result.environment(),
            result.region(),
            result.site(),
            serviceEntitlementsLogDecisions);
    ServiceEntitlements serviceEntitlements = entitlementsManager.serviceEntitlements();
    DataEntitlements dataEntitlements = entitlementsManager.dataEntitlements();
    session.publishServiceEntitlements(serviceEntitlements);
    session.publishDataEntitlements(dataEntitlements);
    EntitlementsManagerImpl.RuntimeInfo entitlementsRuntime = entitlementsManager.runtimeInfo();
    logger.info(
        "[Session][Entitlements] implementation={} eventsEnabled={} eventsTransport={} eventsConnection={} eventsTopic={}",
        entitlementsRuntime.implementation(),
        entitlementsRuntime.eventsEnabled(),
        entitlementsRuntime.eventsTransport(),
        entitlementsRuntime.eventsConnection(),
        entitlementsRuntime.eventsTopic());
    logger.info(
        "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=managers.entitlements elapsedMs={}",
        elapsedMillis(phaseStartNanos));

    phaseStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
    ServiceManager serviceManager = new ServiceManagerImpl(session, checkpointStore);
    DataOptions dataOptions = cfg.dataOptions() == null ? DataOptions.builder().build() : cfg.dataOptions();
    if (result.controlPlaneConnection() == null && dataOptions.service().enabled()) {
      logger.warn(
          "[Session][DiscoveryRecovery] data service plane disabled in recovered mode (control-plane unavailable)");
      dataOptions =
          DataOptions.builder()
              .withDirect(dataOptions.direct())
              .withService(dataOptions.service())
              .withServiceEnabled(false)
              .build();
    }
    logger.debug(
        "[DataManager] directEnabled={} serviceEnabled={} queryService={} ingestService={}",
        dataOptions.direct().enabled(),
        dataOptions.service().enabled(),
        Strings.trimToNull(dataOptions.service().queryService()),
        Strings.trimToNull(dataOptions.service().ingestService()));
    logger.info(
        "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=managers.service-manager elapsedMs={}",
        elapsedMillis(phaseStartNanos));

    phaseStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
    SchemaManager schemaRegistryManager =
        new SchemaManagerImpl(
            () -> discoveryManager.discoveryCache(),
            result::group,
            () -> connectionManager,
            () -> deleteManager);
    session.publishSchemaRegistryManager(schemaRegistryManager);
    StreamManagerImpl streamManager =
        new StreamManagerImpl(
            () -> discoveryManager.discoveryCache(),
            result::group,
            () -> schemaRegistryManager,
            () -> connectionManager,
            () -> deleteManager,
            session);
    logger.info(
        "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=managers.schema-stream elapsedMs={}",
        elapsedMillis(phaseStartNanos));

    phaseStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
    DataManagers dataPlanes =
        new DataPlanesImpl(
            dataOptions,
            cache,
            result.group(),
            result.appName(),
            cfg.kerberosUsername(),
            cfg.kerberosPrincipal(),
            cfg.kerberosKeytab(),
            cfg.trustCert(),
            result.controlPlaneConnection(),
            session::statusScheduler,
            connectionManager,
            dataEntitlements,
            session,
            checkpointStore);
    logger.info(
        "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=managers.data-planes elapsedMs={}",
        elapsedMillis(phaseStartNanos));

    phaseStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
    CatalogManager assetCatalogService =
        new CatalogServiceImpl(
            cache,
            serviceEntitlements,
            dataEntitlements,
            session.defaultCatalogSubject(),
            null,
            Strings.firstNonBlank(result.environment(), "dev"));
    logger.info(
        "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=managers.catalog elapsedMs={}",
        elapsedMillis(phaseStartNanos));

    phaseStartNanos = System.nanoTime();
    ConfigManagerImpl configsCore =
        new ConfigManagerImpl(
            cache,
            result.group(),
            result.appName(),
            result.instance(),
            sessionId,
            result.controlPlaneConnection(),
            result.environmentDefinition());
    logger.info(
        "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=managers.configs elapsedMs={}",
        elapsedMillis(phaseStartNanos));
    logger.info(
        "[Session][StartupTiming] phase=managers.complete elapsedMs={}",
        elapsedMillis(initializeStartNanos));

    return new StartedManagers(
        cache,
        discoveryManager,
        deleteManager,
        entitlementsManager,
        serviceEntitlements,
        dataEntitlements,
        serviceManager,
        schemaRegistryManager,
        streamManager,
        dataPlanes,
        assetCatalogService,
        configsCore);
  }

  record StartedManagers(
      DiscoveryCache discoveryCache,
      DiscoveryManager discoveryManager,
      DeleteManager deleteManager,
      EntitlementsManagerImpl entitlementsManager,
      ServiceEntitlements serviceEntitlements,
      DataEntitlements dataEntitlements,
      ServiceManager serviceManager,
      SchemaManager schemaRegistryManager,
      StreamManagerImpl streamManager,
      DataManagers dataPlanes,
      CatalogManager assetCatalogService,
      ConfigManagerImpl configsCore) {}

  private static long elapsedMillis(long startNanos) {
    return Math.max(0L, (System.nanoTime() - startNanos) / 1_000_000L);
  }
}





FILE: SessionImplShutdown.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session;

import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledExecutorService;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.ControlConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceManager;
import org.slf4j.Logger;

final class SessionImplShutdown {
  private SessionImplShutdown() {}

  static void stopManagedServices(ServiceManager manager, Logger logger) {
    if (manager == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      manager.stopAll();
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      logger.warn("Failed to stop managed services during session stop: {}", ex.toString());
    }
  }

  static void closeControlConnection(ControlConnection control) {
    if (control == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      control.amps().client().disconnect();
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }
    try {
      control.amps().client().close();
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }
  }

  static void closeStatusScheduler(ScheduledExecutorService scheduler) {
    if (scheduler == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      scheduler.shutdownNow();
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }
  }

  static void registerShutdownHook(AtomicBoolean shutdownHookRegistered, Thread shutdownHook) {
    if (!shutdownHookRegistered.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      Runtime.getRuntime().addShutdownHook(shutdownHook);
    } catch (IllegalStateException ex) {
      shutdownHookRegistered.set(false);
    }
  }

  static void unregisterShutdownHook(AtomicBoolean shutdownHookRegistered, Thread shutdownHook) {
    if (!shutdownHookRegistered.compareAndSet(true, false)) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      Runtime.getRuntime().removeShutdownHook(shutdownHook);
    } catch (IllegalStateException | IllegalArgumentException ignore) {
    }
  }

  static void closeQuietlyFromShutdownHook(Runnable closeAction) {
    try {
      closeAction.run();
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }
  }
}

FILE: SessionVmArgs.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.session;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Properties;
import java.util.Set;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.amps.factory.AmpsFactoryOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class SessionVmArgs implements AutoCloseable {
  private static final Set<String> ALLOWLIST =
      Set.of(
          "java.security.krb5.conf",
          "sun.security.krb5.config",
          "java.security.krb5.realm",
          "java.security.krb5.kdc",
          "javax.security.auth.useSubjectCredsOnly",
          "sun.security.krb5.debug");

  private final Map<String, PreviousValue> previousValues;
  private final List<AppliedProperty> appliedProperties;
  private boolean closed;

  private SessionVmArgs(
      Map<String, PreviousValue> previousValues, List<AppliedProperty> appliedProperties) {
    this.previousValues = previousValues;
    this.appliedProperties = appliedProperties;
  }

  public static SessionVmArgs applyKerberosOptions(AmpsFactoryOptions.Kerberos kerberos) {
    if (kerberos == null || !kerberos.isEnabled()) {
      return null;
    }
    Map<String, String> updates = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    String krb5Path = Strings.trimToNull(kerberos.getKrb5ConfPath());
    if (krb5Path != null) {
      updates.put("java.security.krb5.conf", krb5Path);
      updates.put("sun.security.krb5.config", krb5Path);
      updates.put("javax.security.auth.useSubjectCredsOnly", "false");
    }
    String realm = Strings.trimToNull(kerberos.realm());
    if (realm != null) {
      updates.put("java.security.krb5.realm", realm);
    }
    String kdc = Strings.trimToNull(kerberos.kdc());
    if (kdc != null) {
      updates.put("java.security.krb5.kdc", kdc);
    }
    if (kerberos.debugEnabled()) {
      updates.put("sun.security.krb5.debug", "true");
    }
    if (updates.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    return applyUpdates(updates);
  }

  public List<AppliedProperty> appliedProperties() {
    return List.copyOf(appliedProperties);
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    if (closed) {
      return;
    }
    closed = true;
    for (Map.Entry<String, PreviousValue> entry : previousValues.entrySet()) {
      String key = entry.getKey();
      PreviousValue previous = entry.getValue();
      if (previous.hadValue) {
        System.setProperty(key, previous.value);
      } else {
        System.clearProperty(key);
      }
    }
  }

  private static SessionVmArgs applyUpdates(Map<String, String> updates) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(updates, "updates");
    Properties props = System.getProperties();
    Map<String, PreviousValue> previousValues = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    List<AppliedProperty> appliedProperties = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : updates.entrySet()) {
      String key = entry.getKey();
      String value = entry.getValue();
      if (!ALLOWLIST.contains(key)) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("System property not allowlisted: " + key);
      }
      if (value == null) {
        continue;
      }
      boolean hadValue = props.containsKey(key);
      String previous = hadValue ? props.getProperty(key) : null;
      previousValues.put(key, new PreviousValue(hadValue, previous));
      System.setProperty(key, value);
      appliedProperties.add(new AppliedProperty(key, value, hadValue));
    }
    if (appliedProperties.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    return new SessionVmArgs(previousValues, appliedProperties);
  }

  public record AppliedProperty(String key, String value, boolean overwritten) {}

  private record PreviousValue(boolean hadValue, String value) {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.app;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonIgnoreProperties;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.annotation.JsonProperty;

/**
 * Portable app metrics payload (JSON field names use snake_case, units are explicit).
 *
 * <p>Schema (units): process.pid (id), process.uptime_ms (millis), process.start_time_ms (epoch
 * ms), process.threads.count (count), process.fd.open/max (count), cpu.process.percent (0..100),
 * cpu.system.percent (0..100), cpu.load_1m/5m/15m (load), mem.*_bytes (bytes), gc.time_ms
 * (millis), disk.root.*_bytes (bytes), net.rx_bytes/tx_bytes (bytes).</p>
 */
@JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
public record AppMetrics(
    ProcessMetrics process,
    CpuMetrics cpu,
    MemMetrics mem,
    GcMetrics gc,
    DiskMetrics disk,
    NetMetrics net,
    HostMetrics host) {

  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record ProcessMetrics(
      Long pid,
      @JsonProperty("uptime_ms") Long uptimeMs,
      @JsonProperty("start_time_ms") Long startTimeMs,
      String command,
      String jvm,
      ThreadsMetrics threads,
      FileDescriptorMetrics fd) {}

  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record ThreadsMetrics(Integer count, Integer daemon) {}

  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record FileDescriptorMetrics(Long open, Long max) {}

  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record CpuMetrics(
      Integer cores,
      CpuPercent process,
      CpuPercent system,
      @JsonProperty("load_1m") Double load1m,
      @JsonProperty("load_5m") Double load5m,
      @JsonProperty("load_15m") Double load15m) {}

  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record CpuPercent(Double percent) {}

  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record MemMetrics(ProcessMemoryMetrics process, SystemMemoryMetrics system) {}

  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record ProcessMemoryMetrics(
      @JsonProperty("rss_bytes") Long rssBytes,
      @JsonProperty("heap_used_bytes") Long heapUsedBytes,
      @JsonProperty("heap_max_bytes") Long heapMaxBytes,
      @JsonProperty("nonheap_used_bytes") Long nonheapUsedBytes) {}

  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record SystemMemoryMetrics(
      @JsonProperty("total_bytes") Long totalBytes,
      @JsonProperty("free_bytes") Long freeBytes) {}

  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record GcMetrics(Long count, @JsonProperty("time_ms") Long timeMs) {}

  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record DiskMetrics(RootDiskMetrics root) {}

  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record RootDiskMetrics(
      @JsonProperty("free_bytes") Long freeBytes,
      @JsonProperty("total_bytes") Long totalBytes) {}

  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record NetMetrics(
      @JsonProperty("rx_bytes") Long rxBytes, @JsonProperty("tx_bytes") Long txBytes) {}

  @JsonIgnoreProperties(ignoreUnknown = true)
  public record HostMetrics(String name, String address, String os) {}
}


FILE: AppMetricsCollector.java
