package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.app;

import com.sun.management.OperatingSystemMXBean;
import com.sun.management.UnixOperatingSystemMXBean;
import java.io.File;
import java.lang.management.GarbageCollectorMXBean;
import java.lang.management.ManagementFactory;
import java.lang.management.MemoryMXBean;
import java.lang.management.MemoryUsage;
import java.lang.management.RuntimeMXBean;
import java.lang.management.ThreadMXBean;
import java.net.InetAddress;
import java.util.List;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class AppMetricsCollector {

  private static final int COMMAND_LIMIT = 256;

  private final RuntimeMXBean runtimeMxBean = ManagementFactory.getRuntimeMXBean();
  private final MemoryMXBean memoryMxBean = ManagementFactory.getMemoryMXBean();
  private final ThreadMXBean threadMxBean = ManagementFactory.getThreadMXBean();
  private final List<GarbageCollectorMXBean> gcBeans = ManagementFactory.getGarbageCollectorMXBeans();
  private final java.lang.management.OperatingSystemMXBean osBean =
      ManagementFactory.getOperatingSystemMXBean();
  private final OperatingSystemMXBean sunOsBean =
      osBean instanceof OperatingSystemMXBean ? (OperatingSystemMXBean) osBean : null;
  private final UnixOperatingSystemMXBean unixOsBean =
      osBean instanceof UnixOperatingSystemMXBean ? (UnixOperatingSystemMXBean) osBean : null;
  private final int cores =
      osBean == null ? 0 : Math.max(1, osBean.getAvailableProcessors());
  private final long pid = resolvePid();

  private Long lastCpuTimeNs;
  private Long lastCpuSampleNs;

  public AppMetricsCollector() {}

  public synchronized AppMetrics collect() {
    AppMetrics.ProcessMetrics process = buildProcessMetrics();
    AppMetrics.CpuMetrics cpu = buildCpuMetrics();
    AppMetrics.MemMetrics mem = buildMemMetrics();
    AppMetrics.GcMetrics gc = buildGcMetrics();
    AppMetrics.DiskMetrics disk = buildDiskMetrics();
    AppMetrics.HostMetrics host = buildHostMetrics();

    if (process == null && cpu == null && mem == null && gc == null && disk == null && host == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return new AppMetrics(process, cpu, mem, gc, disk, null, host);
  }

  private AppMetrics.ProcessMetrics buildProcessMetrics() {
    Long pidValue = pid > 0 ? pid : null;
    Long uptimeMs = null;
    Long startTimeMs = null;
    String command = null;
    String jvm = null;
    AppMetrics.ThreadsMetrics threads = null;
    AppMetrics.FileDescriptorMetrics fd = null;

    try {
      long uptime = runtimeMxBean.getUptime();
      uptimeMs = uptime > 0 ? uptime : null;
      long start = runtimeMxBean.getStartTime();
      startTimeMs = start > 0 ? start : null;
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }

    try {
      ProcessHandle.Info info = ProcessHandle.current().info();
      if (info != null) {
        command =
            info.commandLine().map(value -> trimAndLimit(value, COMMAND_LIMIT)).orElse(null);
        if (command == null) {
          command = info.command().map(value -> trimAndLimit(value, COMMAND_LIMIT)).orElse(null);
        }
      }
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }

    try {
      String vendor = System.getProperty("java.vendor");
      String version = System.getProperty("java.version");
      String combined = combine(vendor, version);
      jvm = combined == null ? null : trimAndLimit(combined, COMMAND_LIMIT);
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }

    try {
      int count = threadMxBean.getThreadCount();
      int daemon = threadMxBean.getDaemonThreadCount();
      if (count > 0 || daemon > 0) {
        threads = new AppMetrics.ThreadsMetrics(count > 0 ? count : null, daemon > 0 ? daemon : null);
      }
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }

    try {
      if (unixOsBean != null) {
        long open = unixOsBean.getOpenFileDescriptorCount();
        long max = unixOsBean.getMaxFileDescriptorCount();
        Long openValue = open >= 0 ? open : null;
        Long maxValue = max >= 0 ? max : null;
        if (openValue != null || maxValue != null) {
          fd = new AppMetrics.FileDescriptorMetrics(openValue, maxValue);
        }
      }
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }

    if (!hasValue(pidValue, uptimeMs, startTimeMs, command, jvm, threads, fd)) {
      return null;
    }
    return new AppMetrics.ProcessMetrics(pidValue, uptimeMs, startTimeMs, command, jvm, threads, fd);
  }

  private AppMetrics.CpuMetrics buildCpuMetrics() {
    Integer coresValue = cores > 0 ? cores : null;
    AppMetrics.CpuPercent process = null;
    AppMetrics.CpuPercent system = null;
    Double load1m = null;

    Double processPercent = readProcessCpuPercent();
    if (processPercent != null) {
      process = new AppMetrics.CpuPercent(processPercent);
    }
    Double systemPercent = readSystemCpuPercent();
    if (systemPercent != null) {
      system = new AppMetrics.CpuPercent(systemPercent);
    }
    try {
      double load = osBean == null ? -1 : osBean.getSystemLoadAverage();
      load1m = load >= 0 ? load : null;
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }

    if (!hasValue(coresValue, process, system, load1m)) {
      return null;
    }
    return new AppMetrics.CpuMetrics(coresValue, process, system, load1m, null, null);
  }

  private Double readProcessCpuPercent() {
    try {
      if (sunOsBean != null) {
        double direct = sunOsBean.getProcessCpuLoad();
        if (direct >= 0) {
          return clampPercent(direct * 100.0);
        }
      }
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }
    return computeProcessCpuPercentFallback();
  }

  private Double computeProcessCpuPercentFallback() {
    if (sunOsBean == null || cores <= 0) {
      return null;
    }
    long nowNs = System.nanoTime();
    long cpuTimeNs;
    try {
      cpuTimeNs = sunOsBean.getProcessCpuTime();
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      return null;
    }
    if (cpuTimeNs <= 0) {
      lastCpuTimeNs = cpuTimeNs;
      lastCpuSampleNs = nowNs;
      return null;
    }
    if (lastCpuTimeNs == null || lastCpuSampleNs == null) {
      lastCpuTimeNs = cpuTimeNs;
      lastCpuSampleNs = nowNs;
      return null;
    }
    long deltaCpu = cpuTimeNs - lastCpuTimeNs;
    long deltaWall = nowNs - lastCpuSampleNs;
    lastCpuTimeNs = cpuTimeNs;
    lastCpuSampleNs = nowNs;
    if (deltaCpu <= 0 || deltaWall <= 0) {
      return null;
    }
    double ratio = deltaCpu / (double) deltaWall;
    double percent = ratio * 100.0 / cores;
    return clampPercent(percent);
  }

  private Double readSystemCpuPercent() {
    try {
      if (sunOsBean != null) {
        double load = sunOsBean.getSystemCpuLoad();
        if (load >= 0) {
          return clampPercent(load * 100.0);
        }
      }
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }
    return null;
  }

  private AppMetrics.MemMetrics buildMemMetrics() {
    AppMetrics.ProcessMemoryMetrics process = null;
    AppMetrics.SystemMemoryMetrics system = null;

    try {
      MemoryUsage heap = memoryMxBean.getHeapMemoryUsage();
      MemoryUsage nonheap = memoryMxBean.getNonHeapMemoryUsage();
      Long heapUsed = heap == null ? null : positiveOrNull(heap.getUsed());
      Long heapMax = heap == null ? null : positiveOrNull(heap.getMax());
      Long nonheapUsed = nonheap == null ? null : positiveOrNull(nonheap.getUsed());
      if (heapUsed != null || heapMax != null || nonheapUsed != null) {
        process = new AppMetrics.ProcessMemoryMetrics(null, heapUsed, heapMax, nonheapUsed);
      }
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }

    try {
      if (sunOsBean != null) {
        Long total = positiveOrNull(sunOsBean.getTotalPhysicalMemorySize());
        Long free = positiveOrNull(sunOsBean.getFreePhysicalMemorySize());
        if (total != null || free != null) {
          system = new AppMetrics.SystemMemoryMetrics(total, free);
        }
      }
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }

    if (process == null && system == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return new AppMetrics.MemMetrics(process, system);
  }

  private AppMetrics.GcMetrics buildGcMetrics() {
    long totalCount = 0L;
    long totalTime = 0L;
    boolean countKnown = false;
    boolean timeKnown = false;
    for (GarbageCollectorMXBean bean : gcBeans) {
      if (bean == null) {
        continue;
      }
      long count = bean.getCollectionCount();
      if (count >= 0) {
        totalCount += count;
        countKnown = true;
      }
      long time = bean.getCollectionTime();
      if (time >= 0) {
        totalTime += time;
        timeKnown = true;
      }
    }
    if (!countKnown && !timeKnown) {
      return null;
    }
    return new AppMetrics.GcMetrics(countKnown ? totalCount : null, timeKnown ? totalTime : null);
  }

  private AppMetrics.DiskMetrics buildDiskMetrics() {
    try {
      File root = new File(System.getProperty("user.dir", "."));
      long total = root.getTotalSpace();
      long free = root.getFreeSpace();
      Long totalValue = positiveOrNull(total);
      Long freeValue = positiveOrNull(free);
      if (totalValue == null && freeValue == null) {
        return null;
      }
      return new AppMetrics.DiskMetrics(new AppMetrics.RootDiskMetrics(freeValue, totalValue));
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private AppMetrics.HostMetrics buildHostMetrics() {
    String name = null;
    String address = null;
    String os = null;
    try {
      InetAddress host = InetAddress.getLocalHost();
      name = Strings.trimToNull(host.getHostName());
      address = Strings.trimToNull(host.getHostAddress());
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }
    try {
      String osName = Strings.trimToNull(System.getProperty("os.name"));
      String osVersion = Strings.trimToNull(System.getProperty("os.version"));
      String osArch = Strings.trimToNull(System.getProperty("os.arch"));
      String label = combine(osName, osVersion);
      if (label != null && osArch != null) {
        label = label + " (" + osArch + ")";
      } else if (label == null) {
        label = osArch;
      }
      os = Strings.trimToNull(label);
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }
    if (!hasValue(name, address, os)) {
      return null;
    }
    return new AppMetrics.HostMetrics(name, address, os);
  }

  private static boolean hasValue(Object... values) {
    if (values == null) {
      return false;
    }
    for (Object value : values) {
      if (value != null) {
        return true;
      }
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static Long positiveOrNull(long value) {
    return value > 0 ? value : null;
  }

  private static long resolvePid() {
    try {
      return ProcessHandle.current().pid();
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      return -1L;
    }
  }


  private static String trimAndLimit(String value, int limit) {
    String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (trimmed == null || limit <= 0) {
      return trimmed;
    }
    return trimmed.length() <= limit ? trimmed : trimmed.substring(0, limit);
  }

  private static String combine(String left, String right) {
    String a = Strings.trimToNull(left);
    String b = Strings.trimToNull(right);
    if (a == null && b == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if (a == null) {
      return b;
    }
    if (b == null) {
      return a;
    }
    return a + " " + b;
  }

  private static Double clampPercent(double value) {
    if (Double.isNaN(value) || Double.isInfinite(value)) {
      return null;
    }
    if (value < 0) {
      return 0.0;
    }
    if (value > 100.0) {
      return 100.0;
    }
    return value;
  }
}

FILE: AppStatusCache.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.app;

import com.crankuptheamps.client.Command;
import com.crankuptheamps.client.Message;
import java.time.Clock;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.concurrent.CountDownLatch;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.ControlConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.StatusCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryTopics;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionStatusApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class AppStatusCache implements StatusCache {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AppStatusCache.class);
  private static final String TOPIC_STATUS = DiscoveryTopics.STATUS;
  private static final String FILTER_STATUS_APP = "/type='STATUS_APP'";

  private final ControlConnection control;
  private final Clock clock;
  private final ConcurrentHashMap<String, StatusSnapshot> aggregateStatuses = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
  private final ConcurrentHashMap<String, StatusSnapshot> instanceStatuses = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
  private final AtomicBoolean started = new AtomicBoolean(false);
  private final AtomicBoolean recovered = new AtomicBoolean(false);
  private final CountDownLatch recoveryLatch = new CountDownLatch(1);
  private volatile ControlConnection.Subscription subscription;

  public AppStatusCache(ControlConnection control) {
    this(control, Clock.systemUTC());
  }

  AppStatusCache(ControlConnection control, Clock clock) {
    this.control = Objects.requireNonNull(control, "control");
    this.clock = Objects.requireNonNull(clock, "clock");
  }

  public void start() throws Exception {
    if (!started.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
      awaitRecovery(Duration.ofSeconds(30));
      return;
    }
    Command command = new Command(Message.Command.SOWAndSubscribe);
    command.setTopic(TOPIC_STATUS);
    command.setOptions("oof");
    command.setFilter(FILTER_STATUS_APP);
    subscription =
        control
            .sowAndSubscribe(
                command.getTopic(),
                command.getOptions(),
                command.getFilter(),
                message -> handleMessage(message.raw()));
    awaitRecovery(Duration.ofSeconds(30));
    LOGGER.debug("Status cache ready topics={} enabledTypes={} appCount={} instanceCount={}", List.of(TOPIC_STATUS), List.of("STATUS_APP"), aggregateStatuses.size(), instanceStatuses.size());
  }

  public void startShared() {
    if (!started.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
      awaitRecovery(Duration.ofSeconds(30));
    }
  }

  public boolean recovered() {
    return recovered.get();
  }

  public int size() {
    return aggregateStatuses.size();
  }

  public int instanceSize() {
    return instanceStatuses.size();
  }

  public List<DefinitionStatusApp> listLatestStatusApps() {
    return aggregateStatuses.values().stream()
        .sorted(Comparator.comparing(StatusSnapshot::appKey, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .map(StatusSnapshot::status)
        .toList();
  }

  public List<DefinitionStatusApp> listLatestStatusAppInstances() {
    return instanceStatuses.values().stream()
        .sorted(Comparator.comparing(StatusSnapshot::instanceKey, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER))
        .map(StatusSnapshot::status)
        .toList();
  }

  public Optional<DefinitionStatusApp> getLatestStatusApp(String group, String appName) {
    String key = appKey(group, appName);
    if (key == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    StatusSnapshot snapshot = aggregateStatuses.get(key);
    return snapshot == null ? Optional.empty() : Optional.of(snapshot.status());
  }

  public Optional<Instant> getLatestStatusAppReceivedTimeUtc(String group, String appName) {
    String key = appKey(group, appName);
    if (key == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    StatusSnapshot snapshot = aggregateStatuses.get(key);
    return snapshot == null ? Optional.empty() : Optional.of(snapshot.receivedTimeUtc());
  }

  public Optional<DefinitionStatusApp> getLatestStatusAppInstance(
      String group, String appName, String instance) {
    String key = instanceKey(group, appName, instance);
    if (key == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    StatusSnapshot snapshot = instanceStatuses.get(key);
    return snapshot == null ? Optional.empty() : Optional.of(snapshot.status());
  }

  public Optional<Instant> getLatestStatusAppInstanceReceivedTimeUtc(
      String group, String appName, String instance) {
    String key = instanceKey(group, appName, instance);
    if (key == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    StatusSnapshot snapshot = instanceStatuses.get(key);
    return snapshot == null ? Optional.empty() : Optional.of(snapshot.receivedTimeUtc());
  }

  public void stop() {
    ControlConnection.Subscription id = subscription;
    if (id != null) {
      try {
        id.close();
      } catch (Exception ignore) {
      }
      subscription = null;
    }
    aggregateStatuses.clear();
    instanceStatuses.clear();
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    stop();
  }

  public void awaitRecovery(Duration timeout) {
    long millis = timeout == null ? 30000L : Math.max(1L, timeout.toMillis());
    try {
      boolean done = recoveryLatch.await(millis, TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS);
      if (!done) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "AppStatusCache initial recovery did not complete (GroupEnd not observed)");
      }
    } catch (InterruptedException ex) {
      Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
      throw new IllegalStateException("Interrupted while waiting for AppStatusCache recovery", ex);
    }
  }

  private void handleMessage(Message message) {
    if (message == null) {
      return;
    }
    int command = message.getCommand();
    if (command == Message.Command.GroupEnd) {
      recovered.set(true);
      recoveryLatch.countDown();
      return;
    }
    if (command != Message.Command.SOW
        && command != Message.Command.Publish
        && command != Message.Command.OOF) {
      return;
    }
    String payload = message.getData();
    if (Strings.isBlank(payload)) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      Definition definition = DiscoveryCodec.decode(payload);
      if (!(definition instanceof DefinitionStatusApp status)) {
        return;
      }
      String appKey = appKey(status.group(), status.name());
      String instanceKey = instanceKey(status.group(), status.name(), status.instance());
      if (appKey == null || instanceKey == null) {
        return;
      }
      if (command == Message.Command.OOF) {
        removeInstance(appKey, instanceKey);
        return;
      }
      StatusSnapshot snapshot =
          new StatusSnapshot(status, Instant.now(clock), appKey, instanceKey);
      instanceStatuses.put(instanceKey, snapshot);
      aggregateStatuses.compute(
          appKey,
          (ignored, current) ->
              current == null || snapshot.receivedTimeUtc().isAfter(current.receivedTimeUtc())
                  ? snapshot
                  : current);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      LOGGER.warn("Ignoring malformed status message command={} reason={}", command, ex.toString());
    }
  }

  private void removeInstance(String appKey, String instanceKey) {
    StatusSnapshot removed = instanceStatuses.remove(instanceKey);
    if (removed == null) {
      return;
    }
    aggregateStatuses.compute(
        appKey,
        (ignored, current) -> {
          if (current == null || !instanceKey.equals(current.instanceKey())) {
            return current;
          }
          return latestAggregateFor(appKey);
        });
  }

  private StatusSnapshot latestAggregateFor(String appKey) {
    if (appKey == null) {
      return null;
    }
    List<StatusSnapshot> candidates = new ArrayList<>();
    for (StatusSnapshot snapshot : instanceStatuses.values()) {
      if (snapshot == null || !appKey.equals(snapshot.appKey())) {
        continue;
      }
      candidates.add(snapshot);
    }
    if (candidates.isEmpty()) {
      return null;
    }
    candidates.sort(Comparator.comparing(StatusSnapshot::receivedTimeUtc).reversed());
    return candidates.get(0);
  }

  private static String appKey(String group, String appName) {
    String normalizedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    String normalizedApp = Strings.trimToNull(appName);
    if (normalizedGroup == null || normalizedApp == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return normalizedGroup + "::" + normalizedApp;
  }

  public void onStatusMessage(Message message) {
    handleMessage(message);
  }

  private static String instanceKey(String group, String appName, String instance) {
    String resolvedAppKey = appKey(group, appName);
    String normalizedInstance = Strings.trimToNull(instance);
    if (resolvedAppKey == null || normalizedInstance == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return resolvedAppKey + "::" + normalizedInstance;
  }

  private record StatusSnapshot(
      DefinitionStatusApp status, Instant receivedTimeUtc, String appKey, String instanceKey) {}
}







FILE: AppStatusKey.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.app;

import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Stable identifier for an app status SOW record. */
public final class AppStatusKey {

  private final String group;
  private final String app;
  private final String instance;

  public AppStatusKey(String group, String app, String instance) {
    this.group = Strings.trimToEmpty(group);
    this.app = Strings.trimToEmpty(app);
    this.instance = Strings.trimToEmpty(instance);
  }

  public String group() {
    return group;
  }

  public String app() {
    return app;
  }

  public String instance() {
    return instance;
  }

  /** Stable SOW key, e.g. {@code group=core|app=positions|instance=instance1}. */
  public String sowKey() {
    return "group=" + group + "|app=" + app + "|instance=" + instance;
  }

  @Override
  public boolean equals(Object o) {
    if (this == o) {
      return true;
    }
    if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) {
      return false;
    }
    AppStatusKey that = (AppStatusKey) o;
    return Objects.equals(group, that.group)
        && Objects.equals(app, that.app)
        && Objects.equals(instance, that.instance);
  }

  @Override
  public int hashCode() {
    return Objects.hash(group, app, instance);
  }

  @Override
  public String toString() {
    return sowKey();
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data;

import java.nio.file.Path;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceRunOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class DataOptions {
  private final DirectOptions direct;
  private final ServiceOptions service;

  private DataOptions(Builder builder) {
    this.direct =
        builder.directBuilder == null
            ? (builder.direct == null ? DirectOptions.builder().build() : builder.direct)
            : builder.directBuilder.build();
    this.service =
        builder.serviceBuilder == null
            ? (builder.service == null ? ServiceOptions.builder().build() : builder.service)
            : builder.serviceBuilder.build();
    validate();
  }

  public DirectOptions direct() {
    return direct;
  }

  public ServiceOptions service() {
    return service;
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  private void validate() {
    if (service.enabled() && service.queryService() == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "DataOptions service.enabled=true requires service.queryService");
    }
    if (!service.enabled()) {
      if (service.queryService() != null
          || service.ingestService() != null
          || service.serviceOptions() != null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException(
            "DataOptions service.enabled=false cannot specify service.*");
      }
    }
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private DirectOptions direct;
    private ServiceOptions service;
    private DirectOptions.Builder directBuilder;
    private ServiceOptions.Builder serviceBuilder;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withDirect(DirectOptions value) {
      direct = value;
      directBuilder = null;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withService(ServiceOptions value) {
      service = value;
      serviceBuilder = null;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withDirectEnabled(boolean value) {
      ensureDirectBuilder().withEnabled(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withServiceEnabled(boolean value) {
      ensureServiceBuilder().withEnabled(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withServiceQueryService(String value) {
      ensureServiceBuilder().withQueryService(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withServiceIngestService(String value) {
      ensureServiceBuilder().withIngestService(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withServiceOptions(ServiceRunOptions value) {
      ensureServiceBuilder().withServiceOptions(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withServiceTlsTrustCert(Path trustCertPem) {
      ensureServiceBuilder().withTlsTrustCert(trustCertPem);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withServiceTlsClientTrustCert(Path trustCertPem) {
      ensureServiceBuilder().withTlsClientTrustCert(trustCertPem);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withServiceTlsCertChain(Path certChainPem) {
      ensureServiceBuilder().withTlsCertChain(certChainPem);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withServiceTlsPrivateKey(Path privateKeyPem) {
      ensureServiceBuilder().withTlsPrivateKey(privateKeyPem);
      return this;
    }

    public DataOptions build() {
      return new DataOptions(this);
    }

    private DirectOptions.Builder ensureDirectBuilder() {
      if (directBuilder != null) {
        return directBuilder;
      }
      directBuilder = direct == null ? DirectOptions.builder() : direct.toBuilder();
      direct = null;
      return directBuilder;
    }

    private ServiceOptions.Builder ensureServiceBuilder() {
      if (serviceBuilder != null) {
        return serviceBuilder;
      }
      serviceBuilder = service == null ? ServiceOptions.builder() : service.toBuilder();
      service = null;
      return serviceBuilder;
    }
  }

  public static final class DirectOptions {
    private final boolean enabled;

    private DirectOptions(Builder builder) {
      this.enabled = builder.enabled;
    }

    public boolean enabled() {
      return enabled;
    }

    public Builder toBuilder() {
      return builder().withEnabled(enabled);
    }

    public static Builder builder() {
      return new Builder();
    }

    public static final class Builder {
      private boolean enabled = true;

      private Builder() {}

      public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
        enabled = value;
        return this;
      }

      public DirectOptions build() {
        return new DirectOptions(this);
      }
    }
  }

  public static final class ServiceOptions {
    private final boolean enabled;
    private final String ingestService;
    private final String queryService;
    private final ServiceRunOptions serviceOptions;

    private ServiceOptions(Builder builder) {
      this.enabled = builder.enabled;
      this.ingestService = Strings.trimToNull(builder.ingestService);
      this.queryService = Strings.trimToNull(builder.queryService);
      this.serviceOptions =
          builder.serviceOptionsBuilder == null
              ? builder.serviceOptions
              : builder.serviceOptionsBuilder.build();
    }

    public boolean enabled() {
      return enabled;
    }

    public String ingestService() {
      return ingestService;
    }

    public String queryService() {
      return queryService;
    }

    public ServiceRunOptions serviceOptions() {
      return serviceOptions;
    }

    public Builder toBuilder() {
      Builder builder = builder().withEnabled(enabled).withIngestService(ingestService).withQueryService(queryService);
      if (serviceOptions != null) {
        builder.withServiceOptions(serviceOptions);
      }
      return builder;
    }

    public static Builder builder() {
      return new Builder();
    }

    public static final class Builder {
      private boolean enabled;
      private String ingestService;
      private String queryService;
      private ServiceRunOptions serviceOptions;
      private ServiceRunOptions.Builder serviceOptionsBuilder;

      private Builder() {}

      public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
        enabled = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withIngestService(String value) {
        ingestService = Strings.trimToNull(value);
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withQueryService(String value) {
        queryService = Strings.trimToNull(value);
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withServiceOptions(ServiceRunOptions value) {
        serviceOptions = value;
        serviceOptionsBuilder = null;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withTlsTrustCert(Path trustCertPem) {
        ensureServiceOptionsBuilder().withTlsTrustCert(trustCertPem);
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withTlsClientTrustCert(Path trustCertPem) {
        ensureServiceOptionsBuilder().withTlsClientTrustCert(trustCertPem);
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withTlsCertChain(Path certChainPem) {
        ensureServiceOptionsBuilder().withTlsCertChain(certChainPem);
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withTlsPrivateKey(Path privateKeyPem) {
        ensureServiceOptionsBuilder().withTlsPrivateKey(privateKeyPem);
        return this;
      }

      public ServiceOptions build() {
        return new ServiceOptions(this);
      }

      private ServiceRunOptions.Builder ensureServiceOptionsBuilder() {
        if (serviceOptionsBuilder != null) {
          return serviceOptionsBuilder;
        }
        serviceOptionsBuilder =
            serviceOptions == null ? ServiceRunOptions.builder() : copyServiceOptions(serviceOptions);
        serviceOptions = null;
        return serviceOptionsBuilder;
      }

      private static ServiceRunOptions.Builder copyServiceOptions(ServiceRunOptions value) {
        ServiceRunOptions options = value == null ? ServiceRunOptions.defaults() : value;
        return ServiceRunOptions.builder()
            .withInstanceName(options.instanceName())
            .withBindHost(options.bindHost())
            .withBindPort(options.bindPort())
            .withAdvertiseHost(options.advertiseHost())
            .withAdvertisePort(options.advertisePort())
            .withTlsCertChain(options.tlsCertChain())
            .withTlsPrivateKey(options.tlsPrivateKey())
            .withTlsTrustCert(options.tlsTrustCert())
            .withTlsClientTrustCert(options.clientTrustCert())
            .requireClientCertificates(options.requireClientCertificates())
            .withInterceptors(options.interceptors())
            .withDatasetIds(options.datasetIds())
            .withProxyMode(options.proxyMode())
            .withPreferredRegion(options.preferredRegion())
            .withGroup(options.group())
            .withCallCount(options.callCount())
            .withCallDelayMillis(options.callDelayMillis());
      }
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data;

import java.util.Map;
import java.util.function.BiFunction;
import java.util.function.UnaryOperator;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.IngestTransformer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.IngestPayload;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.IngestPayloadJson;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.IngestRuntime;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.agent.IngestAgent;

public interface IngestManager {
  ParquetManager parquet();

  IngestAdmin admin();

  default IngestAgent agent() {
    return agent(IngestAgent.Options.defaults());
  }

  default IngestAgent agent(IngestAgent.Builder builder) {
    IngestAgent.Builder resolved = builder == null ? IngestAgent.builder() : builder;
    return agent(resolved.build());
  }

  default IngestAgent agent(IngestAgent.Options options) {
    throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Ingest agent is not supported");
  }

  default boolean exists(String ingestName) {
    if (ingestName == null || ingestName.isBlank()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("ingestName is required");
    }
    return admin().getModel(ingestName).isPresent();
  }

  IngestRuntime open(String ingestName);

  IngestRuntime start(String ingestName);

  default IngestRuntime start(String ingestName, IngestRuntimeOptions options) {
    IngestRuntimeOptions resolved = options == null ? IngestRuntimeOptions.builder().build() : options;
    if (resolved.parquetMaxRowsPerFile() != null || resolved.parquetMaxIdleMillis() != null) {
      setParquetRollPolicy(
          ingestName, resolved.parquetMaxRowsPerFile(), resolved.parquetMaxIdleMillis());
    }
    if (resolved.parquetFilenamePrefix() != null) {
      setParquetFilenamePrefix(ingestName, resolved.parquetFilenamePrefix());
    }
    return start(ingestName);
  }

  void stop(String ingestName);

  void append(String ingestName, IngestPayload payload);

  default void append(String ingestName, Map<String, ?> payload) {
    if (payload == null || payload.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("payload is required");
    }
    final String json;
    try {
      json = DiscoveryCodec.mapper().writeValueAsString(payload);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("payload map must be JSON serializable", ex);
    }
    append(ingestName, new IngestPayloadJson(json));
  }

  void appendIpc(String ingestName, byte[] arrowIpcStreamBytes);

  default void setParquetRollPolicy(String ingestName, Integer maxRowsPerFile, Long maxIdleMillis) {
    throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Parquet roll policy override is not supported");
  }

  default void clearParquetRollPolicy(String ingestName) {
    setParquetRollPolicy(ingestName, null, null);
  }

  default void setParquetFilenamePrefix(String ingestName, String parquetFilenamePrefix) {
    throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Parquet filename prefix override is not supported");
  }

  default void clearParquetFilenamePrefix(String ingestName) {
    setParquetFilenamePrefix(ingestName, null);
  }

  record IngestRuntimeOptions(
      Integer parquetMaxRowsPerFile,
      Long parquetMaxIdleMillis,
      String ampsConnectionInstance,
      String parquetFilenamePrefix,
      Boolean ampsLogIncoming,
      Boolean ampsLogOutgoing,
      UnaryOperator<String> ampsPayloadTransformer,
      BiFunction<String, Integer, String> ampsPayloadTransformerWithCommand,
      Boolean ampsPersistOofAsRows) {
    public static Builder builder() {
      return new Builder();
    }

    public Builder toBuilder() {
      return builder()
          .withParquetMaxRowsPerFile(parquetMaxRowsPerFile)
          .withParquetMaxIdleMillis(parquetMaxIdleMillis)
          .withAmpsConnectionInstance(ampsConnectionInstance)
          .withParquetFilenamePrefix(parquetFilenamePrefix)
          .withAmpsLogIncoming(ampsLogIncoming)
          .withAmpsLogOutgoing(ampsLogOutgoing)
          .withAmpsPayloadTransformer(ampsPayloadTransformer)
          .withAmpsPayloadTransformerWithCommand(ampsPayloadTransformerWithCommand)
          .withAmpsPersistOofAsRows(ampsPersistOofAsRows);
    }

    public static IngestRuntimeOptions defaults() {
      return builder().build();
    }

    public static IngestRuntimeOptions parquetRollPolicy(int maxRowsPerFile, long maxIdleMillis) {
      return builder().withParquetRollPolicy(maxRowsPerFile, maxIdleMillis).build();
    }

    public static final class Builder {
      private Integer parquetMaxRowsPerFile;
      private Long parquetMaxIdleMillis;
      private String ampsConnectionInstance;
      private String parquetFilenamePrefix;
      private Boolean ampsLogIncoming;
      private Boolean ampsLogOutgoing;
      private UnaryOperator<String> ampsPayloadTransformer;
      private BiFunction<String, Integer, String> ampsPayloadTransformerWithCommand;
      private Boolean ampsPersistOofAsRows;

      public Builder withParquetRollPolicy(int maxRowsPerFile, long maxIdleMillis) {
        parquetMaxRowsPerFile = maxRowsPerFile;
        parquetMaxIdleMillis = maxIdleMillis;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withParquetMaxRowsPerFile(Integer value) {
        parquetMaxRowsPerFile = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withParquetMaxIdleMillis(Long value) {
        parquetMaxIdleMillis = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withAmpsConnectionInstance(String value) {
        ampsConnectionInstance = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withParquetFilenamePrefix(String value) {
        parquetFilenamePrefix = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withAmpsLogIncoming(Boolean value) {
        ampsLogIncoming = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withAmpsLogOutgoing(Boolean value) {
        ampsLogOutgoing = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withAmpsPayloadTransformer(UnaryOperator<String> value) {
        ampsPayloadTransformer = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withAmpsPayloadTransformerWithCommand(
          BiFunction<String, Integer, String> value) {
        ampsPayloadTransformerWithCommand = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withAmpsTransformer(IngestTransformer value) {
        ampsPayloadTransformerWithCommand =
            value == null ? null : value.asPayloadTransformerWithCommand();
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withAmpsPersistOofAsRows(Boolean value) {
        ampsPersistOofAsRows = value;
        return this;
      }

      public IngestRuntimeOptions build() {
        return new IngestRuntimeOptions(
            parquetMaxRowsPerFile,
            parquetMaxIdleMillis,
            ampsConnectionInstance,
            parquetFilenamePrefix,
            ampsLogIncoming,
            ampsLogOutgoing,
            ampsPayloadTransformer,
            ampsPayloadTransformerWithCommand,
            ampsPersistOofAsRows);
      }
    }
  }
}

FILE: RowManager.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public interface RowManager extends AutoCloseable {
  boolean check();

  RowResult query(DataQuery query);

  default RowResult querySql(String sql) {
    return querySql(sql, -1);
  }

  default RowResult querySql(String sql, int limit) {
    throw new UnsupportedOperationException("SQL query is not supported by this data manager");
  }

  default long rowCount(String tableIdentifier) {
    String resolved = Strings.requireNonBlank(tableIdentifier, "tableIdentifier");
    RowResult result = querySql("select count(*) as row_count from " + resolved, 1);
    return parseRowCount(result);
  }

  private static long parseRowCount(RowResult result) {
    if (result == null || result.rows().isEmpty() || result.rows().get(0).isEmpty()) {
      return 0L;
    }
    Object count = result.rows().get(0).get(0);
    if (count instanceof Number number) {
      return number.longValue();
    }
    String text = String.valueOf(count);
    if (text == null || text.isBlank()) {
      return 0L;
    }
    return Long.parseLong(text.trim());
  }

  @Override
  void close();
}


FILE: RowResult.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.List;

public record RowResult(List<String> columns, List<List<Object>> rows) {
  public RowResult {
    columns = immutableCopy(columns);
    rows = immutableNestedCopy(rows);
  }

  private static <T> List<T> immutableCopy(List<? extends T> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    return Collections.unmodifiableList(new ArrayList<>(values));
  }

  private static List<List<Object>> immutableNestedCopy(List<List<Object>> values) {
    if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<List<Object>> copy = new ArrayList<>(values.size());
    for (List<Object> row : values) {
      copy.add(immutableCopy(row));
    }
    return Collections.unmodifiableList(copy);
  }
}

FILE: TabularStreamOptions.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class TabularStreamOptions {
  public enum Start {
    LATEST,
    RESUME,
    BEGINNING,
    FROM_SEQUENCE
  }

  private static final int DEFAULT_BATCH_MAX_ROWS = 256;
  private static final int DEFAULT_FLUSH_MILLIS = 250;

  private final Start start;
  private final Long fromSequence;
  private final int batchMaxRows;
  private final int flushMillis;
  private final String subscriptionId;
  private final String filterSql;
  private final Boolean publicAccess;

  private TabularStreamOptions(Builder builder) {
    this.start = builder.start;
    this.fromSequence = builder.fromSequence;
    this.batchMaxRows = builder.batchMaxRows;
    this.flushMillis = builder.flushMillis;
    this.subscriptionId = builder.subscriptionId;
    this.filterSql = builder.filterSql;
    this.publicAccess = builder.publicAccess;
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public static TabularStreamOptions defaults() {
    return builder().build();
  }

  public Start start() {
    return start;
  }

  public Long fromSequence() {
    return fromSequence;
  }

  public int batchMaxRows() {
    return batchMaxRows;
  }

  public int flushMillis() {
    return flushMillis;
  }

  public String subscriptionId() {
    return subscriptionId;
  }

  public String filterSql() {
    return filterSql;
  }

  public Boolean publicAccess() {
    return publicAccess;
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private Start start = Start.LATEST;
    private Long fromSequence;
    private int batchMaxRows = DEFAULT_BATCH_MAX_ROWS;
    private int flushMillis = DEFAULT_FLUSH_MILLIS;
    private String subscriptionId = "default";
    private String filterSql;
    private Boolean publicAccess;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withStart(Start value) {
      this.start = value == null ? Start.LATEST : value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withFromSequence(Long value) {
      this.fromSequence = value;
      this.start = value == null ? this.start : Start.FROM_SEQUENCE;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withBatchMaxRows(int value) {
      this.batchMaxRows = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withFlushMillis(int value) {
      this.flushMillis = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSubscriptionId(String value) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      this.subscriptionId = normalized == null ? "default" : normalized;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withFilter(String value) {
      this.filterSql = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPublic(boolean value) {
      this.publicAccess = value;
      return this;
    }

    public TabularStreamOptions build() {
      if (start == Start.FROM_SEQUENCE) {
        if (fromSequence == null || fromSequence < 0L) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("fromSequence must be >= 0 when start=FROM_SEQUENCE");
        }
      }
      if (batchMaxRows <= 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("batchMaxRows must be > 0");
      }
      if (flushMillis <= 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("flushMillis must be > 0");
      }
      if (Strings.trimToNull(subscriptionId) == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("subscriptionId is required");
      }
      return new TabularStreamOptions(this);
    }
  }
}

FILE: DuckdbCatalogImplRelation.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.catalog;

import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.Locale;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Exceptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class DuckdbCatalogImplRelation {

  private DuckdbCatalogImplRelation() {}

  static String duckdbViewName(String group, String namespace, String name) {
    return sanitizeIdentifier(group)
        + "__"
        + sanitizeIdentifier(namespace)
        + "__"
        + sanitizeIdentifier(name);
  }

  static String sanitizeIdentifier(String value) {
    String token = Strings.requireNonBlank(value, "identifier");
    StringBuilder normalized = new StringBuilder(token.length());
    for (int index = 0; index < token.length(); index++) {
      char ch = token.charAt(index);
      if (Character.isLetterOrDigit(ch) || ch == '_') {
        normalized.append(ch);
      } else {
        normalized.append('_');
      }
    }
    String resolved = Strings.trimToNull(normalized.toString());
    return resolved == null ? "dataset" : resolved;
  }

  static String quoteIdentifier(String identifier) {
    String value = Strings.requireNonBlank(identifier, "identifier");
    return "\"" + value.replace("\"", "\"\"") + "\"";
  }

  static String stripTrailingSemicolon(String sql) {
    String value = Strings.requireNonBlank(sql, "sql").trim();
    while (value.endsWith(";")) {
      value = value.substring(0, value.length() - 1).trim();
    }
    return value;
  }

  static String typeToken(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.type() == null) {
      return "UNKNOWN";
    }
    return definition.type().name();
  }

  static boolean isDuckdbActive(DefinitionDataset.DuckdbBinding binding) {
    if (binding == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String targetType = Strings.trimToNull(binding.targetType());
    return "DUCKDB_ACTIVE".equalsIgnoreCase(targetType);
  }

  static String resolveDuckDbActiveDatabasePath(DefinitionDataset.DuckdbBinding binding) {
    String configuredPath = Strings.trimToNull(binding.databasePath());
    if (Boolean.FALSE.equals(binding.memory())) {
      return Strings.requireNonBlank(configuredPath, "DUCKDB_ACTIVE databasePath is required");
    }
    if (configuredPath != null) {
      return configuredPath;
    }
    Path defaultPath =
        Path.of("data", "lite", "duckdb-active", sanitizeIdentifier(binding.relationName()) + ".duckdb")
            .toAbsolutePath()
            .normalize();
    try {
      Path parent = defaultPath.getParent();
      if (parent != null) {
        Files.createDirectories(parent);
      }
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to initialize DUCKDB_ACTIVE database directory for " + binding.relationName(),
          ex);
    }
    return defaultPath.toString();
  }

  static String parquetFromPath(
      String uri, String glob, String defaultParquetGlob, boolean hivePartitioning) {
    String base = normalizePathForDuckdb(Strings.requireNonBlank(uri, "parquetPath"));
    String resolvedGlob = Strings.trimToNull(glob);
    if (resolvedGlob == null) {
      resolvedGlob = defaultParquetGlob;
    }
    String parquetGlob = base.endsWith("/") ? base + resolvedGlob : base + "/" + resolvedGlob;
    StringBuilder sql =
        new StringBuilder("read_parquet('").append(escapeSqlLiteral(parquetGlob)).append("'");
    if (hivePartitioning) {
      sql.append(", hive_partitioning=true");
    }
    return sql.append(")").toString();
  }

  static String normalizePathForDuckdb(String value) {
    if (isS3Uri(value)) {
      String normalized = value;
      if (normalized.regionMatches(true, 0, "s3a://", 0, 6)) {
        normalized = "s3://" + normalized.substring(6);
      }
      return trimTrailingSlash(normalized);
    }
    return Path.of(value).normalize().toString().replace('\\', '/');
  }

  static boolean isS3Uri(String value) {
    return value.regionMatches(true, 0, "s3://", 0, 5)
        || value.regionMatches(true, 0, "s3a://", 0, 6);
  }

  static String trimTrailingSlash(String value) {
    int end = value.length();
    while (end > 0 && value.charAt(end - 1) == '/') {
      end--;
    }
    return end == value.length() ? value : value.substring(0, end);
  }

  static String escapeSqlLiteral(String value) {
    return value.replace("'", "''");
  }

  static boolean isMissingParquetFilesError(IllegalStateException ex) {
    String message = ex == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(ex.getMessage());
    if (message == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String lower = message.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return lower.contains("no files found that match the pattern");
  }

  static boolean isMissingDuckdbRelationError(IllegalStateException ex) {
    String message = ex == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(ex.getMessage());
    if (message == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String lower = message.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return lower.contains("table with name") && lower.contains("does not exist");
  }

  static boolean isS3CredentialUnavailableError(IllegalStateException ex) {
    String root = Exceptions.rootMessageNullable(ex);
    if (root == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String lower = root.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return lower.contains("s3 credentials are encrypted but no kek was provided")
        || lower.contains("unable to decrypt s3 credential with provided kek");
  }

  static String qualifiedNameKey(String namespace, String name) {
    return (namespace + "." + name).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  static String qualifiedNameKey(String group, String namespace, String name) {
    return (group + "." + namespace + "." + name).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

public record DuckdbDatasetPrepareRequest(

    rowManager = Objects.requireNonNull(rowManager, "rowManager");

  public boolean isCatalogMode() {
    return mode == DuckdbDatasetPrepareMode.CATALOG;

FILE: DuckdbDatasetProviderDuckdb.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.catalog;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class DuckdbDatasetProviderDuckdb implements DuckdbDatasetProvider {
  @Override
  public String providerId() {
    return "duckdb";
  }

  @Override
  public boolean supports(DuckdbDatasetPrepareRequest request) {
    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = request.definition().binding();
    return binding != null && binding.duckdb() != null;
  }

  @Override
  public DuckdbPreparedDataset prepare(DuckdbDatasetPrepareRequest request) {
    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = request.definition().binding();
    DefinitionDataset.DuckdbBinding duckdbBinding = binding == null ? null : binding.duckdb();
    if (duckdbBinding == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "NO_DUCKDB_BINDING datasetId=" + request.canonicalDatasetId());
    }

    if (request.isQueryMode()) {
      request.rowManager().prepareDatasetForQuery(request.datasetId());
      return DuckdbPreparedDataset.noOp(request.datasetId(), request.relationName());
    }

    String installSql = catalogInstallSql(request.relationName(), duckdbBinding);
    DuckdbDatasetProviderSupport.execStatements(request.session(), installSql);
    return DuckdbPreparedDataset.installed(request.datasetId(), request.relationName(), null);
  }

  private static String catalogInstallSql(
      String relationName, DefinitionDataset.DuckdbBinding duckdbBinding) {
    String viewName = DuckdbCatalogImplRelation.quoteIdentifier(relationName);
    if (DuckdbCatalogImplRelation.isDuckdbActive(duckdbBinding)) {
      String relation =
          Strings.requireNonBlank(duckdbBinding.relationName(), "dataset.duckdb.relationName");
      if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(duckdbBinding.memory())) {
        return "create or replace view "
            + viewName
            + " as select * from "
            + DuckdbCatalogImplRelation.quoteIdentifier(relation);
      }
      String attachAlias = "active__" + DuckdbCatalogImplRelation.sanitizeIdentifier(relationName);
      String databasePath = DuckdbCatalogImplRelation.resolveDuckDbActiveDatabasePath(duckdbBinding);
      String attachSql =
          "attach if not exists '"
              + DuckdbCatalogImplRelation.escapeSqlLiteral(databasePath.replace('\\', '/'))
              + "' as "
              + DuckdbCatalogImplRelation.quoteIdentifier(attachAlias);
      String createSql =
          "create or replace view "
              + viewName
              + " as select * from "
              + DuckdbCatalogImplRelation.quoteIdentifier(attachAlias)
              + "."
              + DuckdbCatalogImplRelation.quoteIdentifier(relation);
      return attachSql + ";\n" + createSql;
    }
    String relation =
        Strings.requireNonBlank(duckdbBinding.relationName(), "dataset.duckdb.relationName");
    return "create or replace view " + viewName + " as select * from " + relation;
  }
}



FILE: DuckdbDatasetProviderOdbc.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.catalog;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.duckdb.OdbcRuntimeGuard;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.duckdb.OdbcSessionSupport;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class DuckdbDatasetProviderOdbc implements DuckdbDatasetProvider {
  @Override
  public String providerId() {
    return "odbc";
  }

  @Override
  public boolean supports(DuckdbDatasetPrepareRequest request) {
    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = request.definition().binding();
    if (binding == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if (binding.odbc() != null) {
      return true;
    }
    DefinitionDataset.ExternalBinding external = binding.external();
    return external != null && OdbcRuntimeGuard.isOdbcType(external.externalType());
  }

  @Override
  public DuckdbPreparedDataset prepare(DuckdbDatasetPrepareRequest request) {
    if (request.isCatalogMode()) {
      return DuckdbPreparedDataset.noOp(request.datasetId(), request.relationName());
    }
    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = request.definition().binding();
    DefinitionDataset.OdbcBinding odbc = binding == null ? null : binding.odbc();
    if (odbc == null) {
      DefinitionDataset.ExternalBinding external = binding == null ? null : binding.external();
      String reference = external == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(external.reference());
      throw OdbcSessionSupport.queryFailed(
          request.canonicalDatasetId(),
          reference,
          null,
          "missing_dataset_odbc_binding",
          null);
    }
    OdbcSessionSupport.OdbcHandle handle =
        OdbcSessionSupport.installDatasetView(
            request.session(), request.discoveryCache(), request.datasetId(), odbc);
    return DuckdbPreparedDataset.installed(request.datasetId(), request.relationName(), handle);
  }
}



FILE: DuckdbDatasetProviderParquet.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.catalog;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class DuckdbDatasetProviderParquet implements DuckdbDatasetProvider {
  private static final String DEFAULT_PARQUET_GLOB = "**/*.parquet";

  @Override
  public String providerId() {
    return "parquet";
  }

  @Override
  public boolean supports(DuckdbDatasetPrepareRequest request) {
    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = request.definition().binding();
    return binding != null && binding.parquet() != null;
  }

  @Override
  public DuckdbPreparedDataset prepare(DuckdbDatasetPrepareRequest request) {
    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = request.definition().binding();
    DefinitionDataset.ParquetBinding parquet = binding == null ? null : binding.parquet();
    if (parquet == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "NO_PARQUET_BINDING datasetId=" + request.canonicalDatasetId());
    }
    String uri = Strings.requireNonBlank(parquet.uri(), "dataset.parquet.uri");
    String connectionName = Strings.trimToNull(parquet.connectionName());
    boolean s3 = DuckdbCatalogImplRelation.isS3Uri(uri);

    if (s3) {
      if (request.isQueryMode()) {
        if (connectionName == null || connectionName.isBlank()) {
          throw new IllegalStateException(
              "Dataset PARQUET S3 connectionName is required: " + request.canonicalDatasetId());
        }
      }
      if (connectionName != null) {
        request
            .rowManager()
            .ensureS3ConfiguredForCatalogInstall(
                request.session(), connectionName, request.canonicalDatasetId());
      }
    }

    if (request.isQueryMode()) {
      return DuckdbPreparedDataset.noOp(request.datasetId(), request.relationName());
    }

    String parquetExpression =
        DuckdbCatalogImplRelation.parquetFromPath(
            uri,
            parquet.glob(),
            DEFAULT_PARQUET_GLOB,
            Boolean.TRUE.equals(parquet.hivePartitioning()));
    String sql =
        "create or replace view "
            + DuckdbCatalogImplRelation.quoteIdentifier(request.relationName())
            + " as select * from "
            + parquetExpression;
    DuckdbDatasetProviderSupport.execStatements(request.session(), sql);
    return DuckdbPreparedDataset.installed(request.datasetId(), request.relationName(), null);
  }
}


FILE: DuckdbDatasetProviderRegistry.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.catalog;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.stream.Collectors;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionDataset;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class DuckdbDatasetProviderRegistry {
  private final List<DuckdbDatasetProvider> providers;

  public DuckdbDatasetProviderRegistry(List<DuckdbDatasetProvider> providers) {
    if (providers == null || providers.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("providers is required");
    }
    List<DuckdbDatasetProvider> ordered = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DuckdbDatasetProvider provider : providers) {
      ordered.add(Objects.requireNonNull(provider, "provider"));
    }
    this.providers = List.copyOf(ordered);
  }

  public static DuckdbDatasetProviderRegistry defaults() {
    return new DuckdbDatasetProviderRegistry(
        List.of(
            new DuckdbDatasetProviderOdbc(),
            new DuckdbDatasetProviderParquet(),
            new DuckdbDatasetProviderDuckdb()));
  }

  public DuckdbPreparedDataset prepare(DuckdbDatasetPrepareRequest request) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(request, "request");
    List<DuckdbDatasetProvider> matches = new ArrayList<>();
    for (DuckdbDatasetProvider provider : providers) {
      if (provider.supports(request)) {
        matches.add(provider);
      }
    }
    if (matches.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "NO_DUCKDB_DATASET_PROVIDER datasetId="
              + request.canonicalDatasetId()
              + " bindingType="
              + bindingType(request.definition()));
    }
    if (matches.size() > 1) {
      List<String> providerIds =
          matches.stream()
              .map(DuckdbDatasetProvider::providerId)
              .sorted(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
              .collect(Collectors.toList());
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "AMBIGUOUS_DUCKDB_DATASET_PROVIDER datasetId="
              + request.canonicalDatasetId()
              + " providers="
              + providerIds);
    }
    DuckdbPreparedDataset prepared = matches.get(0).prepare(request);
    if (prepared == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "DUCKDB_DATASET_PROVIDER_RETURNED_NULL datasetId="
              + request.canonicalDatasetId()
              + " provider="
              + matches.get(0).providerId());
    }
    return prepared;
  }

  private static String bindingType(DefinitionDataset definition) {
    if (definition == null || definition.binding() == null) {
      return "UNKNOWN";
    }
    DefinitionDataset.Binding binding = definition.binding();
    if (binding.odbc() != null) {
      return "EXTERNAL/ODBC";
    }
    if (binding.external() != null) {
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(
          Strings.trimToNull(binding.external().externalType()), "EXTERNAL");
    }
    if (binding.parquet() != null) {
      return "PARQUET";
    }
    if (binding.duckdb() != null) {
      return "DUCKDB";
    }
    return definition.type() == null ? "UNKNOWN" : definition.type().name();
  }

  public List<String> providerIds() {
    List<String> ids =
        providers.stream()
            .map(DuckdbDatasetProvider::providerId)
            .sorted(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER.thenComparing(Comparator.naturalOrder()))
            .collect(Collectors.toList());
    return List.copyOf(ids);
  }
}


FILE: DuckdbDatasetProviderSupport.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.catalog;

import java.sql.SQLException;
import java.sql.Statement;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.duckdb.DuckdbSession;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class DuckdbDatasetProviderSupport {
  private DuckdbDatasetProviderSupport() {}

  static void execStatements(DuckdbSession session, String sql) {
    if (sql == null || sql.isBlank()) {
      return;
    }
    String[] statements = sql.split(";\\s*\\n|;\\s*$|;\\s*");
    for (String statementSql : statements) {
      String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(statementSql);
      if (trimmed == null) {
        continue;
      }
      try (Statement statement = session.createStatement()) {
        statement.execute(trimmed);
      } catch (SQLException ex) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("DuckDB SQL failed: " + ex.getMessage(), ex);
      }
    }
  }
}



FILE: DuckdbPreparedDataset.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.catalog;

import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.dataset.DatasetId;

public final class DuckdbPreparedDataset implements AutoCloseable {
  private final DatasetId datasetId;
  private final String relationName;
  private final boolean installed;
  private final AutoCloseable cleanup;

  private DuckdbPreparedDataset(
      DatasetId datasetId, String relationName, boolean installed, AutoCloseable cleanup) {
    this.datasetId = Objects.requireNonNull(datasetId, "datasetId");
    this.relationName = Objects.requireNonNull(relationName, "relationName");
    this.installed = installed;
    this.cleanup = cleanup;
  }

  public static DuckdbPreparedDataset installed(
      DatasetId datasetId, String relationName, AutoCloseable cleanup) {
    return new DuckdbPreparedDataset(datasetId, relationName, true, cleanup);
  }

  public static DuckdbPreparedDataset noOp(DatasetId datasetId, String relationName) {
    return new DuckdbPreparedDataset(datasetId, relationName, false, null);
  }

  public DatasetId datasetId() {
    return datasetId;
  }

  public String relationName() {
    return relationName;
  }

  public boolean installed() {
    return installed;
  }

  @Override
  public void close() throws Exception {
    if (cleanup != null) {
      cleanup.close();
    }
  }

  public static void closeQuietly(DuckdbPreparedDataset prepared) {
    if (prepared == null) {
      return;
    }
    try {
      prepared.close();
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
      // best-effort cleanup only
    }
  }
}

FILE: CheckpointKey.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.checkpoints;

import java.util.Locale;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public record CheckpointKey(String group, CheckpointType type, String name, String scope) {
  public CheckpointKey {
    group = Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "checkpoint.group");
    type = type == null ? CheckpointType.INGEST : type;
    name = Strings.requireNonBlank(name, "checkpoint.name");
    scope = Strings.requireNonBlank(scope, "checkpoint.scope");
  }

  public String normalizedGroup() {
    return normalizeToken(group);
  }

  public String normalizedType() {
    return type.name().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  public String normalizedName() {
    return normalizeToken(name);
  }

  public String normalizedScope() {
    return normalizeToken(scope);
  }

  public static String normalizeToken(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.requireNonBlank(value, "value").trim();
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder(normalized.length());
    for (int i = 0; i < normalized.length(); i++) {
      char current = normalized.charAt(i);
      if (Character.isLetterOrDigit(current) || current == '-' || current == '_' || current == '.') {
        builder.append(Character.toLowerCase(current));
      } else {
        builder.append('_');
      }
    }
    return builder.toString();
  }
}



FILE: CheckpointRecord.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.checkpoints;

import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.TreeMap;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public record CheckpointRecord(CheckpointKey key, Map<String, String> payload, String lastUpdatedUtc) {
  public CheckpointRecord {
    key = Objects.requireNonNull(key, "key");
    payload = normalizePayload(payload);
    lastUpdatedUtc = Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(lastUpdatedUtc), Instant.now().toString());
  }

  public static CheckpointRecord of(CheckpointKey key, Map<String, String> payload) {
    return new CheckpointRecord(key, payload, Instant.now().toString());
  }

  private static Map<String, String> normalizePayload(Map<String, String> source) {
    if (source == null || source.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    TreeMap<String, String> sorted = new TreeMap<>(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : source.entrySet()) {
      if (entry == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      String value = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue());
      if (key != null && value != null) {
        sorted.put(key, value);
      }
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> ordered = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : sorted.entrySet()) {
      ordered.put(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue());
    }
    return ordered.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(ordered);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.checkpoints;

import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Optional;

public interface CheckpointStore {
  Optional<CheckpointRecord> load(CheckpointKey key);

  void save(CheckpointRecord record);

  default void save(CheckpointKey key, Map<String, String> payload) {
    save(CheckpointRecord.of(key, payload));
  }

  void delete(CheckpointKey key);
}



FILE: CheckpointStoreLocal.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.checkpoints;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.nio.file.StandardCopyOption;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;

public final class CheckpointStoreLocal implements CheckpointStore {
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER = DiscoveryCodec.mapper();

  private final Path root;

  public CheckpointStoreLocal(Path root) {
    this.root = Objects.requireNonNull(root, "root").toAbsolutePath().normalize();
  }

  public Path root() {
    return root;
  }

  public Path resolvePath(CheckpointKey key) {
    CheckpointKey resolved = Objects.requireNonNull(key, "key");
    return root
        .resolve(resolved.normalizedGroup())
        .resolve(resolved.normalizedType())
        .resolve(resolved.normalizedName())
        .resolve(resolved.normalizedScope() + ".json");
  }

  @Override
  public Optional<CheckpointRecord> load(CheckpointKey key) {
    Path path = resolvePath(key);
    if (!Files.exists(path)) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    try {
      byte[] bytes = Files.readAllBytes(path);
      if (bytes.length == 0) {
        return Optional.empty();
      }
      CheckpointRecord record = MAPPER.readValue(bytes, CheckpointRecord.class);
      return Optional.of(record);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to load checkpoint file: " + path, ex);
    }
  }

  @Override
  public void save(CheckpointRecord record) {
    CheckpointRecord resolved = Objects.requireNonNull(record, "record");
    Path path = resolvePath(resolved.key());
    Path parent = path.getParent();
    if (parent == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Checkpoint path parent is missing: " + path);
    }
    try {
      Files.createDirectories(parent);
      byte[] payload = MAPPER.writeValueAsString(resolved).getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
      Path temp = parent.resolve(path.getFileName().toString() + ".tmp");
      Files.write(temp, payload);
      Files.move(temp, path, StandardCopyOption.REPLACE_EXISTING, StandardCopyOption.ATOMIC_MOVE);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to save checkpoint file: " + path, ex);
    }
  }

  @Override
  public void delete(CheckpointKey key) {
    Path path = resolvePath(key);
    try {
      Files.deleteIfExists(path);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to delete checkpoint file: " + path, ex);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.checkpoints;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class CheckpointStores {
  private CheckpointStores() {}

  public static CheckpointStoreLocal local(Path root) {
    return new CheckpointStoreLocal(Objects.requireNonNull(root, "root"));
  }

  public static CheckpointStore failFast(String reason) {
    String message =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            Strings.trimToNull(reason),
            "Checkpoint store is not configured. Configure session builder with withCheckpointPath(...)");
    return new CheckpointStore() {
      @Override
      public Optional<CheckpointRecord> load(CheckpointKey key) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(message);
      }

      @Override
      public void save(CheckpointRecord record) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(message);
      }

      @Override
      public void save(CheckpointKey key, Map<String, String> payload) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(message);
      }

      @Override
      public void delete(CheckpointKey key) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(message);
      }
    };
  }

  public static CheckpointStore noOp() {
    return noOp(null);
  }

  public static CheckpointStore noOp(String reason) {
    return new CheckpointStore() {
      @Override
      public Optional<CheckpointRecord> load(CheckpointKey key) {
        return Optional.empty();
      }

      @Override
      public void save(CheckpointRecord record) {
        // checkpoints disabled
      }

      @Override
      public void save(CheckpointKey key, Map<String, String> payload) {
        // checkpoints disabled
      }

      @Override
      public void delete(CheckpointKey key) {
        // checkpoints disabled
      }

      @Override
      public String toString() {
        String normalizedReason = Strings.trimToNull(reason);
        return normalizedReason == null ? "CheckpointStore.noOp" : "CheckpointStore.noOp(" + normalizedReason + ")";
      }
    };
  }
}



FILE: CheckpointType.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.checkpoints;

public enum CheckpointType {
  INGEST,
  VIEW,
  PARQUET_MAINT,
  STREAM
}
