package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest;

import java.util.function.BiFunction;
import java.util.function.UnaryOperator;

@FunctionalInterface
public interface IngestTransformer {
  String transform(String payloadText, Integer ampsCommand);

  default String transform(String payloadText) {
    return transform(payloadText, null);
  }

  default UnaryOperator<String> asPayloadTransformer() {
    return this::transform;
  }

  default BiFunction<String, Integer, String> asPayloadTransformerWithCommand() {
    return this::transform;
  }
}


FILE: SchemaRecord.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest;

import java.lang.reflect.ParameterizedType;
import java.lang.reflect.RecordComponent;
import java.lang.reflect.Type;
import java.math.BigDecimal;
import java.math.BigInteger;
import java.net.URI;
import java.net.URL;
import java.nio.ByteBuffer;
import java.sql.Timestamp;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.LocalDate;
import java.time.LocalDateTime;
import java.time.OffsetDateTime;
import java.time.ZonedDateTime;
import java.util.ArrayDeque;
import java.util.Collection;
import java.util.Date;
import java.util.Deque;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import java.util.UUID;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class SchemaRecord {
  private SchemaRecord() {}

  public static SchemaModel fromRecord(Class<?> recordType) {
    return fromRecord(recordType, Options.builder().build());
  }

  public static SchemaModel fromRecord(Class<?> recordType, Options options) {
    Class<?> resolvedRecordType = Objects.requireNonNull(recordType, "recordType");
    if (!resolvedRecordType.isRecord()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("recordType must be a Java record: " + resolvedRecordType.getName());
    }
    Options resolvedOptions = options == null ? Options.builder().build() : options;
    String schemaName =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(resolvedOptions.name(), toKebabCase(resolvedRecordType.getSimpleName()));
    SchemaModel.Builder builder =
        SchemaModel.builder().withGroup(Strings.trimToNull(resolvedOptions.group())).withName(schemaName).withType(SchemaType.TABULAR);
    appendRecord(
        builder,
        resolvedRecordType,
        null,
        false,
        resolvedOptions,
        new ArrayDeque<>());
    if (resolvedOptions.includeAmpsCommand()) {
      builder.withField("amps_command", SchemaModel.FieldType.STRING, true);
    }
    if (resolvedOptions.includeRecordClassName()) {
      builder.withField("record_class", SchemaModel.FieldType.STRING, true);
    }
    if (resolvedOptions.includePayloadJson()) {
      builder.withField("payload_json", SchemaModel.FieldType.STRING, true);
    }
    return builder.build();
  }

  private static void appendRecord(
      SchemaModel.Builder builder,
      Class<?> recordType,
      String prefix,
      boolean parentNullable,
      Options options,
      Deque<Class<?>> stack) {
    if (stack.contains(recordType)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Cyclic record reference is not supported: " + recordType.getName());
    }
    stack.push(recordType);
    try {
      for (RecordComponent component : recordType.getRecordComponents()) {
        Type declaredType = component.getGenericType();
        Type effectiveType = unwrapOptional(declaredType);
        Class<?> rawType = rawClass(effectiveType);
        if (rawType == null) {
          addField(builder, fieldName(prefix, component.getName(), options), SchemaModel.FieldType.STRING, true);
          continue;
        }

        boolean nullable =
            parentNullable || !component.getType().isPrimitive() || isOptional(declaredType);
        String currentFieldName = fieldName(prefix, component.getName(), options);

        if (rawType.isRecord()) {
          if (options.skipNestedClasses()) {
            continue;
          }
          if (options.nestingMode() == NestingMode.FLATTEN) {
            appendRecord(builder, rawType, currentFieldName, true, options, stack);
          } else {
            addField(builder, jsonFieldName(currentFieldName, options), SchemaModel.FieldType.STRING, nullable);
          }
          continue;
        }

        if (isCollectionLike(rawType) || rawType.isArray()) {
          if (options.skipNestedClasses()) {
            continue;
          }
          addField(builder, jsonFieldName(currentFieldName, options), SchemaModel.FieldType.STRING, true);
          continue;
        }

        addField(builder, currentFieldName, mapFieldType(rawType), nullable);
      }
    } finally {
      stack.pop();
    }
  }

  private static void addField(
      SchemaModel.Builder builder, String name, SchemaModel.FieldType type, boolean nullable) {
    builder.withField(name, type, nullable);
  }

  private static String fieldName(String prefix, String componentName, Options options) {
    String base = options.snakeCaseNames() ? toSnakeCase(componentName) : componentName;
    if (Strings.isBlank(prefix)) {
      return base;
    }
    return prefix + options.flattenSeparator() + base;
  }

  private static String jsonFieldName(String baseName, Options options) {
    if (!options.appendJsonSuffixForNested()) {
      return baseName;
    }
    if (baseName.endsWith("_json")) {
      return baseName;
    }
    return baseName + "_json";
  }

  private static SchemaModel.FieldType mapFieldType(Class<?> type) {
    if (type == String.class
        || CharSequence.class.isAssignableFrom(type)
        || type == UUID.class
        || type == URI.class
        || type == URL.class
        || type.isEnum()) {
      return SchemaModel.FieldType.STRING;
    }
    if (type == boolean.class || type == Boolean.class) {
      return SchemaModel.FieldType.BOOL;
    }
    if (type == byte.class
        || type == Byte.class
        || type == short.class
        || type == Short.class
        || type == int.class
        || type == Integer.class) {
      return SchemaModel.FieldType.INT32;
    }
    if (type == long.class || type == Long.class || type == BigInteger.class) {
      return SchemaModel.FieldType.INT64;
    }
    if (type == float.class
        || type == Float.class
        || type == double.class
        || type == Double.class
        || type == BigDecimal.class) {
      return SchemaModel.FieldType.FLOAT64;
    }
    if (type == LocalDate.class || type == java.sql.Date.class) {
      return SchemaModel.FieldType.DATE;
    }
    if (type == Instant.class
        || type == Date.class
        || type == Timestamp.class
        || type == LocalDateTime.class
        || type == OffsetDateTime.class
        || type == ZonedDateTime.class) {
      return SchemaModel.FieldType.TIMESTAMP;
    }
    if (type == byte[].class || type == ByteBuffer.class) {
      return SchemaModel.FieldType.BINARY;
    }
    return SchemaModel.FieldType.STRING;
  }

  private static boolean isCollectionLike(Class<?> rawType) {
    return Collection.class.isAssignableFrom(rawType) || Map.class.isAssignableFrom(rawType);
  }

  private static boolean isOptional(Type type) {
    Class<?> raw = rawClass(type);
    return raw == Optional.class;
  }

  private static Type unwrapOptional(Type type) {
    if (!(type instanceof ParameterizedType parameterizedType)) {
      return type;
    }
    if (!(parameterizedType.getRawType() instanceof Class<?> rawType) || rawType != Optional.class) {
      return type;
    }
    Type[] args = parameterizedType.getActualTypeArguments();
    return args.length == 1 ? args[0] : Object.class;
  }

  private static Class<?> rawClass(Type type) {
    if (type instanceof Class<?> clazz) {
      return clazz;
    }
    if (type instanceof ParameterizedType parameterizedType) {
      Type raw = parameterizedType.getRawType();
      return raw instanceof Class<?> rawClass ? rawClass : null;
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String toSnakeCase(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.requireNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(value), "value");
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder(normalized.length() + 8);
    for (int index = 0; index < normalized.length(); index++) {
      char ch = normalized.charAt(index);
      if (Character.isUpperCase(ch)) {
        if (index > 0) {
          builder.append('_');
        }
        builder.append(Character.toLowerCase(ch));
      } else if (Character.isLetterOrDigit(ch)) {
        builder.append(Character.toLowerCase(ch));
      } else {
        builder.append('_');
      }
    }
    return builder.toString();
  }

  private static String toKebabCase(String value) {
    return toSnakeCase(value).replace('_', '-').toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }

  public enum NestingMode {
    JSON,
    FLATTEN
  }

  public static final class Options {
    private final String group;
    private final String name;
    private final NestingMode nestingMode;
    private final String flattenSeparator;
    private final boolean snakeCaseNames;
    private final boolean appendJsonSuffixForNested;
    private final boolean includeAmpsCommand;
    private final boolean includeRecordClassName;
    private final boolean includePayloadJson;
    private final boolean skipNestedClasses;

    private Options(Builder builder) {
      this.group = Strings.trimToNull(builder.group);
      this.name = Strings.trimToNull(builder.name);
      this.nestingMode = builder.nestingMode == null ? NestingMode.JSON : builder.nestingMode;
      this.flattenSeparator = Strings.firstNonBlank(builder.flattenSeparator, "_");
      this.snakeCaseNames = builder.snakeCaseNames;
      this.appendJsonSuffixForNested = builder.appendJsonSuffixForNested;
      this.includeAmpsCommand = builder.includeAmpsCommand;
      this.includeRecordClassName = builder.includeRecordClassName;
      this.includePayloadJson = builder.includePayloadJson;
      this.skipNestedClasses = builder.skipNestedClasses;
    }

    public static Builder builder() {
      return new Builder();
    }

    public String group() {
      return group;
    }

    public String name() {
      return name;
    }

    public NestingMode nestingMode() {
      return nestingMode;
    }

    public String flattenSeparator() {
      return flattenSeparator;
    }

    public boolean snakeCaseNames() {
      return snakeCaseNames;
    }

    public boolean appendJsonSuffixForNested() {
      return appendJsonSuffixForNested;
    }

    public boolean includePayloadJson() {
      return includePayloadJson;
    }

    public boolean includeAmpsCommand() {
      return includeAmpsCommand;
    }

    public boolean includeRecordClassName() {
      return includeRecordClassName;
    }

    public boolean skipNestedClasses() {
      return skipNestedClasses;
    }

    public static final class Builder {
      private String group;
      private String name;
      private NestingMode nestingMode = NestingMode.JSON;
      private String flattenSeparator = "_";
      private boolean snakeCaseNames = true;
      private boolean appendJsonSuffixForNested = true;
      private boolean includeAmpsCommand = false;
      private boolean includeRecordClassName = false;
      private boolean includePayloadJson = false;
      private boolean skipNestedClasses = false;

      private Builder() {}

      public Builder withGroup(String value) {
        this.group = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withName(String value) {
        this.name = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withNestingMode(NestingMode value) {
        this.nestingMode = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withFlattenSeparator(String value) {
        this.flattenSeparator = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withSnakeCaseNames(boolean value) {
        this.snakeCaseNames = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withAppendJsonSuffixForNested(boolean value) {
        this.appendJsonSuffixForNested = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withIncludePayloadJson(boolean value) {
        this.includePayloadJson = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withIncludeAmpsCommand(boolean value) {
        this.includeAmpsCommand = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withIncludeRecordClassName(boolean value) {
        this.includeRecordClassName = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withSkipNestedClasses(boolean value) {
        this.skipNestedClasses = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Options build() {
        return new Options(this);
      }
    }
  }
}


FILE: SchemaRecordTransformer.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest;

import com.crankuptheamps.client.Message;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Function;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class SchemaRecordTransformer implements IngestTransformer {
  private final ObjectMapper mapper;
  private final SchemaModel schema;
  private final Function<JsonNode, JsonNode> sourceSelector;
  private final String recordClassName;
  private final boolean skipSowReplay;

  private SchemaRecordTransformer(Builder builder) {
    this.mapper = Objects.requireNonNull(builder.mapper, "mapper");
    this.schema = builder.schema;
    this.sourceSelector = builder.sourceSelector == null ? Function.identity() : builder.sourceSelector;
    this.recordClassName = Strings.trimToNull(builder.recordClassName);
    this.skipSowReplay = builder.skipSowReplay;
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  @Override
  public String transform(String payloadText, Integer ampsCommand) {
    return transform(
        mapper,
        payloadText,
        ampsCommand,
        schema,
        sourceSelector,
        recordClassName,
        skipSowReplay);
  }

  public static String transform(
      ObjectMapper mapper,
      String payloadText,
      Integer ampsCommand,
      SchemaModel schema,
      boolean skipSowReplay) {
    return transform(
        mapper, payloadText, ampsCommand, schema, Function.identity(), null, skipSowReplay);
  }

  public static String transform(
      ObjectMapper mapper,
      String payloadText,
      Integer ampsCommand,
      SchemaModel schema,
      String recordClassName,
      boolean skipSowReplay) {
    return transform(
        mapper, payloadText, ampsCommand, schema, Function.identity(), recordClassName, skipSowReplay);
  }

  public static String transform(
      ObjectMapper mapper,
      String payloadText,
      Integer ampsCommand,
      SchemaModel schema,
      Function<JsonNode, JsonNode> sourceSelector,
      boolean skipSowReplay) {
    return transform(
        mapper, payloadText, ampsCommand, schema, sourceSelector, null, skipSowReplay);
  }

  public static String transform(
      ObjectMapper mapper,
      String payloadText,
      Integer ampsCommand,
      SchemaModel schema,
      Function<JsonNode, JsonNode> sourceSelector,
      String recordClassName,
      boolean skipSowReplay) {
    String payload = Strings.requireNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(payloadText), "payloadText");
    try {
      JsonNode root = mapper.readTree(payload);
      JsonNode source = sourceSelector == null ? root : sourceSelector.apply(root);
      return transform(
          mapper, root, source, payload, ampsCommand, schema, recordClassName, skipSowReplay);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to transform ingest payload: " + Strings.firstNonBlank(ex.getMessage(), "unknown"),
          ex);
    }
  }

  public static String transform(
      ObjectMapper mapper,
      JsonNode root,
      JsonNode source,
      String payloadText,
      Integer ampsCommand,
      SchemaModel schema,
      boolean skipSowReplay) {
    return transform(mapper, root, source, payloadText, ampsCommand, schema, null, skipSowReplay);
  }

  public static String transform(
      ObjectMapper mapper,
      JsonNode root,
      JsonNode source,
      String payloadText,
      Integer ampsCommand,
      SchemaModel schema,
      String recordClassName,
      boolean skipSowReplay) {
    String payload = Strings.requireNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(payloadText), "payloadText");
    String command = normalizedAmpsCommand(ampsCommand);
    if (skipSowReplay && "SOW".equals(command)) {
      return null;
    }
    ObjectNode row = mapper.createObjectNode();
    JsonNode resolvedSource = source == null || source.isMissingNode() ? root : source;
    if (schema != null && schema.getFields() != null) {
      for (SchemaModel.Field field : schema.getFields()) {
        if (field == null || Strings.isBlank(field.getName())) {
          continue;
        }
        String name = field.getName();
        if ("amps_command".equals(name)) {
          row.put(name, command);
          continue;
        }
        if ("record_class".equals(name)) {
          String normalizedRecordClass = Strings.trimToNull(recordClassName);
          if (normalizedRecordClass != null) {
            row.put(name, normalizedRecordClass);
          }
          continue;
        }
        if ("payload_json".equals(name)) {
          row.put(name, payload);
          continue;
        }
        if (name.endsWith("_json")) {
          JsonNode value = findValue(resolvedSource, name.substring(0, name.length() - 5));
          if (value != null && !value.isNull()) {
            row.put(name, value.toString());
          }
          continue;
        }
        JsonNode value = findValue(resolvedSource, name);
        if (value == null || value.isNull()) {
          continue;
        }
        if (value.isContainerNode()) {
          row.put(name, value.toString());
        } else {
          row.set(name, value);
        }
      }
    } else {
      appendAllFields(row, resolvedSource);
    }
    if (!row.has("amps_command")) {
      row.put("amps_command", command);
    }
    if (!row.has("record_class")) {
      String normalizedRecordClass = Strings.trimToNull(recordClassName);
      if (normalizedRecordClass != null) {
        row.put("record_class", normalizedRecordClass);
      }
    }
    if (!row.has("payload_json")) {
      row.put("payload_json", payload);
    }
    try {
      return mapper.writeValueAsString(row);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to encode ingest row payload: " + Strings.firstNonBlank(ex.getMessage(), "unknown"),
          ex);
    }
  }

  private static void appendAllFields(ObjectNode row, JsonNode source) {
    if (row == null || source == null || source.isMissingNode() || !source.isObject()) {
      return;
    }
    var fields = source.fields();
    while (fields.hasNext()) {
      var entry = fields.next();
      String name = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      JsonNode value = entry.getValue();
      if (name == null || value == null || value.isNull()) {
        continue;
      }
      if (value.isContainerNode()) {
        row.put(name + "_json", value.toString());
      } else {
        row.set(name, value);
      }
    }
  }

  public static String normalizedAmpsCommand(Integer ampsCommand) {
    int command = ampsCommand == null ? Message.Command.Publish : ampsCommand.intValue();
    return switch (command) {
      case Message.Command.SOW -> "SOW";
      case Message.Command.OOF, Message.Command.SOWDelete -> "OOF";
      default -> "UPDATE";
    };
  }

  private static JsonNode findValue(JsonNode source, String fieldName) {
    if (source == null || source.isMissingNode() || Strings.isBlank(fieldName)) {
      return null;
    }
    JsonNode direct = source.get(fieldName);
    if (direct != null) {
      return direct;
    }
    String camel = toCamelCase(fieldName);
    if (!fieldName.equals(camel)) {
      JsonNode camelNode = source.get(camel);
      if (camelNode != null) {
        return camelNode;
      }
    }
    String snake = toSnakeCase(fieldName);
    if (!fieldName.equals(snake)) {
      JsonNode snakeNode = source.get(snake);
      if (snakeNode != null) {
        return snakeNode;
      }
    }
    var it = source.fields();
    while (it.hasNext()) {
      var entry = it.next();
      if (entry.getKey() != null && entry.getKey().equalsIgnoreCase(fieldName)) {
        return entry.getValue();
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static String toCamelCase(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null || normalized.indexOf('_') < 0) {
      return Strings.firstNonBlank(normalized, value);
    }
    String[] parts = normalized.split("_");
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder(normalized.length());
    for (int i = 0; i < parts.length; i++) {
      if (parts[i].isEmpty()) {
        continue;
      }
      if (i == 0) {
        builder.append(parts[i].toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
      } else {
        builder.append(parts[i].substring(0, 1).toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT));
        if (parts[i].length() > 1) {
          builder.append(parts[i].substring(1));
        }
      }
    }
    return builder.toString();
  }

  private static String toSnakeCase(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return value;
    }
    StringBuilder builder = new StringBuilder(normalized.length() + 8);
    for (int index = 0; index < normalized.length(); index++) {
      char ch = normalized.charAt(index);
      if (Character.isUpperCase(ch)) {
        if (index > 0) {
          builder.append('_');
        }
        builder.append(Character.toLowerCase(ch));
      } else if (Character.isLetterOrDigit(ch)) {
        builder.append(Character.toLowerCase(ch));
      } else {
        builder.append('_');
      }
    }
    return builder.toString();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private ObjectMapper mapper;
    private SchemaModel schema;
    private Function<JsonNode, JsonNode> sourceSelector;
    private String recordClassName;
    private boolean skipSowReplay;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withMapper(ObjectMapper value) {
      mapper = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSchema(SchemaModel value) {
      schema = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSourceSelector(Function<JsonNode, JsonNode> value) {
      sourceSelector = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRecordClassName(String value) {
      recordClassName = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSkipSowReplay(boolean value) {
      skipSowReplay = value;
      return this;
    }

    public SchemaRecordTransformer build() {
      return new SchemaRecordTransformer(this);
    }
  }
}


FILE: SchemaSampleOptions.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest;

import java.util.Locale;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.amps.AmpsConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format.FormatDecoderJson;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestFormat;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public record SchemaSampleOptions(
    String jsonRootField,
    String jsonMode,
    String nvFixPairDelimiter,
    String nvFixKvDelimiter,
    Boolean nvFixTrimKeys,
    Boolean nvFixTrimValues,
    Integer maxSamples,
    Integer maxBytes,
    IngestFormat format,
    String connectionName,
    String topic,
    String ampsOptions,
    String ampsFilter,
    Boolean ampsSow,
    Long ampsWaitMillis) {
  public static final int DEFAULT_MAX_SAMPLES = 50;
  public static final int DEFAULT_MAX_BYTES = 1_048_576;
  public static final long DEFAULT_AMPS_WAIT_MILLIS = 30_000L;

  public SchemaSampleOptions(
      String jsonRootField,
      String jsonMode,
      String nvFixPairDelimiter,
      String nvFixKvDelimiter,
      Boolean nvFixTrimKeys,
      Boolean nvFixTrimValues,
      Integer maxSamples,
      Integer maxBytes) {
    this(
        jsonRootField,
        jsonMode,
        nvFixPairDelimiter,
        nvFixKvDelimiter,
        nvFixTrimKeys,
        nvFixTrimValues,
        maxSamples,
        maxBytes,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null);
  }

  public SchemaSampleOptions {
    jsonRootField = Strings.trimToNull(jsonRootField);
    String resolvedJsonMode =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(jsonMode), FormatDecoderJson.MODE_OBJECT_PER_MESSAGE);
    resolvedJsonMode = resolvedJsonMode.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if (!FormatDecoderJson.MODE_OBJECT_PER_MESSAGE.equals(resolvedJsonMode)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported JSON mode: " + resolvedJsonMode);
    }
    jsonMode = resolvedJsonMode;

    String resolvedPairDelimiter = Strings.trimToNull(nvFixPairDelimiter);
    nvFixPairDelimiter =
        resolvedPairDelimiter == null ? String.valueOf(AmpsConnection.SOH) : resolvedPairDelimiter;

    String resolvedKvDelimiter = Strings.trimToNull(nvFixKvDelimiter);
    if (resolvedKvDelimiter == null) {
      resolvedKvDelimiter = "=";
    }
    if (resolvedKvDelimiter.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("nvFixKvDelimiter must not be empty");
    }
    nvFixKvDelimiter = resolvedKvDelimiter;

    nvFixTrimKeys = nvFixTrimKeys == null || nvFixTrimKeys;
    nvFixTrimValues = nvFixTrimValues == null || nvFixTrimValues;
    maxSamples = maxSamples == null || maxSamples <= 0 ? DEFAULT_MAX_SAMPLES : maxSamples;
    maxBytes = maxBytes == null || maxBytes <= 0 ? DEFAULT_MAX_BYTES : maxBytes;

    connectionName = Strings.trimToNull(connectionName);
    topic = Strings.trimToNull(topic);
    ampsOptions = Strings.trimToNull(ampsOptions);
    ampsFilter = Strings.trimToNull(ampsFilter);
    ampsSow = ampsSow == null || ampsSow;
    ampsWaitMillis =
        ampsWaitMillis == null || ampsWaitMillis <= 0L ? DEFAULT_AMPS_WAIT_MILLIS : ampsWaitMillis;
  }

  public static SchemaSampleOptions defaults() {
    return new SchemaSampleOptions(
        null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null);
  }

  public static SchemaSampleOptions json(String rootField) {
    return new SchemaSampleOptions(
        rootField, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null);
  }

  public static SchemaSampleOptions nvfix(
      String pairDelimiter, String kvDelimiter, Boolean trimKeys, Boolean trimValues) {
    return new SchemaSampleOptions(
        null, null, pairDelimiter, kvDelimiter, trimKeys, trimValues, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null, null);
  }

  public static SchemaSampleOptions forAmps(
      String connectionName, String topic, IngestFormat format) {
    return defaults().withFormat(format).withConnectionName(connectionName).withTopic(topic);
  }

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest;

import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model.IngestFormat;

public record SchemaSampleRequest(
    IngestFormat format,
    Iterable<String> samples,
    SchemaSampleOptions options) {
  public SchemaSampleRequest {
    format = Objects.requireNonNull(format, "format");
    samples = Objects.requireNonNull(samples, "samples");
    options = options == null ? SchemaSampleOptions.defaults() : options;
  }

  public static SchemaSampleRequest of(IngestFormat format, Iterable<String> samples) {
    return new SchemaSampleRequest(format, samples, SchemaSampleOptions.defaults());
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model;

import java.util.Locale;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public enum IngestFormat {
  JSON,
  NVFIX;

  public static IngestFormat fromToken(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.requireNonBlank(value, "format").toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    return switch (normalized) {
      case "JSON" -> JSON;
      case "NVFIX" -> NVFIX;
      default -> throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported ingest format: " + value);
    };
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ingest.model;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class IngestModel {
  private static final String DEFAULT_NAMESPACE = "default";

  private final String name;
  private final String namespace;
  private final String uuid;
  private final boolean enabled;
  private final String lifecycleStatus;
  private final IngestSchemaMode schemaMode;
  private final SchemaModel schema;
  private final IngestSourceModel source;
  private final IngestTargetModel target;
  private final String datasetId;

  private IngestModel(Builder builder) {
    this.name = builder.name;
    this.namespace = builder.namespace;
    this.uuid = builder.uuid;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
    this.lifecycleStatus = builder.lifecycleStatus;
    this.schemaMode = builder.schemaMode;
    this.schema = builder.schema;
    this.source = builder.source;
    this.target = builder.target;
    this.datasetId = builder.datasetId;
  }

  public String name() {
    return name;
  }

  public String namespace() {
    return namespace;
  }

  public String uuid() {
    return uuid;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  public String lifecycleStatus() {
    return lifecycleStatus;
  }

  public IngestSchemaMode schemaMode() {
    return schemaMode;
  }

  public SchemaModel schema() {
    return schema;
  }

  public IngestSourceModel source() {
    return source;
  }

  public IngestTargetModel target() {
    return target;
  }

  public String datasetId() {
    return datasetId;
  }

  public Builder toBuilder() {
    return builder()
        .withName(name)
        .withNamespace(namespace)
        .withResolvedUuid(uuid)
        .withEnabled(enabled)
        .withResolvedLifecycleStatus(lifecycleStatus)
        .withSchemaMode(schemaMode)
        .withSchema(schema)
        .withSource(source)
        .withTarget(target)
        .withResolvedDatasetId(datasetId);
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String name;
    private String namespace = DEFAULT_NAMESPACE;
    private String uuid;
    private boolean enabled = true;
    private String lifecycleStatus;
    private IngestSchemaMode schemaMode = IngestSchemaMode.STRICT;
    private SchemaModel schema;
    private IngestSourceModel source;
    private IngestTargetModel target;
    private String datasetId;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withName(String value) {
      this.name = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withNamespace(String value) {
      this.namespace = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    Builder withResolvedUuid(String value) {
      this.uuid = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    Builder withResolvedLifecycleStatus(String value) {
      this.lifecycleStatus = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSchemaMode(IngestSchemaMode value) {
      this.schemaMode = value == null ? IngestSchemaMode.STRICT : value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSchema(SchemaModel value) {
      this.schema = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSchema(Consumer<SchemaModel.Builder> customizer) {
      SchemaModel.Builder builder = SchemaModel.builder();
      if (customizer != null) {
        customizer.accept(builder);
      }
      return withSchema(builder.build());
    }

    public Builder withSource(IngestSourceModel value) {
      this.source = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTarget(IngestTargetModel value) {
      this.target = value;
      return this;
    }

    Builder withResolvedDatasetId(String value) {
      this.datasetId = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSourceApi() {
      this.source = IngestSourceApiModel.builder().build();
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSourceApi(IngestSourceApiModel value) {
      this.source = Objects.requireNonNull(value, "sourceApi");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSourceApi(Consumer<IngestSourceApiModel.Builder> customizer) {
      IngestSourceApiModel.Builder builder = IngestSourceApiModel.builder();
      if (customizer != null) {
        customizer.accept(builder);
      }

    }

    public Builder withSourceExternal(Consumer<IngestSourceExternalModel.Builder> customizer) {

    }

    public Builder withTargetDuckDb(IngestTargetDuckDbModel value) {

      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTargetDuckDb(Consumer<IngestTargetDuckDbModel.Builder> customizer) {

      if (customizer != null) {
        customizer.accept(builder);
      }
      return withTargetDuckDbActive(builder.build());

    public Builder withTargetParquet(IngestTargetParquetModel value) {

      return withTargetParquet(builder.build());
    }

    public Builder withTargetExternal(IngestTargetExternalModel value) {
      this.target = Objects.requireNonNull(value, "targetExternal");
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTargetExternal(Consumer<IngestTargetExternalModel.Builder> customizer) {
      IngestTargetExternalModel.Builder builder = IngestTargetExternalModel.builder();
      if (customizer != null) {
        customizer.accept(builder);
      }
      return withTargetExternal(builder.build());
    }

    public IngestModel build() {
      String resolvedName = Strings.requireNonBlank(name, "ingest.name");
      String resolvedNamespace = Strings.firstNonBlank(namespace, DEFAULT_NAMESPACE);
      String resolvedUuid = Strings.trimToNull(uuid);
      String resolvedLifecycle = Strings.trimToNull(lifecycleStatus);
      IngestSchemaMode resolvedSchemaMode = schemaMode == null ? IngestSchemaMode.STRICT : schemaMode;
      String resolvedDatasetId = Strings.trimToNull(datasetId);

      if (schema == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("ingest schema is required");
      }
      if (source == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("ingest source is required");
      }

      this.name = resolvedName;
      this.namespace = resolvedNamespace;
      this.uuid = resolvedUuid;
      this.lifecycleStatus = resolvedLifecycle;
      this.schemaMode = resolvedSchemaMode;
      this.datasetId = resolvedDatasetId;
      IngestTargetModel resolvedTarget = normalizeTarget(target, resolvedName);
      this.target = resolvedTarget;
      this.source =
          normalizeSource(
              source, resolvedName, resolvedNamespace, enabled, resolvedLifecycle, resolvedTarget);
      return new IngestModel(this);
    }

    private static IngestSourceModel normalizeSource(
        IngestSourceModel source,
        String ingestName,
        String namespace,
        boolean enabled,
        String lifecycleStatus,
        IngestTargetModel target) {
      if (source instanceof IngestSourceApiModel api) {
        return api.toBuilder()
            .withResolvedIngestName(Strings.firstNonBlank(api.ingestName(), ingestName))
            .withNamespace(Strings.firstNonBlank(api.namespace(), namespace))
            .withEnabled(api.enabled() == null ? enabled : api.enabled())
            .withLifecycleStatus(Strings.firstNonBlank(api.lifecycleStatus(), lifecycleStatus))
            .build();
      }
      if (source instanceof IngestSourceAmpsModel amps) {
        String normalizedOptions = amps.options();
        if (target instanceof IngestTargetDuckDbActiveModel) {
          normalizedOptions = ensureSubscribeOption(normalizedOptions, "oof");
        }
        return amps.toBuilder()
            .withResolvedIngestName(Strings.firstNonBlank(amps.ingestName(), ingestName))
            .withNamespace(Strings.firstNonBlank(amps.namespace(), namespace))
            .withEnabled(amps.enabled() == null ? enabled : amps.enabled())
            .withLifecycleStatus(Strings.firstNonBlank(amps.lifecycleStatus(), lifecycleStatus))
            .withOptions(normalizedOptions)
            .build();
      }
      if (source instanceof IngestSourceExternalModel external) {
        return external.toBuilder()
            .withResolvedIngestName(Strings.firstNonBlank(external.ingestName(), ingestName))
            .withNamespace(Strings.firstNonBlank(external.namespace(), namespace))
            .withEnabled(external.enabled() == null ? enabled : external.enabled())
            .withLifecycleStatus(Strings.firstNonBlank(external.lifecycleStatus(), lifecycleStatus))
            .build();
      }
      return source;
    }

    private static IngestTargetModel normalizeTarget(IngestTargetModel target, String ingestName) {
      if (target instanceof IngestTargetDuckDbActiveModel duckdbActive) {
        return duckdbActive.toBuilder()
            .withTableName(Strings.firstNonBlank(duckdbActive.tableName(), ingestName))
            .build();
      }
      if (target instanceof IngestTargetExternalModel external) {
        return external.toBuilder().build();
      }
      return target;
    }

    private static String ensureSubscribeOption(String options, String optionToken) {
      String normalizedToken = Strings.requireNonBlank(optionToken, "optionToken");
      String normalizedOptions = Strings.trimToNull(options);
      if (normalizedOptions == null) {
        return normalizedToken;
      }
      for (String token : normalizedOptions.split(";")) {
        String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(token);
        if (normalized != null && normalizedToken.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
          return normalizedOptions;
        }
      }
      return normalizedOptions + ";" + normalizedToken;
    }
  }
}

  public enum Mode {
    STREAM,
    BATCH
  }

  public enum OofHandling {
    DELETE_EVENT,
    MARK_AS_DELETED
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String ingestName;
    private String namespace;
    private String uuid;
    private Boolean enabled;
    private String lifecycleStatus;
    private IngestFormat format;
    private String connectionName;

    private boolean oofHandlingConfigured;
    private String jsonRootField;
    private String nvFixPairDelimiter;
    private String nvFixKvDelimiter;
    private Boolean nvFixTrimKeys;
    private Boolean nvFixTrimValues;

    private Builder() {}

    Builder withResolvedIngestName(String value) {
      this.ingestName = Strings.trimToNull(value);

      return this;
    }

    public Builder withFormat(String value) {
      this.format = IngestFormat.fromToken(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withConnectionName(String value) {
      this.connectionName = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;

    public Builder withTopic(String value) {
      this.topic = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;

    public Builder withSowSubscribe(Boolean value) {
      this.sow = value;
      if (Boolean.TRUE.equals(value)) {

    }

    public Builder withSow() {
      return withSow(Boolean.TRUE);
    }

    public Builder withOptions(String value) {
      this.options = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withFilter(String value) {
      this.filter = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMode(Mode value) {
      this.mode = value == null ? Mode.STREAM : value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withBatchMaxMessages(Integer value) {
      this.batchMaxMessages = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withBatchMaxBytes(Integer value) {
      this.batchMaxBytes = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withBatchFlushMillis(Long value) {
      this.batchFlushMillis = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOofHandling(OofHandling value) {
      this.oofHandling = value == null ? OofHandling.DELETE_EVENT : value;
      this.oofHandlingConfigured = true;
      return this;
    }

    Builder withResolvedOofHandling(OofHandling value, boolean configured) {
      this.oofHandling = value == null ? OofHandling.DELETE_EVENT : value;
      this.oofHandlingConfigured = configured;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOofHandling(String value) {
      String normalized = Strings.requireNonBlank(value, "source.amps.oofHandling");
      if ("DELETE".equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
        this.oofHandling = OofHandling.DELETE_EVENT;
      } else {
        this.oofHandling = OofHandling.valueOf(normalized.toUpperCase(java.util.Locale.ROOT));
      }
      this.oofHandlingConfigured = true;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withJsonRootField(String value) {
      this.jsonRootField = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withNvFixPairDelimiter(String value) {
      this.nvFixPairDelimiter = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withNvFixKvDelimiter(String value) {
      this.nvFixKvDelimiter = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withNvFixTrimKeys(Boolean value) {
      this.nvFixTrimKeys = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withNvFixTrimValues(Boolean value) {
      this.nvFixTrimValues = value;
      return this;
    }

    public IngestSourceAmpsModel build() {
      if (Strings.trimToNull(connectionName) == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("source.amps.connectionName is required");
      }
      if (Strings.trimToNull(topic) == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("source.amps.topic is required");
      }
      if (format == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("source.amps.format is required");
      }
      return new IngestSourceAmpsModel(this);
    }
  }

  private static String normalizedOptions(
      String options, boolean oofHandlingConfigured, boolean sow, boolean sowOnly) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(options);
    if (!oofHandlingConfigured) {
      return normalized;
    }
    if (!sow && !sowOnly) {
      return normalized;
    }
    return ensureSubscribeOption(normalized, "oof");
  }

  private static String ensureSubscribeOption(String options, String optionToken) {
    String normalizedToken = Strings.requireNonBlank(optionToken, "optionToken");
    String normalizedOptions = Strings.trimToNull(options);
    if (normalizedOptions == null) {
      return normalizedToken;
    }
    for (String token : normalizedOptions.split(";")) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(token);
      if (normalized != null && normalizedToken.equalsIgnoreCase(normalized)) {
        return normalizedOptions;
      }
    }
    return normalizedOptions + ";" + normalizedToken;
  }
}

  private static Map<String, String> immutableCopy(Map<String, String> value) {
    if (value == null || value.isEmpty()) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> copy = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : value.entrySet()) {
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
      if (key == null) {
        continue;
      }
      copy.put(key, Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue()));
    }
    return copy.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(copy);
  }
}

  public static final class Builder {
    private String tableName;
    private final List<String> primaryKey = new ArrayList<>();
    private Boolean memory = Boolean.TRUE;
    private String databasePath;
    private String parquetHistoryPath;
    private Boolean persistOnStop = Boolean.FALSE;
    private Boolean createIfMissing = Boolean.TRUE;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withTableName(String value) {
      this.tableName = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPrimaryKey(List<String> values) {
      primaryKey.clear();
      if (values == null) {
        return this;
      }
      LinkedHashSet<String> dedupe = new LinkedHashSet<>();
      for (String value : values) {
        String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
        if (normalized != null) {
          dedupe.add(normalized);
        }
      }
      primaryKey.addAll(dedupe);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder addPrimaryKey(String value) {
      String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      if (normalized == null) {
        return this;
      }
      if (!primaryKey.contains(normalized)) {
        primaryKey.add(normalized);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMemory(Boolean value) {
      this.memory = value == null ? Boolean.TRUE : value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withDatabasePath(String value) {
      this.databasePath = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withParquetHistoryPath(String value) {
      this.parquetHistoryPath = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPersistOnStop(Boolean value) {
      this.persistOnStop = value == null ? Boolean.FALSE : value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withCreateIfMissing(Boolean value) {
      this.createIfMissing = value == null ? Boolean.TRUE : value;
      return this;
    }

    public IngestTargetDuckDbActiveModel build() {
      this.tableName = Strings.trimToNull(tableName);
      if (primaryKey.isEmpty()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("target.duckdbActive.primaryKey is required");
      }
      boolean resolvedMemory = memory == null || memory;
      this.memory = resolvedMemory;
      if (!resolvedMemory) {
        this.databasePath =
            Strings.requireNonBlank(databasePath, "target.duckdbActive.databasePath");
      }
      return new IngestTargetDuckDbActiveModel(this);
    }
  }
}

      return Map.of();

        continue;

      copy.put(key, Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue()));

    private Long maxIdleMillis;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withParquetPath(String value) {
      this.parquetPath = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withGlob(String value) {
      this.glob = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withHivePartitioning(Boolean value) {
      this.hivePartitioning = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPartitionKey(String value) {
      this.partitionKey = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPartitionValueField(String value) {
      this.partitionValueField = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withConnectionName(String value) {
      this.connectionName = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMaxRowsPerFile(Integer value) {
      this.maxRowsPerFile = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMaxIdleMillis(Long value) {
      this.maxIdleMillis = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMaxIdleDuration(Duration value) {
      this.maxIdleMillis = value == null ? null : value.toMillis();
      return this;
    }

    public IngestTargetParquetModel build() {
      this.parquetPath = Strings.trimToNull(parquetPath);
      if (maxRowsPerFile != null && maxRowsPerFile <= 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("target.parquet.maxRowsPerFile must be > 0");
      }
      if (maxIdleMillis != null && maxIdleMillis <= 0L) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("target.parquet.maxIdleMillis must be > 0");
      }
      return new IngestTargetParquetModel(this);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.parquet;

public record ParquetCompactionOptions(
    int minFilesPerGroup,
    int maxFilesPerGroup,
    int maxGroupsPerRun,
    boolean dryRun
) {
  public static ParquetCompactionOptions defaults() {
    return new ParquetCompactionOptions(2, 8, 16, false);
  }

  public ParquetCompactionOptions {
    minFilesPerGroup = minFilesPerGroup <= 1 ? 2 : minFilesPerGroup;
    maxFilesPerGroup = maxFilesPerGroup <= 1 ? 8 : maxFilesPerGroup;
    if (maxFilesPerGroup < minFilesPerGroup) {
      maxFilesPerGroup = minFilesPerGroup;
    }
    maxGroupsPerRun = maxGroupsPerRun <= 0 ? 16 : maxGroupsPerRun;
  }
}



FILE: ParquetCompactionPlanner.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.parquet;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;

public final class ParquetCompactionPlanner {
  public List<List<String>> plan(List<String> parquetFiles, ParquetCompactionOptions options) {
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(parquetFiles == null ? List.of() : parquetFiles);
    sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER.thenComparing(Comparator.naturalOrder()));
    ParquetCompactionOptions resolved =
        options == null ? ParquetCompactionOptions.defaults() : options;
    List<List<String>> groups = new ArrayList<>();
    int index = 0;
    while (index < sorted.size() && groups.size() < resolved.maxGroupsPerRun()) {
      int remaining = sorted.size() - index;
      int groupSize = Math.min(resolved.maxFilesPerGroup(), remaining);
      if (groupSize < resolved.minFilesPerGroup()) {
        break;
      }
      List<String> group = new ArrayList<>(groupSize);
      for (int offset = 0; offset < groupSize; offset++) {
        group.add(sorted.get(index + offset));
      }
      groups.add(List.copyOf(group));
      index += groupSize;
    }
    return List.copyOf(groups);
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.parquet;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.ParquetManager;

public final class ParquetMaintenanceManagerUnsupported implements ParquetManager {
  private final String reason;
  private static final String REMEDIATION =
      "run in DIRECT mode or via a server-side maintenance service.";

  public ParquetMaintenanceManagerUnsupported(String reason) {
    this.reason = reason == null ? null : reason.trim();
  }

  @Override
  public ParquetMaintenanceResult compactDataset(String datasetId, ParquetCompactionOptions options) {
    throw unsupported("parquet.compactDataset");
  }

  @Override
  public ParquetMaintenanceResult compactPartition(
      String datasetId, String partitionSpec, ParquetCompactionOptions options) {
    throw unsupported("parquet.compactPartition");
  }

  @Override
  public ParquetMaintenanceResult applyRetention(String datasetId, ParquetRetentionPolicy policy) {
    throw unsupported("parquet.applyRetention");
  }

  @Override
  public ParquetMaintenanceResult optimizeDataset(String datasetId, ParquetCompactionOptions options) {
    throw unsupported("parquet.optimizeDataset");
  }

  private UnsupportedOperationException unsupported(String operation) {
    StringBuilder message =
        new StringBuilder(operation)
            .append(" is not supported in SERVICE mode; ")
            .append(REMEDIATION);
    if (reason != null && !reason.isBlank()) {
      message.append(" detail=").append(reason);
    }
    return new UnsupportedOperationException(message.toString());
  }
}

FILE: ParquetRetentionPlanner.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.parquet;

import java.time.LocalDate;
import java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Set;

public final class ParquetRetentionPlanner {
  private static final DateTimeFormatter PARTITION_FORMAT = DateTimeFormatter.BASIC_ISO_DATE;

  public List<String> partitionsToDelete(List<String> partitions, ParquetRetentionPolicy policy) {
    List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(partitions == null ? List.of() : partitions);
    sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER.thenComparing(Comparator.naturalOrder()));
    ParquetRetentionPolicy resolved = policy == null ? new ParquetRetentionPolicy(0, null, false) : policy;
    Set<String> keep = new LinkedHashSet<>();

    Integer keepLastPartitions = resolved.keepLastPartitions();
    if (keepLastPartitions != null && keepLastPartitions > 0) {
      int start = Math.max(0, sorted.size() - keepLastPartitions);
      for (int i = start; i < sorted.size(); i++) {
        keep.add(sorted.get(i));
      }
    }

    Integer keepLastDays = resolved.keepLastDays();
    if (keepLastDays != null && keepLastDays > 0) {
      LocalDate threshold = LocalDate.now().minusDays(Math.max(0, keepLastDays.longValue() - 1L));
      for (String partition : sorted) {
        LocalDate parsed = parsePartitionDate(partition);
        if (parsed != null && !parsed.isBefore(threshold)) {
          keep.add(partition);
        }
      }
    }

    List<String> delete = new ArrayList<>();
    for (String partition : sorted) {
      if (!keep.contains(partition)) {
        delete.add(partition);
      }
    }
    return List.copyOf(delete);
  }

  private static LocalDate parsePartitionDate(String partition) {
    if (partition == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String normalized = partition.trim().toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if (!normalized.startsWith("date=") || normalized.length() != "date=yyyyMMdd".length()) {
      return null;
    }
    try {
      return LocalDate.parse(normalized.substring("date=".length()), PARTITION_FORMAT);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      return null;
    }
  }
}

    return new ParquetRetentionPolicy(Math.max(0, partitions), null, false);

FILE: FormatSamplerJson.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.schema;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngestSource;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format.FormatPayloadParsing;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class FormatSamplerJson implements FormatSampler {
  private final ObjectMapper mapper;
  private final String rootField;

  public FormatSamplerJson(DefinitionIngestSource.JsonConfig config) {
    this(config, DiscoveryCodec.mapper());
  }

  FormatSamplerJson(DefinitionIngestSource.JsonConfig config, ObjectMapper mapper) {
    this.mapper = Objects.requireNonNull(mapper, "mapper");
    this.rootField = Strings.trimToNull(config == null ? null : config.rootField());
  }

  @Override
  public FormatSamplerResult parseSamples(List<PayloadSample> samples, FormatSamplerOptions options) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(options, "options");
    List<PayloadSample> input = samples == null ? List.of() : samples;
    List<Map<String, Object>> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    List<String> failures = new ArrayList<>();

    int sampleIndex = 0;
    for (PayloadSample sample : input) {
      sampleIndex++;
      if (sample == null || sample.payload() == null || sample.payload().isEmpty()) {
        failures.add("sample=" + sampleIndex + " reason=empty_payload");
        continue;
      }
      try {
        List<Map<String, JsonNode>> parsed =
            FormatPayloadParsing.parseJsonRows(
                options.ingestId(),
                sample.payload(),
                rootField,
                Integer.MAX_VALUE,
                mapper);
        for (Map<String, JsonNode> row : parsed) {
          Map<String, Object> converted = new LinkedHashMap<>();
          for (Map.Entry<String, JsonNode> entry : row.entrySet()) {
            converted.put(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue());
          }
          rows.add(converted);
        }
      } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
        failures.add(
            "sample="
                + sampleIndex
                + " reason="
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(ex.getMessage()), ex.getClass().getSimpleName()));
      }
    }
    return new FormatSamplerResult(rows, failures, failures.size());
  }
}





FILE: FormatSamplerNvFix.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.schema;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionIngestSource;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.connectors.amps.AmpsConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.format.FormatPayloadParsing;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class FormatSamplerNvFix implements FormatSampler {
  private final String pairDelimiter;
  private final String kvDelimiter;
  private final boolean trimKeys;
  private final boolean trimValues;

  public FormatSamplerNvFix(DefinitionIngestSource.NvFixConfig config) {
    String configuredPairDelimiter = Strings.trimToNull(config == null ? null : config.pairDelimiter());
    String configuredKvDelimiter = Strings.trimToNull(config == null ? null : config.kvDelimiter());
    this.trimKeys = config == null || config.trimKeys() == null || config.trimKeys();
    this.trimValues = config == null || config.trimValues() == null || config.trimValues();
    this.pairDelimiter =
        configuredPairDelimiter == null ? String.valueOf(AmpsConnection.SOH) : configuredPairDelimiter;
    this.kvDelimiter = configuredKvDelimiter == null ? "=" : configuredKvDelimiter;
    if (this.kvDelimiter.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("kvDelimiter must not be empty");
    }
  }

  @Override
  public FormatSamplerResult parseSamples(List<PayloadSample> samples, FormatSamplerOptions options) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(options, "options");
    List<PayloadSample> input = samples == null ? List.of() : samples;
    List<Map<String, Object>> rows = new ArrayList<>();
    List<String> failures = new ArrayList<>();

    int sampleIndex = 0;
    for (PayloadSample sample : input) {
      sampleIndex++;
      if (sample == null || sample.payload() == null || sample.payload().isEmpty()) {
        failures.add("sample=" + sampleIndex + " reason=empty_payload");
        continue;
      }
      try {
        List<Map<String, String>> parsed =
            FormatPayloadParsing.parseNvFixRows(
                options.ingestId(),
                sample.payload(),
                pairDelimiter,
                kvDelimiter,
                trimKeys,
                trimValues,
                Integer.MAX_VALUE);
        for (Map<String, String> row : parsed) {
          Map<String, Object> converted = new LinkedHashMap<>();
          for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : row.entrySet()) {
            String value = entry.getValue();
            if (trimValues && value != null && value.isEmpty()) {
              converted.put(entry.getKey(), null);
            } else {
              converted.put(entry.getKey(), value);
            }
          }
          rows.add(converted);
        }
      } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
        failures.add(
            "sample="
                + sampleIndex
                + " reason="
                + Strings.firstNonBlank(Strings.trimToNull(ex.getMessage()), ex.getClass().getSimpleName()));
      }
    }
    return new FormatSamplerResult(rows, failures, failures.size());
  }
}

FILE: SchemaInference.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.schema;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.JsonNode;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.time.LocalDate;
import java.time.format.DateTimeFormatter;
import java.time.format.DateTimeParseException;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.TreeSet;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.schema.client.InferredField;

public final class SchemaInference {
  private SchemaInference() {}

  public static InferredSchema infer(List<Map<String, Object>> rows, boolean allowNulls) {
    List<Map<String, Object>> inputRows;
    if (rows == null || rows.isEmpty()) {
      inputRows = List.of();
    } else {
      List<Map<String, Object>> normalized = new ArrayList<>(rows.size());
      for (Map<String, Object> row : rows) {
        normalized.add(row == null ? Collections.emptyMap() : row);
      }
      inputRows = List.copyOf(normalized);
    }

    TreeSet<String> allFieldNames = new TreeSet<>();
    for (Map<String, Object> row : inputRows) {
      allFieldNames.addAll(row.keySet());
    }

    TreeSet<String> missingKeysSeen = new TreeSet<>();
    TreeSet<String> widenedFields = new TreeSet<>();
    TreeSet<String> typeConflicts = new TreeSet<>();
    TreeSet<String> parseFailures = new TreeSet<>();
    List<InferredField> inferredFields = new ArrayList<>(allFieldNames.size());

    for (String fieldName : allFieldNames) {
      FieldState state = new FieldState(fieldName);
      for (int rowIndex = 0; rowIndex < inputRows.size(); rowIndex++) {
        Map<String, Object> row = inputRows.get(rowIndex);
        if (!row.containsKey(fieldName)) {
          state.missing = true;
          missingKeysSeen.add(fieldName);
          continue;
        }
        Object raw = row.get(fieldName);
        if (isNullLike(raw)) {
          state.nullObserved = true;
          continue;
        }
        Token actual = detectToken(raw, fieldName, rowIndex + 1, parseFailures);
        MergeResult merge = mergeToken(state.token, actual);
        if (merge.widened) {
          widenedFields.add(fieldName);
        }
        if (merge.conflict) {
          typeConflicts.add(fieldName);
        }
        state.token = merge.token;
      }

      Token resolved = state.token == null ? Token.STRING : state.token;
      boolean nullable = allowNulls && (state.missing || state.nullObserved);
      String notes = null;
      if (typeConflicts.contains(fieldName)) {
        notes = "type_conflict";
      } else if (widenedFields.contains(fieldName)) {
        notes = "widened";
      }
      inferredFields.add(new InferredField(fieldName, resolved.token, nullable, notes));
    }

    return new InferredSchema(
        List.copyOf(inferredFields),
        List.copyOf(missingKeysSeen),
        List.copyOf(typeConflicts),
        List.copyOf(widenedFields),
        List.copyOf(parseFailures),
        parseFailures.size());
  }

  private static boolean isNullLike(Object raw) {
    if (raw == null) {
      return true;
    }
    if (raw instanceof JsonNode node) {
      return node.isNull();
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static Token detectToken(
      Object raw, String fieldName, int rowIndex, TreeSet<String> parseFailures) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(parseFailures, "parseFailures");
    if (raw instanceof JsonNode node) {
      return detectJsonToken(node, fieldName, rowIndex, parseFailures);
    }
    if (raw instanceof Boolean) {
      return Token.BOOL;
    }
    if (raw instanceof Byte
        || raw instanceof Short
        || raw instanceof Integer
        || raw instanceof Long) {
      long value = ((Number) raw).longValue();
      return value >= Integer.MIN_VALUE && value <= Integer.MAX_VALUE ? Token.INT32 : Token.INT64;
    }
    if (raw instanceof Float || raw instanceof Double) {
      return Token.FLOAT64;
    }
    if (raw instanceof Number number) {
      long value = number.longValue();
      return value >= Integer.MIN_VALUE && value <= Integer.MAX_VALUE ? Token.INT32 : Token.INT64;
    }
    if (raw instanceof String text) {
      return detectNvFixStringToken(text);
    }
    parseFailures.add(
        "field="
            + fieldName
            + " row="
            + rowIndex
            + " reason=unsupported_value_type:"
            + raw.getClass().getSimpleName());
    return Token.STRING;
  }

  private static Token detectJsonToken(
      JsonNode node, String fieldName, int rowIndex, TreeSet<String> parseFailures) {
    if (node == null || node.isNull()) {
      return null;
    }
    if (node.isBoolean()) {
      return Token.BOOL;
    }
    if (node.isIntegralNumber()) {
      if (node.canConvertToInt()) {
        return Token.INT32;
      }
      if (node.canConvertToLong()) {
        return Token.INT64;
      }
      parseFailures.add(
          "field=" + fieldName + " row=" + rowIndex + " reason=integral_number_overflow");
      return Token.FLOAT64;
    }
    if (node.isFloatingPointNumber() || node.isNumber()) {
      return Token.FLOAT64;
    }
    if (node.isTextual()) {
      return Token.STRING;
    }
    parseFailures.add(
        "field="
            + fieldName
            + " row="
            + rowIndex
            + " reason=non_scalar_json:"
            + node.getNodeType().name());
    return Token.STRING;
  }

  private static Token detectNvFixStringToken(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    if ("true".equalsIgnoreCase(value) || "false".equalsIgnoreCase(value)) {
      return Token.BOOL;
    }
    if (looksLikeDate(value) && tryParseDate(value)) {
      return Token.DATE32;
    }
    if (looksLikeTimestamp(value) && tryParseTimestamp(value)) {
      return Token.TIMESTAMP;
    }
    Integer asInt = tryParseInt32(value);
    if (asInt != null) {
      return Token.INT32;
    }
    Long asLong = tryParseInt64(value);
    if (asLong != null) {
      return Token.INT64;
    }
    Double asDouble = tryParseFloat64(value);
    if (asDouble != null) {
      return Token.FLOAT64;
    }
    if (tryParseDate(value)) {
      return Token.DATE32;
    }
    if (tryParseTimestamp(value)) {
      return Token.TIMESTAMP;
    }
    return Token.STRING;
  }

  private static MergeResult mergeToken(Token current, Token incoming) {
    if (incoming == null) {
      return new MergeResult(current, false, false);
    }
    if (current == null) {
      return new MergeResult(incoming, false, false);
    }
    if (current == incoming) {
      return new MergeResult(current, false, false);
    }
    if (isNumeric(current) && isNumeric(incoming)) {
      Token widened = widerNumeric(current, incoming);
      return new MergeResult(widened, widened != current, false);
    }
    if ((current == Token.DATE32 && incoming == Token.TIMESTAMP)
        || (current == Token.TIMESTAMP && incoming == Token.DATE32)) {
      return new MergeResult(Token.STRING, true, true);
    }
    if (current == Token.STRING || incoming == Token.STRING) {
      Token other = current == Token.STRING ? incoming : current;
      boolean conflict = !isNumeric(other);
      return new MergeResult(Token.STRING, current != Token.STRING, conflict);
    }
    return new MergeResult(Token.STRING, true, true);
  }

  private static boolean isNumeric(Token token) {
    return token == Token.INT32 || token == Token.INT64 || token == Token.FLOAT64;
  }

  private static Token widerNumeric(Token left, Token right) {
    if (left == Token.FLOAT64 || right == Token.FLOAT64) {
      return Token.FLOAT64;
    }
    if (left == Token.INT64 || right == Token.INT64) {
      return Token.INT64;
    }
    return Token.INT32;
  }

  private static Integer tryParseInt32(String value) {
    try {
      return Integer.valueOf(value);
    } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static Long tryParseInt64(String value) {
    try {
      return Long.valueOf(value);
    } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static Double tryParseFloat64(String value) {
    try {
      double parsed = Double.parseDouble(value);
      if (Double.isFinite(parsed)) {
        return parsed;
      }
      return null;
    } catch (NumberFormatException ex) {
      return null;
    }
  }

  private static boolean tryParseDate(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return false;
    }
    try {
      if (value.length() == 10 && value.charAt(4) == '-' && value.charAt(7) == '-') {
        LocalDate.parse(value);
        return true;
      }
      if (value.length() == 8) {
        LocalDate.parse(value, DateTimeFormatter.BASIC_ISO_DATE);
        return true;
      }
    } catch (DateTimeParseException ex) {
      return false;
    }
    return false;
  }

  private static boolean tryParseTimestamp(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return false;
    }
    try {
      Instant.parse(value);
      return true;
    } catch (DateTimeParseException ex) {
      return tryParseInt64(value) != null;
    }
  }

  private static boolean looksLikeDate(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return (value.length() == 10 && value.charAt(4) == '-' && value.charAt(7) == '-')
        || (value.length() == 8 && allDigits(value));
  }

  private static boolean looksLikeTimestamp(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if (value.contains("T") || value.contains(":") || value.endsWith("Z")) {
      return true;
    }
    return value.length() >= 15 && allDigits(value);
  }

  private static boolean allDigits(String value) {
    for (int i = 0; i < value.length(); i++) {
      char ch = value.charAt(i);
      if (ch < '0' || ch > '9') {
        return false;
      }
    }
    return true;
  }

  private static final class FieldState {
    private final String name;
    private boolean missing;
    private boolean nullObserved;
    private Token token;

    private FieldState(String name) {
      this.name = name;
    }
  }

  private record MergeResult(Token token, boolean widened, boolean conflict) {}

  private enum Token {
    BOOL("BOOL"),
    INT32("INT32"),
    INT64("INT64"),
    FLOAT64("FLOAT64"),
    DATE32("DATE32"),
    TIMESTAMP("TIMESTAMP"),
    STRING("STRING");

    private final String token;

    Token(String token) {
      this.token = token;
    }
  }

  public record InferredSchema(
      List<InferredField> fields,
      List<String> missingKeysSeen,
      List<String> typeConflicts,
      List<String> widenedFields,
      List<String> parseFailures,
      int parseErrorCount
  ) {
    public InferredSchema {
      fields = fields == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(fields);
      missingKeysSeen = missingKeysSeen == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(missingKeysSeen);
      typeConflicts = typeConflicts == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(typeConflicts);
      widenedFields = widenedFields == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(widenedFields);
      parseFailures = parseFailures == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(parseFailures);
      parseErrorCount = Math.max(0, parseErrorCount);
    }

    public Map<String, InferredField> byName() {
      Map<String, InferredField> map = new LinkedHashMap<>();
      for (InferredField field : fields) {
        map.put(field.name(), field);
      }
      return Map.copyOf(map);
    }
  }
}

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class ViewDependencyModel {
  private final String datasetId;
  private final String viewName;

  private ViewDependencyModel(Builder builder) {
    this.datasetId = builder.datasetId;
    this.viewName = builder.viewName;
  }

  public String datasetId() {
    return datasetId;
  }

  public String viewName() {
    return viewName;
  }

  public String reference() {
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(datasetId, viewName);
  }

  public Builder toBuilder() {
    return builder().withDatasetId(datasetId).withViewName(viewName);
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String datasetId;
    private String viewName;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withDatasetId(String value) {
      this.datasetId = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withViewName(String value) {
      this.viewName = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public ViewDependencyModel build() {
      this.datasetId = Strings.trimToNull(datasetId);
      this.viewName = Strings.trimToNull(viewName);
      if (datasetId == null && viewName == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException(
            "view dependency requires datasetId or viewName");
      }
      return new ViewDependencyModel(this);
    }
