package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.views.model;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Consumer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaCompatibility;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaModel;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class ViewModel {
  private static final String DEFAULT_NAMESPACE = "default";
  private static final String DEFAULT_LIFECYCLE_STATUS = "ACTIVE";

  private final String name;
  private final String namespace;
  private final String uuid;
  private final boolean enabled;
  private final String lifecycleStatus;
  private final String outputDatasetId;
  private final ViewQueryModel query;
  private final List<String> dependencies;
  private final SchemaModel schema;
  private final SchemaCompatibility schemaCompatibility;
  private final ViewTargetModel target;
  private final ViewRefreshModel refresh;

  private ViewModel(Builder builder) {
    this.name = builder.name;
    this.namespace = builder.namespace;
    this.uuid = builder.uuid;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
    this.lifecycleStatus = builder.lifecycleStatus;
    this.outputDatasetId = builder.outputDatasetId;
    this.query = builder.query;
    this.dependencies = builder.dependencies.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(builder.dependencies);
    this.schema = builder.schema;
    this.schemaCompatibility = builder.schemaCompatibility;
    this.target = builder.target;
    this.refresh = builder.refresh;
  }

  public String name() {
    return name;
  }

  public String namespace() {
    return namespace;
  }

  public String uuid() {
    return uuid;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  public String lifecycleStatus() {
    return lifecycleStatus;
  }

  public String outputDatasetId() {
    return outputDatasetId;
  }

  public ViewQueryModel query() {
    return query;
  }

  public List<String> dependencies() {
    return dependencies;
  }

  public SchemaModel schema() {
    return schema;
  }

  public SchemaCompatibility schemaCompatibility() {
    return schemaCompatibility;
  }

  public ViewTargetModel target() {
    return target;
  }

  public ViewRefreshModel refresh() {
    return refresh;
  }

  public Builder toBuilder() {
    Builder builder =
        builder()
            .withName(name)
            .withNamespace(namespace)
            .withUuid(uuid)
            .withEnabled(enabled)
            .withLifecycleStatus(lifecycleStatus)
            .withOutputDatasetId(outputDatasetId)
            .withQuery(query)
            .withSchema(schema)
            .withSchemaCompatibility(schemaCompatibility)
            .withTarget(target)
            .withRefresh(refresh);
    builder.withDependencies(dependencies);
    return builder;
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String name;
    private String namespace = DEFAULT_NAMESPACE;
    private String uuid;
    private boolean enabled = true;
    private String lifecycleStatus = DEFAULT_LIFECYCLE_STATUS;
    private String outputDatasetId;
    private ViewQueryModel query;
    private final List<String> dependencies = new ArrayList<>();
    private SchemaModel schema;
    private SchemaCompatibility schemaCompatibility = SchemaCompatibility.BACKWARDS;
    private ViewTargetModel target;
    private ViewRefreshModel refresh = ViewRefreshModel.builder().build();

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withName(String value) {
      this.name = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withNamespace(String value) {
      this.namespace = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withUuid(String value) {
      this.uuid = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withLifecycleStatus(String value) {
      this.lifecycleStatus = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withOutputDatasetId(String value) {
      this.outputDatasetId = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withQuery(ViewQueryModel value) {
      this.query = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withQuery(Consumer<ViewQueryModel.Builder> customizer) {
      ViewQueryModel.Builder builder = ViewQueryModel.builder();
      if (customizer != null) {
        customizer.accept(builder);
      }
      return withQuery(builder.build());
    }

    public Builder withDependencies(List<String> values) {
      this.dependencies.clear();
      if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
        return this;
      }
      LinkedHashSet<String> normalized = new LinkedHashSet<>();
      for (String value : values) {
        String dependency = Strings.trimToNull(value);
        if (dependency != null) {
          normalized.add(dependency);
        }
      }
      List<String> sorted = new ArrayList<>(normalized);
      sorted.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER.thenComparing(Comparator.naturalOrder()));
      this.dependencies.addAll(sorted);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder addDependency(String value) {
      String dependency = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      if (dependency != null) {
        this.dependencies.add(dependency);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder addDependency(ViewDependencyModel value) {
      if (value != null) {
        addDependency(value.reference());
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSchema(SchemaModel value) {
      this.schema = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSchemaCompatibility(SchemaCompatibility value) {
      this.schemaCompatibility = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTarget(ViewTargetModel value) {
      this.target = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRefresh(ViewRefreshModel value) {
      this.refresh = value;
      return this;
    }

    public ViewModel build() {
      this.name = Strings.requireNonBlank(name, "view.name");
      this.namespace = Strings.firstNonBlank(namespace, DEFAULT_NAMESPACE);
      this.uuid = Strings.trimToNull(uuid);
      this.lifecycleStatus = Strings.firstNonBlank(lifecycleStatus, DEFAULT_LIFECYCLE_STATUS);
      this.outputDatasetId = Strings.trimToNull(outputDatasetId);
      this.query = Objects.requireNonNull(query, "view.query");
      this.schema = Objects.requireNonNull(schema, "view.schema");
      this.schemaCompatibility =
          schemaCompatibility == null ? SchemaCompatibility.BACKWARDS : schemaCompatibility;
      this.target = Objects.requireNonNull(target, "view.target");
      this.refresh =
          refresh == null ? ViewRefreshModel.builder().build() : refresh;
      withDependencies(new ArrayList<>(this.dependencies));
      return new ViewModel(this);
    }
  }
}


FILE: ViewQueryModel.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.views.model;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.TreeMap;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class ViewQueryModel {
  private final String sql;
  private final Map<String, String> parameters;

  private ViewQueryModel(Builder builder) {
    this.sql = builder.sql;
    this.parameters = builder.parameters.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(builder.parameters);
  }

  public String sql() {
    return sql;
  }

  public Map<String, String> parameters() {
    return parameters;
  }

  public Builder toBuilder() {
    return builder().withSql(sql).withParameters(parameters);
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String sql;
    private final Map<String, String> parameters = new LinkedHashMap<>();

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withSql(String value) {
      this.sql = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withParameter(String name, String value) {
      String normalizedName = Strings.trimToNull(name);
      String normalizedValue = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      if (normalizedName != null && normalizedValue != null) {
        parameters.put(normalizedName, normalizedValue);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withParameters(Map<String, String> values) {
      parameters.clear();
      if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
        return this;
      }
      TreeMap<String, String> sorted = new TreeMap<>(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
      for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : values.entrySet()) {
        if (entry == null) {
          continue;
        }
        String key = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getKey());
        String val = Strings.trimToNull(entry.getValue());
        if (key != null && val != null) {
          sorted.put(key, val);
        }
      }
      for (Map.Entry<String, String> entry : sorted.entrySet()) {
        parameters.put(entry.getKey(), entry.getValue());
      }
      return this;
    }

    public ViewQueryModel build() {
      this.sql = Strings.requireNonBlank(sql, "view.query.sql");
      Objects.requireNonNull(parameters, "parameters");
      return new ViewQueryModel(this);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.views.model;

public final class ViewRefreshModel {
  private final ViewRefreshType type;
  private final Long intervalMillis;
  private final boolean runOnStart;

  private ViewRefreshModel(Builder builder) {
    this.type = builder.type;
    this.intervalMillis = builder.intervalMillis;
    this.runOnStart = builder.runOnStart;
  }

  public ViewRefreshType type() {
    return type;
  }

  public Long intervalMillis() {
    return intervalMillis;
  }

  public boolean runOnStart() {
    return runOnStart;
  }

  public Builder toBuilder() {
    return builder().withType(type).withIntervalMillis(intervalMillis).withRunOnStart(runOnStart);
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private ViewRefreshType type = ViewRefreshType.MANUAL;
    private Long intervalMillis;
    private boolean runOnStart;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withType(ViewRefreshType value) {
      this.type = value == null ? ViewRefreshType.MANUAL : value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withIntervalMillis(Long value) {
      this.intervalMillis = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRunOnStart(boolean value) {
      this.runOnStart = value;
      return this;
    }

    public ViewRefreshModel build() {
      this.type = type == null ? ViewRefreshType.MANUAL : type;
      this.intervalMillis = intervalMillis;
      if (this.type == ViewRefreshType.PERIODIC) {
        if (this.intervalMillis == null || this.intervalMillis <= 0L) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("view.refresh.intervalMillis must be > 0 for PERIODIC views");
        }
      } else {
        this.intervalMillis = null;
        this.runOnStart = false;
      }
      return new ViewRefreshModel(this);
    }
  }
}

      }
      return new ViewTargetModel(this);
    }

public interface RecoveryManager {

  record RecoveryStatus(
      Mode mode,
      boolean recoveryEnabled,
      boolean recoveryUsed,
      String reason,
      String snapshotPath,
      String snapshotCreatedTimeUtc,
      String snapshotAge,
      String snapshotTtl,
      int definitionCount) {
    public RecoveryStatus {
      mode = mode == null ? Mode.NOT_STARTED : mode;
      reason = reason == null ? "" : reason;
      snapshotPath = snapshotPath == null ? "" : snapshotPath;
      snapshotCreatedTimeUtc = snapshotCreatedTimeUtc == null ? "" : snapshotCreatedTimeUtc;
      snapshotAge = snapshotAge == null ? "" : snapshotAge;
      snapshotTtl = snapshotTtl == null ? "" : snapshotTtl;
      definitionCount = Math.max(0, definitionCount);
    }
  }

  enum Mode {
    NOT_STARTED,
    LIVE,
    RECOVERED,
    FAILED
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.recovery.manager;

import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.time.Instant;

public record DiscoveryCacheRecoveryResult(
    Mode mode,
    boolean recoveryEnabled,
    boolean recoveryUsed,
    String reason,
    Path snapshotPath,
    Instant snapshotCreatedTimeUtc,
    Duration snapshotAge,
    Duration snapshotTtl,
    int definitionCount,
    Instant evaluatedTimeUtc) {

  public DiscoveryCacheRecoveryResult {
    mode = mode == null ? Mode.NOT_STARTED : mode;
    reason = reason == null ? "" : reason;
    snapshotPath = snapshotPath == null ? null : snapshotPath.toAbsolutePath().normalize();
    snapshotAge = snapshotAge == null || snapshotAge.isNegative() ? null : snapshotAge;
    snapshotTtl = snapshotTtl == null || snapshotTtl.isNegative() ? null : snapshotTtl;
    definitionCount = Math.max(0, definitionCount);
    evaluatedTimeUtc = evaluatedTimeUtc == null ? Instant.now() : evaluatedTimeUtc;
  }

  public static DiscoveryCacheRecoveryResult notStarted() {
    return new DiscoveryCacheRecoveryResult(
        Mode.NOT_STARTED,
        false,
        false,
        "session not started",
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        0,
        Instant.now());
  }

  public static DiscoveryCacheRecoveryResult live(boolean recoveryEnabled, String reason) {
    return new DiscoveryCacheRecoveryResult(
        Mode.LIVE,
        recoveryEnabled,
        false,
        reason,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        null,
        0,
        Instant.now());
  }

  public static DiscoveryCacheRecoveryResult recovered(
      Path snapshotPath,
      Instant snapshotCreatedTimeUtc,
      Duration snapshotAge,
      Duration snapshotTtl,
      int definitionCount,
      String reason) {
    return new DiscoveryCacheRecoveryResult(
        Mode.RECOVERED,
        true,
        true,
        reason,
        snapshotPath,
        snapshotCreatedTimeUtc,
        snapshotAge,
        snapshotTtl,
        definitionCount,
        Instant.now());
  }

  public static DiscoveryCacheRecoveryResult failed(
      boolean recoveryEnabled,
      Path snapshotPath,
      Instant snapshotCreatedTimeUtc,
      Duration snapshotAge,
      Duration snapshotTtl,
      String reason) {
    return new DiscoveryCacheRecoveryResult(
        Mode.FAILED,
        recoveryEnabled,
        false,
        reason,
        snapshotPath,
        snapshotCreatedTimeUtc,
        snapshotAge,
        snapshotTtl,
        0,
        Instant.now());
  }

  public enum Mode {
    NOT_STARTED,
    LIVE,
    RECOVERED,
    FAILED
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.recovery.manager;

import java.time.Instant;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public record DiscoveryCacheSnapshotManifest(
    int schemaVersion,
    String createdTimeUtc,
    int definitionCount,
    String sessionId,
    String group,
    String appName,
    String instance,
    List<DefinitionEntry> definitions) {
  public static final int CURRENT_SCHEMA_VERSION = 1;

  public DiscoveryCacheSnapshotManifest {
    schemaVersion = schemaVersion <= 0 ? CURRENT_SCHEMA_VERSION : schemaVersion;
    createdTimeUtc = Strings.requireNonBlank(createdTimeUtc, "createdTimeUtc");
    definitionCount = Math.max(0, definitionCount);
    sessionId = Strings.trimToNull(sessionId);
    group = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    appName = Strings.trimToNull(appName);
    instance = Strings.trimToNull(instance);
    definitions = definitions == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(definitions);
  }

  public Instant createdInstantUtc() {
    return Instant.parse(createdTimeUtc);
  }

  public record DefinitionEntry(
      String type, String group, String name, String relativePath, String sha256Hex) {
    public DefinitionEntry {
      type = Strings.requireNonBlank(type, "type");
      group = Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "group");
      name = Strings.requireNonBlank(name, "name");
      relativePath = Strings.requireNonBlank(relativePath, "relativePath");
      sha256Hex = Strings.requireNonBlank(sha256Hex, "sha256Hex");
    }
  }
}


FILE: DiscoveryCacheSnapshotService.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.recovery.manager;

import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.ObjectMapper;
import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.SerializationFeature;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.nio.file.AtomicMoveNotSupportedException;
import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.nio.file.StandardCopyOption;
import java.security.MessageDigest;
import java.time.Duration;
import java.time.Instant;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.HexFormat;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.UUID;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.codec.DiscoveryCodec;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.Definition;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvelope;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionType;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class DiscoveryCacheSnapshotService {
  private static final ObjectMapper MAPPER =
      DiscoveryCodec.mapper().copy().configure(SerializationFeature.ORDER_MAP_ENTRIES_BY_KEYS, true);
  private static final String MANIFEST_FILE = "manifest.json";
  private static final String DEFINITIONS_DIR = "definitions";
  private static final Comparator<Definition> SNAPSHOT_ORDER =
      Comparator.comparing(DiscoveryCacheSnapshotService::definitionTypeToken, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
          .thenComparing(DiscoveryCacheSnapshotService::definitionTypeToken)
          .thenComparing(DiscoveryCacheSnapshotService::definitionGroupToken, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
          .thenComparing(DiscoveryCacheSnapshotService::definitionGroupToken)
          .thenComparing(DiscoveryCacheSnapshotService::definitionNameToken, String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER)
          .thenComparing(DiscoveryCacheSnapshotService::definitionNameToken);

  public DiscoveryCacheSnapshotManifest dump(
      DiscoveryCache cache, Path snapshotRoot, SnapshotMetadata metadata) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(cache, "cache");
    Path target = normalizeRoot(snapshotRoot);
    SnapshotMetadata resolvedMetadata = metadata == null ? SnapshotMetadata.empty() : metadata;
    Path tempRoot =
        target
            .getParent()
            .resolve(target.getFileName() + ".tmp-" + UUID.randomUUID().toString().replace("-", ""));
    try {
      Files.createDirectories(tempRoot);
      List<Definition> ordered = new ArrayList<>(cache.allDefinitions());
      ordered.sort(SNAPSHOT_ORDER);

      List<DiscoveryCacheSnapshotManifest.DefinitionEntry> entries = new ArrayList<>(ordered.size());
      for (Definition definition : ordered) {
        DefinitionEnvelope envelope = requireEnvelope(definition);
        String typeToken = normalizeType(envelope.type());
        String groupToken = envelope.group();
        String nameToken = envelope.name();
        String relativePath =
            DEFINITIONS_DIR
                + "/"
                + encodeSegment(typeToken.toLowerCase())
                + "/"
                + encodeSegment(groupToken)
                + "/"
                + encodeSegment(nameToken)
                + ".json";
        Path definitionFile = tempRoot.resolve(relativePath.replace('/', java.io.File.separatorChar));
        ensureWithinRoot(tempRoot, definitionFile);
        Files.createDirectories(definitionFile.getParent());
        byte[] payload = serializeDefinition(definition);
        Files.write(definitionFile, payload);
        entries.add(
            new DiscoveryCacheSnapshotManifest.DefinitionEntry(
                typeToken, groupToken, nameToken, relativePath, sha256(payload)));
      }

      Instant createdTime = Instant.now();
      DiscoveryCacheSnapshotManifest manifest =
          new DiscoveryCacheSnapshotManifest(
              DiscoveryCacheSnapshotManifest.CURRENT_SCHEMA_VERSION,
              createdTime.toString(),
              entries.size(),
              resolvedMetadata.sessionId(),
              resolvedMetadata.group(),
              resolvedMetadata.appName(),
              resolvedMetadata.instance(),
              entries);
      Path manifestPath = tempRoot.resolve(MANIFEST_FILE);
      Files.write(manifestPath, serializeJson(manifest));
      replaceDirectoryAtomically(tempRoot, target);
      return manifest;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      deleteDirectoryQuietly(tempRoot);
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to dump DiscoveryCache snapshot to " + target, ex);
    }
  }

  public LoadedSnapshot load(Path snapshotRoot, Duration ttl) {
    return load(snapshotRoot, ttl, Instant.now());
  }

  LoadedSnapshot load(Path snapshotRoot, Duration ttl, Instant nowUtc) {
    Path root = normalizeRoot(snapshotRoot);
    Duration normalizedTtl =
        ttl == null || ttl.isNegative() ? null : ttl;
    try {
      Path manifestPath = root.resolve(MANIFEST_FILE);
      if (!Files.exists(manifestPath)) {
        throw new IllegalStateException("Snapshot manifest is missing: " + manifestPath);
      }
      DiscoveryCacheSnapshotManifest manifest =
          MAPPER.readValue(Files.readAllBytes(manifestPath), DiscoveryCacheSnapshotManifest.class);
      if (manifest.schemaVersion() != DiscoveryCacheSnapshotManifest.CURRENT_SCHEMA_VERSION) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "Unsupported snapshot schemaVersion="
                + manifest.schemaVersion()
                + " expected="
                + DiscoveryCacheSnapshotManifest.CURRENT_SCHEMA_VERSION);
      }
      if (manifest.definitionCount() != manifest.definitions().size()) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "Snapshot manifest definitionCount mismatch manifest="
                + manifest.definitionCount()
                + " entries="
                + manifest.definitions().size());
      }
      Instant createdTimeUtc = manifest.createdInstantUtc();
      Instant now = nowUtc == null ? Instant.now() : nowUtc;
      Duration snapshotAge = Duration.between(createdTimeUtc, now);
      if (snapshotAge.isNegative()) {
        snapshotAge = Duration.ZERO;
      }
      if (normalizedTtl != null && snapshotAge.compareTo(normalizedTtl) > 0) {
        throw new IllegalStateException(
            "Snapshot expired createdTimeUtc="
                + createdTimeUtc
                + " nowUtc="
                + now
                + " age="
                + snapshotAge
                + " ttl="
                + normalizedTtl);
      }

      List<Definition> definitions = new ArrayList<>(manifest.definitions().size());
      for (DiscoveryCacheSnapshotManifest.DefinitionEntry entry : manifest.definitions()) {
        Path definitionFile = root.resolve(entry.relativePath().replace('/', java.io.File.separatorChar));
        ensureWithinRoot(root, definitionFile);
        if (!Files.exists(definitionFile)) {
          throw new IllegalStateException("Snapshot definition file is missing: " + definitionFile);
        }
        byte[] payload = Files.readAllBytes(definitionFile);
        String digest = sha256(payload);
        if (!entry.sha256Hex().equalsIgnoreCase(digest)) {
          throw new IllegalStateException(
              "Snapshot definition checksum mismatch path="
                  + entry.relativePath()
                  + " expected="
                  + entry.sha256Hex()
                  + " actual="
                  + digest);
        }
        Definition definition =
            DiscoveryCodec.decode(new String(payload, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
        DefinitionEnvelope envelope = requireEnvelope(definition);
        String typeToken = normalizeType(envelope.type());
        if (!entry.type().equalsIgnoreCase(typeToken)
            || !entry.group().equals(envelope.group())
            || !entry.name().equals(envelope.name())) {
          throw new IllegalStateException(
              "Snapshot definition identity mismatch path="
                  + entry.relativePath()
                  + " manifest="
                  + entry.type()
                  + ":"
                  + entry.group()
                  + "/"
                  + entry.name()
                  + " actual="
                  + typeToken
                  + ":"
                  + envelope.group()
                  + "/"
                  + envelope.name());
        }
        definitions.add(definition);
      }

      return new LoadedSnapshot(root, manifest, createdTimeUtc, snapshotAge, normalizedTtl, definitions);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Failed to load DiscoveryCache snapshot from " + root, ex);
    }
  }

  private static Path normalizeRoot(Path root) {
    Path normalized = Objects.requireNonNull(root, "snapshotRoot").toAbsolutePath().normalize();
    if (normalized.getParent() == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("snapshotRoot must have a parent directory: " + normalized);
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  private static String normalizeType(DefinitionType type) {
    if (type == null || type == DefinitionType.UNKNOWN) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Definition envelope type is required");
    }
    return type.name();
  }

  private static DefinitionEnvelope requireEnvelope(Definition definition) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope =
        definition == null ? null : definition.envelope();
    if (envelope == null
        || Strings.trimToNull(envelope.group()) == null
        || Strings.trimToNull(envelope.name()) == null
        || envelope.type() == null
        || envelope.type() == DefinitionType.UNKNOWN) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Definition envelope requires type/group/name");
    }
    return envelope;
  }

  private static String definitionTypeToken(Definition definition) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = requireEnvelope(definition);
    return envelope.type().name();
  }

  private static String definitionGroupToken(Definition definition) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = requireEnvelope(definition);
    return envelope.group();
  }

  private static String definitionNameToken(Definition definition) {
    DefinitionEnvelope envelope = requireEnvelope(definition);
    return envelope.name();
  }

  private static byte[] serializeDefinition(Definition definition) {
    try {
      String json =
          MAPPER.writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(Objects.requireNonNull(definition));
      return (json.endsWith("\n") ? json : json + "\n").getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to serialize definition", ex);
    }
  }

  private static byte[] serializeJson(Object value) {
    try {
      String json =
          MAPPER.writerWithDefaultPrettyPrinter().writeValueAsString(Objects.requireNonNull(value));
      return (json.endsWith("\n") ? json : json + "\n").getBytes(StandardCharsets.UTF_8);
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to serialize JSON", ex);
    }
  }

  private static String sha256(byte[] payload) {
    try {
      MessageDigest digest = MessageDigest.getInstance("SHA-256");
      return HexFormat.of().formatHex(digest.digest(payload == null ? new byte[0] : payload));
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Unable to compute SHA-256", ex);
    }
  }

  private static String encodeSegment(String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.requireNonBlank(value, "segment");
    StringBuilder encoded = new StringBuilder(normalized.length());
    for (int i = 0; i < normalized.length(); i++) {
      char ch = normalized.charAt(i);
      if ((ch >= 'a' && ch <= 'z')
          || (ch >= 'A' && ch <= 'Z')
          || (ch >= '0' && ch <= '9')
          || ch == '-'
          || ch == '_'
          || ch == '.') {
        encoded.append(ch);
        continue;
      }
      encoded.append('_').append(String.format("%02x", (int) ch));
    }
    return encoded.toString();
  }

  private static void ensureWithinRoot(Path root, Path candidate) {
    Path normalizedRoot = root.toAbsolutePath().normalize();
    Path normalizedCandidate = candidate.toAbsolutePath().normalize();
    if (!normalizedCandidate.startsWith(normalizedRoot)) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Snapshot path escapes root root=" + normalizedRoot + " candidate=" + normalizedCandidate);
    }
  }

  private static void replaceDirectoryAtomically(Path tempRoot, Path targetRoot) throws IOException {
    Path parent = targetRoot.getParent();
    Files.createDirectories(parent);
    Path backupRoot =
        parent.resolve(targetRoot.getFileName() + ".bak-" + UUID.randomUUID().toString().replace("-", ""));
    boolean existingMoved = false;
    boolean completed = false;
    try {
      if (Files.exists(targetRoot)) {
        moveDirectory(targetRoot, backupRoot);
        existingMoved = true;
      }
      moveDirectory(tempRoot, targetRoot);
      completed = true;
    } finally {
      if (completed) {
        deleteDirectoryQuietly(backupRoot);
        return;
      }
      if (existingMoved) {
        try {
          if (Files.exists(targetRoot)) {
            deleteDirectoryQuietly(targetRoot);
          }
          moveDirectory(backupRoot, targetRoot);
        } catch (Exception ignore) {
        }
      }
    }
  }

  private static void moveDirectory(Path source, Path target) throws IOException {
    try {
      Files.move(source, target, StandardCopyOption.ATOMIC_MOVE);
    } catch (AtomicMoveNotSupportedException ex) {
      Files.move(source, target, StandardCopyOption.REPLACE_EXISTING);
    }
  }

  private static void deleteDirectoryQuietly(Path directory) {
    if (directory == null || !Files.exists(directory)) {
      return;
    }
    try (var stream = Files.walk(directory)) {
      stream.sorted(Comparator.reverseOrder()).forEach(path -> closeDelete(path));
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }
  }

  private static void closeDelete(Path path) {
    try {
      Files.deleteIfExists(path);
    } catch (Exception ignore) {
    }
  }

  public record SnapshotMetadata(String sessionId, String group, String appName, String instance) {
    public SnapshotMetadata {
      sessionId = Strings.trimToNull(sessionId);
      group = Strings.trimToNull(group);
      appName = Strings.trimToNull(appName);
      instance = Strings.trimToNull(instance);
    }

    public static SnapshotMetadata empty() {
      return new SnapshotMetadata(null, null, null, null);
    }
  }

  public record LoadedSnapshot(
      Path snapshotPath,
      DiscoveryCacheSnapshotManifest manifest,
      Instant createdTimeUtc,
      Duration age,
      Duration ttl,
      List<Definition> definitions) {
    public LoadedSnapshot {
      snapshotPath = snapshotPath == null ? null : snapshotPath.toAbsolutePath().normalize();
      manifest = Objects.requireNonNull(manifest, "manifest");
      createdTimeUtc = Objects.requireNonNull(createdTimeUtc, "createdTimeUtc");
      age = age == null || age.isNegative() ? Duration.ZERO : age;
      ttl = ttl == null || ttl.isNegative() ? null : ttl;
      definitions = definitions == null ? List.of() : List.copyOf(definitions);
    }
  }
}


FILE: RecoveryManagerImpl.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.recovery.manager;

import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.function.Supplier;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.recovery.RecoveryManager;

public final class RecoveryManagerImpl implements RecoveryManager {
  private final Runnable dumpAction;
  private final Supplier<DiscoveryCacheRecoveryResult> statusSupplier;

  public RecoveryManagerImpl(
      Runnable dumpAction, Supplier<DiscoveryCacheRecoveryResult> statusSupplier) {
    this.dumpAction = Objects.requireNonNull(dumpAction, "dumpAction");
    this.statusSupplier = Objects.requireNonNull(statusSupplier, "statusSupplier");
  }

  @Override
  public void dump() {
    dumpAction.run();
  }

  @Override
  public boolean isRecoveryMode() {
    return status().recoveryUsed();
  }

  @Override
  public RecoveryStatus status() {
    DiscoveryCacheRecoveryResult source = statusSupplier.get();
    if (source == null) {
      return new RecoveryStatus(
          Mode.NOT_STARTED, false, false, "unavailable", "", "", "", "", 0);
    }
    return new RecoveryStatus(
        toMode(source.mode()),
        source.recoveryEnabled(),
        source.recoveryUsed(),
        source.reason(),
        source.snapshotPath() == null ? "" : source.snapshotPath().toString(),
        source.snapshotCreatedTimeUtc() == null ? "" : source.snapshotCreatedTimeUtc().toString(),
        source.snapshotAge() == null ? "" : source.snapshotAge().toString(),
        source.snapshotTtl() == null ? "" : source.snapshotTtl().toString(),
        source.definitionCount());
  }

  private static Mode toMode(DiscoveryCacheRecoveryResult.Mode source) {
    if (source == null) {
      return Mode.NOT_STARTED;
    }
    return switch (source) {
      case NOT_STARTED -> Mode.NOT_STARTED;
      case LIVE -> Mode.LIVE;
      case RECOVERED -> Mode.RECOVERED;
      case FAILED -> Mode.FAILED;
    };
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashSet;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class SchemaModel {
  private static final String DEFAULT_LIFECYCLE_STATUS = "ACTIVE";
  private static final String DEFAULT_VERSION_NAME = "1.0.0";
  private static final int DEFAULT_VERSION_NUM = 1;
  private static final String SCHEMA_FORMAT_TABULAR = "FLOW_TABULAR_V1";
  private static final String SCHEMA_FORMAT_TRANSPORT = "FLOW_TRANSPORT_V1";
  private static final String SCHEMA_FORMAT_MAPPING = "FLOW_MAPPING_V1";
  private static final String SCHEMA_FORMAT_METASET = "FLOW_METASET_V1";

  private final String group;
  private final String name;
  private final SchemaType type;
  private final List<Field> fields;
  private final String schemaFormat;
  private final String hash;
  private final Integer versionNum;
  private final String versionName;
  private final SchemaCompatibility compatibility;
  private final Boolean enabled;
  private final String lifecycleStatus;

  private SchemaModel(Builder builder) {
    this.group = builder.group;
    this.name = builder.name;
    this.type = builder.type;
    this.fields = builder.fields.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(builder.fields);
    this.schemaFormat = builder.schemaFormat;
    this.hash = builder.hash;
    this.versionNum = builder.versionNum;
    this.versionName = builder.versionName;
    this.compatibility = builder.compatibility;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
    this.lifecycleStatus = builder.lifecycleStatus;
  }

  public String getGroup() {
    return group;
  }

  public String getName() {
    return name;
  }

  public SchemaType getType() {
    return type;
  }

  public List<Field> getFields() {
    return fields;
  }

  public String getSchemaFormat() {
    return schemaFormat;
  }

  public String getHash() {
    return hash;
  }

  public Integer getVersionNum() {
    return versionNum;
  }

  public String getVersionName() {
    return versionName;
  }

  public SchemaCompatibility getCompatibility() {
    return compatibility;
  }

  public Boolean getEnabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  public String getLifecycleStatus() {
    return lifecycleStatus;
  }

  public Builder toBuilder() {
    return builder()
        .withGroup(group)
        .withName(name)
        .withType(type)
        .withFields(fields)
        .withSchemaFormat(schemaFormat)
        .withHash(hash)
        .withVersionNum(versionNum)
        .withVersionName(versionName)
        .withCompatibility(compatibility)
        .withEnabled(enabled)
        .withLifecycleStatus(lifecycleStatus);
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public enum FieldType {
    STRING("STRING"),
    BOOL("BOOL"),
    INT32("INT32"),
    INT64("INT64"),
    FLOAT64("FLOAT64"),
    DATE("DATE"),
    TIMESTAMP("TIMESTAMP"),
    BINARY("BINARY");

    private final String token;

    FieldType(String token) {
      this.token = token;
    }

    public String token() {
      return token;
    }

    public static FieldType fromToken(String value) {
      String normalized = Strings.requireNonBlank(value, "field.type").toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
      return switch (normalized) {
        case "STRING", "VARCHAR", "TEXT", "UTF8" -> STRING;
        case "BOOL", "BOOLEAN" -> BOOL;
        case "INT32", "INT", "INTEGER" -> INT32;
        case "INT64", "BIGINT", "LONG" -> INT64;
        case "FLOAT64", "DOUBLE", "FLOAT" -> FLOAT64;
        case "DATE", "DATE32" -> DATE;
        case "TIMESTAMP" -> TIMESTAMP;
        case "BINARY", "VARBINARY", "BYTES" -> BINARY;
        default -> throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported schema field type: " + value);
      };
    }
  }

  public static final class Field {
    private final String name;
    private final FieldType type;
    private final boolean nullable;
    private final String description;

    private Field(Builder builder) {
      this.name = builder.name;
      this.type = builder.type;
      this.nullable = builder.nullable;
      this.description = builder.description;
    }

    public String name() {
      return name;
    }

    public String getName() {
      return name;
    }

    public FieldType type() {
      return type;
    }

    public FieldType getType() {
      return type;
    }

    public boolean nullable() {
      return nullable;
    }

    public boolean isNullable() {
      return nullable;
    }

    public String description() {
      return description;
    }

    public String getDescription() {
      return description;
    }

    public Builder toBuilder() {
      return builder()
          .withName(name)
          .withType(type)
          .withNullable(nullable)
          .withDescription(description);
    }

    public static Builder builder() {
      return new Builder();
    }

    public static final class Builder {
      private String name;
      private FieldType type = FieldType.STRING;
      private boolean nullable = true;
      private String description;

      private Builder() {}

      public Builder withName(String value) {
        this.name = Strings.trimToNull(value);
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withType(FieldType value) {
        this.type = value == null ? FieldType.STRING : value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withNullable(boolean value) {
        this.nullable = value;
        return this;
      }

      public Builder withDescription(String value) {
        this.description = Strings.trimToNull(value);
        return this;
      }

      public Field build() {
        this.name = Strings.requireNonBlank(name, "field.name");
        this.type = Objects.requireNonNull(type, "field.type");
        this.description = Strings.trimToNull(description);
        return new Field(this);
      }
    }
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String group;
    private String name;
    private SchemaType type;
    private final List<Field> fields = new ArrayList<>();
    private String schemaFormat;
    private String hash;
    private Integer versionNum;
    private String versionName;
    private SchemaCompatibility compatibility;
    private Boolean enabled;
    private String lifecycleStatus;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withGroup(String value) {
      this.group = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withName(String value) {
      this.name = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withType(SchemaType value) {
      this.type = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withField(Field value) {
      if (value != null) {
        this.fields.add(value);
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withField(String name, FieldType type, boolean nullable) {
      return withField(Field.builder().withName(name).withType(type).withNullable(nullable).build());
    }

    public Builder withFields(List<Field> values) {
      this.fields.clear();
      if (values != null) {
        for (Field field : values) {
          if (field != null) {
            this.fields.add(field);
          }
        }
      }
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSchemaFormat(String value) {
      this.schemaFormat = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withHash(String value) {
      this.hash = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withVersionNum(Integer value) {
      this.versionNum = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withVersionName(String value) {
      this.versionName = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withCompatibility(SchemaCompatibility value) {
      this.compatibility = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(Boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withLifecycleStatus(String value) {
      this.lifecycleStatus = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public SchemaModel build() {
      this.group = Strings.trimToNull(group);
      this.name = Strings.trimToNull(name);
      this.schemaFormat = Strings.trimToNull(schemaFormat);
      this.hash = Strings.trimToNull(hash);
      this.versionName = Strings.firstNonBlank(versionName, DEFAULT_VERSION_NAME);
      this.versionNum = versionNum == null ? DEFAULT_VERSION_NUM : versionNum;
      this.compatibility = compatibility == null ? SchemaCompatibility.BACKWARDS : compatibility;
      this.enabled = enabled == null ? Boolean.TRUE : enabled;
      this.lifecycleStatus = Strings.firstNonBlank(lifecycleStatus, DEFAULT_LIFECYCLE_STATUS);
      validateFields(fields);
      if (type != null) {
        this.schemaFormat = Strings.firstNonBlank(schemaFormat, schemaFormatForType(type));
      }
      return new SchemaModel(this);
    }

    private static void validateFields(List<Field> values) {
      if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("schema requires at least one field");
      }
      LinkedHashSet<String> names = new LinkedHashSet<>();
      int validated = 0;
      for (Field field : values) {
        if (field == null) {
          continue;
        }
        validated++;
        String normalized = Strings.requireNonBlank(field.getName(), "field.name").toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
        if (!names.add(normalized)) {
          throw new IllegalArgumentException("duplicate field name: " + field.getName());
        }
      }
      if (validated == 0) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("schema requires at least one field");
      }
    }

    private static String schemaFormatForType(SchemaType value) {
      return switch (value) {
        case TABULAR -> SCHEMA_FORMAT_TABULAR;
        case TRANSPORT -> SCHEMA_FORMAT_TRANSPORT;
        case MAPPING -> SCHEMA_FORMAT_MAPPING;
        case METASET -> SCHEMA_FORMAT_METASET;
      };
    }
  }
}


FILE: SchemaModels.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.schema.client.InferredField;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.schema.client.SchemaSampleResult;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class SchemaModels {
  private static final Comparator<InferredField> INFERRED_FIELD_ORDER =
      Comparator.comparing(SchemaModels::fieldNameLower)
          .thenComparing(field -> Strings.requireNonBlank(field.name(), "inferredField.name"));

  private SchemaModels() {}

  public static SchemaModel fromSample(
      String schemaName,
      SchemaType type,
      SchemaCompatibility compatibility,
      SchemaSampleResult sample) {
    String resolvedName = Strings.requireNonBlank(schemaName, "schemaName");
    SchemaSampleResult resolvedSample = java.util.Objects.requireNonNull(sample, "sample");
    SchemaType resolvedType = type == null ? SchemaType.TABULAR : type;
    SchemaCompatibility resolvedCompatibility =
        compatibility == null ? SchemaCompatibility.BACKWARDS : compatibility;
    List<SchemaModel.Field> fields = toFields(resolvedSample.inferredFields());
    return SchemaModel.builder()
        .withName(resolvedName)
        .withType(resolvedType)
        .withCompatibility(resolvedCompatibility)
        .withFields(fields)
        .build();
  }

  private static List<SchemaModel.Field> toFields(List<InferredField> inferredFields) {
    List<InferredField> nonNull = new ArrayList<>();
    if (inferredFields != null) {
      for (InferredField inferredField : inferredFields) {
        if (inferredField != null) {
          nonNull.add(inferredField);
        }
      }
    }
    if (nonNull.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("sample inferredFields must not be empty");
    }
    if (!isDeterministic(nonNull)) {
      nonNull.sort(INFERRED_FIELD_ORDER);
    }
    List<SchemaModel.Field> fields = new ArrayList<>(nonNull.size());
    for (InferredField inferred : nonNull) {
      fields.add(
          SchemaModel.Field.builder()
              .withName(inferred.name())
              .withType(toFieldType(inferred.arrowTypeToken()))
              .withNullable(inferred.nullable())
              .build());
    }
    return List.copyOf(fields);
  }

  private static boolean isDeterministic(List<InferredField> fields) {
    for (int i = 1; i < fields.size(); i++) {
      if (INFERRED_FIELD_ORDER.compare(fields.get(i - 1), fields.get(i)) > 0) {
        return false;
      }
    }
    return true;
  }

  private static SchemaModel.FieldType toFieldType(String arrowTypeToken) {
    String normalized = Strings.requireNonBlank(arrowTypeToken, "inferredField.arrowTypeToken");
    String upper = normalized.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT);
    try {
      return SchemaModel.FieldType.fromToken(upper);
    } catch (IllegalArgumentException ex) {
      return switch (upper) {
        case "INT8", "INT16" -> SchemaModel.FieldType.INT32;
        case "UINT8", "UINT16", "UINT32", "UINT64" -> SchemaModel.FieldType.INT64;
        case "FLOAT16", "FLOAT32", "HALF", "REAL" -> SchemaModel.FieldType.FLOAT64;
        case "DATE64" -> SchemaModel.FieldType.DATE;
        default -> throw ex;
      };
    }
  }

  private static String fieldNameLower(InferredField field) {
    return Strings.requireNonBlank(field.name(), "inferredField.name").toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
  }
}

import java.io.File;

public final class ServiceRunOptions {
  private final String instanceName;
  private final String bindHost;
  private final Integer bindPort;
  private final String advertiseHost;
  private final Integer advertisePort;
  private final Path tlsCertChain;
  private final Path tlsPrivateKey;

  private final boolean proxyMode;

    this.bindHost = Strings.trimToNull(builder.bindHost);
    this.bindPort = builder.bindPort;

    this.tlsTrustCert = builder.tlsTrustCert;

    this.requireClientCertificates = builder.requireClientCertificates;
    this.interceptors =
        builder.interceptors == null || builder.interceptors.isEmpty()
            ? List.of()
            : List.copyOf(builder.interceptors);
    this.datasetIds =
        builder.datasetIds == null || builder.datasetIds.isEmpty()
            ? List.of()
            : List.copyOf(builder.datasetIds);
    this.proxyMode = builder.proxyMode;
    this.preferredRegion = Strings.trimToNull(builder.preferredRegion);
    this.group = Strings.trimToNull(builder.group);
    this.routingKey = Strings.trimToNull(builder.routingKey);
    this.callCount = builder.callCount;
    this.callDelayMillis = builder.callDelayMillis;
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String instanceName;
    private String bindHost;
    private Integer bindPort;
    private String advertiseHost;
    private Integer advertisePort;
    private Path tlsCertChain;
    private Path tlsPrivateKey;
    private Path tlsTrustCert;
    private Path clientTrustCert;
    private boolean requireClientCertificates;
    private List<Object> interceptors = List.of();
    private List<String> datasetIds = List.of();
    private boolean proxyMode;
    private String preferredRegion;
    private String group;
    private String routingKey;
    private Integer callCount;
    private Long callDelayMillis;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withInstanceName(String value) {
      this.instanceName = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withBindHost(String value) {
      this.bindHost = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withBindPort(Integer value) {
      this.bindPort = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withAdvertiseHost(String value) {
      this.advertiseHost = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withAdvertisePort(Integer value) {
      this.advertisePort = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTlsCertChain(Path value) {
      this.tlsCertChain = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTlsPrivateKey(Path value) {
      this.tlsPrivateKey = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTlsCertChain(File value) {
      this.tlsCertChain = value == null ? null : value.toPath();
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTlsPrivateKey(File value) {
      this.tlsPrivateKey = value == null ? null : value.toPath();
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTlsTrustCert(Path trustCertPem) {
      this.tlsTrustCert = trustCertPem;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTlsTrustCert(File trustCertPem) {
      this.tlsTrustCert = trustCertPem == null ? null : trustCertPem.toPath();
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTlsClientTrustCert(Path trustCertPem) {
      this.clientTrustCert = trustCertPem;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTlsClientTrustCert(File trustCertPem) {
      this.clientTrustCert = trustCertPem == null ? null : trustCertPem.toPath();
      return this;
    }

    public Builder requireClientCertificates(boolean value) {
      this.requireClientCertificates = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withInterceptor(Object interceptor) {
      if (interceptor == null) {
        return this;
      }
      if (interceptors.isEmpty()) {
        interceptors = new ArrayList<>();
      } else if (!(interceptors instanceof ArrayList<?>)) {
        interceptors = new ArrayList<>(interceptors);
      }
      interceptors.add(interceptor);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withInterceptors(Collection<?> values) {
      if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
        this.interceptors = List.of();
        return this;
      }
      List<Object> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
      for (Object value : values) {
        if (value != null) {
          normalized.add(value);
        }
      }
      this.interceptors = normalized.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(normalized);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withDatasetIds(Collection<String> values) {
      if (values == null || values.isEmpty()) {
        this.datasetIds = List.of();
        return this;
      }
      List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
      for (String value : values) {
        String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
        if (trimmed != null) {
          normalized.add(trimmed);
        }
      }
      this.datasetIds = normalized.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(normalized);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder addDatasetId(String value) {
      String trimmed = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      if (trimmed == null) {
        return this;
      }
      if (datasetIds.isEmpty()) {
        datasetIds = new ArrayList<>();
      } else if (!(datasetIds instanceof ArrayList<?>)) {
        datasetIds = new ArrayList<>(datasetIds);
      }
      datasetIds.add(trimmed);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withProxyMode(boolean value) {
      this.proxyMode = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withPreferredRegion(String value) {
      this.preferredRegion = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withGroup(String value) {
      this.group = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withRoutingKey(String value) {
      this.routingKey = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withCallCount(Integer value) {
      this.callCount = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withCallDelayMillis(Long value) {
      this.callDelayMillis = value;
      return this;
    }

    public ServiceRunOptions build() {
      return new ServiceRunOptions(this);
    }
  }
}

FILE: ServiceAdvertise.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common;

import java.net.InetAddress;
import java.net.UnknownHostException;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

/** Utilities for resolving and validating routable advertise hosts. */
public final class ServiceAdvertise {

  private ServiceAdvertise() {}

  public static boolean isWildcardHost(String host) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(host);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return true;
    }
    return "*".equals(normalized)
        || "0.0.0.0".equals(normalized)
        || "::".equals(normalized)
        || "[::]".equals(normalized)
        || "0:0:0:0:0:0:0:0".equals(normalized);
  }

  public static String requireRoutableHost(String host, String contextLabel) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(host);
    if (!isWildcardHost(normalized)) {
      return normalized;
    }
    String label = Strings.trimToNull(contextLabel);
    String prefix = label == null ? "Host" : label;
    throw new IllegalStateException(
        prefix + " must be routable; wildcard/blank hosts are not allowed");
  }

  public static String resolveAdvertiseHost(
      String explicitAdvertiseHost, String runtimePlacementHost) {
    return resolveAdvertiseHost(explicitAdvertiseHost, runtimePlacementHost, true);
  }

  public static String resolveAdvertiseHost(
      String explicitAdvertiseHost,
      String runtimePlacementHost,
      boolean allowLocalHostFallback) {
    String explicit = Strings.trimToNull(explicitAdvertiseHost);
    if (!isWildcardHost(explicit)) {
      return explicit;
    }
    String runtime = Strings.trimToNull(runtimePlacementHost);
    if (!isWildcardHost(runtime)) {
      return runtime;
    }
    if (!allowLocalHostFallback) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Cannot resolve advertise host from explicit advertise.host or runtime placement host.");
    }
    String localHost = resolveLocalHost();
    if (!isWildcardHost(localHost)) {
      return localHost;
    }
    throw new IllegalStateException(
        "Cannot resolve advertise host from explicit advertise.host, runtime placement host, or local hostname.");
  }

  public static int resolveAdvertisePort(Integer explicitAdvertisePort, int boundPort) {
    return resolveAdvertisePort(explicitAdvertisePort, boundPort > 0 ? Integer.valueOf(boundPort) : null);
  }

  public static Integer resolveAdvertisePort(
      Integer explicitAdvertisePort, Integer boundPort) {
    if (explicitAdvertisePort != null && explicitAdvertisePort > 0) {
      return explicitAdvertisePort;
    }
    return boundPort != null && boundPort > 0 ? boundPort : null;
  }

  private static String resolveLocalHost() {
    try {
      InetAddress local = InetAddress.getLocalHost();
      return Strings.trimToNull(local.getHostName());
    } catch (UnknownHostException ignore) {
      return null;
    }
  }
}




FILE: ServiceEndpointSelector.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service.ServiceHbCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service.ServiceStatusInstance;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing.ServiceRoutingContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing.ServiceRoutingMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing.ServiceRoutingStrategies;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing.ServiceRoutingState;

public final class ServiceEndpointSelector {
  private ServiceEndpointSelector() {}

  public static ServiceHbCache.Target chooseRoundRobin(ServiceHbCache statusCache, String serviceId) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(statusCache, "statusCache");
    String unavailableMessage = "No available instances for service: " + serviceId;
    ServiceHbCache.Target target =
        statusCache.chooseTargetRoundRobin().orElseThrow(() -> new IllegalStateException(unavailableMessage));
    ServiceAdvertise.requireRoutableHost(target.host, "grpc target host");
    if (target.port <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(unavailableMessage);
    }
    return target;
  }

  public static ServiceHbCache.Target choose(
      ServiceHbCache statusCache,
      String serviceId,
      ServiceRoutingMode routingMode,
      ServiceRoutingContext routingContext,
      ServiceRoutingState routingState) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(statusCache, "statusCache");
    ServiceRoutingMode mode = routingMode == null ? ServiceRoutingMode.ROUND_ROBIN : routingMode;
    if (mode == ServiceRoutingMode.ROUND_ROBIN) {
      return chooseRoundRobin(statusCache, serviceId);
    }
    return choose(listTargets(statusCache), serviceId, mode, routingContext, routingState);
  }

  public static List<ServiceHbCache.Target> listTargets(ServiceHbCache statusCache) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(statusCache, "statusCache");
    return statusCache.listUp().stream().map(ServiceStatusInstance::asTarget).toList();
  }

  public static ServiceHbCache.Target choose(
      List<ServiceHbCache.Target> targets,
      String serviceId,
      ServiceRoutingMode routingMode,
      ServiceRoutingContext routingContext,
      ServiceRoutingState routingState) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(targets, "targets");
    ServiceRoutingMode mode = routingMode == null ? ServiceRoutingMode.ROUND_ROBIN : routingMode;
    if (targets.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("No available instances for service: " + serviceId);
    }
    ServiceRoutingState state = routingState == null ? new ServiceRoutingState() : routingState;
    ServiceHbCache.Target target =
        ServiceRoutingStrategies.strategyFor(mode).select(targets, serviceId, routingContext, state);
    if (target == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("No available instances for service: " + serviceId);
    }
    ServiceAdvertise.requireRoutableHost(target.host, "grpc target host");
    if (target.port <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("No available instances for service: " + serviceId);
    }
    return target;
  }

}


FILE: ServiceInstanceResolver.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common;

import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.concurrent.ConcurrentHashMap;
import java.util.concurrent.ScheduledExecutorService;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.ControlConnection;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.status.service.ServiceHbCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing.ServiceRoutingContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing.ServiceRoutingMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing.ServiceRoutingState;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class ServiceInstanceResolver implements AutoCloseable {
  private static final String NO_AVAILABLE_INSTANCES_PREFIX = "No available instances for service:";
  private static final long INITIAL_DISCOVERY_WAIT_MILLIS = 5000L;
  private static final long INITIAL_DISCOVERY_POLL_MILLIS = 100L;

  @FunctionalInterface
  public interface ServiceCacheFactory {
    ServiceHbCache createServiceHbCache(String group, String serviceName) throws Exception;
  }

  private final ServiceCacheFactory serviceCacheFactory;
  private final Map<String, ServiceHbCache> caches = new ConcurrentHashMap<>();
  private final java.util.Set<String> pendingInitialSelection = ConcurrentHashMap.newKeySet();

  public ServiceInstanceResolver(
      ControlConnection controlPlaneConnection, ScheduledExecutorService statusScheduler) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(controlPlaneConnection, "controlPlaneConnection");
    this.serviceCacheFactory =
        (group, serviceName) -> {
          ServiceHbCache cache =
              new ServiceHbCache(
                  controlPlaneConnection,
                  Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "service group"),
                  Strings.requireNonBlank(serviceName, "service name"),
                  new ServiceHbCache.Config(),
                  statusScheduler);
          boolean success = false;
          try {
            cache.start();
            success = true;
            return cache;
          } finally {
            if (!success) {
              cache.close();
            }
          }
        };
  }

  public ServiceInstanceResolver(ServiceCacheFactory serviceCacheFactory) {
    this.serviceCacheFactory = Objects.requireNonNull(serviceCacheFactory, "serviceCacheFactory");
  }

  public ServiceHbCache.Target chooseRoundRobin(String group, String serviceName, String serviceId) {
    String resolvedGroup = Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "service group");
    String resolvedServiceName = Strings.requireNonBlank(serviceName, "service name");
    String resolvedServiceId = Strings.requireNonBlank(serviceId, "service id");
    String cacheKey = cacheKey(resolvedGroup, resolvedServiceName);
    try {
      ServiceHbCache cache = serviceCache(resolvedGroup, resolvedServiceName);
      try {
        ServiceHbCache.Target selected =
            ServiceEndpointSelector.chooseRoundRobin(cache, resolvedServiceId);
        pendingInitialSelection.remove(cacheKey);
        return selected;
      } catch (IllegalStateException ex) {
        if (INITIAL_DISCOVERY_WAIT_MILLIS <= 0L
            || !isNoAvailableInstancesError(ex)) {
          throw ex;
        }
        if (!pendingInitialSelection.contains(cacheKey)) {
          throw ex;
        }
        return waitForInitialTarget(cacheKey, cache, resolvedServiceId, ex);
      }
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      throw ex;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to resolve service endpoint for service: "
              + resolvedServiceName
              + " ("
              + resolvedServiceId
              + ")",
          ex);
    }
  }

  public ServiceHbCache.Target choose(
      String group,
      String serviceName,
      String serviceId,
      ServiceRoutingMode routingMode,
      ServiceRoutingContext routingContext,
      ServiceRoutingState routingState) {
    ServiceRoutingMode mode = routingMode == null ? ServiceRoutingMode.ROUND_ROBIN : routingMode;
    if (mode == ServiceRoutingMode.ROUND_ROBIN) {
      return chooseRoundRobin(group, serviceName, serviceId);
    }
    String resolvedGroup = Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "service group");
    String resolvedServiceName = Strings.requireNonBlank(serviceName, "service name");
    String resolvedServiceId = Strings.requireNonBlank(serviceId, "service id");
    String cacheKey = cacheKey(resolvedGroup, resolvedServiceName);
    try {
      ServiceHbCache cache = serviceCache(resolvedGroup, resolvedServiceName);
      java.util.List<ServiceHbCache.Target> targets =
          selectTargetsWithInitialWait(cache, cacheKey, resolvedServiceId);
      return ServiceEndpointSelector.choose(
          targets, resolvedServiceId, mode, routingContext, routingState);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      throw ex;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to resolve service endpoint for service: "
              + resolvedServiceName
              + " ("
              + resolvedServiceId
              + ")",
          ex);
    }
  }

  public java.util.List<ServiceHbCache.Target> listTargets(
      String group, String serviceName, String serviceId) {
    String resolvedGroup = Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "service group");
    String resolvedServiceName = Strings.requireNonBlank(serviceName, "service name");
    String resolvedServiceId = Strings.requireNonBlank(serviceId, "service id");
    String cacheKey = cacheKey(resolvedGroup, resolvedServiceName);
    try {
      ServiceHbCache cache = serviceCache(resolvedGroup, resolvedServiceName);
      return selectTargetsWithInitialWait(cache, cacheKey, resolvedServiceId);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      throw ex;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to resolve service endpoint for service: "
              + resolvedServiceName
              + " ("
              + resolvedServiceId
              + ")",
          ex);
    }
  }

  public void ensureServiceCache(String group, String serviceName) {
    String resolvedGroup = Strings.requireNonBlank(group, "service group");
    String resolvedServiceName = Strings.requireNonBlank(serviceName, "service name");
    try {
      serviceCache(resolvedGroup, resolvedServiceName);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      throw ex;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to initialize service status cache for service: "
              + resolvedServiceName
              + " (group="
              + resolvedGroup
              + ")",
          ex);
    }
  }

  private ServiceHbCache serviceCache(String group, String serviceName) throws Exception {
    String cacheKey = cacheKey(group, serviceName);
    ServiceHbCache existing = caches.get(cacheKey);
    if (existing != null) {
      return existing;
    }
    ServiceHbCache created = serviceCacheFactory.createServiceHbCache(group, serviceName);
    if (created == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(
          "Failed to initialize service status cache for service: "
              + serviceName
              + " (group="
              + group
              + ")");
    }
    ServiceHbCache raced = caches.putIfAbsent(cacheKey, created);
    if (raced != null) {
      created.close();
      return raced;
    }
    pendingInitialSelection.add(cacheKey);
    return created;
  }

  private ServiceHbCache.Target waitForInitialTarget(
      String cacheKey, ServiceHbCache cache, String serviceId, IllegalStateException lastError) {
    long deadlineNanos =
        System.nanoTime() + TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS.toNanos(INITIAL_DISCOVERY_WAIT_MILLIS);
    IllegalStateException last = lastError;
    while (System.nanoTime() < deadlineNanos) {
      long remainingNanos = Math.max(0L, deadlineNanos - System.nanoTime());
      long remainingMillis = TimeUnit.NANOSECONDS.toMillis(remainingNanos);
      long sleepMillis = Math.max(1L, Math.min(INITIAL_DISCOVERY_POLL_MILLIS, remainingMillis));
      try {
        Thread.sleep(sleepMillis);
      } catch (InterruptedException interrupted) {
        Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
        throw last;
      }
      try {
        ServiceHbCache.Target selected = ServiceEndpointSelector.chooseRoundRobin(cache, serviceId);
        pendingInitialSelection.remove(cacheKey);
        return selected;
      } catch (IllegalStateException ex) {
        if (!isNoAvailableInstancesError(ex)) {
          throw ex;
        }
        last = ex;
      }
    }
    throw last;
  }

  private java.util.List<ServiceHbCache.Target> selectTargetsWithInitialWait(
      ServiceHbCache cache, String cacheKey, String serviceId) {
    java.util.List<ServiceHbCache.Target> targets = ServiceEndpointSelector.listTargets(cache);
    if (!targets.isEmpty()) {
      pendingInitialSelection.remove(cacheKey);
      return targets;
    }
    if (INITIAL_DISCOVERY_WAIT_MILLIS <= 0L || !pendingInitialSelection.contains(cacheKey)) {
      return targets;
    }
    return waitForInitialTargets(cache, cacheKey, serviceId);
  }

  private java.util.List<ServiceHbCache.Target> waitForInitialTargets(
      ServiceHbCache cache, String cacheKey, String serviceId) {
    long deadlineNanos =
        System.nanoTime() + TimeUnit.MILLISECONDS.toNanos(INITIAL_DISCOVERY_WAIT_MILLIS);
    while (System.nanoTime() < deadlineNanos) {
      long remainingNanos = Math.max(0L, deadlineNanos - System.nanoTime());
      long remainingMillis = TimeUnit.NANOSECONDS.toMillis(remainingNanos);
      long sleepMillis = Math.max(1L, Math.min(INITIAL_DISCOVERY_POLL_MILLIS, remainingMillis));
      try {
        Thread.sleep(sleepMillis);
      } catch (InterruptedException interrupted) {
        Thread.currentThread().interrupt();
        break;
      }
      java.util.List<ServiceHbCache.Target> targets = ServiceEndpointSelector.listTargets(cache);
      if (!targets.isEmpty()) {
        pendingInitialSelection.remove(cacheKey);
        return targets;
      }
    }
    return ServiceEndpointSelector.listTargets(cache);
  }

  private static boolean isNoAvailableInstancesError(IllegalStateException ex) {
    if (ex == null) {
      return false;
    }
    String message = Strings.trimToNull(ex.getMessage());
    return message != null && message.startsWith(NO_AVAILABLE_INSTANCES_PREFIX);
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    for (ServiceHbCache cache : caches.values()) {
      if (cache == null) {
        continue;
      }
      try {
        cache.close();
      } catch (Exception ignore) {
      }
    }
    caches.clear();
    pendingInitialSelection.clear();
  }

  private static String cacheKey(String group, String serviceName) {
    return group + "/" + serviceName;
  }
}


================================================================================
PACKAGE: org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight.ingest
