package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight.ingest;

import java.io.ByteArrayOutputStream;
import java.nio.charset.StandardCharsets;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.regex.Pattern;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.CallStatus;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightDescriptor;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightProducer;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightStream;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.NoOpFlightProducer;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.PutResult;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.VectorSchemaRoot;
import org.apache.arrow.vector.ipc.ArrowStreamWriter;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.cache.DiscoveryCache;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.data.IngestManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.services.ServiceEntitlements;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.headers.FabricRequestHeaders;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.identity.RequestIdentity;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.identity.RequestIdentityResolver;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight.FlightSqlRequestHeadersMiddleware;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight.kerberos.FlightKerberosServerMiddlewareFactory;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.slf4j.Logger;
import org.slf4j.LoggerFactory;

public final class FlightIngestProducer extends NoOpFlightProducer implements AutoCloseable {
  private static final Logger LOGGER = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FlightIngestProducer.class);

  static final int MAX_IPC_BYTES = 64 * 1024 * 1024;
  private static final String COMMAND_PREFIX = "ingest:";
  private static final Pattern INGEST_NAME_PATTERN = Pattern.compile("^[A-Za-z0-9._-]+$");
  private static final String OPERATION_INGEST_PUT = "flight.ingest.put";
  private static final String WRITE_DENIED_PREFIX = "WRITE_DENIED ";

  private final IngestManager ingestManager;
  private final ServiceEntitlements serviceEntitlements;
  private final String serviceResourceId;
  private final DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache;
  private final String runtimeEnvironment;

  public FlightIngestProducer(
      IngestManager ingestManager,
      ServiceEntitlements serviceEntitlements,
      String serviceResourceId,
      DiscoveryCache DiscoveryCache,
      String runtimeEnvironment) {
    this.ingestManager = Objects.requireNonNull(ingestManager, "ingestManager");
    this.serviceEntitlements = Objects.requireNonNull(serviceEntitlements, "serviceEntitlements");
    this.serviceResourceId = Objects.requireNonNull(serviceResourceId, "serviceResourceId");
    this.DiscoveryCache = DiscoveryCache;
    this.runtimeEnvironment = Strings.trimToNull(runtimeEnvironment);
  }

  @Override
  public Runnable acceptPut(
      FlightProducer.CallContext context,
      FlightStream flightStream,
      FlightProducer.StreamListener<PutResult> ackStream) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(flightStream, "flightStream");
    Objects.requireNonNull(ackStream, "ackStream");
    return () -> {
      RequestIdentity identity = resolveIdentity(context);
      RequestIdentityResolver.runAsRequestIdentity(
          identity,
          () -> {
            String subject = identity.effectiveUserSubject();
            String ingestName = requireIngestName(flightStream.getDescriptor());
            authorizeInvoke(subject, ingestName);
            byte[] ipcBytes = readIpcBytes(flightStream, ingestName);
            LOGGER.info("[FlightIngest][request] serviceId={} ingestName={} subject={} bytes={}", serviceResourceId, ingestName, safeSubject(subject), ipcBytes.length);

            try {
              ingestManager.appendIpc(ingestName, ipcBytes);
            } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
              throw mapIngestFailure(ex, ingestName, subject);
            }
            ackStream.onCompleted();
          });
    };
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {}

  private RequestIdentity resolveIdentity(FlightProducer.CallContext context) {
    FlightSqlRequestHeadersMiddleware middleware =
        context == null ? null : context.getMiddleware(FlightSqlRequestHeadersMiddleware.KEY);
    FabricRequestHeaders baseHeaders =
        middleware == null ? FabricRequestHeaders.empty(null) : middleware.requestHeaders();
    String principal = kerberosPrincipal(context);
    FabricRequestHeaders headers = baseHeaders.withAuthenticatedPrincipal(principal);
    try {
      RequestIdentity identity =
          RequestIdentityResolver.resolve(headers, DiscoveryCache, runtimeEnvironment);
      logRequestEntry(identity, middleware);
      return identity;
    } catch (RequestIdentityResolver.ResolutionException ex) {
      throw toFlightRuntime(ex);
    }
  }

  private void logRequestEntry(
      RequestIdentity identity, FlightSqlRequestHeadersMiddleware middleware) {
    String callSummary = middleware == null ? null : middleware.callSummary();
    Map<String, String> headers = middleware == null ? Map.of() : middleware.headerSnapshot();
    LOGGER.info("[Request] transport=ARROW_FLIGHT_INGEST call={} requestId={} caller={} user={} delegatedUser={} headers={}", Strings.firstNonBlank(callSummary, "<unknown>"), identity.requestId(), safeCaller(identity.callerAppSubject()), identity.effectiveUserSubject(), Strings.firstNonBlank(identity.delegatedUserSubject(), "<none>"), headers);
  }

  private void authorizeInvoke(String callerSubject, String ingestName) {
    ServiceEntitlements.Decision decision =
        serviceEntitlements.authorize(
            new ServiceEntitlements.Identity(callerSubject, null),
            new ServiceEntitlements.Request(
                ServiceEntitlements.Transport.ARROW_FLIGHT_INGEST,
                ServiceEntitlements.Action.INVOKE,
                serviceResourceId,
                OPERATION_INGEST_PUT,
                null,
                ingestName,
                Map.of(),
                Map.of()));
    if (decision == null || !decision.allowed()) {
      String reason = decision == null ? "DENIED" : Strings.firstNonBlank(decision.reason(), "DENIED");
      LOGGER.info("[FlightIngest][deny] serviceId={} ingestName={} subject={} reason={}", serviceResourceId, ingestName, safeSubject(callerSubject), reason);
      throw CallStatus.UNAUTHORIZED
          .withDescription(
              reason
                  + " [serviceId="
                  + serviceResourceId
                  + ", ingestName="
                  + ingestName
                  + ", subject="
                  + safeSubject(callerSubject)
                  + "]")
          .toRuntimeException();
    }
  }

  private RuntimeException mapIngestFailure(RuntimeException ex, String ingestName, String subject) {
    if (ex instanceof org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightRuntimeException flightException) {
      return flightException;
    }
    String details = errorContext(ingestName, subject);
    String message = Strings.trimToNull(ex.getMessage());
    if (ex instanceof IllegalArgumentException) {
      return CallStatus.INVALID_ARGUMENT
          .withDescription((message == null ? "Invalid ingest request" : message) + " [" + details + "]")
          .withCause(ex)
          .toRuntimeException();
    }
    if (ex instanceof IllegalStateException) {
      if (message != null && message.startsWith(WRITE_DENIED_PREFIX)) {
        LOGGER.info("[FlightIngest][deny] serviceId={} ingestName={} subject={} reason={}", serviceResourceId, ingestName, safeSubject(subject), message);
        return CallStatus.UNAUTHORIZED
            .withDescription(message + " [" + details + "]")
            .withCause(ex)
            .toRuntimeException();
      }
      if (message != null && message.toLowerCase().contains("access denied for dataset")) {
        LOGGER.info("[FlightIngest][deny] serviceId={} ingestName={} subject={} reason={}", serviceResourceId, ingestName, safeSubject(subject), message);
        return CallStatus.UNAUTHORIZED
            .withDescription(message + " [" + details + "]")
            .withCause(ex)
            .toRuntimeException();
      }
      if (isInvalidArgumentMessage(message)) {
        return CallStatus.INVALID_ARGUMENT
            .withDescription(message + " [" + details + "]")
            .withCause(ex)
            .toRuntimeException();
      }
    }
    LOGGER.error("[FlightIngest][unexpected] {}", details, ex);
    return CallStatus.INTERNAL
        .withDescription((message == null ? "Ingest append failed" : message) + " [" + details + "]")
        .withCause(ex)
        .toRuntimeException();
  }

  private static boolean isInvalidArgumentMessage(String message) {
    String lower = message == null ? "" : message.toLowerCase();
    return lower.contains("unknown ingest")
        || lower.contains("ingest name is required")
        || lower.contains("ingest is disabled")
        || lower.contains("unsupported ingest input.type")
        || lower.contains("ingest datasetid is required")
        || lower.contains("ingest outputschemaid is required")
        || lower.contains("expected schema")
        || lower.contains("schema mismatch")
        || lower.contains("dataset not found")
        || lower.contains("invalid partition value")
        || lower.contains("partition value field")
        || lower.contains("arrow ipc")
        || lower.contains("supports parquet datasets only")
        || lower.contains("supports local filesystem parquet datasets only");
  }

  private static String requireIngestName(FlightDescriptor descriptor) {
    if (descriptor == null) {
      throw CallStatus.INVALID_ARGUMENT
          .withDescription("Flight descriptor is required")
          .toRuntimeException();
    }
    if (!descriptor.isCommand()) {
      throw CallStatus.INVALID_ARGUMENT
          .withDescription("Flight descriptor command is required")
          .toRuntimeException();
    }
    byte[] commandBytes = descriptor.getCommand();
    String command =
        Strings.trimToNull(commandBytes == null ? null : new String(commandBytes, StandardCharsets.UTF_8));
    if (command == null) {
      throw CallStatus.INVALID_ARGUMENT
          .withDescription("Flight descriptor command is required")
          .toRuntimeException();
    }
    if (!command.startsWith(COMMAND_PREFIX)) {
      throw CallStatus.INVALID_ARGUMENT
          .withDescription("Flight descriptor command must start with ingest:")
          .toRuntimeException();
    }
    String ingestName = Strings.trimToNull(command.substring(COMMAND_PREFIX.length()));
    if (ingestName == null || !INGEST_NAME_PATTERN.matcher(ingestName).matches()) {
      throw CallStatus.INVALID_ARGUMENT
          .withDescription("Invalid ingest name in Flight descriptor command")
          .toRuntimeException();
    }
    return ingestName;
  }

  private static byte[] readIpcBytes(FlightStream flightStream, String ingestName) {
    VectorSchemaRoot root = flightStream.getRoot();
    if (root == null
        || root.getSchema() == null
        || root.getSchema().getFields() == null
        || root.getSchema().getFields().isEmpty()) {
      throw CallStatus.INVALID_ARGUMENT
          .withDescription("Arrow stream schema is required for ingestName=" + ingestName)
          .toRuntimeException();
    }

    try (BoundedByteArrayOutputStream out = new BoundedByteArrayOutputStream(MAX_IPC_BYTES);
        ArrowStreamWriter writer = new ArrowStreamWriter(root, null, out)) {
      writer.start();
      while (flightStream.next()) {
        writer.writeBatch();
      }
      writer.end();
      return out.toByteArray();
    } catch (PayloadTooLargeException ex) {
      throw CallStatus.INVALID_ARGUMENT
          .withDescription(
              "Arrow IPC payload exceeds max bytes " + MAX_IPC_BYTES + " for ingestName=" + ingestName)
          .withCause(ex)
          .toRuntimeException();
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      throw ex;
    } catch (Exception ex) {
      throw CallStatus.INTERNAL
          .withDescription("Failed to read Flight doPut stream for ingestName=" + ingestName)
          .withCause(ex)
          .toRuntimeException();
    }
  }

  private String errorContext(String ingestName, String subject) {
    return "serviceId="
        + serviceResourceId
        + ", ingestName="
        + (Strings.trimToNull(ingestName) == null ? "<unknown>" : ingestName)
        + ", subject="
        + safeSubject(subject);
  }

  private static String safeSubject(String subject) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(subject);
    return normalized == null ? "<unknown>" : normalized;
  }

  private static String safeCaller(String callerAppSubject) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(callerAppSubject);
    return normalized == null ? "<none>" : normalized;
  }

  private static String kerberosPrincipal(FlightProducer.CallContext context) {
    if (context == null) {
      return null;
    }
    FlightKerberosServerMiddlewareFactory.ServerMiddleware middleware =
        context.getMiddleware(FlightKerberosServerMiddlewareFactory.KEY);
    return middleware == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(middleware.principal());
  }

  private static RuntimeException toFlightRuntime(RequestIdentityResolver.ResolutionException ex) {
    if (ex.code() == RequestIdentityResolver.Code.PERMISSION_DENIED) {
      return CallStatus.UNAUTHORIZED
          .withDescription(ex.getMessage())
          .withCause(ex)
          .toRuntimeException();
    }
    return CallStatus.UNAUTHENTICATED
        .withDescription(ex.getMessage())
        .withCause(ex)
        .toRuntimeException();
  }

  private static final class BoundedByteArrayOutputStream extends ByteArrayOutputStream {
    private final int maxBytes;

    private BoundedByteArrayOutputStream(int maxBytes) {
      this.maxBytes = maxBytes;
    }

    @Override
    public synchronized void write(int b) {
      ensureCapacityFor(1);
      super.write(b);
    }

    @Override
    public synchronized void write(byte[] b, int off, int len) {
      ensureCapacityFor(len);
      super.write(b, off, len);
    }

    private void ensureCapacityFor(int len) {
      if (len <= 0) {
        return;
      }
      long nextSize = (long) count + len;
      if (nextSize > maxBytes) {
        throw new PayloadTooLargeException("Arrow IPC payload exceeds max bytes " + maxBytes);
      }
    }
  }

  private static final class PayloadTooLargeException extends RuntimeException {
    private PayloadTooLargeException(String message) {
      super(message);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight.ingest;

import java.io.File;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightProducer;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightServerMiddleware;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight.FlightSqlServiceRuntime;

/**
 * Flight ingest runtime that reuses the same server bootstrap path as Flight SQL.
 */
public final class FlightIngestServiceRuntime implements AutoCloseable {
  private final FlightSqlServiceRuntime delegate;

  private FlightIngestServiceRuntime(FlightSqlServiceRuntime delegate) {
    this.delegate = Objects.requireNonNull(delegate, "delegate");
  }

  public static FlightIngestServiceRuntime start(Config cfg, FlightProducer producer) throws Exception {
    Objects.requireNonNull(cfg, "cfg");
    FlightSqlServiceRuntime runtime = FlightSqlServiceRuntime.start(cfg.toDelegate(), producer);
    return new FlightIngestServiceRuntime(runtime);
  }

  public int port() {
    return delegate.port();
  }

  public void blockUntilShutdown() throws InterruptedException {
    delegate.blockUntilShutdown();
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    delegate.close();
  }

  public static final class Config {
    public String bindHost;
    public int bindPort;
    public String advertiseHost;
    public Integer advertisePort;
    public boolean portFailback;
    public int portFailbackAttempts = 5;
    public boolean tlsEnabled;
    public File certChainPem;
    public File privateKeyPem;
    public boolean kerberosEnabled;
    public String kerberosSpn;
    public String kerberosPrincipal;
    public File kerberosKeytab;
    public String kerberosRealm;
    public Map<FlightServerMiddleware.Key<?>, FlightServerMiddleware.Factory<? extends FlightServerMiddleware>>
        middlewares = Map.of();

    private FlightSqlServiceRuntime.Config toDelegate() {
      FlightSqlServiceRuntime.Config cfg = new FlightSqlServiceRuntime.Config();
      cfg.bindHost = bindHost;
      cfg.bindPort = bindPort;
      cfg.advertiseHost = advertiseHost;
      cfg.advertisePort = advertisePort;
      cfg.portFailback = portFailback;
      cfg.portFailbackAttempts = portFailbackAttempts;
      cfg.tlsEnabled = tlsEnabled;
      cfg.certChainPem = certChainPem;
      cfg.privateKeyPem = privateKeyPem;
      cfg.kerberosEnabled = kerberosEnabled;
      cfg.kerberosSpn = kerberosSpn;
      cfg.kerberosPrincipal = kerberosPrincipal;
      cfg.kerberosKeytab = kerberosKeytab;
      cfg.kerberosRealm = kerberosRealm;
      cfg.middlewares = middlewares;
      return cfg;
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.flight.kerberos;

import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Base64;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.CallHeaders;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.CallInfo;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.CallStatus;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightServerMiddleware;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.RequestContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.grpc.GrpcKerberosAcceptor;

public final class FlightKerberosServerMiddlewareFactory
    implements FlightServerMiddleware.Factory<FlightKerberosServerMiddlewareFactory.ServerMiddleware> {
  public static final FlightServerMiddleware.Key<ServerMiddleware> KEY =
      FlightServerMiddleware.Key.of("fabric-flight-kerberos");

  private static final String NEGOTIATE_PREFIX = "Negotiate ";
  private static final String AUTHORIZATION = "authorization";

  private final GrpcKerberosAcceptor acceptor;

  private FlightKerberosServerMiddlewareFactory(GrpcKerberosAcceptor acceptor) {
    this.acceptor = Objects.requireNonNull(acceptor, "acceptor");
  }

  public static FlightServerMiddleware.Factory<ServerMiddleware> login(
      String acceptorPrincipal, Path keytabPath, Path krb5ConfPath) {
    GrpcKerberosAcceptor acceptor =
        GrpcKerberosAcceptor.login(acceptorPrincipal, keytabPath, krb5ConfPath);
    return new FlightKerberosServerMiddlewareFactory(acceptor);
  }

  @Override
  public ServerMiddleware onCallStarted(
      CallInfo callInfo, CallHeaders incomingHeaders, RequestContext requestContext) {
    String authorization = headerValue(incomingHeaders, AUTHORIZATION);
    if (authorization == null) {
      throw CallStatus.UNAUTHENTICATED
          .withDescription("Missing Kerberos Negotiate token")
          .toRuntimeException();
    }
    try {
      byte[] token = decodeNegotiateToken(authorization);
      GrpcKerberosAcceptor.AcceptResult result = acceptor.accept(token);
      if (result == null || !result.established()) {
        throw CallStatus.UNAUTHENTICATED
            .withDescription("SPNEGO accept did not establish context")
            .toRuntimeException();
      }
      String principal = trimToNull(result.sourcePrincipal());
      if (principal == null) {
        throw CallStatus.UNAUTHENTICATED
            .withDescription("Kerberos principal not available")
            .toRuntimeException();
      }
      return new ServerMiddleware(principal);
    } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
      if (ex instanceof org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightRuntimeException) {
        throw ex;
      }
      throw CallStatus.UNAUTHENTICATED
          .withDescription("Kerberos authentication failed")
          .withCause(ex)
          .toRuntimeException();
    }
  }

  private static String headerValue(CallHeaders headers, String key) {
    if (headers == null || key == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String direct = trimToNull(headers.get(key));
    if (direct != null) {
      return direct;
    }
    String normalizedKey = key.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    for (String candidate : headerKeys(headers)) {
      if (candidate != null && candidate.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT).equals(normalizedKey)) {
        String value = trimToNull(headers.get(candidate));
        if (value != null) {
          return value;
        }
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  private static byte[] decodeNegotiateToken(String authorizationHeader) {
    String value = authorizationHeader == null ? "" : authorizationHeader.trim();
    if (!startsWithIgnoreCase(value, NEGOTIATE_PREFIX)) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unsupported authorization scheme; expected Negotiate");
    }
    String tokenPart = value.substring(NEGOTIATE_PREFIX.length()).trim();
    if (tokenPart.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Negotiate token is empty");
    }
    return Base64.getDecoder().decode(tokenPart);
  }

  private static boolean startsWithIgnoreCase(String value, String prefix) {
    if (value.length() < prefix.length()) {
      return false;
    }
    return value.substring(0, prefix.length()).toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT)
        .equals(prefix.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT));
  }

  private static List<String> headerKeys(CallHeaders headers) {
    if (headers == null) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<String> keys = new ArrayList<>();
    headers.keys().forEach(keys::add);
    return keys;
  }

  private static String trimToNull(String value) {
    if (value == null) {
      return null;
    }
    String trimmed = value.trim();
    return trimmed.isEmpty() ? null : trimmed;
  }

  public static final class ServerMiddleware implements FlightServerMiddleware {
    private final String principal;

    private ServerMiddleware(String principal) {
      this.principal = principal;
    }

    public String principal() {
      return principal;
    }

    @Override
    public void onBeforeSendingHeaders(CallHeaders outgoingHeaders) {}

    @Override
    public void onCallCompleted(CallStatus callStatus) {}

    @Override
    public void onCallErrored(Throwable throwable) {}
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.manager;

import io.grpc.ClientInterceptor;
import io.grpc.ForwardingServerCallListener;
import io.grpc.Metadata;
import io.grpc.ServerCall;
import io.grpc.ServerInterceptor;
import io.grpc.Status;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Locale;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.entitlements.core.services.ServiceEntitlements;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.headers.FabricRequestHeaders;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.identity.CallerAppContext;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.identity.CallerAppIdentity;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.identity.RequestIdentity;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.security.identity.RequestIdentityResolver;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceRunOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.grpc.GrpcKerberosContextKeys;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class ServiceManagerImplInterceptors {

  private ServiceManagerImplInterceptors() {}

  static List<ServerInterceptor> extractServerInterceptors(ServiceRunOptions options) {
    if (options == null || Strings.isEmpty(options.interceptors())) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<ServerInterceptor> interceptors = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Object candidate : options.interceptors()) {
      if (candidate == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (candidate instanceof ServerInterceptor interceptor) {
        interceptors.add(interceptor);
      } else {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException(
            "Unsupported gRPC server interceptor type: " + candidate.getClass().getName());
      }
    }
    return interceptors;
  }

  static List<ClientInterceptor> extractClientInterceptors(ServiceRunOptions options) {
    if (options == null || Strings.isEmpty(options.interceptors())) {
      return List.of();
    }
    List<ClientInterceptor> interceptors = new ArrayList<>();
    for (Object candidate : options.interceptors()) {
      if (candidate == null) {
        continue;
      }
      if (candidate instanceof ClientInterceptor interceptor) {
        interceptors.add(interceptor);
      } else {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException(
            "Unsupported gRPC client interceptor type: " + candidate.getClass().getName());
      }
    }
    return interceptors;
  }

  static boolean shouldFallbackToUserSubject(
      ServiceEntitlements.Decision decision,
      String primarySubject,
      String appSubject,
      String userSubject) {
    String normalizedPrimary = Strings.trimToNull(primarySubject);
    String normalizedApp = Strings.trimToNull(appSubject);
    String normalizedUser = Strings.trimToNull(userSubject);
    if (normalizedPrimary == null
        || normalizedApp == null
        || normalizedUser == null
        || normalizedUser.equalsIgnoreCase(normalizedPrimary)) {
      return false;
    }
    if (!normalizedPrimary.equalsIgnoreCase(normalizedApp)) {
      return false;
    }
    return isAbstainDecision(decision);
  }

  static String decisionReason(ServiceEntitlements.Decision decision) {
    if (decision == null) {
      return "DENIED";
    }
    return Strings.trimToNull(decision.reason()) == null ? "DENIED" : decision.reason();
  }

  static boolean decisionAllowed(ServiceEntitlements.Decision decision) {
    return decision != null && decision.allowed();
  }

  static String safeCaller(String callerAppSubject) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(callerAppSubject);
    return normalized == null ? "<none>" : normalized;
  }

  static Map<String, String> snapshotGrpcHeaders(Metadata headers) {
    if (headers == null) {
      return Map.of();
    }
    List<String> keys = new ArrayList<>(headers.keys());
    keys.sort(String.CASE_INSENSITIVE_ORDER);
    LinkedHashMap<String, String> snapshot = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    for (String rawKey : keys) {
      String key = Strings.trimToNull(rawKey);
      if (key == null) {
        continue;
      }
      String normalizedKey = key.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
      if (snapshot.containsKey(normalizedKey)) {
        continue;
      }
      String value;
      if (normalizedKey.endsWith(Metadata.BINARY_HEADER_SUFFIX)) {
        value = "<binary>";
      } else {
        Metadata.Key<String> metadataKey = Metadata.Key.of(key, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER);
        Iterable<String> all = headers.getAll(metadataKey);
        StringBuilder joined = new StringBuilder();
        int count = 0;
        if (all != null) {
          for (String candidate : all) {
            String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(candidate);
            if (normalized == null) {
              continue;
            }
            if (count > 0) {
              joined.append("|");
            }
            joined.append(normalized);
            count++;
            if (count >= 3) {
              break;
            }
          }
        }
        value = count == 0 ? null : joined.toString();
      }
      snapshot.put(normalizedKey, redactHeaderValue(normalizedKey, value));
    }
    return Map.copyOf(snapshot);
  }

  static String startOperationName(ServiceEntitlements.Transport transport) {
    if (transport == ServiceEntitlements.Transport.ARROW_FLIGHT_SQL) {
      return "flight_sql.start";
    }
    if (transport == ServiceEntitlements.Transport.ARROW_FLIGHT_INGEST) {
      return "flight_ingest.start";
    }
    return "grpc.start";
  }

  static String resolveGrpcAuthenticatedPrincipal(
      DefinitionService.IdentityMode identityMode, Metadata headers) {
    String kerberosPrincipal = Strings.trimToNull(GrpcKerberosContextKeys.authenticatedPrincipal());
    if (kerberosPrincipal != null || identityMode != DefinitionService.IdentityMode.APP) {
      return kerberosPrincipal;
    }
    FabricRequestHeaders requestHeaders = FabricRequestHeaders.fromGrpc(headers, null);
    CallerAppIdentity callerApp = requestHeaders.callerApp();
    return callerApp == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(callerApp.asSubject());
  }

  static DefinitionService.IdentityMode resolveGrpcIdentityMode(DefinitionService.Grpc grpc) {
    if (grpc == null || grpc.identityMode() == null) {
      return DefinitionService.IdentityMode.USER;
    }
    return grpc.identityMode();
  }

  static Status statusFor(RequestIdentityResolver.ResolutionException ex) {
    if (ex.code() == RequestIdentityResolver.Code.PERMISSION_DENIED) {
      return Status.PERMISSION_DENIED;
    }
    return Status.UNAUTHENTICATED;
  }

  static <ReqT> ServerCall.Listener<ReqT> scopedServerListener(
      ServerCall.Listener<ReqT> delegate, RequestIdentity identity) {
    return new ForwardingServerCallListener.SimpleForwardingServerCallListener<>(delegate) {
      @Override
      public void onMessage(ReqT message) {
        RequestIdentityResolver.runAsRequestIdentity(identity, () -> super.onMessage(message));
      }

      @Override
      public void onHalfClose() {
        RequestIdentityResolver.runAsRequestIdentity(identity, super::onHalfClose);
      }

      @Override
      public void onCancel() {
        RequestIdentityResolver.runAsRequestIdentity(identity, super::onCancel);
      }

      @Override
      public void onComplete() {
        RequestIdentityResolver.runAsRequestIdentity(identity, super::onComplete);
        CallerAppContext.clear();
      }

      @Override
      public void onReady() {
        RequestIdentityResolver.runAsRequestIdentity(identity, super::onReady);
      }
    };
  }

  private static boolean isAbstainDecision(ServiceEntitlements.Decision decision) {
    if (decision == null || decision.allowed()) {
      return false;
    }
    String reason = Strings.trimToNull(decision.reason());
    return reason != null && reason.toUpperCase(Locale.ROOT).startsWith("ABSTAIN");
  }

  private static String redactHeaderValue(String key, String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      return "<empty>";
    }
    String normalizedKey = Strings.trimToNull(key);
    String token = normalizedKey == null ? "" : normalizedKey.toLowerCase(Locale.ROOT);
    if (token.contains("authorization")
        || token.contains("token")
        || token.contains("cookie")
        || token.contains("set-cookie")) {
      return "<redacted>";
    }
    if (normalized.length() > 256) {
      return normalized.substring(0, 256) + "...";
    }
    return normalized;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.manager;

import io.grpc.BindableService;
import java.io.File;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.Objects;
import java.util.Optional;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionSchema;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionService;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.routing.ServiceRoutingMode;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.ServiceRunOptions;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.services.common.ServiceAdvertise;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

final class ServiceManagerImplRegistry {

  private ServiceManagerImplRegistry() {}

  static DefinitionService requireDefinition(ServiceManagerImpl manager, String name) {
    String serviceName = normalizeServiceName(name);
    if (serviceName == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("service name is required");
    }
    if (manager.session().discoveryCache() == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException("Session must be started before using services");
    }
    String group =
        manager.session().context() == null
            ? null
            : manager.session().context().getGroup();
    Optional<DefinitionService> definition =
        manager.session().discoveryCache().get(DefinitionService.class, group, serviceName);
    if (definition.isEmpty()) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("Unknown service: " + serviceName);
    }
    resolveSchema(manager, definition.get());
    return definition.get();
  }

  static DefinitionService.Grpc requireGrpc(DefinitionService service, String serviceName) {
    if (service == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("service definition is required");
    }
    if (service.serviceType() != null && service.serviceType() != DefinitionService.ServiceType.GRPC) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Service is not gRPC: " + serviceName + " type=" + service.serviceType());
    }
    if (service.grpc() == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("grpc config is required for service: " + serviceName);
    }
    return service.grpc();
  }

  static DefinitionService.Arrow requireArrowFlightSql(
      DefinitionService service, String serviceName) {
    if (service == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("service definition is required");
    }
    if (service.serviceType() != null
        && service.serviceType() != DefinitionService.ServiceType.ARROW_FLIGHT_SQL) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Service is not Arrow Flight SQL: "
              + serviceName
              + " type="
              + service.serviceType());
    }
    if (service.arrow() == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("arrow config is required for service: " + serviceName);
    }
    return service.arrow();
  }

  static DefinitionService.Arrow requireArrowFlightIngest(
      DefinitionService service, String serviceName) {
    if (service == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("service definition is required");
    }
    if (service.serviceType() != DefinitionService.ServiceType.ARROW_FLIGHT_INGEST) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Service is not Arrow Flight ingest: "
              + serviceName
              + " type="
              + service.serviceType());
    }
    if (service.arrow() == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("arrow config is required for service: " + serviceName);
    }
    return service.arrow();
  }

  static boolean isArrowFlightSqlService(DefinitionService service) {
    if (service == null) {
      return false;
    }
    if (service.serviceType() == DefinitionService.ServiceType.ARROW_FLIGHT_SQL) {
      return true;
    }
    return service.serviceType() == null && service.arrow() != null;
  }

  static boolean isArrowFlightIngestService(DefinitionService service) {
    if (service == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return service.serviceType() == DefinitionService.ServiceType.ARROW_FLIGHT_INGEST;
  }

  static BindableService toBindableService(String serviceName, Object implementation) {
    if (implementation instanceof BindableService bindable) {
      return bindable;
    }
    throw new IllegalArgumentException(
        "Service implementation must be io.grpc.BindableService for "
            + serviceName
            + ": "
            + (implementation == null ? "null" : implementation.getClass().getName()));
  }

  static int resolveBindPort(DefinitionService.Grpc grpc, ServiceRunOptions options) {
    Integer bindPortFromDefinition = grpc.bind() == null ? null : grpc.bind().port();
    Integer bindPort = firstNonNull(options.bindPort(), bindPortFromDefinition);
    if (bindPort == null || bindPort <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("grpc.bind.port must be configured and > 0");
    }
    return bindPort;
  }

  static int resolveBindPort(DefinitionService.Arrow arrow, ServiceRunOptions options) {
    Integer bindPortFromDefinition = arrow.bind() == null ? null : arrow.bind().port();
    Integer bindPort = firstNonNull(options.bindPort(), bindPortFromDefinition);
    if (bindPort == null || bindPort <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("arrow.bind.port must be configured and > 0");
    }
    return bindPort;
  }

  static String resolveBindHost(DefinitionService.Grpc grpc, ServiceRunOptions options) {
    String bindHostFromDefinition = grpc.bind() == null ? null : grpc.bind().host();
    String bindHost = firstNonBlank(options.bindHost(), bindHostFromDefinition);
    return bindHost == null ? "0.0.0.0" : bindHost;
  }

  static String resolveBindHost(DefinitionService.Arrow arrow, ServiceRunOptions options) {
    String bindHostFromDefinition = arrow.bind() == null ? null : arrow.bind().host();
    String bindHost = firstNonBlank(options.bindHost(), bindHostFromDefinition);
    return bindHost == null ? "0.0.0.0" : bindHost;
  }

  static String resolveAdvertiseHost(
      ServiceManagerImpl manager, DefinitionService.Grpc grpc, ServiceRunOptions options) {
    String advertiseFromDefinition = grpc.advertise() == null ? null : grpc.advertise().host();
    String bindHostFromDefinition = grpc.bind() == null ? null : grpc.bind().host();
    String runtimePlacementHost = manager.session().runtimePlacementHost();
    String advertiseHost =
        firstNonBlank(options.advertiseHost(), advertiseFromDefinition, bindHostFromDefinition);
    String resolved = ServiceAdvertise.resolveAdvertiseHost(advertiseHost, runtimePlacementHost);
    return ServiceAdvertise.requireRoutableHost(resolved, "grpc advertise host");
  }

  static String resolveAdvertiseHost(
      ServiceManagerImpl manager, DefinitionService.Arrow arrow, ServiceRunOptions options) {
    String advertiseFromDefinition = arrow.advertise() == null ? null : arrow.advertise().host();
    String bindHostFromDefinition = arrow.bind() == null ? null : arrow.bind().host();
    String runtimePlacementHost = manager.session().runtimePlacementHost();
    String advertiseHost =
        firstNonBlank(options.advertiseHost(), advertiseFromDefinition, bindHostFromDefinition);
    String resolved = ServiceAdvertise.resolveAdvertiseHost(advertiseHost, runtimePlacementHost);
    return ServiceAdvertise.requireRoutableHost(resolved, "arrow advertise host");
  }

  static int resolveAdvertisePort(
      DefinitionService.Grpc grpc, ServiceRunOptions options, int bindPort) {
    Integer advertiseFromDefinition = grpc.advertise() == null ? null : grpc.advertise().port();
    Integer advertisePort = firstNonNull(options.advertisePort(), advertiseFromDefinition);
    Integer resolved =
        ServiceAdvertise.resolveAdvertisePort(advertisePort, bindPort > 0 ? bindPort : null);
    if (resolved == null || resolved <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Unable to resolve gRPC target port; configure grpc.bind.port or grpc.advertise.port");
    }
    return resolved;
  }

  static int resolveAdvertisePort(
      DefinitionService.Arrow arrow, ServiceRunOptions options, int bindPort) {
    Integer advertiseFromDefinition = arrow.advertise() == null ? null : arrow.advertise().port();
    Integer advertisePort = firstNonNull(options.advertisePort(), advertiseFromDefinition);
    Integer resolved =
        ServiceAdvertise.resolveAdvertisePort(advertisePort, bindPort > 0 ? bindPort : null);
    if (resolved == null || resolved <= 0) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Unable to resolve Arrow target port; configure arrow.bind.port or arrow.advertise.port");
    }
    return resolved;
  }

  static boolean tlsEnabled(DefinitionService.Grpc grpc) {
    return grpc.tls() != null && Boolean.TRUE.equals(grpc.tls().enabled());
  }

  static boolean tlsEnabled(DefinitionService.Arrow arrow) {
    return arrow.tls() != null && Boolean.TRUE.equals(arrow.tls().enabled());
  }

  static boolean kerberosEnabled(DefinitionService.Grpc grpc) {
    return grpc.kerberos() != null && grpc.kerberos().enabled();
  }

  static boolean kerberosEnabled(DefinitionService.Arrow arrow) {
    return arrow.kerberos() != null && arrow.kerberos().enabled();
  }

  static String sessionKerberosPrincipal(ServiceManagerImpl manager) {
    return Strings.trimToNull(manager.session().kerberosPrincipal());
  }

  static File sessionKerberosKeytab(ServiceManagerImpl manager) {
    Path keytab = manager.session().kerberosKeytab();
    return keytab == null ? null : keytab.toFile();
  }

  static File toFile(Path path) {
    return path == null ? null : path.toFile();
  }

  static <T> T firstNonNull(T first, T second) {
    return first != null ? first : second;
  }

  static <T> T firstNonNull(T first, T second, T third) {
    if (first != null) {
      return first;
    }
    return second != null ? second : third;
  }

  static String firstNonBlank(String... values) {
    return Strings.firstNonBlank(values);
  }

  static ServiceRoutingMode requireGrpcRoutingMode(DefinitionService service, String usage) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(service, "service");
    String serviceId = serviceId(service);
    DefinitionService.Grpc grpc = service.grpc();
    if (grpc == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Invalid routing configuration for serviceId=" + serviceId + ": missing field grpc");
    }
    DefinitionService.Routing routing = grpc.routing();
    if (routing == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Invalid routing configuration for serviceId="
              + serviceId
              + ": missing field grpc.routing (required for "
              + usage
              + ")");
    }
    return ServiceRoutingMode.requireSupported(routing.mode(), serviceId, "grpc.routing.mode", usage);
  }

  static ServiceRoutingMode requireArrowRoutingMode(DefinitionService service, String usage) {
    Objects.requireNonNull(service, "service");
    String serviceId = serviceId(service);
    DefinitionService.Arrow arrow = service.arrow();
    if (arrow == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Invalid routing configuration for serviceId=" + serviceId + ": missing field arrow");
    }
    DefinitionService.Routing routing = arrow.routing();
    if (routing == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException(
          "Invalid routing configuration for serviceId="
              + serviceId
              + ": missing field arrow.routing (required for "
              + usage
              + ")");
    }
    return ServiceRoutingMode.requireSupported(routing.mode(), serviceId, "arrow.routing.mode", usage);
  }

  static String resolveGroupName(ServiceManagerImpl manager) {
    if (manager.session().context() != null) {
      String group = Strings.trimToNull(manager.session().context().getGroup());
      if (group != null) {
        return group;
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  static String requireValue(String value, String label) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized == null) {
      throw new IllegalStateException(label + " is required");
    }
    return normalized;
  }

  static String runningServiceKey(String serviceName, String instanceId) {
    return serviceName + "::" + Strings.nullToEmpty(instanceId);
  }

  static boolean isServiceKeyForName(String key, String serviceName) {
    if (Strings.isBlank(key) || Strings.isBlank(serviceName)) {
      return false;
    }
    return key.equals(serviceName) || key.startsWith(serviceName + "::");
  }

  static String serviceId(DefinitionService service) {
    String resourceId = service == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(service.resourceId());
    if (resourceId != null) {
      return resourceId;
    }
    String group =
        service != null && service.envelope() != null
            ? Strings.trimToNull(service.envelope().group())
            : null;
    String name =
        service != null && service.envelope() != null
            ? Strings.trimToNull(service.envelope().name())
            : null;
    if (group != null && name != null) {
      return "service:" + group + "/" + name;
    }
    return "<unknown>";
  }

  static String resolveServiceName(DefinitionService service) {
    if (service == null || service.envelope() == null) {
      return "<unknown>";
    }
    String name = Strings.trimToNull(service.envelope().name());
    return name == null ? "<unknown>" : name;
  }

  static String resolveGroup(ServiceManagerImpl manager, DefinitionService service) {
    if (service != null && service.envelope() != null) {
      String group = Strings.trimToNull(service.envelope().group());
      if (group != null) {
        return group;
      }
    }
    return manager.session().context() == null
        ? null
        : manager.session().context().getGroup();
  }

  static String normalizeServiceName(String name) {
    return Strings.trimToNull(name);
  }

  static UnsupportedOperationException unsupported(String operation) {
    return new UnsupportedOperationException(operation + " is not implemented yet");
  }

  static Optional<DefinitionSchema> resolveSchema(ServiceManagerImpl manager, DefinitionService service) {
    if (service == null || service.schemaRef() == null) {
      return Optional.empty();
    }
    Optional<DefinitionSchema> schema = manager.session().discoveryCache().getSchema(service.schemaRef());
    if (schema.isEmpty()) {
      manager
          .logger()
          .warn(
              "Service schemaRef not found for resourceId={} schemaRef={}",
              service.resourceId(),
              service.schemaRef());
    }
    return schema;
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.streams;

public interface Stream extends AutoCloseable {

  StreamPublishResult publish(byte[] payload, StreamPublishOptions options);

  default StreamPublishResult publish(byte[] payload) {
    return publish(payload, null);
  }

  default StreamPublishResult publish(Object value) {
    return publish(value, null);
  }

  StreamPublishResult publish(Object value, StreamPublishOptions options);

  StreamSubscription subscribeBytes(StreamBytesListener listener);

  default <T> StreamSubscription subscribe(
      Class<T> targetType, StreamListener<T> listener) {
    return subscribe(targetType, listener, StreamSubscribeOptions.defaults());
  }

  default <T> StreamSubscription subscribe(
      Class<T> targetType, StreamListener<T> listener, StreamSubscribeOptions options) {
    throw new UnsupportedOperationException("Typed stream subscribe is not supported");
  }

  @Override
  default void close() {}
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.streams;

import java.util.List;
import java.util.Optional;

public interface StreamManager {
  void register(StreamModel model);

  default void upsert(StreamModel model) {
    register(model);
  }

  default void delete(String streamName) {
    delete(streamName, DeleteOptions.streamOnly());
  }

  void delete(String streamName, DeleteOptions options);

  Optional<StreamModel> getModel(String streamName);

  List<StreamModel> listModels();

  default boolean exists(String streamName) {
    return getModel(streamName).isPresent();
  }

  default Stream start(String streamName) {
    return start(streamName, StreamRunOptions.defaults());
  }

  Stream start(String streamName, StreamRunOptions options);

  Stream runtime(String streamName);

  List<Stream> runtimes();

  record DeleteOptions(boolean deleteSchemaDefinition) {
    public static Builder builder() {
      return new Builder();
    }

    public static DeleteOptions streamOnly() {
      return builder().build();
    }

    public static DeleteOptions withSchemaDefinition() {
      return builder().withDeleteSchemaDefinition(true).build();
    }

    public static final class Builder {
      private boolean deleteSchemaDefinition;

      public Builder withDeleteSchemaDefinition(boolean value) {
        deleteSchemaDefinition = value;
        return this;
      }

      public DeleteOptions build() {
        return new DeleteOptions(deleteSchemaDefinition);
      }
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.streams;

import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import java.util.Objects;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.schemas.SchemaModel;

public final class StreamModel {
  public static final int INITIAL_VERSION_NUM = 1;
  public static final String INITIAL_VERSION_NAME = "1.0.0";
  public static final String DEFAULT_NAMESPACE = "default";

  private final String name;
  private final String namespace;
  private final String uuid;
  private final boolean enabled;
  private final String lifecycleStatus;
  private final Integer versionNum;
  private final String versionName;
  private final String streamId;
  private final Transport transport;
  private final Address address;
  private final String connectionName;
  private final String schemaName;
  private final String schemaId;
  private final String schemaKey;
  private final SchemaModel schema;
  private final String messageType;
  private final Serde serde;
  private final SchemaCompatibilityMode compatibilityMode;
  private final SchemaResolutionPolicy resolutionPolicy;
  private final List<String> connectionRefs;
  private final List<String> dependencyRefs;

  private StreamModel(Builder builder) {
    this.name = builder.name;
    this.namespace = builder.namespace;
    this.uuid = builder.uuid;
    this.enabled = builder.enabled;
    this.lifecycleStatus = builder.lifecycleStatus;
    this.versionNum = builder.versionNum;
    this.versionName = builder.versionName;
    this.streamId = builder.streamId;
    this.transport = builder.transport;
    this.address = builder.address;
    this.connectionName = builder.connectionName;
    this.schemaName = builder.schemaName;
    this.schemaId = builder.schemaId;
    this.schemaKey = builder.schemaKey;
    this.schema = builder.schema;
    this.messageType = builder.messageType;
    this.serde = builder.serde;
    this.compatibilityMode = builder.compatibilityMode;
    this.resolutionPolicy = builder.resolutionPolicy;
    this.connectionRefs =
        builder.connectionRefs.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(builder.connectionRefs);
    this.dependencyRefs =
        builder.dependencyRefs.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(builder.dependencyRefs);
  }

  public String name() {
    return name;
  }

  public String namespace() {
    return namespace;
  }

  public String uuid() {
    return uuid;
  }

  public boolean enabled() {
    return enabled;
  }

  public String lifecycleStatus() {
    return lifecycleStatus;
  }

  public Integer versionNum() {
    return versionNum;
  }

  public String versionName() {
    return versionName;
  }

  public String streamId() {
    return streamId;
  }

  public Transport transport() {
    return transport;
  }

  public Address address() {
    return address;
  }

  public String connectionName() {
    return connectionName;
  }

  public String schemaName() {
    return schemaName;
  }

  public String schemaId() {
    return schemaId;
  }

    return schemaKey;

    return schema;

    return messageType;

    return serde;

    return compatibilityMode;
  }

    return resolutionPolicy;
  }

  public List<String> connectionRefs() {
    return connectionRefs;
  }

  public List<String> dependencyRefs() {
    return dependencyRefs;
  }

  public Builder toBuilder() {
    return builder()
        .withName(name)
        .withNamespace(namespace)
        .withUuid(uuid)
        .withEnabled(enabled)
        .withLifecycleStatus(lifecycleStatus)
        .withVersionNum(versionNum)
        .withVersionName(versionName)
        .withStreamId(streamId)
        .withTransport(transport)
        .withAddress(address)
        .withConnectionName(connectionName)
        .withSchemaName(schemaName)
        .withSchemaId(schemaId)
        .withSchemaKey(schemaKey)
        .withSchema(schema)
        .withMessageType(messageType)
        .withSerde(serde)
        .withCompatibilityMode(compatibilityMode)
        .withResolutionPolicy(resolutionPolicy)
        .withConnectionRefs(connectionRefs)
        .withDependencyRefs(dependencyRefs);
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public static String buildStreamId(String group, String namespace, String name) {
    String resolvedGroup = Strings.trimToNull(group);
    String resolvedNamespace = Strings.trimToNull(namespace);
    String resolvedName = Strings.trimToNull(name);
    if (resolvedGroup == null || resolvedNamespace == null || resolvedName == null) {
      return null;
    }
    return "stream:" + resolvedGroup + "/" + resolvedNamespace + "/" + resolvedName;
  }

  public enum Transport {
    AMPS
  }

  public enum Serde {
    NVFIX,
    JSON,
    PROTOBUF,
    BYTES
  }

  public enum SchemaCompatibilityMode {
    NONE,
    BACKWARD,
    FORWARD,
    FULL,
    TRANSITIVE_BACKWARD,
    TRANSITIVE_FULL
  }

  public enum SchemaResolutionPolicy {
    EXACT_ID,
    LATEST,
    COMPATIBLE
  }

  public record Address(String topic, String channel, String streamId) {
    public Address {
      topic = Strings.trimToNull(topic);
      channel = Strings.trimToNull(channel);
      streamId = Strings.trimToNull(streamId);
    }

    public static Address topic(String topic) {
      return new Address(topic, null, null);
    }
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private String name;
    private String namespace = DEFAULT_NAMESPACE;
    private String uuid;
    private boolean enabled = true;
    private String lifecycleStatus = "ACTIVE";
    private Integer versionNum = INITIAL_VERSION_NUM;
    private String versionName = INITIAL_VERSION_NAME;
    private String streamId;
    private Transport transport = Transport.AMPS;
    private Address address;
    private String connectionName;
    private String schemaName;
    private String schemaId;
    private String schemaKey;
    private SchemaModel schema;
    private String messageType;
    private Serde serde = Serde.JSON;
    private SchemaCompatibilityMode compatibilityMode = SchemaCompatibilityMode.BACKWARD;
    private SchemaResolutionPolicy resolutionPolicy = SchemaResolutionPolicy.COMPATIBLE;
    private List<String> connectionRefs = List.of();
    private List<String> dependencyRefs = List.of();

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withName(String value) {
      this.name = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withNamespace(String value) {
      this.namespace = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withUuid(String value) {
      this.uuid = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withEnabled(boolean value) {
      this.enabled = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withLifecycleStatus(String value) {
      this.lifecycleStatus = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withVersionNum(Integer value) {
      this.versionNum = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withVersionName(String value) {
      this.versionName = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withStreamId(String value) {
      this.streamId = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTransport(Transport value) {
      this.transport = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withAddress(Address value) {
      this.address = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withTopic(String value) {
      this.address = Address.topic(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withConnectionName(String value) {
      this.connectionName = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSchemaName(String value) {
      this.schemaName = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSchemaId(String value) {
      this.schemaId = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSchemaKey(String value) {
      this.schemaKey = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSchema(SchemaModel value) {
      this.schema = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMessageType(String value) {
      this.messageType = Strings.trimToNull(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSerde(Serde value) {
      this.serde = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withCompatibilityMode(SchemaCompatibilityMode value) {
      this.compatibilityMode = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withResolutionPolicy(SchemaResolutionPolicy value) {
      this.resolutionPolicy = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withConnectionRefs(List<String> value) {
      this.connectionRefs = normalizeRefs(value);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withDependencyRefs(List<String> value) {
      this.dependencyRefs = normalizeRefs(value);
      return this;
    }

    public StreamModel build() {
      this.name = Strings.requireNonBlank(name, "stream.name");
      this.namespace = Strings.firstNonBlank(namespace, DEFAULT_NAMESPACE);
      this.uuid = Strings.trimToNull(uuid);
      this.lifecycleStatus = Strings.firstNonBlank(lifecycleStatus, "ACTIVE");
      this.versionNum = versionNum == null || versionNum <= 0 ? INITIAL_VERSION_NUM : versionNum;
      this.versionName = Strings.firstNonBlank(versionName, INITIAL_VERSION_NAME);
      this.transport = transport == null ? Transport.AMPS : transport;
      this.connectionName = Strings.requireNonBlank(connectionName, "stream.connectionName");
      this.serde = Objects.requireNonNull(serde, "stream.serde");
      this.compatibilityMode =
          compatibilityMode == null ? SchemaCompatibilityMode.BACKWARD : compatibilityMode;
      this.resolutionPolicy =
          resolutionPolicy == null ? SchemaResolutionPolicy.COMPATIBLE : resolutionPolicy;
      this.address = Objects.requireNonNull(address, "stream.address");
      String topic = Strings.trimToNull(address.topic());
      if (topic == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException("stream.address.topic is required");
      }
      this.address = new Address(topic, address.channel(), address.streamId());
      this.streamId = Strings.trimToNull(streamId);
      this.schemaName = Strings.trimToNull(schemaName);
      this.schemaId = Strings.trimToNull(schemaId);
      this.schemaKey = Strings.trimToNull(schemaKey);
      this.messageType = Strings.trimToNull(messageType);
      this.connectionRefs = normalizeRefs(connectionRefs);
      this.dependencyRefs = normalizeRefs(dependencyRefs);
      if (serde != Serde.BYTES
          && schema == null
          && schemaName == null
          && schemaKey == null
          && schemaId == null) {
        throw new IllegalArgumentException(
            "stream schema is required for serde " + serde.name());
      }
      return new StreamModel(this);
    }

    private static List<String> normalizeRefs(List<String> refs) {
      if (refs == null || refs.isEmpty()) {
        return List.of();
      }
      List<String> normalized = new ArrayList<>();
      for (String ref : refs) {
        String value = Strings.trimToNull(ref);
        if (value != null) {
          normalized.add(value);
        }
      }
      return normalized.isEmpty() ? List.of() : List.copyOf(normalized);
    }
  }
}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.streams;

import java.util.LinkedHashMap;
import java.util.Map;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class StreamPublishOptions {
  private final Map<String, byte[]> headers;
  private final String schemaId;
  private final String messageType;
  private final String contentType;

  private StreamPublishOptions(Builder builder) {
    this.headers = builder.headers.isEmpty() ? Map.of() : Map.copyOf(builder.headers);
    this.schemaId = Strings.trimToNull(builder.schemaId);
    this.messageType = Strings.trimToNull(builder.messageType);
    this.contentType = Strings.trimToNull(builder.contentType);
  }

  public Map<String, byte[]> headers() {
    return headers;
  }

  public String schemaId() {
    return schemaId;
  }

  public String messageType() {
    return messageType;
  }

  public String contentType() {
    return contentType;
  }

  public static Builder builder() {
    return new Builder();
  }

  public static final class Builder {
    private final Map<String, byte[]> headers = new LinkedHashMap<>();
    private String schemaId;
    private String messageType;
    private String contentType;

    private Builder() {}

    public Builder withHeaders(Map<String, byte[]> values) {
      if (Strings.isEmpty(values)) {
        return this;
      }
      values.forEach(this::withHeader);
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withHeader(String key, byte[] value) {
      String trimmedKey = Strings.trimToNull(key);
      if (trimmedKey == null || value == null) {
        return this;
      }
      headers.put(trimmedKey, value.clone());
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withSchemaId(String value) {
      this.schemaId = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withMessageType(String value) {
      this.messageType = value;
      return this;
    }

    public Builder withContentType(String value) {
      this.contentType = value;
      return this;
    }

    public StreamPublishOptions build() {
      return new StreamPublishOptions(this);
    }
  }
}

FILE: FabricArrowFlightOtel.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.manager;

import io.opentelemetry.api.common.Attributes;
import io.opentelemetry.api.trace.Span;
import io.opentelemetry.api.trace.SpanKind;
import java.lang.reflect.InvocationHandler;
import java.lang.reflect.InvocationTargetException;
import java.lang.reflect.Method;
import java.lang.reflect.Proxy;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.List;
import org.apache.arrow.flight.FlightProducer;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.OtelManager;

public final class FabricArrowFlightOtel {
  private FabricArrowFlightOtel() {}

  public static FlightProducer instrumentServer(
      OtelManager runtime,
      FlightProducer delegate,
      String group,
      String appName,
      String serviceName,
      String transport) {
    if (runtime == null || !runtime.enabled() || delegate == null) {
      return delegate;
    }
    List<Class<?>> interfaces = new ArrayList<>();
    interfaces.add(FlightProducer.class);
    if (delegate instanceof AutoCloseable) {
      interfaces.add(AutoCloseable.class);
    }
    InvocationHandler handler =
        (proxy, method, args) ->
            invoke(runtime, delegate, method, args, group, appName, serviceName, transport);
    Object proxied =
        Proxy.newProxyInstance(
            delegate.getClass().getClassLoader(), interfaces.toArray(new Class<?>[0]), handler);
    return (FlightProducer) proxied;
  }

  private static Object invoke(
      OtelManager runtime,
      FlightProducer delegate,
      Method method,
      Object[] args,
      String group,
      String appName,
      String serviceName,
      String transport)
      throws Throwable {
    if (method.getDeclaringClass() == Object.class) {
      return method.invoke(delegate, args);
    }
    String name = method.getName();
    if ("close".equals(name)) {
      return method.invoke(delegate, args);
    }
    Attributes base =
        FabricOtelAttributes.common(group, appName, serviceName, transport, null, name);
    long startedAt = System.nanoTime();
    Span span =
        FabricOtelSupport.startSpan(
            runtime,
            "fabric." + transport + ".server." + name,
            SpanKind.SERVER,
            base);
    boolean finished = false;
    try {
      Object result = method.invoke(delegate, args);
      FabricOtelSupport.endSpan(runtime, span, base, startedAt, null);
      finished = true;
      return result;
    } catch (InvocationTargetException ex) {
      Throwable cause = ex.getCause() == null ? ex : ex.getCause();
      FabricOtelSupport.endSpan(runtime, span, base, startedAt, cause);
      finished = true;
      throw cause;
    } catch (Throwable ex) {
      FabricOtelSupport.endSpan(runtime, span, base, startedAt, ex);
      finished = true;
      throw ex;
    } finally {
      if (!finished) {
        FabricOtelSupport.endSpan(runtime, span, base, startedAt, null);
      }
    }
  }
}


FILE: FabricGrpcOtelInterceptors.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.manager;

import io.grpc.ClientCall;
import io.grpc.ClientInterceptor;
import io.grpc.ForwardingClientCall;
import io.grpc.ForwardingClientCallListener;
import io.grpc.ForwardingServerCall;
import io.grpc.ForwardingServerCallListener;
import io.grpc.Metadata;
import io.grpc.ServerCall;
import io.grpc.ServerCallHandler;
import io.grpc.ServerInterceptor;
import io.grpc.Status;
import io.opentelemetry.api.common.Attributes;
import io.opentelemetry.api.trace.Span;
import io.opentelemetry.api.trace.SpanKind;
import io.opentelemetry.context.Context;
import io.opentelemetry.context.Scope;
import io.opentelemetry.context.propagation.TextMapGetter;
import io.opentelemetry.context.propagation.TextMapSetter;
import java.util.concurrent.atomic.AtomicBoolean;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.OtelManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class FabricGrpcOtelInterceptors {
  private static final TextMapSetter<Metadata> METADATA_SETTER =
      (carrier, key, value) -> {
        if (carrier == null || key == null || value == null) {
          return;
        }
        carrier.put(Metadata.Key.of(key, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER), value);
      };
  private static final TextMapGetter<Metadata> METADATA_GETTER =
      new TextMapGetter<>() {
        @Override
        public Iterable<String> keys(Metadata carrier) {
          return carrier == null ? java.util.List.of() : carrier.keys();
        }

        @Override
        public String get(Metadata carrier, String key) {
          if (carrier == null || key == null) {
            return null;
          }
          return carrier.get(Metadata.Key.of(key, Metadata.ASCII_STRING_MARSHALLER));
        }
      };

  private FabricGrpcOtelInterceptors() {}

  public static ClientInterceptor client(
      OtelManager runtime, String group, String appName, String serviceName) {
    return new ClientInterceptor() {
      @Override
      public <ReqT, RespT> ClientCall<ReqT, RespT> interceptCall(
          io.grpc.MethodDescriptor<ReqT, RespT> method,
          io.grpc.CallOptions callOptions,
          io.grpc.Channel next) {
        String endpoint = method == null ? "<unknown>" : Strings.firstNonBlank(method.getFullMethodName(), "<unknown>");
        Attributes base =
            FabricOtelAttributes.common(group, appName, serviceName, "grpc", null, endpoint);
        long startedAt = System.nanoTime();
        Context parent = Context.current();
        Span span =
            FabricOtelSupport.startSpan(
                runtime, "fabric.grpc.client", SpanKind.CLIENT, base, parent);
        Context spanContext = span == null ? parent : parent.with(span);
        AtomicBoolean ended = new AtomicBoolean(false);

        ClientCall<ReqT, RespT> delegate = next.newCall(method, callOptions);
        return new ForwardingClientCall.SimpleForwardingClientCall<>(delegate) {
          @Override
          public void start(Listener<RespT> responseListener, Metadata headers) {
            Metadata outgoing = headers == null ? new Metadata() : headers;
            runtime
                .openTelemetry()
                .getPropagators()
                .getTextMapPropagator()
                .inject(spanContext, outgoing, METADATA_SETTER);
            Listener<RespT> wrapped =
                new ForwardingClientCallListener.SimpleForwardingClientCallListener<>(
                    responseListener) {
                  @Override
                  public void onClose(Status status, Metadata trailers) {
                    finish(status, null);
                    super.onClose(status, trailers);
                  }
                };
            try (Scope ignored = spanContext.makeCurrent()) {
              super.start(wrapped, outgoing);
            } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
              finish(Status.UNKNOWN, ex);
              throw ex;
            }
          }

          @Override
          public void cancel(String message, Throwable cause) {
            finish(Status.CANCELLED, cause);
            super.cancel(message, cause);
          }

          private void finish(Status status, Throwable explicitError) {
            if (!ended.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
              return;
            }
            Throwable error = explicitError;
            if (error == null && status != null && !status.isOk()) {
              error =
                  new IllegalStateException(
                      status.getCode().name() + ":" + Strings.firstNonBlank(status.getDescription(), ""));
            }
            FabricOtelSupport.endSpan(runtime, span, base, startedAt, error);
          }
        };
      }
    };
  }

  public static ServerInterceptor server(
      OtelManager runtime, String group, String appName, String serviceName) {
    return new ServerInterceptor() {
      @Override
      public <ReqT, RespT> ServerCall.Listener<ReqT> interceptCall(
          ServerCall<ReqT, RespT> call,
          Metadata headers,
          ServerCallHandler<ReqT, RespT> next) {
        String endpoint =
            call == null || call.getMethodDescriptor() == null
                ? "<unknown>"
                : Strings.firstNonBlank(call.getMethodDescriptor().getFullMethodName(), "<unknown>");
        Attributes base =
            FabricOtelAttributes.common(group, appName, serviceName, "grpc", null, endpoint);
        long startedAt = System.nanoTime();
        Context extracted =
            runtime
                .openTelemetry()
                .getPropagators()
                .getTextMapPropagator()
                .extract(Context.current(), headers, METADATA_GETTER);
        Span span =
            FabricOtelSupport.startSpan(
                runtime, "fabric.grpc.server", SpanKind.SERVER, base, extracted);
        Context spanContext = span == null ? extracted : extracted.with(span);
        AtomicBoolean ended = new AtomicBoolean(false);
        java.util.function.BiConsumer<Status, Throwable> finish =
            (status, explicitError) -> {
              if (!ended.compareAndSet(false, true)) {
                return;
              }
              Throwable error = explicitError;
              if (error == null && status != null && !status.isOk()) {
                error =
                    new IllegalStateException(
                        status.getCode().name()
                            + ":"
                            + Strings.firstNonBlank(status.getDescription(), ""));
              }
              FabricOtelSupport.endSpan(runtime, span, base, startedAt, error);
            };

        ServerCall<ReqT, RespT> wrappedCall =
            new ForwardingServerCall.SimpleForwardingServerCall<>(call) {
              @Override
              public void close(Status status, Metadata trailers) {
                finish.accept(status, null);
                super.close(status, trailers);
              }
            };
        try (Scope ignored = spanContext.makeCurrent()) {
          ServerCall.Listener<ReqT> delegate = next.startCall(wrappedCall, headers);
          return new ForwardingServerCallListener.SimpleForwardingServerCallListener<>(delegate) {
            @Override
            public void onMessage(ReqT message) {
              try (Scope ignored = spanContext.makeCurrent()) {
                super.onMessage(message);
              }
            }

            @Override
              public void onHalfClose() {
                try (Scope ignored = spanContext.makeCurrent()) {
                  super.onHalfClose();
                } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
                  finish.accept(Status.UNKNOWN, ex);
                  throw ex;
                }
              }

            @Override
              public void onCancel() {
                try (Scope ignored = spanContext.makeCurrent()) {
                  super.onCancel();
                } finally {
                  finish.accept(Status.CANCELLED, null);
                }
              }

            @Override
              public void onComplete() {
                try (Scope ignored = spanContext.makeCurrent()) {
                  super.onComplete();
                } finally {
                  finish.accept(Status.OK, null);
                }
              }

            @Override
            public void onReady() {
              try (Scope ignored = spanContext.makeCurrent()) {
                super.onReady();
              }
            }
          };
        } catch (RuntimeException ex) {
          finish.accept(Status.UNKNOWN, ex);
          throw ex;
        }
      }
    };
  }
}


FILE: FabricOtelAttributes.java
