package org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.manager;

import io.opentelemetry.api.common.AttributeKey;
import io.opentelemetry.api.common.Attributes;
import io.opentelemetry.api.common.AttributesBuilder;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class FabricOtelAttributes {
  public static final AttributeKey<String> FABRIC_GROUP = AttributeKey.stringKey("fabric.group");
  public static final AttributeKey<String> FABRIC_APP_NAME =
      AttributeKey.stringKey("fabric.app.name");
  public static final AttributeKey<String> FABRIC_SERVICE_NAME =
      AttributeKey.stringKey("fabric.service.name");
  public static final AttributeKey<String> FABRIC_TRANSPORT =
      AttributeKey.stringKey("fabric.transport");
  public static final AttributeKey<String> FABRIC_SUBJECT =
      AttributeKey.stringKey("fabric.subject");
  public static final AttributeKey<String> FABRIC_ENDPOINT =
      AttributeKey.stringKey("fabric.endpoint");
  public static final AttributeKey<String> FABRIC_OUTCOME =
      AttributeKey.stringKey("fabric.outcome");

  private FabricOtelAttributes() {}

  public static Attributes common(
      String group,
      String appName,
      String serviceName,
      String transport,
      String subject,
      String endpoint) {
    AttributesBuilder builder = Attributes.builder();
    putIfPresent(builder, FABRIC_GROUP, group);
    putIfPresent(builder, FABRIC_APP_NAME, appName);
    putIfPresent(builder, FABRIC_SERVICE_NAME, serviceName);
    putIfPresent(builder, FABRIC_TRANSPORT, transport);
    putIfPresent(builder, FABRIC_SUBJECT, subject);
    putIfPresent(builder, FABRIC_ENDPOINT, endpoint);
    return builder.build();
  }

  public static Attributes withOutcome(Attributes base, boolean success) {
    AttributesBuilder builder = Attributes.builder();
    if (base != null) {
      builder.putAll(base);
    }
    builder.put(FABRIC_OUTCOME, success ? "success" : "error");
    return builder.build();
  }

  private static void putIfPresent(
      AttributesBuilder builder, AttributeKey<String> key, String value) {
    String normalized = Strings.trimToNull(value);
    if (normalized != null) {
      builder.put(key, normalized);
    }
  }
}



FILE: FabricOtelEnablement.java
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
package org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.manager;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvironment;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionService;

public final class FabricOtelEnablement {
  private FabricOtelEnablement() {}

  public static boolean isEnvironmentOtelEnabled(DefinitionEnvironment environment) {
    DefinitionEnvironment.Otel otel = environment == null ? null : environment.otel();
    if (otel == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return Boolean.TRUE.equals(otel.enabled());
  }

  public static boolean isAppOtelEnabled(DefinitionApp app) {
    if (app == null || app.otel() == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return Boolean.TRUE.equals(app.otel().enabled());
  }

  public static boolean isServiceOtelEnabled(DefinitionService service) {
    if (service == null || service.otel() == null) {
      return false;
    }
    return Boolean.TRUE.equals(service.otel().enabled());
  }

  public static boolean isGrpcClientTracingEnabled(DefinitionService service) {
    DefinitionService.Otel otel = service == null ? null : service.otel();
    return isServiceTransportEnabled(service, otel == null ? null : otel.grpcClientTracing());
  }

  public static boolean isGrpcServerTracingEnabled(DefinitionService service) {
    DefinitionService.Otel otel = service == null ? null : service.otel();
    return isServiceTransportEnabled(service, otel == null ? null : otel.grpcServerTracing());
  }

  public static boolean isArrowFlightClientTracingEnabled(DefinitionService service) {
    DefinitionService.Otel otel = service == null ? null : service.otel();
    return isServiceTransportEnabled(
        service, otel == null ? null : otel.arrowFlightClientTracing());
  }

  public static boolean isArrowFlightServerTracingEnabled(DefinitionService service) {
    DefinitionService.Otel otel = service == null ? null : service.otel();
    return isServiceTransportEnabled(
        service, otel == null ? null : otel.arrowFlightServerTracing());
  }

  public static boolean isArrowFlightSqlClientTracingEnabled(DefinitionService service) {
    DefinitionService.Otel otel = service == null ? null : service.otel();
    return isServiceTransportEnabled(
        service, otel == null ? null : otel.arrowFlightSqlClientTracing());
  }

  public static boolean isArrowFlightSqlServerTracingEnabled(DefinitionService service) {
    DefinitionService.Otel otel = service == null ? null : service.otel();
    return isServiceTransportEnabled(
        service, otel == null ? null : otel.arrowFlightSqlServerTracing());
  }

  private static boolean isServiceTransportEnabled(DefinitionService service, Boolean value) {
    if (!isServiceOtelEnabled(service)) {
      return false;
    }
    return value == null || Boolean.TRUE.equals(value);
  }
}



FILE: FabricOtelSupport.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.manager;

import io.opentelemetry.api.common.Attributes;
import io.opentelemetry.api.trace.Span;
import io.opentelemetry.api.trace.SpanKind;
import io.opentelemetry.api.trace.StatusCode;
import io.opentelemetry.context.Context;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.OtelManager;

public final class FabricOtelSupport {
  private FabricOtelSupport() {}

  public static Span startSpan(
      OtelManager runtime, String spanName, SpanKind kind, Attributes attributes) {
    return startSpan(runtime, spanName, kind, attributes, Context.current());
  }

  public static Span startSpan(
      OtelManager runtime,
      String spanName,
      SpanKind kind,
      Attributes attributes,
      Context parentContext) {
    if (runtime == null || !runtime.enabled() || !runtime.tracesEnabled()) {
      return null;
    }
    Context parent = parentContext == null ? Context.current() : parentContext;
    Span span = runtime.tracer().spanBuilder(spanName).setSpanKind(kind).setParent(parent).startSpan();
    if (attributes != null) {
      span.setAllAttributes(attributes);
    }
    return span;
  }

  public static void endSpan(
      OtelManager runtime,
      Span span,
      Attributes attributes,
      long startedAtNanos,
      Throwable error) {
    boolean success = error == null;
    if (span != null) {
      if (attributes != null) {
        span.setAllAttributes(attributes);
      }
      if (success) {
        span.setStatus(StatusCode.OK);
      } else {
        span.recordException(error);
        span.setStatus(StatusCode.ERROR, error.getMessage());
      }
      span.end();
    }
    if (runtime != null && runtime.enabled()) {
      runtime.recordRequest(System.nanoTime() - startedAtNanos, FabricOtelAttributes.withOutcome(attributes, success));
    }
  }

  public static Span currentSpan() {
    return Span.current();
  }

  public static void setCurrentSpanAttributes(Attributes attributes) {
    Span current = Span.current();
    if (!current.getSpanContext().isValid() || !current.isRecording() || attributes == null) {
      return;
    }
    current.setAllAttributes(attributes);
  }
}


FILE: OtelManagerImpl.java

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.manager;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.CloseSupport;
import io.opentelemetry.api.OpenTelemetry;
import io.opentelemetry.api.common.AttributeKey;
import io.opentelemetry.api.common.Attributes;
import io.opentelemetry.api.metrics.DoubleHistogram;
import io.opentelemetry.api.metrics.LongCounter;
import io.opentelemetry.api.metrics.Meter;
import io.opentelemetry.api.trace.Tracer;
import io.opentelemetry.api.trace.propagation.W3CTraceContextPropagator;
import io.opentelemetry.context.propagation.ContextPropagators;
import io.opentelemetry.exporter.otlp.http.metrics.OtlpHttpMetricExporter;
import io.opentelemetry.exporter.otlp.http.trace.OtlpHttpSpanExporter;
import io.opentelemetry.sdk.OpenTelemetrySdk;
import io.opentelemetry.sdk.metrics.SdkMeterProvider;
import io.opentelemetry.sdk.metrics.export.PeriodicMetricReader;
import io.opentelemetry.sdk.resources.Resource;
import io.opentelemetry.sdk.resources.ResourceBuilder;
import io.opentelemetry.sdk.trace.SdkTracerProvider;
import io.opentelemetry.sdk.trace.export.BatchSpanProcessor;
import java.util.concurrent.TimeUnit;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionApp;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.control.discovery.definitions.DefinitionEnvironment;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.OtelManager;
import org.pronzato.fabric.api.util.Strings;

public final class OtelManagerImpl implements OtelManager {
  private static final String INSTRUMENTATION_SCOPE = "fabric-lite";
  private static final AttributeKey<String> SERVICE_NAME = AttributeKey.stringKey("service.name");
  private static final AttributeKey<String> SERVICE_NAMESPACE =
      AttributeKey.stringKey("service.namespace");
  private static final AttributeKey<String> SERVICE_VERSION =
      AttributeKey.stringKey("service.version");
  private static final AttributeKey<String> DEPLOYMENT_ENV =
      AttributeKey.stringKey("deployment.environment.name");

  private final OpenTelemetrySdk sdk;
  private final SdkTracerProvider tracerProvider;
  private final SdkMeterProvider meterProvider;
  private final OtlpHttpSpanExporter spanExporter;
  private final OtlpHttpMetricExporter metricExporter;
  private final boolean tracesEnabled;
  private final boolean metricsEnabled;
  private final Tracer tracer;
  private final Meter meter;
  private final LongCounter requestCounter;
  private final DoubleHistogram requestDuration;

  private OtelManagerImpl(
      OpenTelemetrySdk sdk,
      SdkTracerProvider tracerProvider,
      SdkMeterProvider meterProvider,
      OtlpHttpSpanExporter spanExporter,
      OtlpHttpMetricExporter metricExporter,
      boolean tracesEnabled,
      boolean metricsEnabled) {
    this.sdk = sdk;
    this.tracerProvider = tracerProvider;
    this.meterProvider = meterProvider;
    this.spanExporter = spanExporter;
    this.metricExporter = metricExporter;
    this.tracesEnabled = tracesEnabled;
    this.metricsEnabled = metricsEnabled;
    this.tracer = sdk.getTracer(INSTRUMENTATION_SCOPE);
    this.meter = sdk.getMeter(INSTRUMENTATION_SCOPE);
    if (metricsEnabled) {
      this.requestCounter =
          meter.counterBuilder("fabric.requests")
              .setDescription("Fabric request count")
              .setUnit("{request}")
              .build();
      this.requestDuration =
          meter.histogramBuilder("fabric.request.duration")
              .setDescription("Fabric request duration")
              .setUnit("ms")
              .build();
    } else {
      this.requestCounter = null;
      this.requestDuration = null;
    }
  }

  public static OtelManager create(
      DefinitionEnvironment environment, DefinitionApp app, String defaultServiceName) {
    DefinitionEnvironment.Otel environmentOtel =
        environment == null ? null : environment.otel();
    DefinitionApp.Otel appOtel = app == null ? null : app.otel();
    if (environmentOtel == null || appOtel == null) {
      throw new IllegalArgumentException("OTEL config must be present in environment and app");
    }

    boolean tracesEnabled = !Boolean.FALSE.equals(environmentOtel.tracesEnabled());
    boolean metricsEnabled = !Boolean.FALSE.equals(environmentOtel.metricsEnabled());
    String endpoint = Strings.trimToNull(environmentOtel.otlpEndpoint());
    Resource resource = buildResource(environment, app, defaultServiceName);

    OtlpHttpSpanExporter spanExporter = null;
    var tracerBuilder = SdkTracerProvider.builder().setResource(resource);
    if (tracesEnabled && endpoint != null) {
      spanExporter =
          OtlpHttpSpanExporter.builder()
              .setEndpoint(exporterEndpoint(endpoint, "/v1/traces"))
              .build();
      tracerBuilder.addSpanProcessor(BatchSpanProcessor.builder(spanExporter).build());
    }
    SdkTracerProvider tracerProvider = tracerBuilder.build();

    OtlpHttpMetricExporter metricExporter = null;
    var meterBuilder = SdkMeterProvider.builder().setResource(resource);
    if (metricsEnabled && endpoint != null) {
      metricExporter =
          OtlpHttpMetricExporter.builder()
              .setEndpoint(exporterEndpoint(endpoint, "/v1/metrics"))
              .build();
      meterBuilder.registerMetricReader(
          PeriodicMetricReader.builder(metricExporter).setInterval(10, TimeUnit.SECONDS).build());
    }
    SdkMeterProvider meterProvider = meterBuilder.build();

    OpenTelemetrySdk sdk =
        OpenTelemetrySdk.builder()
            .setTracerProvider(tracerProvider)
            .setMeterProvider(meterProvider)
            .setPropagators(ContextPropagators.create(W3CTraceContextPropagator.getInstance()))
            .build();
    return new OtelManagerImpl(
        sdk,
        tracerProvider,
        meterProvider,
        spanExporter,
        metricExporter,
        tracesEnabled,
        metricsEnabled);
  }

  @Override
  public boolean enabled() {
    return true;
  }

  @Override
  public boolean tracesEnabled() {
    return tracesEnabled;
  }

  @Override
  public boolean metricsEnabled() {
    return metricsEnabled;
  }

  @Override
  public OpenTelemetry openTelemetry() {
    return sdk;
  }

  @Override
  public Tracer tracer() {
    return tracer;
  }

  @Override
  public Meter meter() {
    return meter;
  }

  @Override
  public void recordRequest(long durationNanos, Attributes attributes) {
    if (!metricsEnabled || requestCounter == null || requestDuration == null) {
      return;
    }
    Attributes safe = attributes == null ? Attributes.empty() : attributes;
    requestCounter.add(1L, safe);
    requestDuration.record(Math.max(0d, durationNanos / 1_000_000d), safe);
  }

  @Override
  public void close() {
    CloseSupport.closeQuietly(tracerProvider);
    CloseSupport.closeQuietly(meterProvider);
  }

  private static Resource buildResource(
      DefinitionEnvironment environment, DefinitionApp app, String defaultServiceName) {
    DefinitionEnvironment.Otel environmentOtel =
        environment == null ? null : environment.otel();
    DefinitionApp.Otel appOtel = app == null ? null : app.otel();
    String serviceName =
        Strings.firstNonBlank(
            appOtel == null ? null : appOtel.serviceName(),
            app == null || app.envelope() == null ? null : app.envelope().name(),
            defaultServiceName,
            "fabric-lite");
    String namespace = environmentOtel == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(environmentOtel.serviceNamespace());
    String serviceVersion = appOtel == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(appOtel.serviceVersion());
    String deploymentEnvironment =
        environmentOtel == null ? null : Strings.trimToNull(environmentOtel.deploymentEnvironment());

    ResourceBuilder builder = Resource.getDefault().toBuilder();
    builder.put(SERVICE_NAME, serviceName);
    builder.put(SERVICE_NAMESPACE, Strings.firstNonBlank(namespace, "fabric"));
    builder.put(SERVICE_VERSION, Strings.firstNonBlank(serviceVersion, "unknown"));
    builder.put(DEPLOYMENT_ENV, Strings.firstNonBlank(deploymentEnvironment, "unknown"));
    return builder.build();
  }

  private static String exporterEndpoint(String endpoint, String suffix) {
    String normalized = Strings.requireNonBlank(endpoint, "otel endpoint");
    if (normalized.endsWith("/")) {
      normalized = normalized.substring(0, normalized.length() - 1);
    }
    if (normalized.endsWith(suffix)) {
      return normalized;
    }
    return normalized + suffix;
  }

}

package org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.manager;

import io.opentelemetry.api.OpenTelemetry;
import io.opentelemetry.api.common.Attributes;

import org.pronzato.fabric.api.telemetry.OtelManager;

public final class OtelManagerNoop implements OtelManager {
  private static final OtelManager INSTANCE = new OtelManagerNoop();

  private final OpenTelemetry otel = OpenTelemetry.noop();
  private final Tracer tracer = otel.getTracer("fabric-lite");
  private final Meter meter = otel.getMeter("fabric-lite");

  private OtelManagerNoop() {}

  public static OtelManager instance() {
    return INSTANCE;
  }

  @Override
  public boolean enabled() {
    return false;
  }

  @Override
  public boolean tracesEnabled() {
    return false;
  }

  @Override
  public boolean metricsEnabled() {
    return false;
  }

  @Override
  public OpenTelemetry openTelemetry() {
    return otel;
  }

  @Override
  public Tracer tracer() {
    return tracer;
  }

  @Override
  public Meter meter() {
    return meter;
  }

  @Override
  public void recordRequest(long durationNanos, Attributes attributes) {}

  @Override
  public void close() {}
}
